Ukongeza , enziwe namalungiselelo okumisela iikomiti zewadi , njengamaqumrhu acebisayo enziwe ngabathunywa abaphuma kumasipala nakubahlali ukuhambisa ngendlela izidingo zabahlali nokunika izincomo kwibhunga . Inkqubo entlantlu-mbini yewadi nabathunywa eyakhiwe ngolwalamano ithetha ukuba abahlali banabathunywa ababanyulileyo nabaphendula kubo , abaza kuhambisa bade baqwalasele okuchaphazela abahlali . Chaza ubuchule obahlukeneyo kungquzulwano . Ukonga komhlalaphantsi nomsantsa wenzuzo yomngcipheko kumele uvalwe ngokulungiswa , kuquka namaqalela agunyazisiweyo , kucingelwa ukuxhasa la magalelo kubasebenzi abanomvuzo osezantsi nabamaxesha athile . Imvelaphi yangaphakathi : yenziwe ngumasipala uqobo , umzekelo , iirhafu neenkonzo ezinjengengqeshiso yezakhiwo kunye nemirhumo yomsebenzisi okanye iirhafu . Ukwakhiwa kwexesha elimisiweyo labahlali , uhlalutyo lwezimbo eziyimikhwa yethuba elide ukuze kuchongwe iinguqu-nguquko ezibuyelelayo ezisentloko kwaye kwenziwe ukuba abahlali babe nako ukuchonga ngokuhlalutya impumelelo okanye intsilelo yeentlobo ngeentlobo zongenelelo eziye zaphunyezwa ngelinge lokuphucula uphuhliso loluntu . Isazobe se-Venn , uhlalutyo lweempiliso , ingqiqo ngamacandelo nemisebenzi yokwalatha indlela zivelisa ukrwaqulo kwimeko yangoku yabahlali kwaye zikhanyisa iimpawu zobume belizwe , ubume bemeko engqongileyo nezezithuba , kananjalo njengohlalutyo lweempiliso neenkonzo zoluntu . Ukubeka iliso kwindlela eqhuba ngayo iprojekthi kubaluleke kakhulu ekuqinisekiseni ukuba ihamba ngokwesicwangciso nokuba imingcipheko emitsha neenguqu ezintsha ziyabonwa , zize ke zilungiselelwe kwixesha elizayo xa kuqhutywa . Amaqela eprojekthi asebenzisa iziphumo ekubekeni iliso kwinkqubo yeprojekthi . Iziphumo ziinkalo ekujoliswa kuzo ezibonakalisayo ukuba ngaba zifezekisekile na iinjongo zeprojekthi . Ngamanye amaxesha iziphumo kuthiwa ' ziziphumo ezingqinisisekayo ngobunjalo bazo ' . Iziphumo kufuneka ukuba zifaneleke , zanele , zithi gca , zikwazi ukungqinisiseka , zingabi nazindleko ziphezulu kwaye zifumaneke . Ii-CDW ngabantu abangovimba abasekelwe eluntwini nabasebenza kwimimandla abonyulelwe yona , apho bahlala khona nalapho baphendulwa khona kwimisebenzi yabo . Baxhaswa luluhlu lwamasebe karhulumente , ingakumbi urhulumente wengingqi . UMjikelo woNikezelo lweeNkonzo uboniswe kuluhlu olukwiphepha lama-28 . Lubonisa amanqanaba omjikelo noxanduva lomgangatho ngamnye karhulumente . Inqanam lamalungiselelo eenkonzo kulapho umsebenzi nokugcinwa kwenzeka khona , nokungowona malungiselelo eenkonzo . Likhusele okusingqongileyo kwendalo ngazo zonke iindlela , kushiyelwa isizukulwane esilandelayo ubuncinane umnikelo wexabiso elilinganayo . I-MFMA , 2003 ifuna ukuba uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala lungqinelane ne-IDP . Ukudibanisa uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala ne-IDP luqinisekisa ukuba amalungu ebhunga anoxanduva lokunikeza inkcazo kuluntu kwimimandla yalo kwakunye nokuba iimfuno zabo babameleyo ziyaqwalaselwa ukuze zibe yinene . Imiba ephambili ephawuliweyo kwi-IDP kufuneka idityaniswe kwinkcitho yekapitali kuhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala . UMgaqo-siseko woMzantsi Afrika unika isakhelo jikelele nalapho kungaqulunqwa khona imithetho nemimiselo . Unika amalungelo , inkululeko , igunya nokhuselo kubo bonke abantu kweli lizwe . Umisa amanqanam amathathu karhulumente welizwe - akazwelonke , awamaphondo nawengingqi . UMgaqo-siseko ubophelela urhulumente wengingqi ukuba athathe umsebenzi wophuhliso ngokuwunikezela eminye imisebenzi yophuhliso kurhulumente wengingqi . Ukulawula inguqu ngokubanzi : Ukuliqwalasela ifuthe leenguqu kwiinkalo eziphambili , nokuzinxibelelanisa nokwazi emakwenziwe ngazo . Ukuba nombono kwenza ukuba amalungu abahlali anambithe iminqweno yawo yophuhliso lwabahlali . Kunamandla ngakumbi xa , njengakumsebenzi olandelayo , kusekwe phezu kophengululo lwempahla exabisekileyo neenkonzo . Oku kukhuthaza abantu ukuphuhlisa umbono othembekileyo nonako ukufezeka kunye namanyathelo okuphumeza umbono . Umsebenzi ongakumbi kufuneka wenziwe ukugxininisa uxanduva abemi abanalo kuphuhliso olulolwabo nasekusebenzeni nabanye abakuluntu ekusombululeni iinkxalabo nemingeni . Intetho , " hlala uzole kwaye urhulumente uya kunikezela " kumele ukuba ivukelwe - ayinabunyani kwaye ayikho kugcino lwenkqubo karhulumente waseMzantsi Afrika . Zithini iziphumo zenkqubo malunga nophuhliso lwabasebenzi kunye nokuxhotyiswa kwamakhosikazi ? Olwamadoda lona ? Ingaba imeko nemo yamakhosikazi iphucukile ngenxa yenkqubo ? Unyulo olusesikweni , olukhululekileyo , olunobulungisa noluthembekileyo oluqhutywa ligunya elingenamkhethe lonyulo linika abemi ithuba lokwenza ukhetho lwabo . UMSEBENZI 2 Njengeqela , xoxa ngemiba ephambili yesicwangciso sewadi nize niphawule amanqanaba ekufuneka enze isicwangciso . Abuze nayiphina imali esetyenziswe ngokungafanelekanga abeva ngayo baze bacele ukuba iphandwe . Abathathi-nxaxheba bazahlula ngokwamaqela amancinci baze babhekiselele kwiziphumo ezithathu abazibeke phambili kumsebenzi odlulileyo . Abathathi-nxaxheba baziqhelanisa nenyathelo ngalinye lokwakha isicwangciso sewadi ngomdlalo-linganiso . Ababhexeshi abanikwe umsebenzi bayancedisa kule nkqubo , amaqela abhala phantsi iinkcukacha zabo kwifliptshathi ukuze iqela ngalinye limenywe ukuba linike ingcaciso kwingxoxo yomntu wonke . Bhexesha ingxoxo kumsebenzi oxoxa ngeempendulo zabathathi-nxaxheba kwaye ukuba bangasebenzisa iziphakamiso zabo kuluhlu lokukhangela baze bakhethe ezinye iindlela abangazisebenzisa ukubhexesha ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu . Izalathisi zeziphumo zilinganisa ' okuphume kwiprojekthi ' . Izalathisi kufuneka zimiselwe luluntu okanye noluntu ekubhekiselelwe kulo . Izalathisi zinentsingiselo kuphela ukuba zinxulumene nabantu ekubhekiselelwe kubo . Inani labantu abasuka kumaqela ekujoliswe kuwo kubulungisa kwezengqesho kwimigangatho emithathu ephambili yolawulo ngokuthobelana nesicwangciso esamkelweyo sikamasipala sobulungisa kwezengqesho . Aqinisekise ukuba amalungu oluntu ayazi ngesishwankathelo sohlahlo lwabiwo-mali nokukodwa okunxulumene newadi . Izikhokelo aziyiyo imithetho , kodwa zisisakhelo esinganceda oomasipala ukuba basungule iiKomiti zeWadi . Oomasipala bengingqi bahlukile kwaye badinga ukuqamba iindlela zokufumana izisombululo zabo zeengxaki abajamelana nazo ekuhlaleni . Oomasipala badinga ukuyila owabo umgaqo-nkqubo weeKomiti zeWadi nekufuneka wamkelwe libhunga likaMasipala . Ingaba iKomiti yeWadi inazo iindlela zokukhuthaza ngokusebenzayo ukuthatha inxaxheba kwamakhosikazi ngeKomiti yeWadi nezicwangciso-qhinga ukwandisa ukumelwa kwawo kwimigangatho yokwenza izigqibo ? Zeziphi ? ISicwangciso soPhuhliso sikaZwelonke sijolise ekubhangiseni ubuhlwempu nasekunciphiseni ukungalingani ngowama-2030 . UMzantsi Afrika ungafezekisa ezi njongo ngokufumana amandla ebantwini bawo , ukukhulisa uqoqosho olubandakanyayo , ukwakha ubunakho , ukufezekisa amandla oburhulumente nokuphakamisa ubunkokheli nobambiswano kuluntu luphela . Ukufezekiswa okuyimpumelelo kwesi sicwangciso kufuna ubunkokheli obunamandla obuvela kurhulumente , kumashishini , kubasebenzi nakuluntu lukarhulumente . Uvandlakanyo lwamaqela achaphazelekayo yinto ekufuneka imana ikrotyelwa njengokuba kuqhutywa nje ngeprojekthi . Kufuneka luhanjiswe novandlakanyo lweengxaki , zingahlulwa . Uphicotho lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwesini lunceda oorhulumente ukuba bagqibe ngendlela imigaqo-nkqubo ekufuneka ilungiselelwe ngayo , nendlela izixhobo zokusebenza ekufuneka zabiwe ngayo . Uphicotho lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwesini lunikezela amakhosikazi anesalathiso sesibophelelo sikarhulumente ukuba ajonge iimfuno ezizodwa zamakhosikazi namalungelo kukhathalelo lwempilo , imfundo nomsebenzi . Iintlanganiso ezibanjwa emva kweenyanga ezimbini zokubeka iliso zibalulekile kwikomiti emva kokuba isicwangciso siphuhliswe njengendlela yokukhuthaza abantu malunga nokufezekiswa kwesicwangciso nokugcina abantu bephendula ngenkqubela abayenzileyo . Ukudityaniswa kwenyathelo loluntu kummandla neempendulo ekuqinisekiseni ugqithiso lwengxelo kwibhunga . Ukunyusa ukukhula koqoqosho ngaphaya komyinge we-5 ekhulwini ngonyaka kuya kufuna ukuba amashishini nabasebenzi baqinisele umbono ekwabelwanayo ngawo . Ilizwe alikaqalisi ukulwa nezinto zasekuhlaleni ezinegalelo kurhwaphilizo . Imbali yoMzantsi Afrika yenkxaso nenkuthazo ebonelelwa ngurhulumente yenza mfiliba ngakumbi imigangatho yeenqobo ezisesikweni . Amava amanye amazwe abonisa ukuba ngentando yopolitiko nokusebenza okugcinakalayo kwezicwangciso-qhinga ezichanekileyo , urhwaphilizo lungancitshiswa ngokubonakalayo nokuthenjwa luluntu kubuyiselwe . Ukukhetha abantu abafanelekileyo kumcimbi othile . Umzekelo , ukuba ngumcimbi ongezempilo , oonompilo , izigulane , abentetho-ntuthuzelo kukhathalelo lwasekhaya , abacebisi basekuhlaleni , njl. bangaba ngabantu abaza kudinga ukubandakanywa . Ukumelwa kwamaqela anomdla - Zeziphi iinkqubo ezikhoyo ukuze ndifumane igalelo elisuka kumaqela awohlukeneyo anomdla ? Ingaba kufuneka ndiseke iintlanganiso zarhoqo neqela ngalinye elinomdla ? Qinisekisa ukuba uthathe ixesha lokwazisa iKomiti yeWadi kwiqela ngalinye elinomdla uze ulinikeze iinkcukacha zakho zoqhagamshelwano . Umbhexeshi uba ngumkhokeli aze alawule inkqubo . IiKomiti zeWadi zingabizwa ukuba zizokubhexesha intlanganiso ukuze zifumane igalelo loluntu kwisiCwangciso soPhuhliso oluManyanisiweyo okanye kwisiseko seNkqubo yoLawulo loKwenziwa koMsebenzi ( PMS ) . Amaqela abahlali aqukaniswa ngabantu beemvelaphi ezahluka-hlukeneyo , imidla eyahluka-hlukeneyo , iinkcubeko ezahluka-hlukeneyo , amaqela ezenkolo , eentlanga neengeniso . Ukulungelelanisa nokunika indawo le midla yahluka-hlukeneyo ngumceli-mngeni omkhulu . Imibandela efana nemithombo yobutyebi enyiniweyo , ukufikelela kuyo nolawulo lwayo zizinto ezandisa le miceli-mngeni . Ababhexeshi be-CBP kufuneka baqinisekise umelo olusebenzayo ngamathuba enkqubo yezicwangciso baze banike ithuba lokuvakaliswa kwemidla eyahluka-hlukeneyo , impikiswano nokuvunyelwana ngayo . Indima yabo kukudala ubume bemeko eqinisekisa inxaxheba eyiyeyona inkulu yamaqela kwinkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso . Ithini imigaqo neenkqubo zeenkqubo zokwenza izigqibo ? Ingaba ziqala phezulu ukuya ezantsi ? Ingaba zivumela ukuthatha inxaxheba ? Ingaba akhona amathuba okwenza ilinge kubasebenzi abaphuma ngaphandle , abaphathi nabanye abangekho kulawulo ; ukwenzela ukuba negalelo kwizigqibo eziphambili zeKomiti yeWadi ? Ukuthatha inxaxheba okubonwa ziiarhente zangaphandle njengendlela yokufezekisa iinjongo , ngakumbi ngeendleko ezicuthiweyo . Abantu bangathatha inxaxheba ngokwenza amaqela ahlangabezana neenjongo ezinxulumene neprojekthi . Ukubandakanyeka okulolo hlobo kukholisa ukuvela kuphela emva kokuba iiarhente zangaphandle sezenze izigqibo ezikhulu . Ibhunga elikhethiweyo yiforam yokugqibela yokwenza isigqibo ngee-IDP . Indima yedemokrasi ethatha inxaxheba kukwazisa , uthetha-thethwano nokuphosa igalelo kwezo zigqibo , ngexesha lenkqubo yocwangciso / ukwenziwa kwesigqibo . Ncedisa abathathi-nxaxheba ngamanqaku esifundo kwiphepha lama-75 ukuya kwelama-76 . Abathathi-nxaxheba mabazobe iajenda yentlanganiso yeKomiti yeWadi nentlanganiso kawonke-wonke . Ibhunga libhengeze ithenda yokunikezela ipasele zokutya kubahlali . Ithenda yanikwa umntu wangaphandle , kodwa abanye bacinga ukuba sikhona isikhundla sokwenza lo msebenzi kumgangatho wengingqi . Ikhontraka isebenzise abantu bangaphandle abangawaziyo ummandla , ngamanye amaxesha iipasele zokutya azifiki kubantu bazo . Kukho unxibelelwano olungeluhlanga phakathi kwekhontraka , iKomiti yeWadi noluntu . Sele kukho iingxaki ezininzi ezivelayo kwaye uluntu lucinga ukuba iKomiti yeWadi kufuneka kubekho ekwenzayo ngale ngxaki . Ngowama-2030 , abantu abahlala eMzantsi Afrika kumele bazive bekhuselekile kwaye bangabi noloyiko lolwaphulo mthetho . Amabhinqa , abantwana namaqela asemngciphekweni kumele bazive bekhuselekile . Kumele bathembele kwisixokelelwano sobulungisa bolwaphulo-mthetho ukuze sinqande ngokuyimpumelelo ze kutshutshiswe nabophuli-mthetho abadlakathekisa umntu nokhuseleko loluntu . INkonzo yamaPolisa aseMzantsi Afrika namapolisa esixeko kumele abe ngamaziko obungcali anabasebenzi abanezakhono , abanentlonelo , abangabantu abaneenqobo ezisesikweni abaxabise imisebenzi yabo nokukhonza uluntu . IiKomiti zeWadi zibalulekile ekuqinisekiseni ukuthatha inxaxheba kwabahlali bengingqi kwimisebenzi kamasipala . Oku kuquka ukubeka esweni umsebenzi kamasipala nokuphosa igalelo kwi-PMS . Kukho imfuno esemthethweni kamasipala yokuba aquke iikomiti zengingqi , kwiiKomiti zeWadi , ekumiseni ii-KPI neethagethi zomsebenzi kwakunye nokuqinisekisa ukuthatha inxaxheba kwabahlali ekubekeni esweni nasekuhleleni ngokutsha izalathisi . Kungakho imidla ephikisanayo kwiiwadi ezahlukeneyo kumasipala kwaye le midla kufuneka iqwalaselwe xa kusenziwa i-PMS . IKomiti yeWadi nganye kumasipala inganomdla wokuqinisekisa ukuba umdla wayo iqukiwe . Umzekelo , iwadi enoshishino oluncinci nezinga eliphezulu lokungabikho kwemisebenzi lingafuna ukubeka phambili ukudala indawo ekhuthaza ushishino . Enye iwadi inganesikhululo seenqwelo-moya kuze ukuxhalaba kwayo kube yingxolo nongcoliseko . I-PMS kufuneka izame ukuquka imidla emininzi kangangoko ikwaqwalasela okuyinene kumasipala lowo . Urhulumente wengingqi udinga ukuqinisekisa ukuba kukho ulawulo olululo ukukhusela ingeniso , iiasethi nemali nezakhiwo zikamasipala ekuyichitheni , kwilahleko nasebuseleni . Kubalulekile ukuba kufunyaniswe iimfuno zabahlali phambi kokuba kuqhutywe iprojekthi okanye umsebenzi wophuhliso kwindawo leyo . Le dayagram ikweli phepha lilandelayo ibonakalisa eminye yemiba ebalulekileyo efanele ukuqwalaselwa . Yasabela njani inkqubo koondoqo bamaqela awodwa ekujoliswe kuwo phakathi kwamakhosikazi namadoda ekubhekiselelwe kuwo ? Umphulaphuli - ukubhexesha kufuna izakhono zokumamela , jonga iSahluko 2 xa ufuna ulwazi olongeziweyo ngezakhono zokumamela . Eyona ndlela iqhelekileyo yokubonakalisa ifuthe lengxaki nezinto eziyibangayo kukusebenzisa umthi wengxaki . Injongo yalo mzobo wedayagram kukubonisa imiba abanqwenela ukuyoyisa abamaqela achaphazelekayo , bancedise ekuqulunqweni kweenjongo zeeprojekthi ezifanelekileyo nezithe ngqo . Iinkqubo zikarhulumente zokuthengiselana zenza mfiliba umda kwimiba yorhwaphilizo , nenkqubo yokuthengiselana karhulumente iye yenziwa yanamagunya karhulumente agqithisileyo . Ugxininiso lokuthobela ngokutikisha ibhokisi kwenza inkqubo ibe nendleko , ibengumthwalo , ingabi nampumelelo nokuvuleleka kubuqhetseba . Sicebisa ukujongwa okusembindini kubaniki maxabiso abakhulu nabexesha elide , kwenziwe kungabi semthethweni ukuba abasebenzi bakarhulumente basebenze kuhlobo oluthile lamashishini nokwenza abantu babenoxanduva lokulahlekelwa kumatyala angqiniweyo orhwaphilizo . Ungenelelo luthelekelelwa ekongezeni phakathi komyinge we-0.1 ne-0.2 ekhulwini ngonyaka kwizinga lokukhula kwenani labemi kwixesha lika-2030 . Ukungabikho kwexesha - Amalungu asekuhlaleni ixesha elininzi adla ixesha nemigudu ezama ukuphila kwaye abafumaneki lula ukuza ezintlanganisweni . Oku kudla ngokwenzeka koomama nakumalungu angasebenziyo asekuhlaleni . I-PMS ne-IDP zisebenza kunye njengomasipala njengoko zisenza imilinganiselo yokuba usebenza kangakanani umasipala kwi-IDP , njengoko i-IDP isisiseko sonikezelo lweenkonzo nophuculo lwabahlali . I-PMS kufuneka ijongane neemeko zikamasipala . Kufuneka ithungelane noovimba bakamasipala ngokuhambelana nemiba ephambili , iinjongo eziphambili , izalathisi neethagethi ezikwi-IDP yabo . UMphathiswa kaRhulumente wePhondo neNgingqi umise inani lee-KPI ezinyanzelisiweyo . Oomasipala kufuneka badibanise oku nezinye ii-KPI ezisebenzayo kwii-PMS zabo . Isicwangciso esisebenzayo esisekwe kubahlali sifuna ukubandakanywa kwawo onke amaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya afana nabahlali , amalungu ebhunga , amagosa aseburhulumenteni kamasipala , amalungu amaqonga olawulo lwabahlali afana neeKomiti zeWadi nee-CBO , abaniki beenkonzo , iinkokeli zomthonyama , amaqela anomdla kwingingqi nabeshishini lengingqi kwinkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso . Iqela ngalinye elichaphazeleka ngokwegunya linendima eliyidlalayo kwi-CBP . Ukongeza kwintando yopolitiko , urhwaphilizo kumele luliwe kwimida emithathu : ukunqanda , ukuthintela nemfundo . Ukunqanda kunceda abantu baqonde ukuba bangabanjwa kwaye bagwetywe . Ukuthintela kumalunga nenkqubo ( ulwazi , uphicotho njalo njalo njalo ) eyenza kubenzima ekuqhubeni urhwaphilizo . Ubukhulu borhwaphilizo ekuhlaleni kufuneka buliwe ngokujolisa kwiinqobo ezisemgangathweni , ngemfundo . Intlaninge yobuthathaka bobume kumele koyiswe ukuba i-Afrika iza kutolika ukukhula okukhawulezayo nemfuno ephezulu yeempahla zorhwebo zibe yingqesho enyukayo namazinga okuphila . Ngokubalulekileyo , amakhonkco othutho oluphantsi nothungelwano lwezakhiwo , nangokunjalo nemiqobo yexabiso okanye yokungabikho kwexabiso , inyusa indleko yokwenza ushishino nokutotoba kutyalo-mali norhwebo lwangaphakathi . Amaziko omthetho abuthathaka , kwaye , nakwezinye iimeko , ulawulo oluphantsi anyusa imingcipheko yotyalo-mali . Umfanekiso uphucuka ngokuthe chu , kodwa imingeni ihleli ihleli ihleli , kuquka nakuPhuhliso loLuntu kuMazantsi e-Afrika ( SADC ) , olujongene nemiqobo enxulumene kwizakhiwo , imiqobo kurhwebo nakulawulo . Logama uMzantsi Afrika uya kufumanisa kunzima ukukhuphisana ekwenzeni izinto ngabanezakhono ezisezantsi ngenxa yobume bendleko ephezulu , amazwe amaninzi kwilizwekazi angakhuphisana njengoko iindleko zokuvelisa zinyuka kwi-East Asia . Imigaqo elandelwayo enempumelelo kufuneka iphonononge indlela iiyantlukwano ezingathi zivunywe kwaye zixatyiswe ngayo ukwenzela ukuba onke amalungu oluntu ekuhlaleni abe angaqukwa kwindlela enceda umasipala ukuba aphumeze iinjongo zakhe ekuqinisekiseni ukuhanjiswa kweenkonzo okunempumelelo ngokuba uluntu luthathe inxaxheba . Kodwa ke , ukukhuthaza nokwamkela ukungafani akukho malunga nokumisa izinto emakujoliswe kuzo kuphela , okanye kwa ukufunda ukuxabisa iiyantlukwano zabantu , koko kufuna ukuba kudalwe ulwamkelo kwaye kukhuthazwe unyamezelwano nokuhloniphana . Funda umzekelo wophando okwiSahluko 5 , 5.6 nize nifunde ngokwamaqela ngendlela onokujongana ngayo nenqanam ngalinye . Abathathi-nxaxheba bajonga umzobo okwiphepha 15 oqwalasela inqanam ngalinye kwinkqubo yonxibelelwano . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zibe namalungu angekho ngaphezulu kwe-10 akhethiweyo namele iintlobo-ntlobo zabahlali . Ibhunga ngalinye lenza imithetho yokukhetha amalungu eKomiti yeWadi . Kodwa ke , amalungu ayakhethwa , nokuba kungevoti efihliweyo kwintlanganiso yabahlali okanye ngokwenani lezandla eziphakanyisiweyo , kufuneka kuvunyelwane ngawo onke amaqela achaphazelekayo nengxelo ecacileyo yenkqubo kufuneka ifumaneke kuwonke-wonke ukuze luyijonge ukuba lunqwenela njalo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka abe ngamalungu evoti abhalisiweyo kwaye kufuneka abe ngamalungu athatha inxaxheba , athenjiweyo nahloniphekileyo eluntwini ingakumbi kwicandelo alimeleyo . Ababhexeshi bewadi - abanokufunyanwa kumalungu anyuliweyo eKomiti yeWadi okanye asenokuba ngamalungu ahloniphekileyo oluntu afana namavolontiya , iinkokeli zenkolo nezezimvo , okanye abantu abanolwazi eluntwini abafana nabasebenzi bakarhulumente abathathe umhlalaphantsi , iititshala , inkokeli yeqela labafazi , njl.njl. Kuzo zonke iziganeko mababe semandleni babe nothakazelelo lokunceda kuphuhliso nempumezo yezicwangciso ezisekwe kubahlali . Kumsebenzi olandelayo iziphumo ezinqwenelekayo kumaqela ezentlalo zongezelelwa kwi-SWOT kuwo onke amaqela ezentlalo ahluka-hlukeneyo , kudaleke ingcinga ebanzi yabahlali . Oku kukwanceda ngokushiya-shiyaniswa kweziphumo eziphambili . Lingakanani ixesha elifunekayo lokugqitywa kweenkqubo namaphulo aseWadini yawo ? Imfundo ephezulu . Ukusebenza kwamaziko akhoyo kusukela kwaphezulu ehlabathini ukuya kwaphakathi . Ukuphuculwa kobulunga obuqhubekayo buyafuneka njengokuba isixokelelwano sisanda kwisantya esiphakathi . Umngeni omkhulu kukuba imfundo yesikolo ephantsi yandisa indleko yokuveliswa kwabathweswe izidanga , nenani elincinci ngokubonakalyo labafundi abamnyama abathweswe izidanga kwiiyunivesithi . Ukuthatha inxaxheba okwandayo nesantya sothweso sidanga , kunomkhethe wedigri yeyunivesithi yeminyaka emine , kudityaniswe nezifundo zokuwelisa nenkxaso engakumbi kwiiyunivesithi ekuncedeni abafundi abamnyama abasuka kumakhaya angathathi ntweni , kungahle kuveze iziphumo eziphezulu . Ikomiti yeWadi ifanele ukuba nesicwangciso sonyaka esandlala ngokucacileyo izinto ekufuneka zenziwe kuqala ngokokushiyana kwazo nezinto elindele ukuziphumeza . Oku kuya kunceda iKomiti yeWadi ukubona ukuba ingaba ikuphumezile na oko ebithe iza kukwenza . Kwakhona oko kuya kunceda iKomiti yeWadi ukunika ingxelo kumasipala , njengoko inako ukunika ingxelo ngenyanga nganye ithelekise nesicwangciso sayo samanyathelo . Ukuba usebenzisa isixhobo esinjenge-overhead , okanye ifliptshathi , funda ukuyisebenzisa kwangaphambili . Isicwangciso - IKomiti yeWadi isebenza ngokusondeleyo kuceba ukufumana izinto emazibekwe phambili nokuqinisekisa ukuba le miba iphambili iyaqukwa xa kusenziwa uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali naxa kusenziwa izicwangciso zeprojekthi . IKomiti yeWadi idinga ukuba nesicwangciso sonyaka esandlala ngokucacileyo izinto eziphambili nokuba iceba ukuphumeza ntoni . Oku kuza kunceda iKomiti yeWadi ukubona ukuba iyiphumezile na into ebifuna ukuyiphumeza . Kwakhona iza kunceda iKomiti yeWadi ukuba inike ingxelo kumasipala , kuba inganika ingxelo rhoqo ngenyanga ikhangela kwisicwangciso sayo sezinto eza kuzenza . Ngumbono omhle kwiKomiti yeWadi ukulungiselela intlanganiso eyodwa ngokukhawuleza kangangoko ukwenza isicwangciso sokuza kwenziwa . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka aqinisekise ukuba isicwangciso sawo siyafikeleleka sinokuphunyezwa . Isicwangciso sisixhobo sokuchaza indawo apho abahlali bafuna ukuya khona , sisixhobo sokufaka izindululo kwi-IDP , sokubeka iliso kwinkqubo yokufezekisa isicwangciso , kwaye sinokuhlaziywa ngonyaka ngamnye njengoko zisiya phambili iiprojekthi , kuvela nemicimbi ephambili emitsha . Xa sesiphuhlisiwe isicwangciso , kunokuphuculwa ubunini ngokuqwalasela ukuba yeyiphi enye indlela ekunokunxityelelwa ngayo iziqulatho kuluhlu olubanzi lwamaqela abahlali , kubandakanywa izishwankathelo zeelwimi zengingqi , iipowusta , imidlalo yeqonga . Oku kufanele ukuxoxwa kwintlanganiso yabahlali yokugqibezela . Kubalulekile ukuba imiba ephambili efana nombono kunye neenjongo ziguqulelwe kulwimi lwabantu bendawo . Ukuguqula uqoqosho kukwathetha ukutshintsha iipatheni zobunini nolawulo . Ukuzakuthi ga ngoku , imizamo yokutshintshela ubunini bezinto ezivelisayo akukavezi ziphumo ezinqwenelekayo , nezikimu zokwabelana ngobunini zabaqeshwa zidlala indima ebonakala kancinci . Inyathelo elizithembileyo nemigqalisela ethe gca ziyimfuneko . Izixhobo zenkqubo zokukhuthaza icandelo labucala ukuba litshintshe iipatheni zobunini okuquka amakhadi okunika inqaku ngokuzithandela , ukufunyanwa kowiso-mthetho , amalungiselelo eempepha-mvume ( afana nothungelwano ngocingo nemigodi ) nemali yophuhliso . Isikhundla samaziko sibaluleke kakhulu kwimpumelelo yale ndlela , kuquka nokubuyiselwa ekujonganeni nonxulumano ekukhutshiswana ngalo phakathi kwamaqumrhu emveli nawomgaqo-siseko . Ingaba uluhlu lovavanyo ( nokubeka esweni ) luquka iimfuneko ezicacileyo zokuqinisekisa ukubandakanywa kwesini nolwazi lokungahlulwa ngokwesini ? Ukunciphisa indleko yokuphila kwimizi yabakwizinga lemisebenzi esezantsi abanomvuzo ophantsi . Ukungalingani nobuhlwempu kungajongwana nako ngokunyusa iingeniso ngokukhula kwemveliso nokunciphisa indleko yokuphila . Ukuzibophelela kumgangatho wokuphila ongowona umncinane kuya kuqinisekisa ukuba yonke imizi ingathatha inxaxheba ngokunentsingiselo kuqoqosho . Iindleko zokutya , uthutho lwabahambi nezindlu kumele zicuthwe , logama kuphakanyiswa ubulunga bemfundo nokhathalelo lwempilo olusimahla okanye olunendleko esezantsi . IKomiti yeWadi ingasungula ikomitana ikomitana okanye ezimbini ibandakanye imibutho yasekuhlaleni kwezi komitana . Bonke ababandakanyekayo ewadini bayakhuthazwa ukuba bathathe inxaxheba kwiikomitana ezihambelanayo nomdla wabo . Indlela esekwe ekomeleleni isuka kwisicwangciso esisekwe kwiingxaki , esijolisa kwizithintelo , iye kwindlela yombono ekhangela apho uluntu lunqwenela ukuba khona nendlela yokuya apho . ISicwangciso soPhuhliso Olumanyanisiweyo ( Integrated Development Plan ( IDP ) ) ) siyamxelela umasipala ngeenjongo , kwaye neeprojekthi eziqhutywayo ziyachazwa sisicwangciso esi . Kwangokunjalo , isicwangciso sewadi sikholisa ngokuba siyibeke imiqathango yeeprojekthi ezikhethiweyo yiKomiti yeWadi . Ukhuseleko lwasekuhlaleni luzisa imbumba yamanyama yasekuhlaleni kubomi nokuqinisekisa umgangatho wokuphila osisiseko . Lukwadlala indima ebaluleke kakhulu ekuncedeni imizi nokulawula imingcipheko yobomi yeentsapho , nokuthomalalisa ukutshintsha kweshishini lezabasebenzi , kunegalelo kuqoqosho olubhetyebhetye kakhulu . Ibhunga leWadi Z limise izikhokelo zokunyulwa kweKomiti yeWadi . Umasipala ubhengeze kwii-ofisi zebhunga , ezikolweni , kumaziko enkolo , iiklinikhi zengingqi kwakunye nezinye iindawo zikawonke-wonke ukuba kuza kusekwa iKomiti yeWadi nendima kunye nemisebenzi yayo . Isaziso sicacisa kwiphetshana lolwazi ukuba umbutho okanye icandelo ( lize lichaze amacandelo ) angathumela unyulo kwibhunga lengingqi . Eli phetshana likwachaza nomhla wonyulo , indawo nexesha lize limeme abavoti ababhalisiweyo ukuba bazimase oku . Entlanganisweni , amagama abantu abanyuliweyo afundiwe waze umntu ngamnye onyuliweyo waziswa kwintlanganiso waze wacelwa ukuba azichaze ukuba ungubani na , emele eliphina icandelo . Abanyulwa bebengama-28 . Amagama abanyulwa abhalwe kwiphepha lokuvota baze abathathi-nxaxheba entlanganisweni bacelwa ukuba bavotele amalungu ali-10 . Abagqatswa abali-10 abafumene iivoti ezininzi baseka iKomiti yeWadi . Okwesibini , umasipala kufuneka amise ukuba zeziphina iinkonzo ekufuneka zandisiwe okanye ziphuculwe . Ingaba iindawo ezithile zoluntu kummandla zimdaka kakhulu okanye azihoywanga ? Umanejala kamasipala uqeshwe libhunga kwikhontraka yokwenziwa komsebenzi wolawulo lweminyaka emihlanu . Uyintloko yolawulo lwebhunga ekwanoxanduva lokulawula iimali , ukuqesha nokululeka abasebenzi . Amagosa kamasipala asebenzela ulawulo aze azalisekise imigaqo-nkqubo yebhunga . Isiphumo seli nqanam yi-IDP eyamkelweyo kamasipala . Ulawulo olulandeliswayo - Ikomiti yeWadi inako ukucela iingxelo ezinikwa rhoqo malunga neeprojekthi neenkonzo . Ulawulo lwenkqubo yemfundo . Ukunciphisa imiphetho yolawulo lwabantu abasemagunyeni kuya kwenza ukuba ubutyebi bufumaneke ngakumbi ekuxhaseni izikolo nootitshala . Umthetho jikelele oqhelekileyo kukuba amangenelelo , axhasayo nalungisayo omabini , kufuneka alamane ngokugqwethiweyo ekusebenzeni kwesikolo . Ngale ndlela , izikolo eziqhuba kakuhle zinganikwa inkululeko yokuqhubekeka nomsebenzi , nje ukuba kukho ukuphucuka okubonakalayo . Senza iingcebiso ezizodwa ezijoliswe kwinkxaso engcono ezikolweni , ukubonelela izinto eziyimfuneko ezisisiseko kwimfundo elungileyo nokulinganisela izinto ezilungileyo . Sicebisa ukuba kubekho ugayo lokuphucula amaziko kwizikolo ezihlelelekileyo , ingakumbi emaphandleni . Xa iphela le seshoni abahlali baya kuba nombono wothetha-thethwano owabiwayo ukwenzela uphuhliso lwabahlali . I-Local Government : Municipal Finance Management Act , 2003 ( MFMA ) ihambelana kakhulu ne-Municipal Systems Act ( MSA ) , 2000 njengoko yomibini ijongana neenkqubo zangaphakathi kurhulumente wengingqi ; iinkqubo zothethwano ; iinkqubo zokwenziwa komsebenzi kunye neendlela zokuphucula uxanduva lokunikeza inkcazo . I-MFMA icacisa indlela inkqubo yezemali kamasipala esebenza ngayo kwakunye nendima edlalwa ngamalungu ebhunga ekwenzeni ukuba isebenze . Kubonisa uvelwano nentlonipho komnye , nokuba ukholelwa entweni na , amazwi okanye indlela yokuziphatha . Kukho iziphumo zorhwebo ekumele zithathelwe ingqalelo ekuzuzeni kwizimbiwa . UMzantsi Afrika uphulukana nesabelo soshishino lwamazwe ngamazwe kwiimveliso ezifana neferokhrowum . Nangona kunjalo , ukusetyenzwa kwenyathelo lokuqala okanye ukunyityilikiswa kufuna amandla kunye neemali ezininzi , okunokuxhuzula amandla neemali kude kwamanye amacandelo . UMzantsi Afrika kumele ube nomkhethe malunga neengingqi ojonge ukuxhasa inzuzo yenyathelo lokuqala kuzo . Iingingqi emazijongwe kuqala kumele zibandakanye ezo apho isikhundla esifanelekileyo sele sikhona kakade , okanye apho ukuzuza kungathi kukhokelele kukwenziwa kwezinto okukumsinga osezantsi . Ukuzuzisa zonke izimbiwa zelizwe akukuba kuyenzeka kungekuko ukuba kuyimfuneko ekuphuhliseni icandelo lokuvelisa elikhulu . Vuma uze wamkele umsindo wakho . Cinga ngawo . Musa ukwenza ngathi awunawo okanye ungafuni ukujongana nawo . Ukuba wenza njalo , ungenzeka ngexesha elingafanelekanga uze ke uye ebantwini abangengabo . Uphicotho lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali oluqinisekisa ukubandakanywa kweemfuno zamakhosikazi lubhekiselela kuphicotho lwenkcitho nengeniso karhulumente kumakhosikazi namantombazana ngokuthelekisa namadoda namakhwenkwe . Uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwesini asilohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwahlukileyo ukwenzela amakhosikazi kwaye alujonganga kuphela ukwandisa ukuchitha kwiiprojekthi eziphathelele kumakhosikazi . Into oluyenzayo kukuqinisekisa ukuba iimfuno zamakhosikazi ziyaqukwa kwaye ziyanikezelwa . Esi sisicwangciso soMzantsi Afrika . Sibonelela ngobume besicwangciso-qhinga esibanzi esikhokela izinto ezingundoqo emazikhethwe namanyathelo . Impumelelo yaso iya kuxhomekeka kubo bonke abemi boMzantsi Afrika ekuthatheni uxanduva ngesicwangciso , bekhokelwe nguMongameli nayiKhabhinethi . Ikomiti yeWadi imele imidla engafaniyo ebandakanya amaqela obomi besixeko okanye abahlawuli beenkonzo , imibutho yophuhliso , imibutho yabasebenzi , imibutho yamashishini , amaqela abafazi , ulutsha kunye nemibutho esekwe kwinkolo . Ulawulo lweeprojekthi lubandakanya ukuqhutywa kwesicwangciso , kubandakanya uvandlakanyo lwendlela ezihamba ngayo izinto nokuhlaziywa kwesicwangciso eso ngokweengxaki okanye iinguqulelo zeemeko eziye zivele njengokuba kuqhutywa nje . eYiphutha mandulo , amadoda ayehlala ekhaya kwaye esenza umsebenzi wokoluka . Amakhosikazi ayephatha ishishini losapho . Amakhosikazi ayefumana ilifa lepropati kwaye amadoda ayengalifumani . Amacwecwe emiba yeeprojekthi ' angumsebenzi wephepha ' ofuna ukulungiswa unikelwe kwibhunga okanye kumasebe amacandelo . Ayingxelo yento ekugqitywe kuyo ukuze onke amaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya akwazi ukuyibeka iliso inkqubela phambili . Imvelaphi enokubakho yongquzulwano kwiiwadi zabathathi-nxaxheba . Ukusekwa kwezilinganiso ezintsha nobume besithuba bukazwelonke . Ubudlelwane nemibutho yasekuhlaleni njengemibutho engekho ngaphantsi kukarhulumente , imibutho esekelwe kwinkolo inganika iqonga lokunika imiba nolwazi olunikezelwa kubahlali noluvela kubahlali . Umsebenzi 2 Phawula imithetho-siseko ephambili yokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu jikelele . UMBUZO 2 Ungazisombulula njani iingxaki zonikezelo lweenkonzo ? Izixhobo ezenza i-LFA zingasetyenziswa ekucukucezeni le projekthi icetywayo , ngeenjongo zokuvavanya ukufaneleka kwayo nokuba ingakwazi na ukwenzeka . Kumxholo weeKomiti zeWadi abadlali-ndima bangakhuthaza umgaqo-nkqubo osebenzayo nobonakalayo wokucwangcisa umba wesini kuyo yonke imigaqo-nkqubo neenkqubo , ukwenzela ukuba phambi kokuba izigqibo zithathwe uphicotho lweziphumo kumakhosikazi namadoda lube luyenziwa . I-PCM isekelwe kumjikelo weprojekthi kwaye iziqwalasela ngokutsha zonke iinkalo zeprojekthi ngalo lonke ixesha iqhuba iprojekthi . Oku ke kuthetha ukuba naziphi na inguqulelo okanye imingeni iyabandakanywa ekuqulunqweni nasekucwangcisweni kwenyathelo elilandelayo . Kwi-LFA iziphumo ngelinye ixesha kuye kuthiwe ' ziziphumo ezingqinisiseka ngokungathathi cala ' . Oku kunjalo , kuba kaloku nabani na kufuneka akwazi ukuba azingqinisise iziphumo ' ngaphandle kokuthatha icala ' aze naye afikelele kwisiphumo esifanayo ; kungakhathaliseki nokuba , ngokwezimvo , umntu lowo ungqinisisayo ume phi na . Inyhikityha yeHIV / AIDS ibonise ubunakho boMzantsi Afrika bokwenza iimpazamo zasekuhlaleni nezopolitiko ezisisikhumbuzo - nakanjalo nobunakho bokuzilungisa nokufezekisa inkqubo enkulu ngokusebenzayo . Impumelelo yesixokelelwano sempilo ekulawuleni inyikityha kwiminyaka emihlanu edlulileyo iyancomeka . Kodwa akukho sithuba sokwaneliseka . Kukho imfuno eqhubekekayo yemfundo , uthintelo , uvavanyo nonyango . Ukuthotywa kwesantya sosuleleko olutsha kuya kunciphisa isinyanzeliso kwisixokelelwano sempilo yoluntu . Kodwa , nkqu ukuba kukho usuleleko olutsha , kuya kuhlala kukho inani elivisayo labantu abaneHIV abafuna unyango , bebeka imingeni eqhubekekayo kwisantya sokusuleleka sisifo sephepha nomgcipheko wokuveza ubunzima bokungeva mayeza kweHIV . Inyhikityha neempembelelo zayo kwinkqubo yoluntu kungathanda ukuba nenkani ubuncinane kwesinye isizukulwane . Kusenokwenzeka zibe zibini . Inkqubo makuvunyelwane ngayo ngabo bonke abachaphazelekayo kanti iingxelo ezibhalwe ngokucacileyo zendlela ekuqhutywa ngayo mazifumaneke kuwonke-wonke ukuze aziphicothe . Isini iba yingqikelelo etyhutyha yonke imiba yobomi . Umbono wokulingana ngokwesini awukunyini ukuthatha inxaxheba kwamadoda ; ngokuphikisayo , uvumela umsebenzi ongcono noxhathise macala phakathi kwamadoda namakhosikazi , okuya kuthi ngembuyekezo kukhokelele kwiziphumo zolondolozo eziphucukileyo . Amanyathelo okulungisa kwiindawo zomsebenzi kumele ajoliswe kuphuhliso lorhwebo , ukufikelela kuqeqesho , ukubhekela phambi kokufundela ubungcali nokucebisa . Iphepha leNgcaciso-nkqubo ngoRhulumente weeNgingqi lisisakhelo somgaqo-nkqubo wokuqala wesizwe esenzelwe urhulumente weengingqi kwithuba elisemva korhulumente wocalucalulo . Iphepha leNgcaciso-nkqubo ngoRhulumente weeNgingqi ligqabaza ngemfuneko karhulumente weengingqi yokungqiyama ngophuhliso . Liphakamisa umbono ngendima karhulumente weengingqi malunga nophuhliso . Imibutho esebenza ekuhlaleni ukuphuhlisa nokuxhobisa abantu kufanele ithathe umba wesini ngokungqongqo . Amadela- kufa ophuhliso amaninzi abona ' abantu ' njengeqela lawo ajolise kulo kwaye awazami ukuqonda iinyaniso ezahlukileyo zobomi bamadoda namakhosikazi . Nakwiimeko apho amakhosikazi axelwa ngokukodwa njengeqela ekujoliswe kulo elibalulekileyo , uphicotho olufanelekileyo kunqabile ukuba lwenziwe malunga negalelo iprojekthi okanye umgaqo-nkqubo oya kuba nalo kubomi bamakhosikazi . Ngaxesha Ngaxesha , imibutho iyasilela ukufumana imibono negalelo lamakhosikazi kwiiprojekthi ezinegalelo ngqo kubomi bawo . Intlanganiso eyandulela ukwenziwa kwentlanganiso mayibanjwe kwiveki enye okanye ezimbini phambi kweveki engundoqo yokwenziwa kwesicwangciso . Iinkokeli mazikhuthazwe ukusuka kumacandelo ahluka-hlukeneyo oluntu ukulungiselela iveki yokwenziwa kwesicwangciso nokukhuthaza ubunini babahlali nendima yabo xa kusakhiwa inkqubo . Isishwankathelo esingezantsi sigqabaza ngeempawu eziphambili zentlanganiso eyandulela ukwenziwa kwesicwangciso nenkqubo . Zidala ubume bemeko yokumamela engenaluphazamiseko apho abantu banengqwalasela kwaye bekwazi ukumamela ngokuzikisa . Ulawulo lweeprojekthi lusebenzisa isixhobo esakhayo esithi siwancede amaqela achaphazelekayo ekubeni ayiqonde nzulu eyona mfuno yawo iphambili ngokubaluleka , aliqonde kananjalo nefuthe lengxaki leyo . Ngokuqulunqa umthi wengxaki zonke iimbangi zengxaki kwakunye nefuthe layo zingakwazi ukuqwalaselwa . Ukuqal'ugwebe ngumbono ocingwe phambi kokuyibona into okanye ukukhetha , okukwachazwa njengoluvo oluchithayo , ukuthelekelela okubi emntwini okanye kwilungelo lomntu . IKomiti yeWadi ilandele imiba yomibini kunye nekomiti eququzelelayo kwaze emva kweenyanga ezi-3 , kwafakelwa izibane zasesitalatweni yaze iKomiti yeWadi yasebenzisana neForam yobuPolisa ekuhlaleni ukugcina ucwangco kummandla . Abantu bathatha inxaxheba ngokwenza izindululo bengaxhomekekanga kumaziko angaphandle malunga nemithombo yezinto ezisetyenziswayo namacebiso ezobuchule abawafunayo , kodwa babe nolawulo phezu kwendlela ephatha ngayo imithombo yezinto ezisetyenziswayo . Ingaba kukho iindawo ezinexabiso malunga nokuphilisana kwendalo , ulondolozo okanye ukuzihlaziya , umz . imimandla emanzi , amachibi , amachweba emilambo , amadama , imilambo ? Kubalulekile ukukhumbula ukuba iiKPI zisebenza kwiiyunithi zolawulo nezabasebenzi , nakuzo zonke iinkampani kuquka nezokunikezela iinkonzo umasipala anesivumelwano nazo ukuba zinikezele ezo nkonzo . I-Luckytown yidolophu encinci eseMpuma-Koloni ( okanye nakweliphi iphondo ) . Kwindawo ethile yale dolophu abantu bahlala ezindlwini ezakhiwe kakuhle kwiiplothi ezinkulu zomhlaba . Abanye banemingxuma yabo yezitsala-manzi kanti kwezinye abanini banemifuno embalwa nemithi yeziqhamo . Phambi kuka-1994 le ndawo yedolophu yayinabahlali abamhlophe kuphela kwaza emva koko kwamana kufika iintsapho ezimbalwa ezivela kwiilokishi ezikufutshane . Umanyano lasekuhlaleni lufuna ukumisela isicwangciso-qhinga . Ukuba uMzantsi Afrika ubhalisa inkqubela-phambili ekupheliseni ucalucalulo lobunini nokulawulwa koqoqosho kungekho kuncitshiswa kobuhlwempu nokungalingani , ukuguquka kuya kuba kokungenabunyani . Ngokufanayo , ukuba ubuhlwempu nokungalingani buncitshiswe ngaphandle kokutshintsha ngokubonakalayo iipatheni zobunini , inkqubela-phambili yelizwe iya kuba yexokozelayo necekethekileyo . Inkqubo entlantlu-mbini yewadi nokumela okulungeleleneyo kuthetha ukuba abahlali babakhethe ngqo abameli babo kwaye baphendule kubo , ukudlulisela phambili nokuqwalasela okubachaphazelayo . Ukubeka iliso nokwenza umlinganiselo wonikezelo lweenkonzo yinkqubo yokuvavanya inkqubela-phambili ekufezekiseni iinjongo ezimiswe kwangaphambili kwicandelo elikhulu ngalinye lwevoti yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali ngokuhambelana necandelo 27(4) le-PFMA . Iithagethi zomsebenzi zimiselwe ukuphucula ixabiso elifanelekileyo , inkqubela-phambili nokusebenza kukonke kwemilinganiselo yonikezelo lweenkonzo . Inkqubo yokuvavanya inkqubela-phambili ingasetyenziswa njengesixhobo sokuzivavanya , ukumisa iinjongo , ukubeka iliso kwinkqubela-phambili nokubhexesha uqhagamshelwano nabathengi bangaphandle . UMSEBENZI 1 Phawula abathathi-nxaxheba abahlukeneyo noxanduva lwabo ngokunxulumene nesicwangciso senkonzo . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kuyagunyazisa xa abantu besenza izigqibo ezizezabo nabazikhethela ngokwabo . Ukuthatha inxaxheba okusebenzayo kucwangciso ngabantu abafumana inzuzo , oko kukuthi , imimandla ejongelwe phantsi , imibutho yamakhosikazi , amaqela olutsha , imibutho yoluntu kwimimandla , abahlali , njl-njl kuyafuneka . Isicwangciso sophuhliso olumanyanisiweyo bubuchule obuquka umasipala ewonke nabemi ekufumaneni izisombululo ezingcono kakhulu ekufezekiseni uphuhliso oluncomekayo lwexesha elide . I-IDP sisixhobo esibaluleke kakhulu sokusebenzisa oovimba abafumanekayo ekuhlangabezeni uluhlu oluninzi lweemfuno kummandla . Ikwanceda umasipala ekubeni ajonge ukuba zeziphi na iimfuno ezifunwayo kumacandelo ahlukeneyo - ezinjengempilo , amanzi , izithuthi , ukhuseleko loluntu , urhwebo - nendlela anokuphendula ngayo koku ngendlela elungelelanisiweyo . Qwalasela imisebenzi ye-CBP ngokuyithelekisa naleyo indululwe kwi-IDP ukuqwalasela ukuba ingaba akukho kungenelelana na . Nokuba akukho , kusenokwenzeka kwaye kufaneleke ukubonana nabanye abaniki beenkxaso-mali ngokungqalileyo . Funda oza kuthetha ngako kwangaphambili - usapho lwakho okanye abahlobo ngabantu abanokunceda ekuphumezeni oku . Ukuqonda isithuba sokwandlaleka kwewadi , imibandela yophuhliso ewadini nendlela enxulumene ngayo nendawo . Ukusebenza kukatitshala . Iingcebiso zethu zijonga uqeqesho , imbuyekezo , inkuthazo , ukusebenza ngexesha , umlinganiselo wokusebenza , nenkxaso yokuqulethweyo nokufundisa . Ubungcali neemeko eziphakamisa ukuziphatha kwengcali kumele bakhiwe kabutsha , nokunika ingxelo yokusebenza kufuneka kuphakanyiswe . Oku kuthetha ukuba uphuhliso lobungcali , ukuhlolana kwabasebenza kunye , amaziko esikolo , ukubonelelwa kweemathiriyeli ezixhasa umfundi neenkqubo zokuxhasa utitshala kumele zomelezwe . Ootitshala , bobabini oyedwa nokumgangatho wesikolo , kumele babe noxanduva lokunika ingxelo ngokuqhuba kwabafundi , kuqondwa ngokufanele oko ubume bokufunda . Le dayagram ilandelayo ibonakalisa indlela esithi isigaba ngasinye solawulo lweprojekthi sikhokelele kuvandlakanyo ngokutsha lwezinto ezenziwayo nokuba umjikelo awuhambi ngomgca wempuku ngokwemo yawo . I-Masincedane Development Corporation yasekwa njenge-Section 21 company . Injongo yayo kukuvelisa nokulawula ingxowa-mali nokuzalisekisa izicwangciso-nkqubo ze-LED . Emva koluhlu lweendibano zeengxoxo , uluntu kummandla lwaphawula izicwangciso-nkqubo zenene ezinokuqhutywa yiMasincedane . Ilungu ngalinye labahlali likhululekile ukubeka amaqhezu amathathu ngaso nasiphi isiphumo okanye iziphumo . Umbindi woMgaqo-siseko nguMthetho wamaLungelo . UMthetho wamaLungelo uphakamisa amalungelo abo bonke abahlali nabemi ukuba baphathwe ngokulinganayo nangesidima kungakhathaliseki nokuba bangabaluphi uhlanga , isini , ukutyeba okanye ubume . Inani lamalungelo ezentlalo noqoqosho ayakhuselwa kuMthetho wamaLungelo , njengelungelo lokuhlala kwindawo ecocekileyo , ilungelo lokufumana indlu efanelekileyo , ilungelo lokunikwa inkonzo yezempilo nokutya okulingeneyo namanzi . Luxanduva lukarhulumente wengingqi ekunye namanye amanqanam karhulumente ' ukuhlonipha , akhusele , aphucule ade afezekise ' la malungelo . I-CBP lulwahlulelwano phakathi kwabahlali , umasipala nooceba . Ababhexeshi be-CBP kufuneka basebenze baze benze isicwangciso noceba ngenyathelo ngalinye lenkqubo . Ukuba iYunivesithi yaseTshwane igqibe ekubeni ibonelele imali yemfundo apho abafundi abavela eMpuma Koloni naseGauteng banokukhuphisana , ukuphathwa ngokungalinganiyo akuna kuba kwicala labafundi abavela eMpuma Koloni . Umzekelo , asingabo bonke abathetha uhlobo olunye lwesiNgesi , okanye abakufikelela ngokufanayo kwiintlobo zonxibelelwano . Yintoni umahlulelane kwinkonzo kamasipala ? I-Local Government : Municipal Property Rates Act , 2004 inikezela ulwazi ngorhafiso lomhlaba nezakhiwo ( ipropati ) ngoomasipala bebonke kwaye ikwachaphazela iipropati ezaphuma ngaphandle kwemida kamasipala ngaphambili . Kubalulekile ukuba iiKomiti zeWadi zazi apho zingalufumana khona olu lwazi njengoko iirhafu zepropati zihlala ziyimiba eveliswa rhoqo ngabahlali . Inkoliso yemisebenzi echongwe ngethuba lenkqubo ye-CBP iya kuphunyezwa ziiKomiti zeWadi , kodwa eminye isenokufuna imithombo ebalulekileyo yangaphandle okanye inokusetyenziswa ngempumelelo kwisikali sikamasipala . Ibandakanya ukuthatha izigqibo ngokuba ngubani onoxanduva lweprojekthi nendlela yokusebenzisa imithombo yezinto ezisetyenziswayo . Sakuba sesilungile isicwangciso , inkqubo yokubeka iliso , ukulinganisa nokuphengulula isicwangciso kubalulekile . Izicwangciso maziphengululwe kwintlanganiso yeKomiti yeWadi nganye kunye nasemva kwenyanga nganye ukuya kwezimbini kwintlanganiso kawonke-wonke yabahlali newadi / isithili / umasipala . IiKomiti zeWadi mazinike ingxelo eyenziweyo kwaye zikhanyise naziphi iingxaki eziphakanyisiweyo . Ezi ngxelo kufuneka zibandakanye inxalenye yezezimali eneenkcukacha ngeengxowa-mali ezisetyenzisiweyo . Ibhunga kufuneka lamkele olu hlahlo lwabiwo-mali ngaphambi kokuqala konyaka-mali , emva kwesicwangciso nothetha-thethwano neeKomiti zeWadi kunye namanye amaqela achaphazelekayo kummandla . IiKomiti zeWadi zibalulekile ekuhambiseni uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali kuluntu kummandla nobhexesho lwengxelo esuka kuluntu kummandla isiya kumasipala . Ukuba iiKomiti zeWadi zithatha inxaxheba ekwenzeni isigqibo malunga nokuba umasipala kufuneka achithe imali engakanani , kweziphi na iiprojekthi , oku kuya kuthetha ukuba iwadi yabo ingafumana inzuzo ethe ngqo . Kungenzeka ukuba ukukhula koqoqosho lwehlabathi kwiminyaka elishumi elandelayo kuya kuba sezantsi kunokuba kwakunjalo kokudlulileyo . Oku kuya kufuna umgqalisela omkhulu wenkqubo , ukuphunyezwa ngempumelelo kweenkqubo zoshishino nokuphuculwa kophuhliso lwezakhono . Impilo elungileyo iyimfuneko kubomi obunemveliso nobanezayo . Ingxelo echonga ingxaki ibonisa imingeni enxulumanayo ngokupheleleyo evezwa sisixokelelwano sempilo esiwayo nokunyuka komthwalo wesifo . Isixokelelwano sempilo yoluntu esaphukileyo saseMzantsi Afrika kumele silungiswe . Logama usetyenziso olukhulu lokhathalelo labucala , oluhlawulelwa ngabasebenzisi okanye zii-inshorensi zempilo , yinxenye yesisombululo , ayiyo nto inokusetyenziswa endaweni yokuphuculwa kokhathalelo lwempilo yoluntu . Umzamo wokujonga unobangela nesiphumo ekuphuculeni ubulunga bokhathalelo uyafuneka , ingakumbi kumgangatho wokuqala . Aqinisekise ukuba inkxalabo yoluntu kummandla iviwe . Inxaxheba yeKomiti yeWadi kukuqinisekisa ukuba abo banoxanduva lokuqulunqa isicwangciso bayababandakanya abahlali , baqinisekise kananjalo ukuba abahlali bayithatha ngokupheleleyo inxaxheba kwiprojekthi . Ukuqonda noXilongo - injongo yalo mgangatho kukuyila ithuba lamaqela ewonke ukuba ' aviwe ' nokuwavumela ukuba achaze iimeko zawo . Iqela / umntu ngamnye unethuba lokuchaza imeko yakhe . Emva kokuba iqela ngalinye lichaze imeko yalo , umxolelanisi ushwankathela imiba evelisiweyo aze aqinisekise kumaqela ukuba ukuvile akuchazileyo . Amaqela ayavumelana ngemiba ekufuneka isonjululwe aze ayile indawo efanelekileyo yokusombulula iingxaki . Oku kunokufuna ababhexeshi be-CBP ukuba babambe iintlanganiso eziliqela nomasipala kwangethuba ukuze bavumelane kwaye babambe udliwano-ndlebe ngolwazi olungasentla . Ngoobani abahlali kwaye ziintoni iimpiliso zabo ? ' Ababhexeshi ' mabafumane olu lwazi kwiqela labo baze balubhale phantsi . Iqela malichaze iqela lalo , likhumbule inani labantu kwiqela lalo , nokuba baqeshiwe na kwaye basebenza ntoni , ukuba akunjalo bangaphi abangaphangeliyo , isakhiwo sabantu beentlanga ezenza iqela . UMBONO KARHULUMENTE NGOWOKUBA : ' kwakhiwe inkonzo yoluntu esekelwe kubantu futhi iqhutywa ngabantu , neneempawu zokulingana , ubulunga , ukuyoyika into embi , neendlela zokuziphatha ezamkelekileyo , ezilungiselelwe ngokugqwesayo nezinika inkonzo engenachaphaza ' . Abemi banoxanduva lokunqanda iinkokheli ekuthatheni izigqibo zokuzithandisa ezicingelwe kufutshane , nezenzo zokuzigwagwisa . Intetho kawonkewonke ephilileyo nenkcubeko yoqhankqalazo oluseluxolweni ziya kuba negalelo kukuqondwa nzulu kwemingeni ejongene noluntu nokunyanzelisa ukunika ingxelo phakathi kwamagosa anyuliweyo . Ngokomzekelo , ukuba iziphumo zokufunda kwisikolo zingaphantsi kokulindelekileyo nokusemthethweni , uluntu lunganceda ukulungisa imeko ngokomeleza ulawulo lwesikolo , luqinisekisa ukuba abafundi nootitshala bafika ngexesha , kwaye ubume benkxaso evela kumagosa kawonkewonke buyimpumelelo . Zenza ubomi bamakhosikazi bube lula . Iindima zabo zokwandisa zibanika umthwalo owongezelelekileyo omkhulu . Ngokuqwalasela iinkqubo ezijongene nokhathalelo lwabantwana , ukhathalelo lwempilo olufikelelekayo , ukufikelela emanzini nombane nezithuthi zikawonke-wonke ezisebenza ngokukuko , umthwalo womsebenzi wokukhathalela usapho nekhaya ungancitshiswa . Umsebenzi 3 Jonga uMgaqo-siseko , uze uchonge indima nomsebenzi karhulumente kazwelonke . Ukuphuculwa kokusebenza kombane wemigodi nokusetyenzwa kwezimbiwa ngomyinge we-15 ekhulwini ngo-2030 . Oku kungabandakanya ukuvalwa kweyona mizi-mveliso ebonakalisa ukungasebenzi kakhulu . Abathathi-nxaxheba bakrwela umgca ngezantsi kwamagama aphambili avela kwingxelo nganye kwezilandelayo , umz. ngengeniso ephuculweyo - kusenokuba ' yingeniso ' , ngolwaphulo-mthetho kunokuba ' lukhuselo nokhuseleko ' uze uwabhale kwifliptshathi . Ukubumba kwakhona iidolophukazi , iidolophu namaphandle aseMzantsi Afrika yiprojekthi enzima yexesha elide , efuna ukuphuculwa okumandla nentando yopolitiko . Nangona kunjalo , yiprojekthi eyimfuneko kujongwe iindleko ezinkulu zasekuhlaleni , zokusingqongileyo nezezimali ezinyanzeliswe kukwahlulwa kwesithuba okukhoyo . Ukhuselo nokhuseleko lwabahlali ludinga ubudlelwane namagosa okhuseleko asekuhlaleni kwaye luxhomekeka kubahlali ukuba bancede eminye imiba yokhuseleko nokufumana ukhuseleko lwamalungu asekuhlaleni . Ulawulo lomsebenzi lulungelelaniswe kufutshane nonikezelo lweenkonzo , nalapho oku kuchazwe sisicwangciso-nkqubo se-Batho Pele esaqaliswa ngonyaka ka-1997 . Ngokukodwa , abantu abasebatsha bafanele ukufumana amathuba angcono emfundo noqoqosho , nemizamo engqalileyo iyimfuneko ekubhangiseni ukungalingani ngesini . Ukuphakanyiswa kokulingani ngesini namathuba amakhulukazi kubantu abasebatsha yimixholo edityanisiweyo ethubeleza kwesi sicwangciso siphela . Abezopolitiko banoxanduva lokuqinisekisa ukulandelisa nokufezekisa izicwangciso kanti ukuzinikela kwabo kwinkqubo kunika ukuphila . Inxaxheba yabo ibalulekile ke ngoko . UMthetho obizwa Municipal Systems Act unika ugqaliselo kwizixokelelwano zangaphakathi nolawulo lukamasipala . Kutheni kubalulekile ukuba iikomiti zeeWadi ziqonde kwaye zisebenzise le nkqubo ? NGOKUSEMTHETHWENI , UMASIPALA NGAMNYE KUFUNEKA APHUHLISE INKQUBO YOLAWULO LOMSEBENZI ( PMS ) EYA KWANDISA INKQUBELA-PHAMBILI NOKUSEBENZA , UXANDUVA LOKUSEBENZISA OOVIMBA BAKAMASIPALA NOKUBONISA UKUFEZEKISWA KWEZIPHUMO . I-PMS IYAKWAZI UKUSEBENZA NJENGENDLELA ESISILUMKISO SAKWANGETHUBA NJENGOKO IBONISA UKUNGASEBENZI OKANYE UKUSEBENZA okunganelisiyo , NOKO OKUVUMELA INYATHELO ELIFANELEKILEYO LOKUPHUCULA OKU . Bonke oomasipala bafanele ukulungisa Isicwangciso Sophuhliso Esimanyanisiweyo ( IDP ) . I-IDP ihlela izinto ngokokushiyana kokubaluleka kwazo kuloo mmandla . I-IDP inokubakho iminyaka emihlanu kuphela ukuze emva koko iphengululwe ngonyaka ngamnye . I-Intergovernmental Relations Framework Act , 2005 isekelwe ukunyusa umgangatho nokubhexesha intsebenziswano kulwenziwo lwezigqibo phakathi kwemigangatho emithathu karhulumente ukuze imigaqo-nkqubo nemisebenzi kwimigangatho iyonke ikhuthaze unikezelo lweenkonzo nokufumana iindlela zokuhlangabezana neemfuno zabemi ngendlela esebenzayo . Imigangatho emithathu karhulumente inemfanelo phantsi koMgaqo-siseko yokulungelelanisa nokuthethathethana ngeendlela zokuvumelana ngemiba yolawulo , ezopolitiko nezezimali . Jonga incwadana ethi , Working Together for Development . Nika izizathu zokuyilandelelanisa ngolu hlobo niyilandelelanise ngalo imisebenzi , uze ke ukubonise oko ngeshedyuli , ibha-tshathi okanye ngokunika imizekelo . Ukuphuhlisa ubumxinwa bothutho lwempahla eDurban-Gauteng , kuquka nonxweme olusandula kugrunjwa kwisikhululo senqwelo-moya sakuqala eDurban . Isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali esincomekayo sifuna ukubandakanywa kwabo bonke abachaphazeleka ngokwegunya kwinkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso . Nangona isenokungaqinisekiswa i-100% yenxaxheba yabahlali kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukuba onke amaqela angundoqo ezentlalo nawomnqweno eluntwini ayabandakanyeka . Inxaxheba mayingapheleli kwiinkokeli zengingqi okanye kwabo baqhele ukuya okanye ukuqhuba iintlanganiso zabahlali kuphela . I-CBP ithetha ukuba kufuneka kwenziwe ilinge lokufikelela nakubahlali mhlawumbi abangadlali ndima yakuququzela . Ifuna ixesha , ilinge nokuzinikela . Isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali masikhokelele kwinyathelo elibandakanya amaqela abahlali ngokwawo , kulwahlulelwano noomasipala . Umsebenzi 2 Jonga uMgaqo-siseko , uze uchonge indima nomsebenzi karhulumente wamaphondo nobudlelwane bakhe norhulumente weengingqi . Ukupapashwa nokusasazwa kokufunyenwe kuphando kufuneka kucwangciswe ngokwenene kwakwinqanam locwanciso lweprojekthi . Esi sahluko sijonga iimfuno ze-PMS size sichaze iZalathisi eziPhambili zoMsebenzi ( KPI ) nendlela yokuseka nokusebenzisa ii-KPI nokwenza imilinganiselo yalo msebenzi . Sikwaxoxa ngendima ebalulekileyo edlalwa ngabahlali , kengoko iiKomiti zeWadi , kwinkqubo yohlelo ngokutsha lomsebenzi novavanyo . Kwimo ekubhekiselelwe kuyo yaseMzantsi Afrika akukho mifuziselo yecandelo likawonke-wonke ebekwe emgangathweni ofanayo ngoko ke kuya kubakho iiyantlukwano naphakathi kwemifuziselo esetyenziswa kumasebe ahluka-hlukileyo karhulumente . Amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi afanele ukuziqhelanisa nolawulo lomjikelo weeprojekthi njengoko lo ingumfuziselo okholisa ukusetyenziswa . Ukucukucezwa namagama amabanga okanye amabakala omjikelo weprojekthi asenokwahluka ngokokuxhomekeka kwiarhente enika inkxaso-mali okanye kwisebe likarhulumente . Yenza isigqibo malunga neyona ndlela ingcono yokugqithisa ulwazi . Ungafuna ukulubhala kwifliptshathi , okanye unike abathathi-nxaxheba ikopi yamanqaku aphambili . Ibhunga lengingqi lingakunceda ekwenzeni iikopi . Kwesi sahluko siqwalasela indlela ekholisa ukusetyenziswa , indlela yokusombulula ingxaki . UMSEBENZI 1 IiKomiti zeWadi zinganempembelelo enjani kwisiCwangciso soPhuhliso lweNdawo kuZwelonke ? ESI SAHLUKO SIZA KUJOLISA KWIINDLELA EZIKHETHWA ngazo IIPROJEKTHI kumasipala okanye yiKomiti yeWadi . Siza kukhokela kwisivumelwano sokuba kuqhutywe ngeprojekthi , okanye kusenokufunyaniswa ukuba iprojekthi le ayingekwazeki ukuqhutywa ; ngoko ke mayiyekwe . Ukukhethwa kweprojekthi , ukuphanda ngokwazeka kwayo , uvandlakanyo lweengxaki nolwamaqela achaphazelekayo ; zonke ezi zizinto ezenzekayo kwesi sigaba . Abathathi-nxaxheba baxhoma imifanekiso yabo neepowusta kwigumbi lilonke . Mema abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bajonge imizobo neepowusta zomnye nomnye . Khetha omnye wemizobo uze ucele iqela ukuba liwucacise . IiKomiti zeWadi zingasebenzisa lo mzekelo ukuzinceda ekwenzeni umlinganiselo womsebenzi woomasipala bazo . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwabahlali kurhulumente ngumba osisiseko esibaluleke kakhulu kuyo nayiphina idemokhrasi . Oku kuboniswe kuMgaqo-siseko , iCandelo 152 elichaza ukuba uluntu jikelele kwimimandla kufuneka luthathe inxaxheba kwimiba karhulumente wengingqi , likwachaza nokuba enye yeenjongo eziphambili zikarhulumente wengingqi " kukukhuthaza ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu jikelele kwimimandla nemibutho yoluntu kwimiba karhulumente wengingqi " . Inkqubo ye-CBP kummandla uwonke kamasipala kufuneka yenzeke ngaphambi kwamanyathelo okuqala kwisicwangciso se-IDP nenkqubo yohlelo ngokutsha . I-Municipal Demarcation Act 1998 imisa iinkqubo neendlela zokumisa imida yoomasipala . IBhodi yokuMiswa kweMida sisiphatha-mandla esizimeleyo nesimiselwe ukwenza lo msebenzi . Xa imisa imida , iBhodi iya kuqwalasela uluhlu lwemiba kuquka ubukho bezimali kulo mmandla , ukudityaniswa kwamacandelo ngokobuhlanga nolungelelaniso namacandelo kamasipala xa kusenziwa isigqibo ekumiseni umda kamasipala wengingqi . Kubalulekile ukuba amalungu eKomiti yeWadi aziqhelanise nalo Mthetho ukuze akwazi ukucacisa izigqibo ezenziweyo malunga nemida kamasipala . Abantu bathatha inxaxheba ngoncedo lolumano- ndlebe nangokuphendula imibuzo . Iiarhente zangaphandle zicacisa iingxaki neenkqubo zokuphanda ulwazi , ngokwenza njalo zilawule uhlalutyo . Inkqubo elolo hlobo yolumano-ndlebe ayivumeli nasiphi isabelo kulwenziwo-zigqibo , kananjalo iingcali azinyanzelekanga ukuba zithathe imibono yabantu . Isicwangciso : Abemi , iiNGO , neeCBO namaqela opolitiko basebenza kunye ukunika izindululo kwibhunga ukuba liziqwalasele , nokukhuthaza umasipala ukuba asebenzise izinto anazo ukuphumeza iziseko ukuxhasa ubuqabane nemibutho engekho ngaphantsi kukarhulumente nesenokuba nezakhono zokubhexesha amalinge ophuhliso . Nawuphina umsebenzi onempembelelo kwezemali kufuneka uchaziwe ukuze wamkelwe kuhlahlo lwabiwo-mali . Naziphina izigqibo zemali ezinempembelelo kwinkcitho okanye umvuzo kufuneka zilungisiwe . Ukunika inkcazo kuhamba nokuba noxanduva kwizigqibo ezenziweyo . Ingaba umxholo wemisebenzi neendlela ezisetyenzisiweyo ziya kufaneleka kwaye zihlangabezane neemfuno zamakhosikazi nezamadoda , ngokungananzanga imvelaphi yabo yenkcubeko , inkolo noqoqosho ? Ingaba izixokelelwano ziyasebenza ? Ekupheleni kwale seshoni abathathi-nxaxheba baya belungise isishwankathelo seeprojekthi / imisebenzi abanqwenela ukuyinikela ukwenzela inkxaso-mali ngumasipala okanye abanye abaniki beenkonzo , nesibandakanywe kwi-IDP . Ukusuka ngo-1994 urhulumente waqulunqa umgaqo-nkqubo nezakhelo zowiso-mthetho ezidinga ukuphucula ulawulo lokuthatha inxaxheba . Esi sakhelo siboniswe kumzobo olapha ngezantsi . I-PMS imisa izalathisi zomsebenzi ize kengoko yenze ukuba urhulumente wengingqi nabemi benze imilinganiselo yokufezekisiweyo xa kuthelekiswa nezi zalathisi . Apho kubonakala ukungasebenzi , ibhexesha inyathelo elifunekayo . Iquka amanqanaba ocwangciso , ukulandela nogqithiso lwengxelo novavanyo lwarhoqo ngonyaka lomsebenzi . Enze ilungu labo lebhunga limele ukulwa urhwaphilizo okanye ukusetyenziswa ngendlela engafanelekanga kwengxowa-mali kamasipala . Ukujongela phantsi ngumbono , isimo nonxulumano oluqala phezulu ukuya ezantsi olusekwe kwingqikelelo yokuba ' umkhuseli ' okanye umcebisi usoloko esazi ngcono kunongaphantsi kwakhe . Yintoni engumahluko kwezi meko ? Le nxenye yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali kulapho umasipala eya kwenza khona inzaliso-mali kuphuhliso olutsha lomsebenzi , izibonelelo zomsebenzi okanye ii-aseti zekapitali ezinjengolwakhiwo lweendlela nolwakhiwo-zindlu . Ezi projekthi zingabizwa njengeeprojekthi zekapitali . Urhulumente wengingqi kufuneka azi ukuba le nzaliso-mali iya kuba lixabiso kunyaka ngamnye nalapho imali iya kube ivela khona . Benze ukuba urhulumente , ushishino nazo zonke iinkokheli kuluntu zithathe uxanduva ngamanyathelo abo . Amaziko alungeleyo , anezakhono afana noMkhuseli woLuntu neCandelo loPhando eliLodwa kufuneka axhaswe ngemali ngokwaneleyo kwaye zibonelelwe ngabasebenzi nokungabi nampembelelo yangaphandle . Ukuze ube sisithethi esincomekayo , kufuneka uyazi indlela othetha ngayo . Ukuseka iithagethi zomsebenzi kwinjongo ephambili nganye ( umz. unikezelo lwama-10 000 yemizi ngamalungiselelo okuhanjiswa kwamanzi amdaka kunyaka-mali ozayo ) . Musa ukuphazamisa , mlinde umntu azise ngaphambili izimvo zakhe ngokupheleleyo . Ubuchule obusekelwe kumagunya - oku kuxa iqela lisebenzisa isikhundla salo senene samagunya ekuzameni nasekunyanzeliseni iqela eliphikisana nalo ukuba lithathe inyathelo ngendlela ethile . Obu buchule buxhomekeke kunyanzeliso ukufuna isiphumo . Umzekelo , umkhosi wokhuselo ubamba abaqhankqalazi abavale indlela , okanye umntu onamagunya emsebenzini enze isigqibo sokuba abanye babasebenzi abonwabanga kodwa abakwazi kuchaza izimvo zabo ngenxa yesikhundla esiphezulu somntu owenza ezi zigqibo . Amanyathelo anjalo obuchule obusekelwe kumagunya angaquka ukwala intsebenziswano , uqhankqalazo , imiboniso , inyathelo labasebenzi , ukusetyenziswa ngobuchule kwamajelo eendaba ekuhlaseleni umchasi , imfazwe . Oku kungabangela imeko YOKUWINA / YOKUNGAWINI . Yeyiphi imihla emisiweyo yokugqitywa kwemisebenzi ? Umsebenzi wokuqala unxulumanisa ezona ziphumo zibalulekileyo , uqinisekisa ukuba zonke iinkcukacha zokwenza isicwangciso ziqokelelwe ngokuqaphela . Isicwangciso siceba isicwangciso-qhinga sobume bemithombo eluluntu esintlangothi-ntathu esibandakanya isicwangciso-qhinga soqeqesho sexesha elide , iziphumo ezingcono ezisuka kwisebe lemfundo ephakamileyo nesicwangciso-qhinga sokwabiwa kwemithombo enqabileyo . Umelo ngokwezelizwe lufuna ukuthathelwa ingqalelo ukuqinisekisa ukuba inkqubo isondeza amaqela abahlali ndawonye . Kusenokufuneka iintlanganiso zesindululo nezokubuyiswa kwengxelo kwiindawo ezingaphezu kwendawo enye ukuze kufikelelwe kwiqela elibanzi . Ukumanya bonke abemi boMzantsi Afrika ngenkqubo ebachaphazela bonke ukufikelela kwimpumelelo nokulingana . Imiba ethile igqithiselwa kwiiKomiti zepotfoliyo yebhunga ukuze kuxoxwe ngayo nezindululo . Shwankathela ngokuqaqambisa Iinjongo Zenkulungwane Zophuhliso nendlela oomasipala beengingqi , bekunye nabahlali , ekufuneka befumanise iindlela zokusebenza ukuze bahlangabezane nezi njongo . Phantsi kweMunicipal Structures Act [ Icandelo 32 ] , ibhunga lingadlulisa amanye amagunya liwanike iikomiti . Nangona kubalulekile ukubandakanya iikomiti zewadi kwinkqubo yothethathethwano neza kuphembelela izigqibo , ukunikezelwa kwamagunya kwenziwa ngobulumko . Izigqibo zebhunga kufuneka zenziwe libhunga elinyulwe ngokwedemokrasi , elenza izinto elubala nelizimelayo izenzo zalo . IiKomiti zeWadi azingomaqumrhu asemthethweni nangenza izivumelwano okanye angasiwa enkundleni yamatyala ngeemposiso azenzileyo , ngokungalawuli kakuhle okanye ubuqhophololo . Nokuba ziyintoni na iingxaki ezibangelwa zizigqibo ezibuthathaka oku kuza kuhlala kuluxanduva lwebhunga . Umzamo wethu wokwakhiwa kwesizwe ube nzima ngakumbi kumaxesha okukhula ngokucotha koqoqosho . UMzantsi Afrika awunakumelana nokujikeleza okusingela ezantsi okulola ukuxhala kwasekuhlaleni . Ubunkokheli obomeleleyo buyimfuneko ekunyuseni imbono yomGaqo-siseko . Umnqophiso osemthethweni wasekuhlaleni unganceda ekomelezeni ukulungelelana phakathi kokukhula , kophuhliso nokwakhiwa kwesizwe , kuveza isangqa esilunge kanye . Indlela yokusebenza ye-IDP inika inxaxheba njengenxalenye yenkqubo yokwenza isicwangciso ngokusebenzisa amaqumrhu angqalileyo . La maqumrhu abandakanya Iqonga Leengxoxo Zabameli , amaqela emisebenzi yeeprojekthi kunye neziganeko zezicwangciso-buqili . Umthetho Omiselweyo nawo ukwacacisa imfuneko yolumano-ndlebe kwinqanaba lewadi . Ucacisa imfuno kawonke-wonke yokufaka igalelo kwizicwangciso nokuphawula ngomgangatho wokusebenza kukamasipala . Uphando ngokuthatha inxaxheba kwamaqela olwenziwa ngentsebenziswano neeNGO neeCBO kungangenisa ulwazi oluneenkcukacha ngezidingo neenqobo ezisemgangathweni . Urhwebo lwamazwe ngamazwe lubhekisa kurhwebo lwehlabathi olunyukayo nokuquqela kwabantu okwandayo , izimali , iingcinga nobugcisa obuwele imida kwiminyaka elishumi yakutsha nje . Ezi ntsingiselo zixhase jikelele uphuhliso lwamazwe ahlelelekileyo nanomvuzo ophakathi , okubangela ukuba akwazi ukufikelela kumashishini , kwiimpahla , kwiinkonzo , kwizimali , kubugcisa nezakhono . Urhwebo lwamazwe ngamazwe lukwabanegalelo " kuthungelwano " olukhulayo oluthe lwathoba imiqobo kungenelo nokwandisa ukufikelela kulwazi . Kwixesha eliphakathi , uMzantsi Afrika kufuneka uphendule kule ntsingiselo ngokuxhasa ukuba nokhuphiswano notyalo-mali kumashishini anexabiso elongezelelweyo eliphezulu nokwandisa umthamo wezimbiwa ezithunyelwa ngaphandle . Kwixesha elide , uMzantsi Afrika kumele wenze ngakumbi ekukhuthazeni ukhuphiswano kwiingingqi ezinenzuzo elinganisayo engatsalela abantu abaninzi emsebenzini . Ngokuphucula isiseko sezakhono nokwandisa ukuba nokhuphiswano , uqoqosho lungatshintsha , kulinganisa iimpembelelo ezijikayo zamaxabiso eempahla zorhwebo anyusiweyo kwirandi . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kudliwano-ndlebe lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali egameni labahlali . Udliwano-ndlebe lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali luqinisekisa ukuba iimfuno ze-MFMA ziyaqwalaselwa ngokunxulumene nokuthatha inxaxheba kwabahlali kwinkqubo yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali . Udliwano-ndlebe lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala luvumela iiKomiti zeWadi ukuba zithathe inxaxheba kuphuhliso lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala . Ulwakhiwo lwezikhundla kumalungu eKomiti yeWadi ukuze akwazi ukusebenza njengeengcaphephe zophuhliso kwingingqi kwaye akwazi ukusebenzisana ngenkuthalo ekwanyusa umgangatho obanzi woluntu jikelele kummandla . Iinkqubo ze-IDP ne-CBP neziphumo ezakhiweyo nezazisanayo , zingumjikelezo kwaye ziyaphindaphindeka . Ulwazi oluqulathwe yi-IDP ekhoyo kufuneka lusetyenziswe ekuqaliseni inkqubo ye-CBP , ngexa iziphumo ze-CBP ziya kuphinda ziqaliswe kuhlelo ngokutsha lwe-IDP kunyaka olandelayo . Uphicotho lwesini lwenziwa kwaye lwayoyisa ingxaki . Kwacaca ukuba amakhosikazi ngamafama , kodwa kuncinci abanokuthetha emakhayeni okanye kuluntu . Iimali-mboleko kumakhosikazi , iinkonzo zenkxaso neeforam zokwenza izigqibo ezidityanelweyo zasekwa ukuze imali isetyenziselwe ukujika amafama asokolayo awayephila nzima ukuba babengamafama avelisayo . Ezinye izinto ezingalinganiswa kungaba lunxibelelwano , intsebenziswano nebhunga okanye iindawo zokusebenza iKomiti yeWadi eyimise ngokwayo ukuqinisekisa ukuba amalungu ayo enza imisebenzi yawo njengokuba imiselwe kuwiso-mthetho lokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu . Abantu bathatha inxaxheba kuhlalutyo oludityanelwayo , kuphuhliso lwezicwangciso zamanyathelo nasekubunjweni okanye ekomelezweni kwamaziko engingqi . Inkqubo ibandakanya iindlela zobungcali phakathi kwezifundo ezahluka-hlukeneyo ezizingela amacala ezimvo amaninzi nezisebenzisa iinkqubo ezijolise kuwo onke amacala nezinesakhiwo . Njengoko amaqela selezithathela izigqibo zengingqi aqwalasele nendlela efanele ukusetyenziswa ngayo imithombo , ngoko ke banesabelo ekulondolozweni kwezakhiwo okanye izenzo . Ukuphuhlisa iminqophiso yesithuba yobumelwane ukuzisa uluntu lukarhulumente , amashishini norhulumente kunye ukuze basombulule iingxaki . ESI SAHLUKO SICHAZA INDIMA YEEKOMITI ZEWADI namanye amalungu esicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali . Isahluko 1 sikhanyise ukuba isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali sifuna ukulungiswa ngabantu bengingqi besenzela iwadi yabo , enabanini abangabahlali kwaye kuqinisekiswe inxaxheba yokuzenzela kwabahlali kwimpumezo yaso . IKomiti yeWadi idlala indima ebalulekileyo ekuqinisekiseni nasekukhuseleni inxaxheba yabahlali . Ukusebenza kwabantu ngabanye , ngokwamaqela , nangoBuqabane Babucala noLuntu ( Private Public Partnerships ) abancedayo ukuphumeza iinjongo zesebe okanye zikamasipala kufuneka zibekwe esweni ukuqinisekisa ukuhanjiswa kweenkonzo ezisemgangathweni . Ukusebenza kwabantu ngabanye kuza kuvuzwa ngokwemiqathango yePMS esetyenziswa ngumasipala . Ukuzivavanya nokuvavanywa ngosebenza nabo zizixhobo ezisetyenziswayo ukuvavanya abantu . Isicwangciso sezibonelelo : Ukujonga ukuba zeziphi na izibonelelo ( abantu , izinto zokusebenza , imathiriyeli ) nobungakanani baso ngasinye esiza kufuneka ekwenziweni komsebenzi weprojekthi le . I-CBP imisela inkqubo yenxaxheba yokufumana igalelo labahlali nokwenza isicwangciso esisekwe kwimibandela yomndilili wabantu nendlela olu lwazi lunokunxulumana ngayo nengqiqo ebanzi yesicwangciso sikamasipala . Ngezantsi kukho umzekelo wesishwankathelo sesicwangciso sewadi kwaye sifanele i-IDP . Chaza izintlu ezi-3 zikamasipala uze ucele abathabathi-nxaxheba ukuba bachonge uluhlu angena kulo umasipala wabo . Bancedise ukuba abaqinisekanga . Ingqesho yoluntu kumele yande , kujoliswe kulutsha namabhinqa . Kulindeleke ukuba ingqesho yoluntu iya kubonelela okulingana nezigidi ezi-2 zemisebenzi yesigxina ngowama-2020 . Amaqela abahlali , imibutho nabantu bathatha inxaxheba ngezizathu ezahluka-hlukeneyo ukuze beze nezakhono zobuchule ezahluka-hlukeneyo namava-ngamava anokunceda kwinkqubo leyo . Itheyibhile ekwiphepha lama-21 igqabaza ngohlobo lwenxaxheba noko kubandakanyekayo . Ukunxulumanisa iziphumo ze-CBP neze-IDP yinkqubo engumjikelo . Umjikelo wemisetyenzana echazwe kwi-CBP ufanele ukunxulunyaniswa nomjikelo we-IDP . Oku kuyimfuneko njengoko i-CBP izama ukuqinisekisa ukuba iimfuno zamaqela abahlali ziyachongwa zize zibandakanywe kwi-IDP . Njengoko i-IDP yenzelwe ukukhanyisa imicimbi ephambili yabahlali , xa le mijikelo ingalungelelaniswanga , amaqela abahlali asenokungayiboni kakuhle indlela ye-CBP yokwenza izicwangciso . Umasipala angaseka uphuhliso lweqela elichaphazelekayo apho anokudibanisa abantu abasuka kwii-CBO nee- NGO ; amashishini kwingingqi , ii-SMME , amafama , njl-njl . Eli qela liya kucebisa umasipala ngophuhliso loqoqosho kwingingqi nemiba ye-IDP . Inkqubo yeqela elichaphazelekayo liya kuncedisa iindlela esele zikhona zokuthatha inxaxheba ngaphakathi koomasipala ; ukwenza nzulu ukuthatha inxaxheba kwidemokhrasi nokunyusa inani labantu abanempembelelo nabanini bezigqibo zikamasipala . Ukukhuthaza ubunkokheli obuluqilima kuluntu luphela ukuze lusebenzisane ekusombululeni iingxaki . Kurhulumente ophuhlisayo , imibutho yabasebenzi yabelana ngoxanduva lobulunga beenkonzo ezihanjisiweyo , ekuphuculeni ukusebenza kukarhulumente , nasekulweni urhwaphilizo nokungasebenzi . Zonke iinkcukacha ezidweliswe phantsi Kwendlela zibekwe edongeni ukuze onke amalungu eqela azibone . Umbhexeshi wentlanganiso ujonga zonke iinkxukacha aze ameme igalelo elongezelelekileyo kwiqela . Njengoko le ntlanganiso ikukushiya-shiyanisa iziphumo ngokokubaluleka kwazo oko kuya kwenza isicwangciso sewadi ekufuneka iqela livumelane ngaso malunga nokuba ingaba le micimbi iya kuba yintoni . Kufuneka ukuba kucace gca xa maqela angekho kurhulumente enoxanduva lokuphumeza iinxenye zesicwangciso . Ishishini , abasebenzi noluntu lukarhulumente ngamaqela awahlukeneyo kwaye awafane athethe ngazwi-nye . Nangona kunjalo , amatyathanga oxanduva nokunika ingxelo acace gca , kuquka namahlakani asekuhlaleni , abaluleke kakhulu kwimpumelelo yesicwangciso . Kwiingingqi ezininzi , ishishini , abasebenzi noluntu lukarhulumente lungachonga indlela yokuba negalelo kwisicwangciso sezinto emazijongwe kuqala . Nokuba kunjalo , kwezinye iimeko le ndima iya kufuna ukuba yenziwe ibe semthethweni . Ukusebenzisana ekufezekiseni iinjongo ezizodwa kwisicwangciso kuya kunceda ekwakheni ukuthembana ngaphakathi nakumacandelo . Isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali ngoko ke luhlobo lwesicwangciso senxaxheba esiyilelwe ukukhuthaza intshukumo yabahlali kananjalo senze unxulumano Nesicwangciso Esimanyanisiweyo Sophuhliso ( Integrated Development Plan IDP ) . UMBUZO 4 Zeziphi iindawo zeziphumo eziphambili ( KRAs ) ? Ngenxa yokuba isicwangciso siyilelwe ukuzisa utshintsho olubalulekileyo kwixesha eliphantse libe ngamashumi amabini eminyaka , sifuna iqondo lokungaguquguquki kwenkqubo engxabalazele utshintsho lobunkokheli kurhulumente , kushishino nakubasebenzi . Amabakala amaninzi esicwangciso aya kufuna iminyaka yokuzama ukuveza iziphumo . Ngokomzekelo , inguqulelo kuqoqosho olusezantsi luya kufuna iinkqubo zexesha elide nemithetho yesicwangciso sesithuba iya kuthatha amashumi eminyaka ukuba ikwazi ukumelana nokwahlulwa ngokwemida yomhlaba ebangelwe kukucukulwa kwabantu Ukutshintshwa kwepolisi kumele kufikelelwe ngendlela enenkathalo esekelwe kumava nakubungqina ukuze ilizwe lingaphulukani nokubona iinjongo zexesha elide . Ukuthatha inxaxheba okulungiselelweyo : uninzi loomasipala abatsha bakhulu kakhulu ngokwemigqaliselo yesibalo sabantu nendawo evumela ukuthatha inxaxheba ngokungqalileyo kwesininzi sabahlali kwiinkqubo ezintsonkothileyo zezicwangciso . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwizicwangciso zophuhliso oluhlanganyelweyo , ngoko ke , kudinga imimiselo neenkqubo ezicacisa ukuba ngubani ongathatha inxaxheba okanye kudityanwe naye , egameni likabani , ngayiphi imiba , ngaziphi iindlela zequmrhu , nangeziphi iziphumo . Izindululo nezimvo kufuneka zibhalwe apha ecaleni kweziphumo zibonise iziphumo ezazingalindelwanga kwikholam yezimvo nezindululo . Izinto ezingaphaya kolawulo ekuthe kwadityanwa nazo kufuneka zibhalwe . Ingaba uneengcebiso zophuculo lomsebenzi ? Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwiQonga leeNgxoxo zesiCwangciso soPhuhliso oluManyanisiweyo - ukukhuthaza ukuthatha inxaxheba kwiqonga leengxoxo ngokuthe ngqo okanye ngokumelwa kweKomiti yeWadi ukuba amanye amaqela abanzi kamasipala awekho ekuthatheni inxaxheba . Uphononongo nophuhliso ( R&D ) . Ukujolisa okuhamba kunye kwiR&D nakuhlobo lokufundisa kuya kuphucula ubulunga bemfundo ephezulu , kodwa kungekho ngqwalasela , isikhundla soluntu esinganelanga siya kubambezela ukuveliswa nokwenziwa ntsho kolwazi . Iiyunivesithi kufuneka zibe ngamaziko okugqwesa kumphetho omandla wobuchwepheshe . Ngokutsala umdla wabafundi baphesheya , iiyunivesithi zingenza ingeniso nokwandisa isidibi sezakhono . Abafundi baphesheya abathweswa izidanga kwiiyunivesithi zaseMzantsi Afrika kumele balungele ukuba nemvume yeminyaka esixhenxe yokusebenza ukubakhuthaza ukuba bahlale basebenze apha . Logama uMzantsi Afrika ufuna ukuchitha ngakumbi kwiR&D jikelele , ubume bamaziko nabo kufuneka buphucule ikhonkco phakathi kweemfuno zezinto ezintsha neshishini . Urhulumente kumele abe nobambiswano necandelo labucala ukunyusa umgangatho weR&D , enemithombo ejoliswe ekwakhiweni kwezincedisi zophuhliso lophando ezifunwa kuqoqosho lweli xesha . UMzantsi Afrika unemibutho yeemanyano zorhwebo ezele ngumdla . Ngokwembali , iimanyano zorhwebo zidlale indima enkulu kwipolitiki , ziqonda ukuba imiba ebalulekileyo kumalungu azo azipheleli kumasango omzi-mveliso . Iimanyano ziqhubela phambili imidla yamalungu azo kwaye zililizwi labasebenzi bayo abasenokwenzakala , njengabasebenzi basefama , abasebenza emakhitshini okanye abenza umsebenzi wethutyana . Amalungelo neenzuzo ezinikwa abasebenzi nokunyuka kwemigangatho yokuphila abathe abasebenzi abaninzi bazibona ngo-1994 zenza inzuzo ebonakalayo kwilizwe . Ukuziswa kweenkonzo okugqalisela kubemi xa umasipala ephendula izidingo zabahlali kunokunyanzela izimvo zakhe kubahlali . Sakuba isicwangciso sizotyiwe kwaye sichonga oko kufunwa ngabahlali , kufuneka kuphuhliswe isicwangciso samanyathelo emisetyenzana akwangoko ukuze abahlali baqhubele phambili uphuhliso olulolwabo . Oku kusenokubandakanya iinkxaso-mali ngokwengqiqo yewadi ezifumanekayo , amanyathelo afanele ukuthathwa ngabahlali ukuze iiprojekthi ezithile ziqhubele phambili , kananjalo nemisebenzi yeengingqi eyodwa efana nemibhiyozo yeefestival , isiganeko sokuchola-cholwa kwenkunkuma , njl . Inkqubo ye-CBP ifanele ukwenzeka phambi kokwenziwa kwezicwangciso ze-IDP zamanyathelo okuqala naphambi kwenkqubo yophengululo ukuze i-IDP ifumane ulwazi ngesithili ngasinye sikamasipala . Ukwenziwa kwesicwangciso kufuna ukungqaliswa kwaye kungxalwe ngeenkcukacha kumasipala ngamnye . Kumzekelo wesicwangciso-buqili wokusebenzisa i-CBP njengenxalenye yomjikelo wokwenza isicwangciso , kuqaqanjiswa uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali . Oku kwenziwa kukuba uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lusisigxina lwesicwangciso salo samaxesha onyaka . INKUTHALO - ithetha ukuba oovimba akudlalwa ngabo kwinkonzo enye okanye umxhasi ngelahleko yomnye . Iqela lababhexeshi maliqaphele ukuhlaziya naziphi iinkcukacha ezintsha ezityhilwayo lize lenze izilungiso ukuze iinkcukacha ezibandakanywe kwisicwangciso zibe zezo ziqinisekiswe liqela elibanzi labahlali . Abantu , uluntu kwimimandla , amacandelo namaqela ohlukene nemidla eyohlukeneyo nemiba ephambili . Le miba inegalelo kuluntu olubanzi nolunesiphiwo . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zizive zizithembile kwaye zinaso isakhono sokuphatha zonke ezi mbono zahlukeneyo njengenzuzo kubahlali . Kukho ukunqongophala okukhulu kweendlela , amanzi nokuthungelana kombane , kwaye kuphantse akwabikho kuhanjiswa kwamanzi amdaka . Iinkqubo zokunikwa kwengxelo kufuneka zicaciswe kakuhle kulo naluphi na ulawulo lweprojekthi . Kubalulekile ukuba abantu bazi ukuba bayingenisa kubani na ingxelo , kwaye kufaneleka nini na ukuba umba udluliselwe kwisiphathamandla esingentla . Umba ngamnye kule miba kufuneka kuxoxwe ngawo kuthathwe isigqibo malunga nezigaba zokuqala zomjikelo weprojekthi . Izicwangciso nezicwangciso-qhinga aziyi kukuthathela ngqalelo ukuba amadoda namakhosikazi aneemfuno ezahlukeneyo , iminqweno , ulwazi , nesimilo kwaye iiprojekthi ziyaphulukana nengqiqo , ulwazi , amava , uthungelwano nezibonelelo ezifumaneka kwimibutho yasekuhlaleni yamakhosikazi . Nanjengoko iKomiti yeWadi ikwasebenza njengearhente eququzelela isenzo soluntu kubalulekile ukuqonda ucwangciso lwezimvo ezingundoqo ezamkelekayo zesini kwizicwangciso zesenzo nezicwangciso-qhinga . I-Intergovernmental Relations Framework Act , 2005 ithi imigangatho emithathu karhulumente kufuneka isebenze kunye ukufezekisa uphuculo lwabahlali . Ngokwamaqela ama-4 , zoba uluhlu oluneekholam ezimbini kwiphepha lokushicilela iphephandaba nize nibonisane ngokuvakalisa izimvo iindlela zokuthatha inxaxheba kweeKomiti zeWadi kumanqanaba awahlukeneyo ohlahlo lwabiwo-mali , uphawule izimvo kwikholam yesibini . UNGQUZULWANO YINXENYE YOBOMI BEMIHLA NGEMIHLA . Lwenzeka kowona mgangatho ulula , oko kukuthi , isigqibo sokuba yeyiphi impahla ekufuneka uyinxibile , okanye kokuphi okuphambili kwisicwangciso sosuku lwakho , ingxabano nomntu ozalana naye , umhlobo okanye umntu osebenza naye ukuya kwiimpikiswano zezizwe ngezizwe , iimbambano zopolitiko , okanye ingxabano ngoovimba , nenokubangela ubugebenga nokufa . Njengoko iiKomiti zeWadi zisebenzisana nabantu abaneemfuno ezohlukeneyo nezinto abazilindeleyo kwakunye noomasipala abanovimba abatshintshayo , ungquzulwano lunokwenzeka . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zikwazi ukuphendula kumaxesha ongquzulwano ngendlela eyakhayo . Esi sahluko siphawula iindidi zongquzulwano ezinokuvela nekufuneka amalungu eKomiti yeWadi akwazi ukujongana nazo . Sikwaqwalasela ubuchule bokulawula ungquzulwano ze sinikeze intshayelelo kwizakhono ezisisiseko zolawulo longquzulwano . Qwalasela iimeko ezikwiphepha 68 uze usebenze neqabane lakho ekuphawuleni ubuchule kungquzulwano obusetyenziswe kwimeko nganye . Isicwangciso sijolise kubunako obungundoqo obufunekayo ekuguquleni uqoqosho noluntu . Ukuphumeza obu bunako akuzenzekeli , kwaye abunakuvela ukuba ilizwe liqhubeka ngale ndlela kungayo . Ukuphakama kwamanqanaba odano nokungabi namonde kucebisa ukuba ixesha lelona libaluleke kakhulu : ukusilela ekwenzeni kuya kugrogrisa iinzuzo zedemokhrasi . Ngokukodwa , uMzantsi Afrika kumele ufumane iindlela zokunciphisa ngokungxamisekileyo amazinga axhalabisayo okungaqeshwa kolutsha nokubonelela abantu abaselula ngamathuba abanzi . Sebenzisa umzekelo wophando kubathathi-nxaxheba ukuziqhelanisa nenqanam ngalinye . Banike ixesha lokwenza oku uze ukhethe iqela elahlukeneyo ukubonisa indlela yokwenza inqanam ngalinye . Emva kwenqanam ngalinye , mema amanye amaqela aphose izimvo kokusebenze kakuhle aze anikezele iingcebiso zophuculo . Ngoobani Abasebenzi Bophuhliso Lwabahlali ( CDWs ) ewadini kwaye banokudlala yiphi indima ekunikeni iKomiti yeWadi inkxaso ? Iiprojekthi kufuneka zingqamane ngqo nemiba ephambili ngokubaluleka neenjongo ebeziye zabekwa ngexesha loqulunqo lwesicwangciso . Ubuchule obusekelwe kumalungelo - oku kuxa iqela kungquzulwano likholelwa ekubeni elinye lamalungelo alo lwaphuhliwe lize liye kwisigqeba esithile sifune isigqibo malunga nolu lwaphulo . Iindlela ziquka iinkundla , ukumangalelwa nolamlo . Umzekelo , abahlali baseMoutse bafune ukuqonda malunga nesigwebo somda ogqithisela iMoutse ukusuka kwiphondo laseMpumalanga ukuya eLimpopo enkundleni . Oku kubangele imeko YOKUWINA / YOKUNGAWINI . UMzantsi Afrika kufuneka ukuba ulole umphetho wezinto ezintsha kwaye uqhubekeke unegalelo kwezobunzululwazi behlabathi nokuhambela phambili kwezobugcisa . Oku kufuna utyalo-mali olukhulu kuphononongo nophuhliso , ukusetyenziswa ngcono kwemithombo ekhoyo , namaziko anobukrelekrele ngakumbi aququzelela izinto ezintsha nokukhulisa intsebenziswano phakathi kwezenzululwazi zikawonkewonke namaziko ezobugcisa namasebe abucala . Indleko yasekhaya ephakamileyo yoqhagamshelwano lomnathazwe ( i-intanethi ) yebroadband sisithintelo esimmandla . Bonke abemi boMzantsi Afrika kumele bakwazi ukufumana nokusebenzisa ulwazi ngempumelelo . Ukuza kuthi ga ngoku , amalungiselelo amaziko okulawula ulwazi , unxibelelwano nobume bobugcisa ( ICT ) kufuneka kumiswe ngokungcono ukuqinisekisa ukuba uMzantsi Afrika awuzibhaqi sele ulixhoba " kwiyantlukwano yedijithali " . Umncedisi makaqinisekise ukuba izigqibo ziyathathwa , izicwangciso ziyaphuhliswa kwaye bonke abantu bazinikele . Umncedisi olungileyo uyaziduba ngeziqulatho zentlanganiso okanye zeendibano zocweyo kunye nesimbo sokuqhuba kwazo . Ukukhulisa iinzuzo zale " nzala yokufundwa kwamanani abantu abasaphilayo nabangasaphiliyo " ilizwe lifuna isondlo esingcono nokhathalelo lwempilo , imigangatho yemfundo ephuculweyo , ukufikelela okunyusiweyo kwimfundo ethe xhaxhe nephezulu , ukungena lula kumakhondo omsebenzi nokuhamba okukhulu kwabasebenzi ( ubunakho bokuhamba kuyiwe apho kubonelewa ngemisebenzi ) . Zonke ezi meko zifuna ukuthathelwa ingqalelo kwisicwangciso sikazwelonke . Bobuphi ubuchule obusetyenzisiweyo ? Abathathi-nxaxheba mabakhunjuzwe ngesicwangciso somsebenzi nange-logframe bayiqulunqele iprojekthi yegadi engenisa imali ( kwimisebenzi 2.2 & 3.1 ) . Umthi wengxaki unokugqityezelwa ke ngoku ngokuthi kubhalwe imigca enyukayo apha phakathi kweembangi ezi ngeenjongo zokubonisa unxulumano phakathi kwazo ( kwesi siqingatha somthi singezantsi ) nonxulumano kwiziphumo ( kwesi siqingatha singentla ) . Kufuneka kubhalwe imigca exwesileyo ebonakalisa apho kukho iimbangi ezidibanayo , okanye iziphumo ezidibeneyo .
