Iiprojekthi ezisebenzise ukulingana ngokwesini kwaye zakhuthaza izicwangciso zesenzo sokuvuma ukuquka igalelo lamakhosikazi kwiiKomiti zeWadi zisebenze kakuhle kakhulu kwaye zixhathise macala . Phawula iimfuno zoluntu kummandla uze ucebise iiprojekthi ezinokuphucula ubomi babantu kwiwadi . UMBUZO 1 Yintoni injongo yenkqubo yolawulo lomsebenzi ? Basebenzisane nabanye kuluntu ukubhekisela phambili uphuhliso , kusonjululwe iingxaki kwaye kuphakanyiswe iinkxalabo zabo bangenalizwi nabachwethelwe bucala . Umsebenzi ophambili weeKomiti zeWadi kukuncedisa ooceba abanyulwe ngokwedemokrasi ukufeza amagunya abawanikiweyo ngempumelelo nokumela abantu bewadi . Imfundo ethe xhaxhe noqeqesho ( FET ) . Isixokelelwanlo seFET asinampumelelo . Sincinci kakhulu kwaye nobulunga beziphumo buphantsi . Ukuphuculwa kobulunga obuqhubekekayo buyafuneka njengokuba isixokelelwano sisanda . Ubulunga nokunxulumana kwezifundo kufuna ingqwalasela engxamisekileyo . Xa ubulunga buqalisa ukuphucuka nokuqesheka kwabathweswe izidanga buqala ukwanda , isigunyaziso seenkonzo zeFET kuya kunyuka ngokuzenzekelayo . Ngokulula kukhulisa isebe kungakhange kujoliswe kubulunga kungaphantse kubize kakhulu ngokwexabiso kwaye kutyhafise ebantwini abaselula , okungcolisa igama lesixokelelwana ngokuthe xhaxhe . Ngowama-2030 , icandelo leFET kumele libonelele malunga nomyinge wama-25 ekhulwini wabantu abaselungelweni ngeminyaka , okuthetha ukunyuka ukusuka malunga nama-300 000 namhlanje ukuya kwisigidi esi-1.25 ngowama-2030 . Inkcitho yotyalo-mali eMzantsi Afrika kuwe ukusuka kumyinge ophantsi yangumyinge ongama-30 ekhulwini weGDP kubutsha bowe-1980 ukuya malunga nomyinge we-16 ekhulwini weGDP kubutsha bowama-2000 . Inkcitho yamaziko akhoyo oluntu kananjalo ikumaqondo asezantsi ngemigangatho yembali . Ngokusebenzayo , uMzantsi Afrika uphoswe ukuvezwa kotyalo-mali okusisixa kwiindlela , kumgaqo wololiwe , kumanxweme , kumbane , kumanzi , kugutyulo , kuthutho loluntu nakwizindlu . Ukukhula ngokukhawuleza nangendlela ebandakanya ngakumbi , ilizwe lifuna iqondo eliphezulu lokusetyenziswa kwezimali . Ukubunjwa kwezimali ezinze kwisambuku kufuneka kufike malunga nomyinge wama-30 ekhulwini weGDP ngowama-2030 , apho utyalo-mali lwecandelo loluntu lufikelela kumyinge we-10 ekhulwini weGDP , ukuqonda ifuthe eligcinakalayo ekukhuleni nakwiinkonzo zemizi . Kumsebenzi olandelayo amalungu abahlali ayila ixesha elimisiweyo elilanda umkhondo wembali yabahlali . Ngokuchonga izimbo nemikhwa lo msebenzi ufanele ukuyenza nzulu ingqiqo yabahlali ngemeko yabo ubenze bacinge ngempumelelo yamathuba ongenelelo angaphambili . I-Seymour liziko lonikezelo lweenkonzo elincinci elisemaphandleni kumantla eCiskei . Inenani labemi elimalunga nabantu abangama-3 000 . Malunga nama-80% yabantu kummandla abangenamisebenzi , nama-60% yabantu abangakwaziyo ukufunda nokubhala . Ukwakha urhulumente onobunakho nophuhlisayo . Imingeni emininzi ifuna ingqwalasela , kuquka nokunqongophala okumandundu kwezakhono , isixokelelwano esixananazileyo sothungelwano kumasebe karhulumente , amaqondo aphezulu orhwaphilizo , ubuthathaka bokunika ingxelo , ukuvelela uwiso-mthetho okubuthathaka nembali ende yokwenza mfiliba imigca phakathi kweqela norulumente . Le yimiba yobunzima , efuna ukuzibhenca okuthembakeleyo , ukucwangcisa okwenziwe ngenkathalo nobunkokheli obuthatha izigqibo . Nyula amavolontiya amabini ukuba enze umdlalo-linganiso wemizuzu emithathu uze uwanike imizuzu embalwa ukuba acinge ngendlela aya kuyidlala ngayo indima yawo . Musa ukuvumela ukuba abanye abadlali okanye abathathi-nxaxheba bazibone iindima . Xelela iqela ukuba liya kube libukele umdlalo-linganiso . Bakhumbuze ukuba abadlali ababonisi zimvo zabo , koko izimvo abacelwe ukuba bazidlale . Uxanduva lokunika inkcazo lolunye lwemithetho-siseko ephambili yokuthatha inxaxheba neeKomiti zeWadi , njengooceba abanyuliweyo , banoxanduva lokunika inkcazo kuluntu lommandla elisebenzisana nawo . Ukubeka iliso nokuvavanya iiprojekthi zoluntu ekuhlaleni nogqithiso lwarhoqo lwengxelo eluntwini ngenkqubela-phambili yozalisekiso yindlela esebenza kakhulu yokujonga imiba ethile . Ukunxibelelana okuchanekileyo ngolwazi phakathi kwebhunga noluntu kummandla kunye naphakathi kwamaqela achaphazelekayo ewonke ngumba ophambili . Ulwazi olungachanekanga lungakhokelela kwiingxabano phakathi kwamaqela . Kungakhuthaza ukusasazeka kwamarhe kuze kudale nokubhideka phakathi kwabanye abahlali . Oku kungabuyisela emva uphuhliso okanye inkqubela-phambili ngokwe-IDP okanye ezinye iiprojekthi . IiKomiti zeWadi zisebenzisana nabahlalilwamaqela achaphazelekayo . Oku kuquka ucebawewadi , amagosa kamasipala ukuquka usibonda , umanejala kamasipala , abasebenzi bakamasipala , abasebenzi bophuhliso lwemimandla , iinkokeli zomthonyama noluntu kwimimandla , nabaquka inani lamaqela anomdla awohlukeneyo anjengemibutho esekelwe kwinkolo , ushishino kummandla , amaqela olutsha , amaqela amakhosikazi , imibutho yamafama namanye amaqela kumacandelo nemibutho . Isazisi - Abahlali bangangafani ngokobuhlanga , inkolo , indawo abasuka kuzo , nokunobangela ungquzulwano . Inani labantu abaninzi abasuka kwelinye ilizwe abanolwimi nenkcubeko eyohlukileyo okanye abasuka kwelinye iphondo okanye idolophu bangabangela ungquzulwano . La maqela asekuhlaleni angabonwa njengendlela engentlanga ngamanye amalungu asekuhlaleni . Ulwakhiwo lwezindlu : Isicelo semali kwiBhodi yoLwakhiwo-zindlu kuZwelonke ekuqwalaseleni iingxaki ezinkulu kulwakhiwo-zindlu kummandla kwamkelwe . Kodwa ke , ukulibaziseka ekukhupheni imali enjalo , amabango omhlaba kwisiza sophuhliso kunye nokukhutshwa okucothayo komhlaba karhulumente kuluntu kummandla kulibazise kakhulu ukuzalisekiswa kweprojekthi . Iikomiti zeeWadi zifanele ukwandisa inxaxheba yazo kurhulumente wengingqi . Zinika unxulumano phakathi kwabahlali nebhunga likamasipala . Iikomiti zeeWadi zinako ukunika amacebiso kwilungu lebhunga leWadi elithi lona ligqithisele amacebiso abalulekileyo kuSomlomo kamasipala malunga nemigaqo-nkqubo echaphazela iWadi . Ngowama-2030 , isixokelelwano sempilo kumele sibonelele ukhathalelo olunobulunga kuye wonke ubani , simahla kwindawo yenkonzo , okanye kuhlawulelwe sisibonelelo soluntu okanye bucala ngokuxhaswa yi-inshorensi . Izixokelelwano zempilo zokuqala nezengingqi kumele zibonelele ngokufikelela okunye , ngomgqalisela kuthintelo , kwimfundo , ulawulo lwezifo nonyango . Izibhedlele kumele zisebenze ngokwempumelelo nokusebenzayo , zibonelela ngokhathalelo lobulunga besibini nomgangatho wesithathu kwabo bafuna oko . Iingcali zempilo zangakumbi kumele zibekhona , ingakumbi kuluntu oluhleleleke kakhulu . NKQUBO YOKUVANDLAKANYA IZINTO EZIRHESHIWEYO KUMAKHOSIKAZI NAMADODA KUSO NASIPHI ISENZO ESICWANGCISIWEYO , KUQUKA UWISO-MTHETHO , IMIGAQO-NKQUBO OKANYE IINKQUBO , KUYO NAYIPHI INDAWO NAKUYO YONKE IMIGANGATHO . SISICWANGCISO-QHINGA SOKWENZA AMAXHALA NAMAVA AMAKHOSIKAZI NAMADODA UKUBA ABE NGUMBA OPHAMBILI KUYILO , KUKWENZIWA , KUKUSA ISO NOKUVAVANYWA KWEMIGAQO-NKQUBO NEENKQUBO KUYO YONKE IMIGANGATHO YOPOLITIKO , YOQOQOSHO NEYENTLALO UKWENZELA UKUBA AMAKHOSIKAZI NAMADODA ANGCAMLE NGOKULINGANAYO , KWAYE UKUNGALINGANI AKUGCINWA . INJONGO EPHAMBILI KUKUPHUMEZA UKULINGANA NGOKWESINI . Ukufezekisa ezi zincediso zophuhliso emazijongwe kuqala , , , kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukuba uluntu lwasemaphandleni lungazuza kuwo omabini amaziko ezambuku nokufana nomnatha nokuba amaxabiso ala maziko anobuntununtunu kwiimfuno zoluntu lwasemaphandleni . Ababhexeshi mabanikwe inkxaso ziingcali ze-CBP . Iingcali ziya kunika inkxaso yezobuchule neyolungiselelo lwendlela yokusebenza kwaye ziyakwabelwa uxanduva lweewadi ezithile . Inzululwazi nobugcisa ziyaqhubekeka ngokuguqula indlela iimpahla neenkonzo eziveliswa nezirhwetywa ngayo . Njengelizwe elinengeniso ephakathi , uMzantsi Afrika kufuneka usebenzise ulwazi neemveliso ezintsha ukukhuphisana . Uwodwa nje , indleko ekhuphisanayo engakumbi yemveliso ayiyi kwanela ukwandisa ubukho behlabathi kushishino loMzantsi Afrika . Oku kusebenza kuzo zombini amashishini amatsha namacandelo emveli , afana nemigodi . Izinto ezintsha ziyimfuneko kwilizwe elinengeniso ephakathi ukuze liphuhle . ULUNTU JIKELELE NAPHI NA EHLABATHINI LUBEKA INDLELA OLUBONA NGAYO URHULUMENTE KUHLOBO NOMGANGATHO WEENKONZO OLUZIFUMANA EZANDLENI ZABASEBENZI BEENKONZO ZOLUNTU . UBUSO BUKARHULUMENTE BUBUSO NELIZWI LABANIKEZELI BEENKONZO ABAPHAMBI KWABANTU . YILOO NTO KUPHELA ABANTU ABAYIFUMANAYO , KWAYE UKUBA IINKONZO IINKONZO OKANYE AZINIKWA NGABUBELE , URHULUMENTE UKHAWULEZA ATHATHWE NJENGONGENAMPUMELELO NOLAWULA NGEGQUDU , UKUBA IINKONZO IINKONZO , URHULUMENTE AKAMHLANGA , KODWA UKUBA IINKONZO ZINTLE NORHULUMENTE MHLE , KULULA KANGAKO . OKU YINYANISO ENGQINWA KWIHLABATHI LIPHELA KWAYE AKUKHO MAHLUKO NASEMZANTSI AFRIKA KUNJALO . IMimiselo yoCwangciso lukaMasipala noKwenziwa koMsebenzi , 2001 icacisa ubume beeNkqubo zoLawulo loMsebenzi . Njengoko iiKomiti zeWadi zidlala indima ekubekeni iliso kwindlela esebenzayo kamasipala , amalungu kufuneka aziqonde iziqulathe zemimiselo . Iminyaka elishumi elinesibhozo kulawulo lwesininzi , uMzantsi Afrika usashiyeke noluntu oluphakamileyo ngokungalingani apho abantu abaninzi behlala ebuhlwempini kwaye bembalwa kakhulu abasebenzayo . Ubulunga bemfundo yesikolo kuninzi lwabafundi abamnyama ihlelelekile . Ukwahlulwa kwentlalo ngocalucalulo kuyaqhubeka ukongamela imbonakalo-mhlaba . Isahlulo esikhulu sabantu abasebatsha baziva ukuba izinto ezingangqinelaniyo zifumbile zichasene nabo . Nelifa localucalulo liyaqhubekeka ukumisela amathuba obomi kwisixa esisisininzi . Le mingeni imandla ingalungiswa ngotshintsho lwenyathelo ekusebenzeni kwelizwe . Makuthathelwe ingqalelo kubandakanywe isiphumo esibekwe phambili esivela kumaqela abengawona ebehlelelekile . Ukumisela uthungelwano lweenzululwazi ngokhanyo lwefayibha kuzwelonke , kummandla nakumasipala ekuboneleleni ngomqolo kufikelelo lwebroadband . Utyalo-mali labucala kufuneka lukhokele indlela kule ngingqi , luncediswa ziimali zoluntu ezifunekayo ekuhlangabezeni iinjongo zasekuhlaleni . Iinkqubo ezisebenzayo , imithetho nokulungiswa kwamaziko ekuphumezeni oku okufuneka ngokungxamisekileyo . Ukutshintsha olu qoqosho yiprojekthi engumngeni , neyexesha elide . Ngokushwankathela , sicebisa ukuba kukhuliswe uvimba woluntu , umthamo wemveliso nezincedisi zophuhliso ukunyusaokuthunyelwa kwamanye amazwe , okuya kunyusa imithombo yotyalo-mali kwaye kunciphise ukuxhomekeka kwizimali ezivela ngaphandle . Utyalo-mali oluphakamileyo , oluxhaswa zizinto zoluntu ezingcono nezakhono , luya kwenza ukuba uqoqosho lukhule ngokukhawuleza kwaye kube nemveliso ngakumbi . Ukunyuka kwengqesho nokubanemveliso kuya kukhokelela ekunyukeni kwemivuzo nemigangatho yokuphila nokungalingani okuphantsi . Ukutshintshela uqoqosho lutyekele kutyalo-mali ngakumbi nasekusetyenzisweni okusezantsi kuyimfuneko ekuhlumeni koqoqosho lwexesha elide . Xa sele igqityiwe i-IDP , kufuneka igqithiswe kwibhunga likamasipala ukuze iqwalaselwe kwaye yamkelwe . Ibhunga kufuneka lijonge ukuba i-IDP iyiphawule na imiba ( iingxaki ) ezichaphazela ummandla nobungakanani begalelo lezicwangciso-nkqubo neeprojekthi ekuqwalaseleni ezi ngxaki . Ibhunga kufuneka liphinde liqinisekise ukuba i-IDP iyathobelana nemfuno yomthetho ngaphambi kolwamkelo . Unxibelelwano luthungelwano lwababini . Kukuhamba nokutshintshiselana ngolwazi nezimvo ezisuka komnye umntu ukuya komnye . Yinkqubo apho umntu , oko kukuthi UMTHUMELI , ethumela umyalezo komnye umntu ofumana umyalezo , lowo NGUMAMKELI . Ukuba asiqhagamshelani ngokufanelekileyo , oku kukhokelela ekuxhalabeni , ukungavumelani nokungavisisani okunokubakho . Ngenxa yokuba iiKomiti zeWadi ziluthungelwano olubalulekileyo kunxibelelwano olukumgangatho wengingqi , kufuneka ziqinisekise ukuba ulwazi ezilunikezelayo kubahlali luchanekile kwaye luyaqondakala kumntuni wonke kwaye nalo lugqithisa ulwazi oluchanekileyo kwibhunga kunye namalungu ebhunga . Mabakhunjuzwe abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba ilogframe yitheyibhile nje efanele kubancedisa , ingabathinteli . Kufuneka abantu bayijonge njengoxwebhu oluphilayo oluza kumana lusenziwa iinguqulelo luhlengahlengiswe njengokuba ixesha lisiya lihamba nje . Ngendlela ebambekayo iBatho Pele iza kuchaphazela indlela ekusetyenzwa ngayo ngokusebenzisa iPMS nemisela izalathiso zokusebenza ize incede urhulumente wengingqi nabemi ukuba balinganise umsebenzi besebenzisa ezi zalathiso . Apho ibonisa ukungasebenzi inceda ekukhawuleziseni ungenelelo olufunekayo . Luquka amanqanam esicwangciso , ukulandelela nokunika ingxelo nohlaziyo lonyaka lomsebenzi . Uphuhliso loMzantsi Afrika luchatshazelwe kokwenzekayo kummandla nakwihlabathi . Impumelelo iya kuxhomekeka ekuqondeni nasekuphenduleni kwelizwe kwinkqubela enjalo . Ukongeza kukusingasinga okuthe vetshe kwamanani abantu abasaphilayo nabangasaphiliyo , isicwangciso sixoxa iintsingiselo eziphawulekayo ezintlanu : ukutshintsha koqoqosho kwihlabathi , ubugcisa , okwelizwe jikelele , ukutshintsha kwemozulu nokukhula koqoqosho lwase-Afrika . UMSEBENZI 2 Zeziphi iindlela zokubandakanya abathathi-nxaxheba bangaphandle . Inani lemithetho liphunyeziwe yiPalamente , emva konyulo lonyaka ka-1994 , elixhasa nelomeleza isikhundla soomasipala ekulawuleni imicimbi yabo nasekwenzeni imisebenzi yabo ngendlela ethatha inxaxheba nedityanelweyo . Ukwakhiwa kokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu . Imibutho yoluntu lukarhulumente nokuthatha inxaxheba kwimicimbi yoluntu kuyafuneka ekusekeni uluntu olukhuselekileyo . Amaziko okhuseleko oluntu kumelwe kucingwe ngawo . Iimvula ezinkulu zenze ukhukuliseko kumhlaba ongaphezulu ezigadini . Amanzi aye angena ematankini , into ke leyo eya kuba luncedo kakhulu kwezi nyanga zizayo , kodwa kodwa okuza kufuna ukwenziwa ukuze kubuyiselwe iprojekthi le kwisimo efanele ukuba kuso . Ukugrumba ubutyebi bezimbiwa ukuvelisa ubutyebi bokunyusa imigangatho yokuphila , izakhono namaziko yindlela egcinakalayo . Le ngcinga ikwamkela ' ixabiso lemvelo ' lomntu wonke . Oku kuthetha ukuba wonke umntu unegalelo angalenza kuzo zonke iinkalo zobomi babo . Ikwamkela neekomiti zewadi njengeziko elilikhonkco elidibanisa iinkokeli ezinyuliweyo nabantu . Isixokelelwano esimacala maninzi ekuqeshweni kweentloko zamasebe kumele kwaziswe , kubandakanywe omabini amaqalela opolitiko nolawulo . Eyona mibandela ibaluleke kakhulu kubahlali . Ingaba iKomiti yeWadi ingenza ntoni ukuncedisa ? Kwixesha lokuqala lokwenziwa kwaso , mhlawumbi siya kuqulatha imiba emininzi yenkqubo . Nangona kunjalo , njengoko siphunyezwa kwintlanganiso nganye yeKomiti yeWadi siya kuba yinto esebenziseka ngakumbi njengoko kuqala umsebenzi . Ukuze iprojekthi ibe nempumelelo , kubalulekile ukuba inxaxheba noxanduva lwelungu ngalinye zicaciswa kakuhle . Ilungu ngalinye elibandakanyekayo kwiprojekthi lunoxanduva lokuba liyenze indima yalo ngendlela eyenza igalelo ekufezekisweni kweenjongo zeprojekthi , liqinisekise kanjalo ukuba inempumelelo iprojekthi . Ubungakanani : Ukuqeshwa kwabantu abajongene neendawo zokupaka izithuthi / oonogada bezithuthi abasebenza iishifti ezimbini . IBatho Pele imisela ukuba amasebe ayo yomibini imigangatho , okazwelonke nowamaphondo kufuneka ibe nePMS equka ukumisela izalathiso zokunikezelwa kweenkonzo nemilinganiselo yokulawula loo msebenzi . UMzantsi Afrika kumele uthathe amanyathelo kumba wokuba izigidi zabantu abanakho bafuna ukusebenza . Kwixesha elifutshane , uqoqosho kufuneka ludale imisebenzi kubemi boMzantsi Afrika abangaqeshwanga , abo uninzi lwabo beselula kwaye benezakhono ezisezantsi , logama kuphuculwa izakhono nolwazi kuqoqosho olwahlukileyo kwixa elizayo . Ukunyusa amaqondo engqesho kuya kuba neenzuzo ezingaphaya kwamava okuxhobisa okuba nomsebenzi . Kuya kunceda abantu ekutyaleni kwimfundo yabantwana babo , baphucule amakhaya abo nokulawula imingcipheko yobomi . Kuvela imeko ize impendulo koku ivele ngokoluvo neengqiqo . Ingaba uphando lohlolo lweemfuno / isiseko luquka udliwano-ndlebe lwamakhosikazi namadoda kwaye lumele iindidi zonke zasekuhlaleni ( omncinci / omdala , emaphandleni / ezidolophini , ngeqela lesithethe ? ) Angakwazi amadoda namakhosikazi ukuqhuba udliwano-ndlebe nokuqokelela idatha ? Ulondolozo : Ingaba isixa somhlaba wasendle okanye wendalo wandile okanye ucuthekile ? Kutheni ? Ingaba iindawo ezinokhuselo zisekiwe ? Ingaba kukho imimandla yeemeko zamawa , umhlaba okanye amathambeka aneengxaki malunga nokwakha , umz. amathambeka angumnqantsa , imihlaba exinene ngamanzi , iliwa elingathembekanga eligqumekileyo ? Kuyimfuneko ukuthoba indleko yokuphila kwimizi ehlelelekileyo . Amanye amaqalela esicwangciso aya kubanempembelelo yokunyuswa kwendleko kuqoqosho . Ngokukodwa , ukwenza amaziko abe ngaweli xesha emva kwamashumi eminyaka yotyalo-mali olungaphantsi kungafuna iindleko eziphezulu . Ukuqalisa oku kunyuka , inkqubo kumele ukuba ijolise ekunyuseni ukuba nokhuphiswano nokutyala kumaziko amatsha kwiinkalo ezichaphazela abantu ngokuthe ngqo , okufana nodederhu lwamaxabiso okutya , uthutho lukawonkewonke , imfundo nempilo , nothungelwano ngocingo . Ukusebenza okukhulu kwecandelo loluntu kuya kukhokelela nako kubume bendleko esezantsi kuqoqosho . Qinisekisa ukuba iiprojekthi eziphawuliweyo zinxulumene ngokuthe ngqo nemiba ephambili kunye neenjongo ezaziphawulwe kumanqanaba adlulileyo . YIMFUNEKO ESEMTHETHWENI UKUBA UMASIPALA NGAMNYE APHUHLISE inkqubo yolawulo lomsebenzi ( PMS ) . Injongo ye-PMS kukuba noxanduva lokusebenzisa oovimba bakamasipala , ukuphucula inkuthalo nokusebenza okufanelekileyo kwemibutho kwakunye nokubonisa ukufezekiswa kweziphumo . Ukunyusa uluntu olusebenzayo ekomelezeni uphuhliso , idemokhrasi nokunika ingxelo . Intlanganiso yeqela elikhulu kunye neqela labahlali ngokubanzi apho umsebenzi weveki ubandakanya iMephu Yendlela , iziphumo ezihlanganiselweyo neenkcukacha ngesiphumo ngasinye kuxoxwa ngayo kuze kuvunyelwane ngemicimbi ephambili yoluntu . Chaza ukuba xa oku sekwenziwe phakathi kwabahlali umntu okubhalayo unokusebenzisa imizuzu kanobhala , iingxelo zabahlali namanqaku ababhexeshi ukuze afumane iinkcukacha xa kuyimfuneko oko . Ukuchonga imibandela neqela elinqwenela ukuxoxa ngayo nzulu . Oku kusenokuba kukukhulelwa kolutsha , ubukho beHIV neAIDS okanye nayiphi eminye imibandela echongwa ngabahlali njengebalulekileyo . Ukuhlola iimpembelelo zamandla okanye ukuhluma kwengxaki bhala iminyaka kwifliptshathi uze ubhale phantsi konyaka ngamnye ubuzaza bengxaki . Indlela abasebenzisana ngayo oomasipala namanqanaba karhulumente kazwelonke nawamaphondo . Uyinkosikazi . Ulima imifuno ukwenzela ukuba usapho lutye . Umyeni wakho usebenza kwidolophana kwaye lilungu leKomiti yeWadi yengingqi . Usapho lwakho luyayitya eminye imifuno kwaye eshiyekileyo uyayithengisa emarikeni kwaye oku kukunika imali yokuba uyisebenzise . Ngapha koko awunamali iyeyakho . Umyeni wakho akakuniki imali , uzisa nje ukutya nezinye izinto eziyimfuneko esuka nazo kwidolophana . Kufuneka unemadlana ekhoyo ukwenzela ukuba ube ungathengela abantwana bakho izipho ezincinci , okanye uhlawule iklinikhi xa ufuna ukuya khona . Umyeni wakho ufika ekhaya ze akuxelele ukuba umhlobo wakhe ubonelele ngokuba athengise isivuno sakho semifuno kwidolophu enkulwana . IKhomishoni yamaLungelo oLuntu inamagunya okuphanda iphinde igqithise ingxelo ngamalungelo oluntu , ukuthatha amanyathelo okuqwalasela ukwaphula amalungelo abantu , ukuphanda nokufundisa ngamalungelo abantu . Ukwamkelwa kwendlela ehlanganisiweyo . Ukuphumeza uluntu olukhuselekileyo kuthetha ukulwa oonobangela abasisiseko sobundlobongela , okufuna uluhlu olubanzi lwemithombo karhulumente neyoluntu . Ukwandisa ukomelela kwabantu noqoqosho kutshintsho lwemozulu . Icandelo 29(b) Lomthetho lixoxa ngenkqubo efanele ukulandelwa xa kuphuhliswa i-IDP kwaye libalula ukuba abahlali bengingqi makudityanwe nabo kulumano-ndlebe malunga neemfuno zophuhliso nemiba ephambili ye-IDP kananjalo nokuthatha inxaxheba kuyilo lwayo . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziphuhlise isicwangciso-nkqubo sokuqinisekisa ukuba abahlali bahlala besazi malunga nemiba yebhunga ukuze nebhunga lihlale lisazi malunga nemiba eqhubeka ekuhlaleni neempendulo zalo kwizicwangciso nezigqibo zebhunga . Imbalelwano - ezi ziileta eziya kwikomiti okanye ziileta ezithunyelwa yikomiti . Ileta nganye mayiqwalaselwe yikomiti njengoko iileta zithunyelwa egameni layo . Omnye kweyona misebenzi ebaluleke kakhulu kamasipala kukufumanisa iimfuno zabemi bakhe kunye nendlela engcono yokunikezela ezi mfuno . Bonke abemi boMzantsi Afrika kumele bakhuthazwe ekufundeni ulwimi lwaseAfrika kwaye iinkqubo zikarhulumente kumele zisebenze ekwenzeni oku kube yinene . Ukuphuhlisa amashishini afana nokusetyenzwa komhlaba , ukhenketho , ukuloba namashisini amancinci apho ubunakho bukhona . Yabelanani ngeezimvo neqela lilonke . Ukubeka esweni kumsebenzi wamagosa . Umzekelo wokusombulula ingxaki sisixhobo esisebenza kakhulu ekuncediseni iiKomiti zeWadi . Masijonge umzekelo ongezantsi nokuba ungasetyenziswa njani na . Phendula - uphendule njani kolu ngquzulwano ? Enyanisweni , uninzi lwezi nkcukacha luya kuba luhlanganiselwe kwangaphambili ziingcaphephe ze-CBP , kodwa qwalasela neKomiti yeKomiti noceba xa kukho nayiphi imithombo enoncedo yeenkcukacho enokusetyenziswa . Okujoliswe kuko kwisambuku somhlaba neelwandle phantsi kokhuselo ( okwangoku malunga nezigidi ezi-7.9 zeehekthare zomhlaba , ama-848km onxweme ne-4 172km2 olwandle lukhuselekile ) . Ibhunga likamasipala kwakhona kufuneka lihlole ukuba ingaba lihlangabezana kakuhle kangakanani neenjongo zalo . Oku likwenza ngokubonisana nabahlali kunye nemibutho yabahlali malunga nokusebenza kwalo . Makukhunjulwe : amalungu amaqela achaphazelekayo angaba ngamalungu kumaqela ngamaqela ahlukeneyo , kwaye ke amaqela achaphazelekayo asingaba basoloko bephuma into ngomlomo qha ! Indima yeeKomiti zeeWadi iphinda yolulelwe ekunikeni isakhono nokomeleza amalinge abahlali okuphumeza iinjongo zeeprojekthi abazibandakanye kuzo . Amaqela athatha amanyathelo okanye iikomiti ezisekwe phakathi kwabahlali zokuphumeza iiprojekthi ezithile ziya kuzuza okuthile kulwazi olusisiseko solawulo lweprojekthi . Ukomeleza ubunakho bokucwangcisa bukarhulumente . Ukuqinisekisa ukumelwa kwamaqela achaphazelekayo kwiiprojekthi zeekomiti ezingaphantsi . Incutshe yesini , okanye umntu onolwazi ngemiba yesini , kufanele abe yinxalenye yawo onke amaqela ovavanyo olungundoqo lwenkqubo . Inzame kufanele ukuba yenziwe ukwenzela ukuba amadoda namakhosikazi amelwe kula maqela . Amacandelo ophuhliso kurhulumente wengingqi anjengohlahlo lwabiwo-mali nenkqubo yemimiselo yedolophu , ulawulo olusekelwe kummandla , ulawulo lokusebenza kwabasebenzi bakamasipala nesicwangciso sophuhliso esimanyanisiweyo ( IDP ) kwaye zizonke zinika amathuba okuthatha inxaxheba kwiinkqubo zikamasipala . Ukuphumeza nokugcina olu lungelelwano kufuna umelelo lwezinto ezininzi , ayizizo zonke eziphantsi kolawulo lukarhulumente . Uqoqosho olukhulayo , ukunyuka kwengqesho nemivuzo , ukuwa kokungalingani , ukuphucuka kwenkqubo yemfundo , iimeko ezinobutyebi zoshishino nokuqhubekeka kokufundela ikhondo elithile ziya kuba negalelo elibonakalayo ekumanyeni abantu baseMzantsi Afrika . Iinkqubo ezifana nesenzo sokunikezwa kwamathuba emisebenzi kwababewavinjiwe , ukuxhotyiswa kwabantu abamnyama kuqoqosho nokubuyiselwa komhlaba zezona ziyimpumelelo xa uqoqosho lukhula nenkqubo yemfundo iphucuka . Kungekho ubume obulolo hlobo , la malinge anganyusa amaqondo okujamelana ekuhlaleni . Esi sicwangciso senza iingcebiso ezininzi zokuphucula amandla eenkqubo zokulungisa , ngokukodwa ezo zinxulumene nokwenziwa banzi kwamathuba oqoqosho kwabo babengalungiselelwa ngokwembali . Uthethwano nengxelo - iKomiti yeWadi yenza iqonga , umzekelo , lokwenza amalungiselelo entlanganiso kawonke-wonke yoluntu , ukuqhuba intlanganiso ye-stokvel , ukuqhuba intlanganiso yombutho wezemidlalo , njl-njl , ukunikezela ulwazi nengxelo kubahlalimalunga nezigqibo zebhunga nemiba eveliswe ngabahlali ebichazwe kuceba okanye kwibhunga . Vulela imvula yeengcinga ngeentlobo ezahluka-hlukeneyo zeenkcukacha kumasipala wabo ezinokuba luncedo malunga nokwenziwa kwesicwangciso . Thatha iimpendulo uze uzibhale kwifliptshathi ukuze bonke babone . Indlela ye-WID ithambekela ukubona amakhosikazi njengabafumani abangasebenziyo boncedo lophuhliso , endaweni yokuba babe ziiarhente ezisebenzayo ekuguquleni okanye ekutshintsheni iinyaniso zabo zoqoqosho , zentlalo , zopolitiko nezenkcubeko . Isiphumo esiphambili sibe kukuba amaxhala amakhosikazi ayejongwa ewodwa njengemiba eyahlukileyo , ekhokelela ekusingelweni phantsi kwabo kwinkqubo yesizwe namanye amaqumrhu asekuhlaleni . Ngokwenzekayo , indlela ye-WID iphatha imiba yamakhosikazi njengokuba ayinxulumananga nemiba yophuhliso engundoqo njengemiba yamalungelo oluntu , ulawulo lwedemokhrasi , ukukhuselwa kwendawo , umanyano lwehlabathi , uxolo nokuncitshiswa kwemikhosi , njl . Intloko yolawulo lwenkonzo yoluntu kumele isekwe , ibenoxanduva lokulawula ukuqhubekeka komsebenzi weentloko zamasebe , kuquka namaqela ahlalelayo kugayo , ukuhlolwa kokusebenza neenkqubo zokuqeqesha . Ukuzimasa iintlanganiso zebhunga - yenza uluhlu lwamalungu eKomiti yeWadi uze wabele ilungu ngalinye intlanganiso ekufuneka liyizimase . Izicwangciso ze-IDP zenziwa ngothethwano phakathi kwamasebe nabani na onomdla kwiziphumo . Ukwenziwa kwezigqibo kwenziwa ngendlela engenamfihlo neyedemokhrasi . Oovimba babelwa imisebenzi enceda ekufezekiseni iinjongo ekuvunyelwene ngazo zophuhliso lukamasipala . Obu buchule besicwangciso-nkqubo buyilelwe ukuba neziphumo zemisebenzi eya kuba negalelo kuphuhliso lulonke lommandla njengenzuzo kumntu wonke . IiKomiti zeWadi yindlela yonxibelelwano olusesikweni phakathi kubahlali nebhunga . Ingaba uneentlobo zohlahlo-lwabiwo-mali zosapho ukuba kunjalo ziqulethe ntoni ? Cela abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba banikezele imizekelo yezinto abanokuzibandakanya kwiindleko nomvuzo xa kusenziwa uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwasekhaya . Bhala le miba iphambili kwifliptshathi phantsi kweekholam ezimbini , ezizezi , INKCITHO NOMVUZO . Inkcitho ingaquka ifowuni , umbane , imirhumo yesikolo . Umvuzo ungaquka umvuzo wenyanga , irente ( ukuba kurentwa igumbi kwikhaya labo okanye ngabanini kwipropati engenye ) , umsebenzi owongeziweyo abawenzayo ozisa umvuzo . Ukuxolisa - livela kwigama elithi ' xolisa ' elithetha ukuzolisa okanye ukuphelisa ingxabano . Ibhunga lihlawula ' inkonzo yomlomo ' kwizimvo neziphakamiso zabahlali ukubagcina bonwabile kodwa alenzi nje okanye linike ingqalelo naziphi iziphakamiso neengcebiso . Ipesenti yemizi efikelelayo kumgangatho osisiseko wamanzi , ugutyulo lwelindle , umbane nokuhanjiswa kwenkunkuma engamanzanga . Kubalulekile ukuluqonda ulwimi olusetyenziswa kwi-PCM , nokuba ngawaphi na amagama ebeya kusetyenziswa kweminye imilinganiselo , njengoko amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi kusenokufuneka ukuba zijongane nala magama apha ekuhambeni kwexesha . Ulwimi olusetyenzisiweyo kule modyuli lulwimi oludla ngokusetyenziswa kwiimeko zolawulo lweedolophu nezithili apha eMzantsi Afrika . Umgangatho wokuphila omncinci owamkelekileyo kumele uchazwe , kuquka oko kufunwayo ukwenza abantu baphuhlise ubunakho babo . Le modyuli yahlulwe yaba zizahluko ezine ; esokuqala yintshayelelo ngalo mba wolawulo lweprojekthi , size ke ngasinye kwezinye ezi sithathe isigaba esinye kwezi zithathu . Thatha iimpendulo emaqeleni . Xa engaphezu kweqela elinye amaqela anombuzo ofanayo qiniseka ukuba iqela ngalinye lifaka igalelo . Umzekelo unako ukucela iqela elinye ukuba liphendule umbuzo omnye ukuze elinye liphendule owesibini . Kungenjalo , ungathatha iimpendulo ezimbalwa kwiqela ngalinye uze ugqithele kwiqela elilandelayo . Imithombo nezixhobo ezisetyenziswayo - kuluncedo ukulungisa uludwe kuselithuba nokuchonga izinto ezifunekayo , isixa esifunekayo nento eza kunceda ngayo . Oku kunokubandakanya izinto ezisisiseko ezifana nephepha neepeni kunye neefom , ii-laptop nee-datha projektha . Ulungelelaniso - ungquzulwano lungavela kwisicwangciso-nkqubo esifanelekileyo esinokusetyenziswa ekufezekiseni injongo efanayo . Umzekelo , onke amaqela achaphazelekayo angavumelana ukuba amagosa karhulumente kufuneka anikezele inkonzo esebenza kakhulu . Abanye abahlali bangafuna ukuba iingxowa-mali kufuneka zinikezelwe kuqeqesho olongeziweyo , ngexa abanye banokucinga ukuba iikhompyutha ezongeziweyo zingancedisa ekusombululeni inkonzo engentlanga . Ukunxulumanisa i-CBP ne-IDP kudala ithuba lokuqinisekisa ukuba i-IDP isekwe kwimo ekubhekiselelwe kuyo yengingqi kwaye kunika intsingiselo kwiimfuneko zenxaxheba ezikwi-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 . Ukuba nenxaxheba kwingxoxo ecwangciselwe ngokungaphelelanga nomntu ( nabantu ) abanolwazi ukubakhuthaza ukuba babuze imibuzo . Ukusebenzisa amathuba odliwano-ndlebe ukunceda ukuchonga amaqela azizisulu . Ukusekwa kwamabhunga e-AIDS kwingingqi yoomasipala bebonke abalithoba bengingqi . Amacandelo abucala aqesha malunga nekota ezintathu zabasebenzi boMzantsi Afrika ze anike ingxelo ngokudlulele kwisibini esithathwini sotyalo-mali nenkcitho yeR&D . UMzantsi Afrika ufuna icandelo labucala elinempumelelo elityala kumthamo ovelisayo . Logama injongo yenzuzo iqhuba ushishino , iinkampani azinakukhula ngaphandle kokuba zisebenze kubume apho ingqesho namazinga omvuzo ekhula . Uwiso-mthetho lufuna ukuba amashishini acinge ngokulingana ngokwengqesho , ukuxhotyiswa kwabamnyama kuqoqosho , okusingqongileyo , ukuphuhliswa kwezakhono , okuqulathiweyo kwasekhaya , ukuphuhliswa kwamashishini amancinci , ukuba noxanduva lasekuhlaleni kuluntu nokufunekayo okuninzi kwiindawo ezingundoqo , ezifana nezicwangciso-qhinga zokuphuhlisa iingingqi ezinemigodi . Kulo mxholo unobuzaza , kukumdla wexesha elide kuwo onke amashishini elizwe ukukhula ngokukhawuleza nokuba kuqeshwe abantu abaninzi ngakumbi . Uluhlu kwiphepha elidlulileyo ngumzekelo onokusetyenziswa ekuboniseni iindawo eziphambili zomsebenzi kwisicwangciso somsebenzi . Ii-KRA ziyahlulwa zibe yimisebenzi enemigangatho yeenkonzo zoBUNGAKANANI , UMGANGATHO , IXESHA NEXABISO elidityaniswe kuzo . Ii-KPI nezo zinoxanduva lwemisebenzi eyahlukeneyo kufuneka nazo ziboniswe ukuze kubekho indlela yokubeka iliso kwinkqubela-phambili . Amanqaku adweliswe ngezantsi . Ngenxa yemfano eyodwa yeeprojekthi neminye imingeni enokuthi ivele , esi sigaba sibaluleke ngokukodwa . Isiphumo sesi sigaba sisicwangciso sokusebenza esisesikweni esiya kuthi sibe sisikhokelo seqela leprojekthi ngalo lonke ixesha lokuqhutywa kweprojekthi . Ukungafani kumbutho okanye kuluntu ekuhlaleni kwamkela iiyantlukwano phakathi kwamadoda , amakhosikazi , iinkcubeko neentlanga ukwenzela ukukhuthaza unyamezelo lweeyantlukwano , ukwenzela ukuba oku kungafani kungamkela ezi yantlukwano . Oku kukusebenzela kwintsebenziswano enoxolo , ukwenzela ukuba umbutho okanye uluntu ekuhlaleni lube lungakwazi ukuya kuhlangano nokusebenza kweenjongo zabo eziphambili . Kuya kufuneka ukuba kufunwe umniki wenkxaso yemali yokubonelela ngalo chintsana wokuhlawula oonokhaya , nendleko zesithuthi . Umniki wenkxaso-mali kuya kufuneka ukuba kananjalo akhangele nemali yezi pasile zokutya . Isicwangciso samaxesha sisixhobo esiluncedo esiya kunceda umbhexeshi / ababhexeshi ngokucwangcisa amanyathelo aya kuthathwa xa kuphunyezwa isicwangciso sewadi . Isicwangciso sexesha se-CBP sinokungafani nezinye oko kuxhomekeke kubahlali abasebenza nombhexeshi . Umzekelo , kwisithili esirhweba ngokulima kusenokuba yimfuneko ukuba nemisebenzi ethe chatha ukutshona kwelanga ebandakanya abahlali , kodwa iintlanganiso zezicwangciso samaxesha neKomiti yeWadi zibe semini . Kuluntu apho inkoliso yabahlali yenza imisebenzi yobungcali khona okanye ushishino kusenokuba nzima ukufumana inxaxheba yabahlali ngenxa yoxinzelelo lomsebenzi . Kusenokufuneka ukuba ababhexeshi benze isicwangciso sentshonalanga enye okanye ezimbini ukuze bakwazi ukudibanisa abahlali kunye baze benze ezinye izicwangciso emini . Ubude bexesha obufuneka xa kusenziwa isicwangciso busenokucuthwa xa uhlalutyo lwemeko lugqityiwe okanye kugqitywe inxalenye yalo njengoko oku kunokulondoloza ixesha kulo mba . Ibhunga likamasipala linako kwakhona ukwabela iikomiti zeeWadi imisebenzi namagunya athile . Ibhunga malenze amalungiselelo olawulo ayimfuneko ukuze iikomiti zeeWadi zikwazi ukwenza imisebenzi yazo ngenkuthalo . IZikhokelo zokuSekwa nokuSebenza kweeKomiti zeeWadi zikaMasipala , iGazethe kaRhulumente enguNombolo 27699 , Juni 2005 - iZikhokelo zicacisa ukuba iKomiti yeWadi izimele , ikomiti yeengcebiso kwaye kufuneka ingabinakhethe xa isenza imisebenzi yayo , ingoyiki , ithath'icala kwaye eyona ndima ibalulekileyo edlalwa yiKomiti yeWadi kukusebenza njengomququzeleli wokuqinisekisa ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu jikelele kwimimandla . Kwithuba langoku ubunkokeli bomthonyama sisixokelelwano esitsha kurhulumente wengingqi kwaye asikachazwa ngokucacileyo . Amaqonga ezomthonyama asabalulekile kwimimandla yasemaphandleni . Umzekelo , KwaZulu-Natal isiphatha-mandla somthonyama sengingqi sidlale indima ebalulekileyo kwiprojekthi yaseIsulabasha / Mvunyane yamanzi nococeko lwangasese , iKomiti Yezicwangciso Yesithili saseMaluti . Nangona iindima nemisebenzi yeziphathamandla zomthonyama ingekacaci , zisayidlala indima yazo kwi-CBP kwiindawo zasemaphandleni . Zisebenza njengabathunywa benguquko nanjengomnyango obalulekileyo wokungena kubahlali njengoko zifumana intlonelo eninzi eluntwini ngaloo ndlela ziyakwazi ukuba neempembelelo ebantwini . UKUNGAFANI KUFANA NOMFANEKISO OWENZIWE NGAMATYE AMANCINANE ( MOSAIC ) : bonke abantu abenza umbutho bafana namaceba omfanekiso owenziwe ngamatye amancinane ; bonke bohlukahlukene kodwa balungelelana kunye njengento epheleleyo . Ukusebenza kwesixokelelwano samasebe oburhulumente athungelanayo ngumxholo wengxoxo-mpikiswano eshushu . Amanqwanqwa awahlukeneyo karhulumente elinye lixhomekeke kwelinye kwaye sifuna ukufumanisa iindlela zokuqinisekisa ukuba asebenza kunye ngokuyimpumelelo ngakumbi . Isicwangciso sicebisa ukutshintshwa kwendlela kusuke ekuzameni ukufumana ulungiselelo lwezakhiwo ezitsha , okungazinzisiyo , ekuchongweni nasekusombululeni ubuthathaka kusebenziswano nesikhundla . Ucalucalulo lushiye isithuba somzila ombi . Logama malunga nezigidi ezi-3.2 zemizi iye yazuza kwizindlu ezintsha , [ 1 ] neenkonzo namaziko abonelelwe kuluntu oluninzi , inkqubela phambili enyiniweyo yenziwe ekujikeni ukungabinabulungisa kwesithuba okwendeleyo . Kumanye amaxesha , emva kuka-1994 iinkqubo zibethelele ukwahlulwa kwesithuba ngokubeka izindlu zomvuzo osezantsi kumda weedolophukazi . Umbuzo 2 Ingaba uxwebhu lweprojekthi lubeka iinjongo , iziphumo nezalathiso zokusebenza eziqinisekisa ukubandakanywa kweemfuno zamakhosikazi ezinokufezekiseka kwaye ezicacileyo ngokwezinto ekujoliswe kuzo zophuhliso kwihlabathi ? Indlela elungileyo yokuqalisa kukumema oyena mntu mdala kwiqela ukuba abelane nabanye ngesiganeko sakudala anokusikhumbula . Sebenzisa eso siganeko njengendawo yokuqalisa ixesha elimisiweyo . Qala ngokuzoba umnxeba wobomi ephepheni ulixhome edongeni . Kuluncedo ukufumana abantu bokubhala iziganeko ezikhadini baze babeke iikhadi kumnxeba wexesha . Ukuba ukubhala yingxaki umbhexeshi unokubhala iziganeko kumnxeba wexesha ukwenzela abathathi-nxaxheba beqela . Umnxeba wexesha mawuhlale usekuhleni ukuze wongezwe kwaye ube yingxelo ngoluntu . Ngokusebenzisa amanqaku esifundo kwiphepha lama-87 ukuya kwelama-92 ungabancedisa ngokubanika ulwazi olongezelelweyo . Khanyisa umahluko phakathi kombhexeshi wewadi , umbhexeshi kamasipala nelungu leKomiti yeWadi uze uqinisekise ukuba abathathi-nxaxheba bayayiqonda indima edlalwa yi-CBP nonxulumano neeKomiti zeWadi Iqonga leengxoxo liziqondile izithintelo ezikhoyo kwizikhundla laze labhenela kwiingcebiso zangaphandle , inkxaso nengxowa-mali . Ngonyaka ka-1992 , bacela i-Corplan , i-NGO yoluntu eseMonti ukuba libancedise ngoyilo nozalisekiso lwesicwangciso-nkqubo esifanelekileyo se-LED . Bakwazi ukuqwalasela izithuba ezininzi kubugcisa nolawulo lwedolophu nasekufikeleleni kwiingxowa-mali zezizwe ngezizwe . Ingaba bekukho uqeqesho kwindlela yokusebenzisa izikhokelo zoquko lwesini ukwenzela abasebenzi kulawulo lweprojekthi ? Cela abathathi-nxaxheba bafunde umzekelo wophando ongezantsi baze bafunde amanqanam ahlukeneyo kumzekelo woxolelaniso , xoxa ngokwenzekayo kwinqanam ngalinye ngokujonga amanqaku kwicandelo 5.6 . Ukwakha umoya olungele ukuthatha inxaxheba . Umzekelo ngokunika abahlali amagama neenkcukacha zabantu abangaqhagamshelana nabo ngokuphathelene neenkonzo ezinjengokuqokelelwa kwenkunkuma , iikliniki namagama amagosa ekungasiwa kuwo izikhalazo . Malunga namaqela angalonwabeliyo ilizwi elibhaliweyo , isikhokelo se-AICDD sikhankanya ukusetyenziswa kwembewu , amatye okanye izinti ezikhadini ukuze abathathi-nxaxheba bazibonele indlela ekhule ngayo ingxaki . Zibhalwa ekhadini ebonisa unyaka . Iindima zesini eziziingcinga ezisoloko zimi ziya kuqhutywa kwaye nomsebenzi ongalinganiyo phakathi kwamadoda namakhosikazi awuyi kunanzwa . Oku kuya kuba negalelo elibi kwiziphumo zeprojekthi . Umxholo ophindaphindekayo kwisicwangciso kukuba ikhonkco lokunika ingxelo kufuneka liqiniswe . Uluntu lufuna ukwazi ngokucacileyo ukuba ngubani onika ingxelo kubani . Kufuneka kubekho isixokelelwano sokwenza ukuba zonke iinkokheli kuluntu zikwazi ukunika ingxelo ngendlela eziziphatha ngayo . Kwiqela , cela ilungu elinye kwiqela ngalinye ukuba liphendule omnye wemibuzo , ukuba unamaqela angaphezulu kwesithathu , amaqela ashiyekileyo kufuneka ongeze nje imiba ethile engakhange iqwalaselwe ngaphambili . IiKomiti zeWadi zimele imidla eyohlukeneyo namaqela . Umzekelo , amanye amalungu angamela iqela labahlawuli berhafu , abanye bamele amaqela amakhosikazi , abanye bamele imibutho yophuhliso kunye neminye imibutho yoshishino . Ngaxeshanye , iiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zisebenzisane ukuqinisekisa ukuba iimbono zabahlali zineqonga lokuthetha nokuba iimbono zabo zithathelwa ingqalelo ngendlela apho eyinzuzo kubahlali . Kungangabikho lula ukuphendula zonke iimfuno , kodwa iiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zifune esona siphumo sifanelekileyo nesiyinzuzo eluntwini . IiKomiti zeWadi zingazifumana zikwezinye iimeko zongquzulwano kunye noluntu lwamaqela achaphazelekayo kurhulumente wengingqi ezisebenza nawo , kwaye ngokuba nesakhono esifanelekileyo sokuphelisa okanye ukunciphisa okanye ukusombulula ungquzulwano kuya kuzinceda ekwenzeni imisebenzi yazo . Isakhelo somgaqo-nkqubo sidinga ukukhuthaza abahlali abasebenzayo nababandakanyekayo ekulawuleni uphuhliso lwabo , bebanga amalungelo nokusebenzisa uxanduva lwabo , benika igalelo kumaqumrhu olawulo kwimigangatho eyahlukileyo , singabalula ekumgangatho wewadi nokamasipala . Uninzi loomasipala luzenzele imigaqo-nkqubo okanye izakhelo zabo zolawulo lweeKomiti zeWadi zikamasipala wabo . Le migaqo-nkqubo ilawula ukusungulwa , imisebenzi nokusebenza kweeKomiti zeWadi kumasipala wazo nokunika uyilo lweenkqubo eziza kunceda iiKomiti zeWadi ukuba zisebenze ngempumelelo . Iinkqubo kufuneka zilungiswe kuba umasipala ngamnye wahlukile kwaye kufuneka azame ukumisela iinkqubo ezilungele izidingo zabo ukuze akwazi ukunika inkonzo enempumelelo . URHULUMENTE WENGINGQI WAZIWA njengowona mgangatho karhulumente okufutshane nabantu . Ukubandakanya abahlali ekuphawuleni iimfuno nasekuyileni imigaqo-nkqubo neenkqubo jikelele yindlela esebenzayo ekuphenduleni iimfuno zoluntu kwimimandla . Njengoko kungekho lula ukuba wonke ummi athathe inxaxheba ethe ngqo , iiKomiti zeWadi zikhona njengesigqeba sothungelwano lonxibelelwano . Kodwa ke , iinkqubo zonxibelelwano kufuneka zenzeke ngendlela efanelekileyo . Esi sahluko sijonga indima yeeKomiti zeWadi kwiinkqubo zokwenziwa kwezigqibo zebhunga nendlela eziyizalisekisa ngayo indima yazo ekubambeni ibhunga linoxanduva lokunika inkcazo nasekuphenduleni kwiimfuno zabahlali . Ooceba bewadi banyulwa kwibhunga likamasipala ngabavoti ababhaliswe kwiwadi kwiqela yobumeli kwiqela , la ngamalungu ebhunga e-PR , okanye njengoceba wewadi . Ooceba bewadi bangamela iqela elikhuphisanayo lezopolitiko okanye bazimele okanye njengabameli beqela elinomdla elinjengombutho wabahlawuli berhafu . Indlela yokusebenza ye-CBP inika iiKomiti zeWadi umsebenzi wokwenza izicwangciso ngokuphelela kwaso nenkqubo yempumezo yokwenza iindima zayo nokuthwala uxanduva lwazo . Ineajenda - isicwangciso sewadi - isifezekiso nokubekwa kweliso novavanyo lwesicwangciso sewadi kwaye inika indima eqhuba unyaka wonke . Uceba ngusihlalo weKomiti yeWadi . Usengadlulisela ubusihlalo bentlanganiso kuceba wolungelelwano okanye naliphi ilungu leKomiti yeWadi . IBatho Pele yindlela yokuziphatha phambi kwabanye , yindlela ozilungiselele ngayo ukuvuma amalungelo nezidingo nokuzimisela ukubanceda wenze ubomi babo buxabiseke . IBatho Pele kukuzinikela kwabanye abantu okukhenkceza kwisizukulwana sokuthanda abantu . Unika inkonzo njengomthunywa okhuthaza intshukumo yabahlali , ngakumbi ngenkqubo ye-IDP nangenkqubo yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala . IiKomiti zeWadi azisayi kuphazamisana nomsebenzi webhunga , oku kuquka ukunganikezeli imiyalelo kumagosa anomsebenzi wokwenza izigqibo zomgaqo-nkqubo webhunga . Amalungu eekomiti zeeWadi asebenza ngokuncomeka kangako xa abelwe izikhundla ngokwezakhiwo okanye ngokwamacandelo apho aselezibandakanya khona . Umzekelo , ilungu elimele amafama linokunikwa isikhundla kwezoLimo , okanye ilungu leKomiti yeWadi elingumhlohli linokusebenza kwisikhundla sezeMfundo . Oku akuyonto enako ukwenzeka kwiiWadi ezingasondelelananga kakhulu . Amalungu eekomiti zeeWadi anokufumana ngaphezulu kwesikhundla esinye . Injongo ye-IDP kukuqinisekisa ukuba oovimba abakhoyo koomasipala bajoliswa kunikezelo lweeprojekthi neenkqubo ekufikeleleni kwimiba ephambili yophuhliso ekuvunyelwene ngayo . I-IDP sisixhobo esibalulekileyo esiqinisekisa ukuba iiprojekthi eziphawuliweyo nezenziwe ngumasipala zinxulumene neemfuno zoluntu jikelele kwimimandla . Ukubhekela ngakumsebenzi onesidima kuye wonke ubani , into ejongwa kuqala yexesha elifutshane kumele ibe kukunyusa ingqesho nokuvuza kokungena kwabantu abatsha kwiphungulo labasebenzi , logama kuthathwa inkathalo ekuthinteleni ukubekwa kweminye imisebenzi nokunciphisa iimeko zokusebenza ezikhoyo . Amanye amathuba omsebenzi angangakwazi ukwenza umntu oyedwa aphile ubomi afuna ukubuphila ngoko nangoko . Ukuphakamisa ubomi obugcinakalayo , kubalulekile ukuba iziqu okanye iintsapho ngaphandle komvuzo , zibe zingafikelela kwiinkonzo ezifana nemfundo enobulunga , ukhathalelo lwempilo okanye uthutho loluntu . Kukwabalulekile emntwini olahlekelwa ngumsebenzi ukuba akwazi ukufikelela kumsebenzi kwiinkqubo zomsebenzi woluntu okanye izikimu zokuqeshwa ezisekwe kuluntu . Ngezi ndlela , iinkqubo zoluntu namanyathelo oluntu zongeza kwinzame zoyedwa kwishishini lezemisebenzi , kubonelela ngobomi obugcinakalayo kwabo basebenzayo bahlelelekileyo . Unxibelelwano yinkqubo enzima kuba luquka abantu beendawo ezahlukeneyo . Ke ngoko umgangatho wonxibelelwano ubalulekile . Unxibelelwano luquka inani lemiba eyahlukeneyo . Unxibelelwano lunezixhobo ezininzi ezinjengokuthetha , ukubhala , iingxoxo nokumamela . Ikomiti yeWadi ingakhuthaza uphuhliso loqoqosho lwengingqi ngokugcina abahlali besazi ngezindululo namathuba avelileyo . Banokwazisa amalungu ebhunga ngeengxaki adibene nazo amalungu abahlali afuna ukuqalisa amashishini amancinci . Isicwangiso esisekwe kubahlali sijolisa umbono nasekomeleleni / amathuba kunakwiingxaki . Oku kuthetha ukuba izicwangciso ziphuhliswa phezu kweziphumo ezibekwe phambili zabahlali , kungekho kwiingxaki ezibekwe phambili . IPhepha leNgcaciso-nkqubo lichonga amaqonga ' okuvumela uqulunqo olwakhiwe kakuhle noluza kundulula imigaqo-nkqubo kunye / okanye luphembelele uqulunqo lwemigaqo-nkqubo , kananjalo lube nenxaxheba ekubekweni kweliso nakuvavanyo nakwizindululo zenxaxheba yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali ezijoliswe ekunxulumaniseni izinto eziphambili phakathi kwabahlali neenkqubo zotyalo-mali zemali yokuqalisa ishishini ' . Kweli nqanam , umxolelanisi uyazazisa aze abeke imithetho . Ukuqhutywa nokuvandlakanywa - esi ke sisigaba apho iqhutywayo ngoku iprojekthi , kwaye sibandakanya umba wokusoloko sivandlakanywa , sihlengahlengiswa ngeenjongo zokuqinisekisa ukuba siba nempumelelo . Ooceba bewadi angusihlalo kwiintlanganiso zeKomiti yeWadi kwaye anoxanduva lokubiza iintlanganiso yabahlali . Ooceba balikhonkco phakathi koluntu nebhunga bekwanoxanduva lokugqithisa inkcazo kwiiwadi zabo . IiKomiti zeWadi zinikezela zilikhonkco phakathi koluntu noceba . Ukuqinisekisa ngokuthatha inxaxheba okwandileyo nenkqubela-phambili eya kwisisombululo , umxolelanisi kufuneka avavanye ukungabinamagingxigingxi kwesikhundla ngasinye namaqela : yenza isigqibo ngobume bokuqwalasela imiba ; yenza isigqibo sokuba iintlanganiso ezizodwa ziyafuneka na nomxolelanisi ; qwalasela kumdla weqela ngalinye nokulindelweyo , ingesiso isikhundla ( oko kukuthi , indawo abayithathayo ) ; dala konke okunokubakho ukushicilele ; khuthaza uthungelwano nokwananiselana , umzekelo : ukuseka okunobakho kweklinikhi nezindlu zangasese kuphela kwirenki yeeteksi ne-IDP elandelayo equka izitendi zabathengisi kunye neklinikhi esebenza ngokupheleleyo ; yakha kwiindawo ekuvunyelwene ngazo . Isicwangciso sewadi sisiseko senkqubo ye-CBP yokuqinisekisa inxaxheba yabahlali kwi-IDP . Kubalulekile ukuba kunikwe umgangatho ofanelekileyo wamaxwebhu ukuze isicwangciso sibe negalelo elincomekayo kwi-IDP . I-CBP ikhuthaza uluntu kwimimandla ukuba luze nezisombululo ngokwalo . Injongo yayo kukunyusa umgangatho wezicwangciso ezinyanisekileyo zenyathelo ngokubeka uxanduva oluthile locwangciso emagxeni abemi uqobo . Yintoni imimandla yesithuba yokomelela , ubuthathaka , amathuba avulekileyo nezoyikiso ( eziboniswe kwicwecwe leenkcukacha zobume bemeko nesithuba ) ? Khetha abantu abaza kudlala iindima zamalungu ekomiti , usihlalo , unobhala . Umzekelo : abantu abangama-54 bathathe inxaxheba kwinkqubo yokwenziwa kwesicwangciso . Amaqela abandakanye abasebenzi - bekhola eblowu nabekhola emhlophe , abaziqeshileyo , abaswele ingqesho , abafazi abangatshatanga nabantwana . Ilungu leKomiti yeWadi , uNks Mofolo noceba wengingqi , uNks Smith , bebezile kwiiseshoni . Ababhexeshi ibinguMnu Jones noNks Mpefu . UMnu Mars ovela kwi-dplg ebezile kanti umcwangcisi wedolophu uMnu M Zungu naye ebekhona . Ii-logframezizintlu ezimana ukuzaliswa ngabo balawula iprojekthi . Ezi zintlu zinika isishwankathelo sezicwangciso zeprojekthi . Umsebenzi wokuzalisa ii-logframe ungakhangeleka ngathi untsompothile , kodwa zinika iinkcukacha eziyimfuneko kakhulu , kwaye kuyafuneka ziqondiwe . Kubalulekile oko kwimpumelelo yeprojekthi . Kananjalo ii-logframe ziya kunceda ekumiliseleni uzinzo nasekufundiseni abo banenxaxheba kwiprojekthi leyo . Iinkqubo zolawulo - ezi nkqubo zibandakanya ukulandela ngoqwalaselo kunye nokulinganisa inkqubela-phambili ukuqinisekisa ukuba iinjongo zeprojekthi zihlangatyeziwe , zichonga ukungahambelani nesicwangciso ukuze kuthathwe amanyathelo okulungisa . Zikwabandakanya amanyathelo othintelo-zingxaki xa zicingeleka kwangethuba elingaphambili , kuthelekiswa umgangatho wokusebenza wenene nalowo ukwisicwangciso . Idrafti yomthetho oyilwayo ipapashiwe ukufumana izimvo zabahlali . Ngokuqinisekisa ukuba abathathi-nxaxheba kwinkqubo yeCBP bamelwe kwimicimbi ehambelanayo yeIDP ngezakhiwo neenkqubo ezinikwayo kwinkqubo yeIDP ngokwangoku nequlethwe kwisikhokelo seIDP i-IDP Guide Pack ( ngakumbi abathunywa abakwi-IDP Representative Forum namaqela akwi-Project Task Teams ) . I-KPI nganye kufuneka iquke iithagethi zokwenziwa komsebenzi . IMimiselo inikezela inani leendlela zeethagethi zokwenziwa komsebenzi nezinokunceda iiKomiti zeWadi xa zisenza uvavanyo lomsebenzi kwiithagethi ze-KPI . Le ndlela ibonisa ukubaluleka kohlahlo lwabiwo-mali olukhoyo . Oku kungenxa yokuba i-PMS ayizimeli . I-IDP kufuneka ibe sisikhokelo sokuseka ii-KPI . Ukuba i-KPI iseke iithagethi ekunzima ukuzifezekisa , ayisayi kukwazi ukufikelela kuzo . Urhulumente wengingqi wophuhliso ugxininisa isidingo sokwenzela izinto elubala , ukuzimela izenzo zakho , ukuthethathethana , ukuququzelela ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu nobudlelwane . Kubalulekile ukuba isicwangciso sibhalwe njengoxwebhu ukuze umbono wabahlali uhlale ubhaliwe ukuqinisekisa ukuba usenokusetyenziswa ziziphathamandla zenqanaba eliphezulu nabanye abaniki beenkonzo . Umasipala kufuneka acebisane nabahlali ngaphambi kokuphuhlisa izalathisi zokwenziwa komsebenzi aze avumele uluntu ukuba luthathe inxaxheba kwinkqubo yokuhlela ngokutsha . Iprojekthi nganye iyodwa kwaye inoluhlu lwayo lwemingeni nemiba ekufuneka iqwalaselwe . Isicwangciso esisodwa sifanelekile ke ngoko ukwenzela ukuvumela ukugqiba iprojekthi ngokuyimpumelelo . Ngaxesha Ngaxesha kufuneka kunikwe ingqwalaselo eyodwa ukwenzela ukuqinisekisa ukulingana ngokwesini ekucwangciseni iprojekthi . Ugqithiso lwengxelo negalelo kwiinkqubo zebhunga ukuqinisekisa ngonikezelo lweenkonzo . Lo ngumsebenzi owenziwa ngokuhamba kummandla . Umbhexeshi / Ababhexeshi bakhokela uhambo nabanolwazi abaphambili abamalunga nesithandathu abavela eluntwini . Kufanele ukuthatha iyure ukuya kwezimbini ukuhamba njengoko abantu bengasayi kuba naxesha lokuthatha uhambo olude kunolo . Iziphumo - zeziphi iziphumo zendlela owenze ngayo ? Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi ingulowo kuwo unako ukuba nesikhundla esithile esinokubanceda ukuba bamele abahlali . Ngale ndlela amalungu anendima ecacileyo ayidlalayo ewadini kwaye azuza amava aze aqonde imibandela enxulumene nesikhundla sawo . Amalungu esikhundla kuzo zonke iiWadi ( lawo anoxanduva lwesikhundla esifanayo ) adibana namasebe kamasipala neekomiti zezikhundla ukuze kuxoxwe ngemibandela enxulumene nesikhundla sawo . Uluntu lwase-Seymour lwathatha inxaxheba kuluhlu olubanzi lweeprojekthi zophuhliso ukususela kunyaka ka-1992 - zonke zinamaqondo awahlukeneyo empumelelo . Iiprojekthi ezinkulu ezaqaliswa ngonyaka ka-1992 zichazwe apha ngezantsi . Nangona ingezizo zonke iiprojekthi ezabonakala zinenzuzo ethe ngqo kwezoqoqosho , kufanele ukuba zibonwe njengezinikezela ingqesho noncedo ebantwini abanethemba lokuqeshwa okanye abanethemba lokuqalisa iprojekthi yophuhliso . Makukhunjulwe ukuba uhlahlo-mali lusenokufuna ukuba lube neenkcukacha ezithe kratya okanye eziphungulweyo , ngokwabo zilungiselelwe bona . Abalizi basenokungafuni iinkcukacha ezifanayo nezifunwa liqela leprojekthi . Ezibonisa izinto njengoko zinjalo : Oku kuthetha ukuba sineendlela zokuqinisekisa ( ubukho bedatha , inokwenzeka ngokwexesha , njl . ) ; ukuba zinokufunyanwa kwaye kulula ukuzisebenzisa . Umgaqo-nkqubo wowe-1994 wawusithi urhulumente uya kunika inkxaso yeendleko zokuqalisa umsebenzi weenkonzo ezintsha nesakhiwo esisiseko , kanti ulondolozo lona neendleko zokuqhuba umsebenzi ziya kuhlawulwa ngabasebenzisi . Ngowama-2001 kwavunyelwana ngokuba obona buncinci beenkonzo ezisisiseko buya kunikwa yonke imizi . Oku bekubandakanya ukususwa kwenkunkuma , amanzi , uhlambululo nombane . Intle inkqubela-phambili eseyenziwe malunga nobonelelo lwamanzi nombane . I-Municipal Structures Act , 1998 ne-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 ixhasa uMgaqo-siseko ize ibonise ukubaluleka kokuthatha inxaxheba ikwanikezela nenkqubo-sikhokelo esemthethweni yokusekwa kweeKomiti zeWadi . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka aziqhelanise nale mithetho . Umzekelo , i-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 ichaza iindlela zolawulo ezinjengophuhliso lweziCwangciso zoPhuhliso oluManyanisiweyo ( echazwe ngasentla ) kunye neeNkqubo zoLawulo lokwenziwa koMsebenzi . UMBUZO 3 Zeziphi iinkqubo eziphambili zokubeka iliso novavanyo ezifunekayo ukuqinisekisa unikezelo lweenkonzo , zeziphi izinto ezinokuba yinzuzo ekwenzeni umlinganiselo wenkqubela-phambili ? IiKomiti zeWadi zingancedisa iikomiti ekunikezeni ulwazi malunga ngezihloko ezithile xa kufanelekile . Kukho imfuneko yokuphucula ukusebenza kwezixhobo ezichazwe ngentla , nokuqondwa kweziphumo zorhwebo ezikhoyo . Ukongeza , ugxininiso ngakumbi luyafuneka ekuxhaseni amashishini amancinci , ukukhuthaza urhulumente necandelo labucala ekufumaneni intengiselwano kwimizi-mveliso emincinci , nokwandisa uphuhliso lwabamnyama nabalawuli abangamabhinqa neengcali . Uqoqosho olukhulu ngokukhawuleza olwahlukana kumacandelo amatsha luya kuvula amathuba emizi-mveliso yabantu abamnyama namashishini amancinci , kuphakamisa ukukhula okubandakanyayo . UMzantsi Afrika ayingomnikeli kuphela ekukhutshweni kweegesi ezikhutshwa ziindawo ezigcina izityalo ezifuna ukukhuselwa - usenokwenzakala ngokukodwa ziimpembelelo zokutshintsha kwemozulu kwimpilo , kubomi , amanzi nokutya , kunefuthe ngokungayelelananga kwabahlelelekileyo , ngokukodwa amabhinqa nabantwana . Logama uziqhelanisa nezi nguquko , amashishini nemizi kumele yehlise ifuthe elingalunganga kokusingqongileyo . Oku kuya kufuna iinguquko ezineziphumo ezininzi kwindlela abantu abaphila nabasebenza ngayo . UWISO-MTHETHO LUKARHULUMENTE WEENGINGQI lusekwe ngenjongo yokunika isakhono kuMzantsi Afrika ukuba usebenzele ekunikeni inkxaso yeenkonzo ezisisiseko ngendlela eyakhayo kwaye uphucule ubomi bezentlalo nobezoqoqosho babemi . Njengoko urhulumente weengingqi eyindima karhulumente apho ukunikwa kweenkonzo kwenzeka khona kwinqanaba labahlali kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa nokukhusela inkxaso nenxaxheba yamaqela abahlali . Esi sahluko sigqabaza ngeenjongo nemithetho-siseko yesicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali ( community-based planning - CBP ) . Cela oo-A ukuba baphume egumbini . Xelela oo-B ukuba ngoku baza kumamela . Kodwa ke kufuneka bamamele ngenzondelelo . Oku kuthetha ukuba kufuneka baqwalasele emntwini othethayo , babuze imibuzo xa befuna ukucacelwa kokuthile , banike oomahlulelane babo ingqwalaselo enkulu . Ukuqokelelwa kweemkcukacha eziza mva kumalungu abahlali ngababhexeshi nabameli babahlali . Oku kunokuthatha iintsuku ezimbalwa okanye kunabe ethubeni lexesha , kodwa kugcine uludwe lwamaxesha okusebenza acwangciselweyo . Isahluko 3 sisekwe kwi-Community-Based Planning and the IDP , Guide 2 : Facilitators Guide for Community-Based Planning and Guide for Decision-Makers ( Isicwangciso Esisekwe kubahlali ne-IDP , Isikhokelo 2 : Isikhokelo Sababhexeshi Sesicwangciso Esisekwe kubahlali Nesikhokelo Sabaqulunqi Bezigqibo ) esiphuhliswe yi-AICDD Nemisebenzi Yophuhliso . Ukuguquka kwexesha elide kunaniselwano lwehlabathi notyalo-mali kubumba kabutsha uqoqosho lwehlabathi nepolitiki yamazwe onke . Okuyintloko phakathi kwezi nguquko kukuvela kokukhula ngokukhawulezileyo koqoqosho , ngokukodwa eTshayina , e-Indiya naseBrazil . Emva kwaphantse kwamakhulu amathathu eminyaka eyantlukwano , ukungalingani phakathi kwezizwe kuyancipha . Ukuba nesimo sobudolophu nokuba namashishini eTshayina nase-Indiya kungaphantse kugcine isinyanzeliso sobutyebi bendalo siphezulu kwiminyaka elishumi okanye ngaphezulu . Ukuvela ngakumbi kwabaxumi kumazwe asakhulayo kuya kwandisa amathuba kulo lonke uqoqosho . Umzabalazo ngokuchasene nokucukulwa kwabantu wawumalunga nokwakha uluntu olungacalucaluli ngebala nesini kuqala , apho bonke abantu benamalungelo alinganayo . Nangona kukho inkqubela-phambili engaguqukiyo ukusukela ngowe-1994 , uMzantsi Afrika usahleli unoluntu olwahlukeneyo , apho ubuhlanga busabangela ukwahlukana okungundoqo . Ukucukulwa koyedwa ngeentetha ngebala nobuhlanga kuthe tshitshilili kwaye ucalucalulo luyaqhubekeka . Ubume bamaziko elizwe neentsingiselo zalo ezibanzi nezokuhlala zibenegalelo ekuphelisweni kocalucalulo kancinci kancinci kancinci , kodwa inkqubela-phambili ayanelanga okanye ayinzulu ngokwaneleyo . Nangona inkqubela-phambili yenziwe ekuphuculeni ubomi bamabhinqa ; ucalucalulo , ukuziphatha ngokobudoda nokufikelela okuphantsi kwimfundo enobulunga kuyaqhubeka . Isicwangciso sijongana nezi zinto ngokugqibeleleyo , kuqondwa ukuba izinto emazijongwe kuqala ezingundoqo ezifana nemfundo okanye uphuhliso lwamaphandle kuya kuba nempembelelo eyakha yankulu kakhulu kumabhinqa ahlelelekileyo . ISicwangciso soPhuhliso sikaZwelonke siya kubumba ukwabiwa kwemithombo kumashumi amabini eminyaka ezayo , kodwa asiyi kugqiba ngohlahlo-lwabiwo mali lonyaka . Indlela eyeyona ingcono yokuveza imithombo ekuphumezeni isicwangciso kukukhulisa uqoqosho ngokukhawuleza . Ukuba uqoqosho lukhula ngokugqithise kumyinge wesi-5 ekhulwini ngonyaka , ingeniso karhulumente neenzuzo zemizi-mveliso yabucala iya kuba ngaphaya kokuphindaphindeka kwiminyaka engama-20 ezayo . Ukupheliswa kokuhlanganisa uqukuqelo lwenkxaso-mali kwinkxaso-mali enye yokumiswa kabutsha kwesithuba . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwabemi ukuqinisekisa ukuba urhulumente unoxanduva lokuphendula nokufeza izithembiso zakhe . Ukuba ngabemi akupheleli ekuvoteleni amagosa anyuliweyo oluntu . Amagosa oluntu nawo akunakulindeleka ukuba enze izigqibo ezingcono zabemi ukuba abo bemi ababagcini benolwazi ngezidingo zabo . Abemi bazazi ngcono izinto abazidingayo kwaye kubalulekile ukuba bathathe inxaxheba ekwakheni izisombululo zezi zidingo . Abemi kudingeka ukuba basebenze ngokuhlanganyela norhulumente ukuncedisa kuphuhliso lwabo . Kulapho zingena khona iiKomiti zeWadi kuba zidlala indima ebalulekileyo ukuququzelela inkqubo yokubandakanya abahlali . Izikhokelo zaphuhliswa ngenxa yokuba oomasipala abaninzi bebefuna ukhokelo oluthe chatha malunga nendlela yokusekwa kweeKomiti zeeWadi . Zicebisa ngeendlela oomasipala abanokuhlangabezana ngayo neemfuneko ze-Municipal Structures Act , 1998 kunye ne-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 . Ukuzinikela okuphucukileyo kubalawuli neenkokeli zenkqubo ukwenzela ukusebenza njengegqiza ukwenzela uphando oluphucukileyo nolawulo lophando olunemphumelelo . Oomasipala benemidla eyahlukeneyo kwaye bangafumanisa ukuba bayakhuphisana omnye nomnye . Inkqubo yolawulo lomsebenzi kufuneka iquke uninzi lwalo mdla njengoko lusebenziseka kwaye lugcinekile . Kuya kubakho neemfuno ezahlukeneyo kuluntu olusemaphandleni xa kuthelekiswa noomasipala ezidolophini . Amazinga okuzala kubemi boMzantsi Afrika abamhlophe aqalise ukwehla kwii-1950 nee-1960 , logama amazinga okuzala kuma-Afrika eqalise ukwehla kamva kwii-1970 nasebutsheni bee-1980 . Kuzo zombini iimeko , ukunyuka kokuya kwabantu ezidolophini nemigangatho engcono yemfundo yayizizo ezaziphembelela . Namhlanje , inani labemi baseMzantsi Afrika liyakhula ngomyinge o-1 ekhulwini ngonyaka kwaye ngowama-2030 , kuthelekelelwe ukuba liya kukhula ngomyinge we-0.5 ekhulwini ngonyaka . Iikomiti zeWadi zizakhelo zemibutho ( ngokunjalo nemibutho yamaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya ) kwaye kufuneka zimelwe Kwiqonga Labameli be-IDP nakwiqela elisebenza kunye le-IDP elifanelekileyo . Xa usiva amazwi athi iNkqubo yoLawulo loKwenziwa koMsebenzi oko kuthetha ntoni kuwe ? Ulawulo lwedemokhrasi ludinga ukuthatha inxaxheba ngokwedemokrasi ngokwelizwi labo bonke abasebenzi basekuhlaleni kumgaqo-nkqubo nakwiinkqubo zolawulo . Oku kudinga ukwenziwa kwezigqibo ngokuphandle nangendlela ebeka abantu phambili . Ikwadinga abemi abakwaziyo ukusebenzisa izigqibo , banike igalelo kwiingxoxo-mpikiswano nakwiingxoxo ezichaphazela ubomi babo nokuzazi iingxaki zendawo abahlala kuyo , izakhono nolwazi nokufumana izisombululo zale miceli-mngeni . Ukuthatha inxaxheba yinxalenye ebalulekileyo yolawulo olulungileyo kuba ivumela ukusabalala kolwazi phakathi kwabemi neenkokheli ezinyuliweyo nokuzimela izenzo zabo . Ikwanika ilizwi kwabo bemi abachaphazeleka kakhulu yimigaqo-nkqubo yoluntu . Ukwakha amaziko okwamkela ugesi wendalo owenziwe ulwelo nokwandisa uphononongo lokufumana isibonelelo sogesi ekhaya ( kuquka nokuphanda iindawo ezigcina imitheyini yohlobo oluthile lwelitye elinkumnkum nesaleko selahle ) ukwahlukanisa ukuxubana kombane nokunciphisa ukukhutshwa kwekhabhoni . Kwiqela elincinci xoxani ngeendlela eli sebe elingasebenzisa ngayo iBatho Pele ukuze liphumeze unikezelo lweenkonzo ngendlela ayibona ngayo urhulumente . Musa ukuthatha icala - linda zonke izimvo zichazwe kuqala uze ke wongeze eyakho . Ezinye iimpawu kubomi babahlali zezamaxesha athile ngokuqinisekileyo , ezifana nezimbo zezifo , ukusetyenziswa kwabasebenzi , imijikelo yezolimo , kunye nesondlo . Imisebenzi emibini elandelayo ikhuthaza ingqiqo ngezimbo zemikhwa yamaxesha athile nezamathuba amade . . Ngokwenza ezi zimbo nale mikhwa abenzi bezicwangciso abangafihlisiyo bayakwazi ukucingela kwangethuba elingaphambili iziganeko ezithile baze balunga-lungise izicwangciso zabo nezicwangciso-buqili ngokwaloo ndlela . Umlinganiselo wabemi baseMzantsi Afrika abahlala kwiingingqi zasemaphandleni uhle ngamanqaku omyinge we-10 ekhulwini ukusukela ngo-1994 . Namhlanje , malunga nomyinge wama-60 ekhulwini wenani labemi uhlala ezidolophini . Ngokuhambisana neentsingiselo zehlabathi , ukuhamba kwabantu besuka kumaphandle ukuya kwiidolophu kulindeleke ukuba kuqhubekeke , kwaye ngowama-2030 malunga nomyinge wama-70 ekhulwini wenani labemi baya kuhlala ezidolophini . IGauteng needolophu zaseThekwini naseKapa yeyona mimandla yeedolophu ekhula ngokukhawuleza okukhulu , okuneempembelelo zokucwangcisa nokuhambisa iinkonzo ezisisiseko . Chaza ukuba ibakala lesibini libandakanye uhlalutyo olucokiswayo nohlanganiselo lweenkcukacha eziqokelelwe kwiBakala 1 . Ii-KPIs zihlelwa ngokutsha rhoqo ngonyaka ngumasipala njengenxenye yenkqubo yolungiso lokwenziwa komsebenzi . Ukuba umasipala ulungise i-IDP yakhe , kufuneka alungise nee-KPI zakhe . Ingxelo esuka kuluntu kummandla , kwiiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka iqwalaselwe kuhlelo ngokutsha lwee-KPI . Ngale ndlela , i-PMS ibonwa njengefanelekileyo ngabahlali . Ezolimo : ingaba kubekho iinguquko kwiintlobo zezityalo ezilinywayo ? Kutheni ? Ingaba kukho iinguquko kumanani emfuyo ekuhambeni kweminyaka ? Kutheni ? Iinguquko kufikelelo emadlelweni okutyisa / isixa somhlaba wokutyisa impahla esikhoyo ? Ngubani ofikelelayo ? IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziqhelane nezixhobo neenkqubo ezahlukeneyo ezinokuzinceda ukuba ziqinisekise ukulingana ngokwesini . Ukususa isimo sobujoni kwinkonzo yesipolisa . Isigqibo sokususa ubujoni kubupolisa , kuhanjelwa kude kwimbali yabo yokukhohlakala , bekuyinjongo engundoqo yokutshintsha emva kuka-1994 . Ukuphindwa kubuyiselwe ubujoni kwisipolisa kwiminyaka yakutshanje akufumanaga kuhlonelwa kakhulu kumapolisa okanye kwizantya zokuvalela eziphezulu . Kuphela , ibe negalelo kudushe . Amapolisa kumele asuswe isimo sobujoni kwaye alawulelwe kwinkonzo yobungcali boluntu . Umasipala i-ABC wenza amalungiselelo e-IDP yakhe . Uceba wewadi neKomiti yeWadi babazisile abahlali ukuba kuza kubanjwa intlanganiso ngomhla wama-20 Julayi , ngentsimbi ye- 7.00 ngorhatya kwiHolo yeSixeko . Isaziso sithunyelwe kwiiveki ezimbini ngaphambi kwentlanganiso nemiba ephambili eza kuveliswa entlanganisweni neyimiba ephambili kwi-IDP . Entlanganisweni , uceba wewadi unikeza imiba jikelele ye-IDP aze acele iimpendulo nezimvo . Intlanganiso iyavumelana ukuba amaqela anomdla kufuneka ahlangane ukuze axoxe nge-IDP nabameli babo baze babuye kwiiveki ezimbini ukugqithisa ingxelo . Kuvunyelwene ngomhla nexesha ngumntu wonke entlanganisweni . IMimiselo ichaza ukuba ii-KPI kufuneka kwazeke ukwenza umlinganiselo , zinxulumane nokuthile , zingaqhutywa luluvo oluthile kwaye zicace . Zisebenza kwiiyunithi zolawulo lukamasipala nakubasebenzi , nasiphina isibonelelo sikamasipala kunye nomnikezeli wenkonzo umasipala anesivumelwano naye . Abantu bathatha inxaxheba ngokuxelelwa isigqibo okanye into eseyenzekile . Ibandakanya izaziso zacalanye ezenziwa lulawulo okanye ngabaphathi beprojekthi bengakhange bamamele zimpendulo zabantu . Lo gama kusungulwa inkqubo yokwenza isicwangciso neququzelelwa ngumasipala , i-CBP ilulwahlulelwano phakathi kwewadi nomasipala . Iwadi ingumnini wesicwangciso , imelwe yiKomiti yeWadi . Umasipala uxhobisa ooceba neekomiti zewadi zakhe ngamandla ukuze zincedise kwinkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso eza kwenza ukuba ikomiti nganye iyile ugunyaziso lwethuba lesikhundla . Ukuchongwa nokusebenzisana malunga nezisombululo zeemfuno zabahlali kunye nezinto eziphambili kuncedisa amalungu ebhunga neeKomiti Zewadi ukufeza imisebenzi yawo . Isahluko 2 sisekwe kwi-Community-Based Planning and the IDP , Guide 2 : Facilitators Guide for Community-Based Planning and Guide for Decision-Makers ( Isicwangciso Esisekwe kubahlali ne-IDP , Isikhokelo 2 : Isikhokelo Sababhexeshi Kwisicwangciso Esisekwe kubahlali Nesikhokelo Sabaqulunqi Bezigqibo ) ephuhliswe yi-AICDD Nemisebenzi Yophuhliso . I-MUNICIPAL STRUCTURES ACT , 1998 ifuna oomasipala bahlele rhoqo ngonyaka umsebenzi uwonke kamasipala . ISahluko 6 se-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 sinikezela inkqubo-sikhokelo esemthethweni yolawulo lokwenziwa komsebenzi koomasipala . Ulawulo lokwenziwa komsebenzi kufuneka lube yinxenye yesiCwangciso soPhuhliso oluManyanisiweyo . Udliwano-ndlebe lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali luqinisekisa ukuba iimfuno ze-MFMA , 2003 kufikelelwe kuzo ngokokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu kummandla kwinkqubo yokwenziwa kohlahlo lwabiwo-mali . Udliwano-ndlebe lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali luvumela iiKomiti zeWadi ukuba zithathe inxaxheba kuphuhliso lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala . Yintoni ulawulo lweprojekthi ? Ukubeka esweni kwiingxelo zonikezelo lweenkonzo - I-MFMA ifuna ukuba oomasipala bavelise iingxelo ngenkqubela-phambili yonikezelo lweenkonzo kwimimandla yabo . Ezi ngxelo zinika abahlali iindlela zokubeka uphuhliso esweni . Ngexesha lothethathethwano lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali , amalungu ebhunga , kwiiKomiti zeWadi , kufuneka acebise abahlali ngeziphumo zezigqibo eziphambili kubo . Kukho imfuno engamandla kulawulo lwentsebenziswano nentsebenziswano kumacandelo ewonke . Imithetho-siseko isekiwe ukuqinisekisa ngendawo eliziko elikwaziyo ukusebenza kunikezelo lwezibonelelo zomsebenzi kamasipala , nesebenzisa ubuchule bentsebenziswano . Kwindawo ohlala kuyo inkunkuma ayiqokelelwa rhoqo . Abahlali bendawo sebekhalaze amaxa aliqela kwibhunga likamasipala kodwa ingxaki isaqhuba . Umasipala uphinda athi esinye sezizathu kukuba abahlali abazihlawuli iintlawulo zabo kunye neerhafu kwaye oko kuchaphazela inkonzo , ngakumbi xa ezinye iindawo kwidolophu leyo zihlawula kakuhle aze umasipala abone kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukunikwa kweenkonzo kwezo ndawo . Izixokelelwano ezibuthathaka , nezenza kakubi zenza ukuba kubenzima ukuyamanisa uxanduva , neziphumo zarhoqo ezingenabani onika ingxelo ngazo . Isicwangciso sicaphula umzekelo wokwenzekayo xa amanzi edolophini efunyaniswa ukuba awalungelanga kuselwa . Amajelo osasazo abeka uMphathiswa wemiCimbi yezaManzi ityala . Uluntu lubeka ityala usodolophu . USodolophu ubeka ityala intloko yecandelo lamanzi . Intloko yecandelo lamanzi ibeka ityala kwinjineli yobugcisa . Injineli ithi uhlahlo-lwabiwo mali lokugcina izinto zisebenza luye lwathotywa kwiminyaka emithathu edlulileyo kwaye ngoku amanzi awaseleki . Intloko yezezimali kumasipala ithi uhlahlo-lwabiwo mali luthotywe kuba iindleko zabasebenzi ziye zaphazamisana nenkcitho yokulungisa izinto . Usodolophu uxoxa ngelithi ubume bomvuzo kuyathethwathethwana ngabo kwinqanaba likazwelonke yiManyano yooRhulumente abamaKhaya baseMzantsi Afrika . Imanyano ithi oomasipala bangahlukana nezi zivumelwano ukuba azifikeleleki . Njalo njalo . Iinkokheli zoluntu zikarhulumente zimela abemi kwimiba esondelelene neentliziyo zabo kwaye kumele zithathwe ngondiliseko . Ezi nkokheli zinoxanduva lokuqinisekisa ukuba ukugxeka nokuvukela kuqhutywa ngesidima nokukhula . Nangona iinkokheli zoluntu zikarhulumente maxa wambi ziye zimele kuphela imidla engacingelwanga ukubheka phaya kuluntu olubanzi noluneyantlukwano , zenza inxenye ebaluleke kakhulu kwidemokhrasi ezele udlamko olubandakanya abantu kuphuhliso olulolwabo . Isivumelwano okanye ubuchule obusekelwe emdleni - obu buchule bubona ungquzulwano njengenxenye yendalo kunxulumano lwabantu . Obu buchule abujongi ukuba ngubani ' orayithi ' , ingubani na ' orongo ' kwimeko yongquzulwano , koko bufumana isisombululo esiyinzuzo kuwo onke amaqela . Obu buchule buzama isisombululo SOKUWINA / WINA . Busebenzisa isisombululo seengxaki kunye nokubonisana ngokuvakalisa izimvo nokujongana nongquzulwano ngendlela ekhokelela kwisiphumo esihle emntwini wonke . Apho kufaneleke khona ngemibuzo engasentla , buza ukuba iinguquko ezithile ziwachaphazele njani amaqela ahluka-hlukeneyo ngokwahluka kwawo ( oku kuya kongezelela iinkcukacha malunga nokwahluka ngokwezentlalo ) . Umbono karhulumente wophuhliso kurhulumente wengingqi kukwakha oomasipala abaphilayo ngokwezimali belungele ukuphumeza izidingo zentlalo , zoqoqosho nezisisiseko zabantu ngendlela ekhuthaza ukuthatha inxaxheba ngendlela ezinzileyo . Umsebenzi wophuhliso karhulumente wengingqi uzikiswe nguMgaqo-siseko nangamaxwebhu omgaqo-nkqubo nawowiso-mthetho njengokuba echazwa kwesi sahluko . Ingqiqo kaMnu . Nkosi kukuba abanye abantu kule lali yakhe banekratshi kwaye abamcingeli . Ingqiqo yabantu belali kukuba uMnu . Nkosi ukrwada kwaye unekratshi . Iintlanganiso zikawonke-wonke - langamaqonga asebenzayo ekwabelaneni ngezimvo nolwazi . Amabhunga angabiza intlanganiso kawonke-wonke malunga nemiba ethile okanye ekugqithiseni ingxelo malunga neziphumo zentlanganiso okanye isiganeko esithile ; ukunikezela ingxelo yarhoqo kubahlali malunga neentlanganiso zebhunga neentlanganiso zeKomiti yeWadi , kungenjalo , uceba wewadi egameni leKomiti yeWadi angabisa intlanganiso ekugqithiseni ingxelo malunga nesihloko esithile ukuze lifumane izimvo zabahlali malunga nomba othile . Iprojekthi lilo naliphi na iphulo eliqhutywayo elijoliswe ekuqulunqeni inkonzo okanye isiphumo ngexesha elithe lalisikelwa . Ifanele ukuba ibe nophuculo eza nalo okanye izisa inguqu ethile . Ixesha leprojekthi lifutshane ; alingohalala okanye undofa womsebenzi , linohlahlo-mali oluqingqiweyo , kwaye ikholisa ukuba iqhutywe kube kanye . Urhulumente akanakuzimela zonke izidingo zabemi . Ngelixa abemi besiya kumaziko ovoto ukuya kuvotela iqela abalikhethayo nabacinga ukuba liya kuwumela ngcono umdla wabo , abantu bahlukile nezidingo zabo zahlukile . Nokuba urhulumente angazama kangakanani na akunakwenzeka ukuba afikelele kubo bonke abemi . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwabemi kunganceda ukuvala izithuba kuba bangazalisekisa amalinge karhulumente ngeyabo ngale ndlela babe badlulisa ilizwi labo phambili . Kungenxa yesi sizathu kwasekwa iiKomiti zeWadi ukuze zincedise urhulumente ukuqinisekisa ukuba abemi banegalelo kwizigqibo abachaphazelekayo kuzo . UMthetho Oyilwayo waMalungelo ubandakanya amalungelo ezentlalo-luqoqosho , afana nelungelo lokuphila kubume bemeko enempilo , ukukwazi ukufikelela ngokwaneleyo ekufumaneni indlu , kwiinkonzo zokhathalelo lwempilo nasekutyeni namanzi awaneleyo . Uluhlu lwamajelo eendaba - izikhululo zoonomathotholo boluntu kwingingqi kunye namaphephandaba engingqi yindlela eluncedo yokugqithisa ulwazi . Qinisekisa ukuba uneenkcukacha zoqhagamshelwano namajelo eendaba kwingingqi kwaye uhlala uqhagamshelana nawo rhoqo . Isahluko 1 neSahluko 4 zinika ulwazi ngeentlobo zababhexeshi ababandakanyeka kuphuhliso lweMephu Yendlela ye-CBP namaqela ahluka-hlukeneyo achaphazeleka ngokwegunya afuna ulumano-ndlebe . Ubumi obusebenzayo nokusebenza kwasekuhlaleni kuyimfuneko ekumiliseni idemokhrasi . Urhulumente akakwazi ukuvele asebenze egameni labantu - kumele asebenze nabantu , esebenzisana namanye amaziko ukubonelela ngamathuba okubhekela phambili kuluntu lonke . Ukuqinisekisa ngegalelo loluntu jikelele novavanyo lwesicwangciso-nkqubo somsebenzi ukuze sibonise okulindelwe luluntu kwingingqi . IiKPI kufuneka zihlaziywe ngonyaka njengenxalenye yenkqubo yohlaziyo lokusebenza kwaye ukuba umasipala ulungisa ii-IDP kufuneka ahlaziye nee- KPI . Iingxelo ezivela kwiikomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziqwalaselwe xa kuhlaziywa iiKPI . Le nkqubo iqinisekisa ukunika inkcazo ikwakhuthaza imvumelwano phakathi kwabahlali nebhunga . Ikwasebenzela ukuqinisekisa ukuba iPMS ibonwa njengento ethembekileyo ngabahlali . Ukukhutshwa kwekhabhondayoksayidi neegesi zeendawo ezikhulisela izityalo ezikhuselwa kwimozulu zitshintsha imozulu yomhlaba , zinako nokunyanzelisa indleko ebonakalayo yehlabathi eya kuthi ichaphazele ngokungayelelananga kwabo bahlelelekileyo . Amaqondo obushushu anyukayo , iimvula ezingazinzanga ezingakumbi nezehlo zemozulu ezibaxekileyo zingaphantse zibenoxinezelelo olunzima kwi-Afrika , nokusasazeka okwandayo kwezifo zetropiki nokukhula kweelahleko ( abantu nezimali ) ngenxa yembalela nezikhukhula . Ukutshintsha kwemozulu kunobunako bokunciphisa imveliso yokutya nokufumaneka kwamanzi alungele ukuselwa , okuneziphumo zeepatheni zemfuduko namaqondo empixano . Kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ubukho benxaxheba yabantu abanolwazi neyawo onke amaqela azizisulu kule nkqubo ukuze kuqinisekiswe uluvo lobunini nolawulo phakathi kwabahlali . Bhala imibuzo elandelayo kwifiptshathi ukuze abathathi-nxaxheba bayigqibezele kumaqela abo amancinci ngokusebenzisa iinkcukacha ezikumanqaku esifundo . Omabini amacandelo oluntu nelabucala angadlala indima ebalulekileyo ekwakheni amaziko akhoyo , ukuquka nezincedisi zophuhliso ezikhoyo ezinkulu . Ekuqalekeni kwengontsi yangowama-2009 , icandelo labucala libe nokuthandabuza ekutyaleni amaqondo alo anengeniso yeenzuzo ezigciniweyo kubunakho bokuvelisa . Ngaxeshanye , icandelo loluntu lixhase ukusetyenziswa kunotyalo-mali . Ukuvuma oku , urhulumente ubhengeze ukutshintsha kubume benkcitho ngokubhekiselele kutyalo-mali , imeko yangaphambili eyimfuneko yokuphelisa ukuxinga . Kwixesha , utyalo-mali lwecandelo loluntu lunganceda ukungena ngobuninzi kutyalo-mali labucala . Umasipala weWadi ABC unesaziso esikhulu esichaza iinkonzo azinikezelayo . UMnu . Jones usanda kufudukela kulo masipala uza eofisini ukuza kukhalaza ngokuba izibane esitalatweni sakhe azikhanyi kakuhle . Uxelelwa ukuba ngabe uyavuya kuba unendlu yena . Amaqela ezentlalo afanele ukuba achongwe phambi kokwenziwa kwezicwangciso aze anyanisekiswa kwintlanganiso yokundulula abahlali , kodwa amaqela awongezelelweyo asenokuchongwa ngethuba lokwenza isicwangciso . Funda imeko uze uyile imbono nomnqophiso kamasipala wakho uze wenze isikhokelo sokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu kummandla ukuhlangabezana nale mbono . Ukulungisa iajenda phambi kwentlanganiso . Lowo ngumsebenzi kaSihlalo nonobhala . Ekusebenzeni nee-arhente zikarhulumente ezifanelekileyo malunga nokunika ingxelo kwinkqubela yeenjongo . I-MFMA , 2003 ifuna ukuba oomasipala bavelise iingxelo ngenkqubela-phambili yonikezelo lweenkonzo kwimimandla yabo . Ezo ngxelo zinikezela uluntu kwimimandla ngeendlela zokubeka iliso kuphuhliso . Amaphandle anikezela imingeni eyodwa . Ngaphaya kwesinye kwisithathu sabemi baseMzantsi Afrika bahlala kwiindawo kwakufudulwa kusithiwa " ngoomaziphathe " , nesahlulo esikhulu seli qela sichwethiwe ngokoqoqosho . Iinkqubo ziyimfuneko ukuzisa imizi kwezi ngingqi zibe kwintsingiselo eyintloko yoqoqosho . Nangona kunjalo , kukho iingingqi zamaphandle apho amakhonkco othutho alungileyo nalapho ukuxinaniswa kusenzeka ekungabikhoni kolawulo lokusetyenziswa komhlaba olusebenzayo nolawulo lwedolophu . Abantu bathatha inxaxheba ngokufaka igalelo lemithombo yezinto ezisetyenziswayo , umzekelo , ukusebenza ukuze ufumane ukutya , imali esesandleni okanye ezinye izikhuthazo zezinto eziphathekayo . UMzantsi Afrika ube nenkqubela phambili engummangaliso ekuguqukeni kucalucalulo ukuya kwidemokhrasi . Olu tshintsho lwenzeke ngoxolo nangona imbali yelizwe ibonisa ungquzulwano olunobundlobongela nokohluthwa . Uqeqesho olwaneleyo : Makuqeqeshwe iqela labantu ababini ngewadi nganye abaya kusebenzela kufutshane kwiKomiti yeWadi . Ngokuxhomekeke kumava nezakhono zobuchule zexesha elidlulileyo malunga nempumezo , inkqubo yoqeqesho inokuthatha iintsuku ezinokufikelela kwezili-15 . Ngokwesibalo esisekelwe kuphando , amakhosikazi enza i-67% yomsebenzi wehlabathi , ngelo lixa bazuza i-10% yengeniso yehlabathi . Shicilela ngokubhala ngokuvunyelwene ngako ; yenza onke amaqela asayine ; gqithisa ngqo kwiForam eMele i-IDP . Amaziko akhoyo akayomfuneko nje kukukhula okukhawulezileyo koqoqosho nengqesho ephezulu . Akwaphakamisa ukukhula okubandakanyayo , kubonelela abemi ngezinto zokuphucula ubomi obubobabo nokuphakamisa iingeniso zabo . Amaziko akhoyo ayimfuneko kuphuhliso . Impembelelo yokutshintsha kwemozulu yehlabathi kumda nakwizisombululo zamazwe ngamazwe kumele zifunyanwe , kube kuqwalaselwe iimeko zemimandla nozwelonke . Umsebenzi 1 Jonga uMgaqo-siseko , chonga amacandelo amathathu akhuthaza ulawulo lwedemokhrasi wandule ukuchaza indlela amacandelo achongiweyo alukhuthaza ngayo ulawulo lwedemokhrasi . Ukunika ingxelo kumashishini karhulumente kwenziwe mfiliba yinkqubo enzima , nokuqeshwa okungacacanga , nokuba ngamanye amaxesha , nokungenelela kopolitiko okungeyomfuneko . Sicebisa ukulungiswa kwezikhundla zokunika ingxelo ngokuphuhlisa imiyalelo yemidla yoluntu ebeka ukuba ishishini likarhulumente lilukhonza njani uluntu , kuqinisekiswa inkqubo yokuqesha zigqamile kwaye ziyabonakala , nokuphucula ukusebenzisana phakathi kwenkqubo namasebe achaphazelekayo . Ezi mfuneko zimbini zizinto ezifunekayo kuphuhliso lukazwelonke oluyimpumelelo . Ukumanya uMzantsi Afrika ligalelo elibalulekileyo kwinkqubo yokunciphisa ubuhlwempu nokungalingani nesiphumo esithe ngqo sokuncitshiswa kobuhlwempu ngokuyimpumelelo . Ukwakha uluntu unamathelwano ngokwasekuhlaleni , uMzantsi Afrika kufuneka unciphise ubuhlwempu nokungalingani ngokwandisa amathuba nengqesho ngobandakanyo loqoqosho , imfundo nezakhono , nemilinganiselo yokulungisa ecacileyo ; ukuphakamisa intlonipho yamacala nokubandakanyeka ngokwemfuneko yomgaqo-siseko wokuba uMzantsi Afrika ngowabo bonke abahlala kuwo , kwaye bonke bayalingana phambi komthetho ; nokunabisa ukuxabisa imisebenzi nezibophelelo zabemi omnye komnye . Iishedyuli zeendleko zenza ukuba kukwazeke ukuvandlakanywa kokuhamba kwemali ( kubandakanya namagalelo amaqela achaphazelekayo ) , kananjalo nokuqulunqwa kwemihlaba yeZivumelwano zezeMali . Uphicotho lwesini sisixhobo sokufumanisa umahluko phakathi kwamakhosikazi namadoda ngokuphathelele kwimisebenzi yawo eyodwa , iimeko , iimfuno , ukufikelela nokulawula izibonelelo , nokufikelela kwiinzuzo zophuhliso nokwenza izigqibo . Siphonononga unxulumano lwezi nezinye izinto kumxholo wezentlalo , ezoqoqosho , ezopolitiko nezokusingqongileyo jikelele . Uphicotho lwesini luqulethe , kuqala , ukuqokelela idatha engahlulwanga ngokwesini nolwazi olumalunga nokulinganisa nokujonga ukungalingani ngokwesini malunga noluntu ekuthethwa ngalo . Uphicotho lwesini linyathelo lokuqala locwangciso lokulinganisa nokujonga ukungalingani ngokwesini ukwenzela ukukhuthaza ukulingana ngokwesini . Yenza umsebenzi ongezantsi nabathathi-nxaxheba uze ubhexeshe ingxoxo esekelwe kwimibuzo . INDLELA YE-CBP YOKUSEBENZA INIKA IIKOMITI ZEWADI INKQUBO YOCWANGCISO ENENKUTHALO NOZALISEKISO EKWENZENI IMISEBENZI YAYO NOXANDUVA LWAYO . BANE-AJENDA - ISICWANGCISO SEWADI - KWAYE UZALISEKISO , UKUBEKA ILISO NOVAVANYO LWESICWANGCISO SEWADI KUBANIKA INDIMA EQHUBEKEKAYO ENYAKENI WONKE EKUQWALASELENI IMIBA EPHAMBILI YOLUNTU KWIMIMANDLA ABANYULWE UKUBANCEDA . Abathathi-nxaxheba baphendula imibuzo engezantsi yenqanam ababelwe lona . Izalathisi eziphambili zokwenziwa komsebenzi zinceda urhulumente wengingqi nabemi ekwenzeni imilinganiselo ngokufezekisiweyo . I-KPI ziziphumo ' ezinokwenziwa ' nezinokulinganiswa umasipala avumileyo ukuba uya kuzifezekisa ngexesha elithile . Zinceda ekuthetheni nasekwenzeni umlinganiselo ngendlela ibhunga nomasipala abanikezele ngayo iinkonzo ngokuhambelana nezicwangciso ezichazwe kwi-IDP kwaye ngale ndlela , abemi bayakwazi ukuba babeke olu xanduva lokunika inkcazo kumasipala . I-logframe inika isiseko ekuya kuqulunqelwa phezu kwaso iikhontrakthi ngokuthi izicacise kakuhle iinjongo ekujoliswe kuzo . Kananjalo inceda nasekukhangeleni inqanaba loxanduva noxanduva lokwenza inkcazo yeemanejala zeprojekthi namanye amaqela achaphazelekayo . Ababhexeshi kufuneka bazimisele ukuphatha umba wengxelo ebuyiselwayo evela kwibhunga malunga nohlahlo lwabiwo-mali ngokwengqiqo . Abahlali basenokuziva bengonwabanga xa eminye imicimbi yabo ephambili ngokokubaluleka ingakhethelwanga ukufumana inkxaso-mali . Ingaba imigangatho yeenkonzo emisiweyo iyafikelela kwinqanam le-SMART ? IKomiti yeWadi ifuna ukusungula ziphi iiprojekthi ? Qwalasela izinto ezifana neeprojekthi zophuhliso loqoqosho lwengingqi , uqeqesho lwabaniki bokhathalelo lwasekhaya . Qwalasela ukuba ingaba ezi projekthi zinokwenziwa neminye imibutho yabahlali na ?
