Ukuya ezintlanganisweni zikawonke-wonke : Ezi ntlanganiso zinokubizwa lilungu lebhunga leWadi , yiKomiti yeWadi okanye libhunga . Basenokuxoxa ngesiCwangciso soPhuhliso oluManyanisiweyo ( IDP ) , uhlalo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala okanye eminye imibandela ebalulekileyo . UMthetho oyilwayo ongoXanduva , ophuhliswe liSebe leMfundo esisiSeko namanye , kumele wenziwe udume , kukhuthazwa wonke ubani ukuba aphile iinqobo ezisemgangathweni zoMgaqo-siseko . Uyindoda . Unomsebenzi kwidolophana . Inkosikazi yakho ilima imifuno . Umhlobo wakho ubonelele ngokuba athengise imifuno kwidolophu enkulwana ukwenzela ukufumana imali entle . Uyafuna ukukwenza oku kuba ufuna imali ukwenzela ukuthenga isuti entsha ulungiselela intlanganiso ezayo yebhunga likamasipala . Impendulo nonikezelo lwengxelo kwimbono , uphuhliso lweenjongo eziphambili nezicwangciso-nkqubo nokuphawulwa kweeprojekthi ze-IDP ukuqinisekisa ukuba oku kubonisa imeko ezinqwenela ukuba kuyo iKomiti yeWadi noluntu jikelele kwimimandla . Ukunikezela ngezindlu kufuneka kudityaniswe nokufaka isicelo samancedo , uthethwano lwezomthetho nonikezelo lwezindlu njengomqulu omnye , ngokwenzanjalo kuncedakala umthengi ukuba afikelele ngokupheleleyo kwiinkonzo kungekuko ukufikelela ngamagcuntswana nangokungadibaniyo njengamaqhekeza . Ukuhlanganiswa koqoqosho lommandla kungaphakamisa ukukhula koqoqosho kuwo onke amazwe akumazantsi e-Afrika . Ummandla ukhule ngokukhawulezayo kwiminyaka elishumi edlulileyo , kunemisebenzi enamandla kwizimbiwa , kwezolimo , kuthungelwano ngocingo nokhenketho . Ukuphumeza ukuhlanganiswa koqoqosho kufuna kuchongwe amathuba asebenzayo apho ukusebenzisana kungabonelela ngeenzuzo macala ; utyalo-mali kumaziko akhoyo ; ukomelezwa kweebhloko zorhwebo kummandla , ukuhliswa kwamaxabiso ; nokujongana nemiqobo engabizi xabiso , efana neendawo zemida ezingasebenziyo . Isazobe esilandelayo sibonisa indlela isigaba ngasinye solawulo lweprojekthi esikhokelela ekuhlolweni kwakhona kwezenzo nokuba umjikelo awuthanga ngqo ngokwendalo . Inkqubo yokuqala okutsha enkulukazi nenefuthe ngakumbi , ngokumanyana okusondeleyo nemizi-mveliso esebenza kumacandelo athe gqolo kwisicwangciso-qhinga sokukhula . Mema iqela elinye ukuba ligqithise ingxelo unike ithuba namanye amaqela ukuba anikezele iingcebiso nezimvo . Umbono ' liphupha ' labahlali , apho abahlali banqwenela ukuba khona . Kuthatha ixesha elide ukuvumelana ngombono , ngakumbi kuba njengoko iphupha labemi linokwahluka kakhulu oko kuxhomekeke kwintsukaphi ngokwezentlalo nezoqoqosho zomntu lowo othile . Esi sicwangciso sinombono woMzantsi Afrika apho umntu ngamnye eziva ekhululekile kodwa enamathele kwabanye ; apho umntu ngamnye esamkela ubunakho bakhe obupheleleyo , ilizwe apho ithuba lingamiselwa ngokuzalwa , kodwa ngokubanakho , ngemfundo nokusebenza nzima . Ukuzalisekiswa koluntu olulolo hlobo kuya kufuna inguqu yoqoqosho nemizamo engqalisiweyo ukwakha ubunakho belizwe . Ukubhangisa ubuhlwempu nokunciphisa ukungalingani , uqoqosho lumele lukhule ngokukhawuleza nangeendlela ezizuzisa bonke abemi boMzantsi Afrika . Ungquzulwano - phawula ungquzulwano okhe wanalo , emsebenzini , ekhaya okanye nokuba yeyiphi na imeko . Ixesha elimisiweyo elingezantsi libonisa ezinye zeziganeko ezikhulu ezichaphazela abahlali baseBloemfontein eFree State njengomzekelo . Ukuphakamisa izicwangciso-qhinga zezindlu ezixubeneyo nophuhliso lwedolophu olubumbene ngakumbi ukunceda abantu bafikelele kwizithuba zikawonkewonke namaziko , ii-arhente zikarhulumente , namathuba omsebenzi noshishino . Esi sihloko siqala ngokujonga iinkcazelo zokungafani . Siqhubeka siye kuzamana namacandelo endlela ephumelelayo ukulawula ukungafani kunye neminye imiba ephambili echaphazela ulawulo lokungafani . Isahluko siphela ngoluhlu loqinisekiso ukwenzela ukuyilwa kwesicwangciso sokwenza sokungafani . UMzantsi Afrika ungazuza ekukhuleni okukhawulezayo kumazwe asakhulayo akhokelela kwisinyanzeliso esandayo seempahla zorhwebo neshishini labaxumi elandayo . Ngaxeshanye , ezi ntsingiselo zinika umngeni kumazwe anenzuzo ephakathi ngenxa yokhuphiswano olukhulu ekuveliseni nakwiinkonzo ezithile zolwazi olwenziwa bubungcali . Ukukhula kwamashishini asavelayo kananjalo kwandisa ukhuphiswano lwamazwe , kubeka uxinezelelo olubhekise ezantsi kumvuzo wabasebenzi abanezakhono ezisezantsi kumacandelo anonaniselwano . Ixesha lobunzima lombane langowama-2008 nezinye izinto ezivelileyo ezintsha zichanabe ubuthathaka bamaziko anxulumene neenkampani zikarhulumente ezinoxanduva lamaziko othungelwano . Ukuphepha iingxaki ezinjalo kufuna amalungiselelo amaziko acace gca , iminqophiso yabanini bezabelo ebonakalayo , imigca yokunika ingxelo ecocekileyo nemifunziselo evakalayo yezezimali ukuqinisekisa ugcinakalo . Senza iingcebiso kwingingqi nganye kwezi . Imithetho elawula imimiselo isoloko ibhidisa , kuphithaniswa inkqubo nommiselo . Sicebisa iindlela zokulungisa oku . Ukunqongophala koovimba - umzekelo , imeko echazwe ngasentla . Ngenxa yokunqongophala konikezelo olwaneleyo lwamanzi , kufakelwe impompo esokolise wonke umntu . Okanye , umzekelo , kukho ukunqongophala kolwabiwo lwezindlu , kwaye ungquzulwano lungaveliswa lulwabiwo lwazo nendlela olwenziwe ngayo olu lwabiwo . Uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwarhoqo ngonyaka lukamasipala lubonisa ukuba isetyenziswa phi nakanjani na imali karhulumente ngumasipala . Le yinkcitho kamasipala . Ikwacacisa apho urhulumente wengingqi aya kufumana khona ingeniso . Abathathi-nxaxheba basebenza kumaqela afanayo nakuMsebenzi 1.1 baze baqwalasele umzekelo wophando ukuze baphuhlise isicwangciso-nkqubo soqhagamshelwano . Ukuqhubekeka nokuba nenkqubela-phambili ekunyuseni imivuzo nemigangatho yokuphila , ukuba nemveliso nako makukhule . Ishishini lezabasebenzi laseMzantsi Afrika lisoloko liphawulwa kukukhuphisana phakathi kwemizi-mveliso enengeniso nabaqeshwa abahlawulwa ngokufanelekileyo . Iziphumo ezichazwa kwiinkqubo zothethwathethwano azivumeli abantu abatsha ukuba bangene kwindawo yomsebenzi . Ukujongana namazinga aphezulu okungaqeshwa , ingakumbi kulutsha , imilinganiselo ebalaseleyo iya kuba yimfuneko . Isikhokelo semanyano yabasebenzi singundoqo ekuqinisekiseni ukuba inzuzo ngamalungu ziyagcinakala kwixesha elide . Ukuphumeza oku , imveliso nengqesho kumele zikhule ngokuqhubekekayo . Indlela yokusebenza yesicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali ifuna ukwenziwa kwesicwangciso ngokuqaphela nangokwendlela eyiyo ukuqinisekisa impumelelo . Ithatha ixesha nokuzinikela kwaye ifuna inkxaso yeKomiti yeWadi , ooceba namagosa ebhunga . I-CBP sisixhobo esincomekayo sokunika isakhono kwinjongo ye-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 . Urhulumente wophuhliso kufuneka abe nobunako , kodwa urhulumente onobunakho akaveli ngomthetho , okanye unganowiso-mthetho okanye uvele uwangazeliswe ukuba ubekhona ngobhengezo . Kumele wakhiwe , kubekwe isitena phezu kwesinye , kwiziko ngeziko , ukuze ugcinwe uze uvuselelwe kwixesha elithile . Ufuna ubunkokheli , iinkqubo ezivakalayo , abalawuli abanezakhono nabasebenzi , iindlela zokunika ingxelo ezicacileyo , izixokelelwano ezifanelekileyo , ukusetyenziswa kwemithetho engaguquguqukiyo nenobulungisa . Cinga ngendlela onxibelelana ngayo . UMBUZO 2 Kutheni lubalulekile ? Nika amaqela imizuzu engama-30 yokuphuhlisa uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lomsebenzi kamasipala . Kufuneka babhale phantsi imiba abayicingayo YOMVUZO WOMSEBENZI kunye nemiba ephambili yenkcitho yomsebenzi . Kufuneka bazobe olu luhlu lulandelayo kwiphepha lefliptshathi , bayigcwalise . Ibakala 2 liphela ngentlanganiso enkulu apho abahlali bakwaziyo ukuphengulula , baqwalasele kangangoko baze banyanisekise iinkcukacha ezihlanganiselweyo . Zonke iinkcukacha eziyilwe ngethuba lenkqubo mazibekwe ekuhleni ukuze zibonwe ngabahlali . Abahlali ke ngoko kufuneka bashiya-shiyanise iziphumo ezihlanu ukuze kwenziwe isicwangciso ngethuba lenkqubo yesizwangciso . Beka uluhlu olungezantsi kwi-overhead okanye usebenzise idata projektha . Ukuba akunaso nesinye kwezi zibonelelo , bhala uluhlu kwifliptshathi . Imephu Yendlela ibandakanya amabakala amahlanu acacileyo , ibakala ngalinye lakhela elinye elilandelayo . Isazobe esikwiphepha elilandelayo sinika ingcaciso ngokubanzi Ngemephu Yendlela . UKUNIKA IMITHETHO-SISEKO EYINGXAM , IINDLELA ZOKUSEBENZA NEENKQUBO EZIYIMFUNEKO ZOKUNCEDISA OOMASIPALA UKUBA BAHAMBELE PHAMBILI EKUPHUCULWENI KWEZENTLALO NEZOQOQOSHO ZAMAQELA ABAHLALI BENGINGQI , NOKUQINISEKISA UFIKELELO JIKELELE KWIINKONZO EZIPHAMBILI WONKE UBANI ANOKUKWAZI UKUZIHLAWULELA . La magqabantshintshi sisishwankathelo esikumgangatho ophezulu wesicwangciso . Izahluko ezili-15 zijongana ngokuthe vetshe neengingqi ezinomxholo ommandla , ubonelela ngobungqina , ngeengcebiso nangobume bokuzalisekiswa obuthe gca . Hlobo luni lomsebenzi owenziwa ngamakhosikazi amaninzi ? Chonga izinto ezizezona zixhaphakileyo , iingxaki ezikhoyo nentlawulo eqikelelweyo yolo hlobo lomsebenzi nokuba mangaphi amakhosikazi enza olo hlobo lomsebenzi . Emazantsi kule fomu ngumzekelo wendlela yokuyigcwalisa . Isebe likarhulumente ngalinye kufuneka liphuhlise isiCwangciso soPhuculo loNikezelo lweeNkonzo ( SDIP ) . Ii-SDIP zibalulekile kwinkqubo ye-IDP njengoko ziqwalasela ekwenzeni ' unikezelo ' lweenkonzo oluyimpumelelo , olunenkuthalo nolusebenzayo oluyinene noluzisa imithetho-siseko ye-Batho Pele ebomini ' . Inxenye ye-SDIP yiTshatha yoNikezelo lweeNkonzo . IiKomiti zeWadi kengoko kufuneka ziqonde inkqubo yophuhliso lwe-SDIP nonikezelo lweenkonzo , nokuqinisekisa ukuba uluntu lwazo kwimimandla luyaqonda malunga noku , kwaye luyazi ngamaphepha amalungelo ( charters ) afanelekileyo onikezelo lweenkonzo . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zihlale zisaziswa malunga nokuthatha inxaxheba kuphuhliso , iinjongo eziphambili nonikezelo lukamasipala . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwisicwangciso sonikezelo lweenkonzo kokona kuphambili . Ukuquka amacandelo abucala ngendlela esebenzayo kwii-IDP ukwandisa izicwangciso-nkqubo zophuhliso loqoqosho kummandla nakwingingqi nokuphuhlisa ingeniso nesiseko soovimba bakamasipala . Isimo sokunganxibelelani ngamazwi sinamandla kakhulu ekudluliseni umyalezo phambili . Iintshukumo ezingenabugoci-goci ezifana nokunqwala intloko , ukugcina uqhagamshelwano lweliso , usebenzisa ukuthetha ngobuso okufanelekileyo , izijekulo , ubume bomzimba nokuthetha ngamalungu omzimba zizinto eziluncedisayo unxibelelwano . Kwesi sigaba kufuneka kuqhutywe uvandlakanyo lwezakhono nolwezibonelelo ezikhoyo apha ekuhlaleni . Ngokujolisa ekuqinisweni kwezakhono zabahlali zokukwazi ukukhawulelana neengxaki zabo , kuyakwazeka ukuqhutywa kweeprojekthi ezinozinzo nokuqiniswa kwezakhono zabahlali . Phuhlisa uluhlu lwemibuzo eza kusetyenziswa kudliwano-ndlebe naba bantu ngokunxulumene nophuhliso lwewadi . Imibuzo kufuneka isetyenziswe ekubhexesheni iingxoxo jikelele nasekuncediseni umququzeleli wodliwano-ndlebe ekuxoxeni ngayo yonke imiba ebalulekileyo . Iiprojekthi ezisilelayo ukwamkela amacala ezesini emiba enjengobuhlwempu , iHIV / AIDS , nobundlobongela obenziwa kumakhosikazi okanye ukufikelela kwamakhosikazi kwizidingo ezisisiseko , izibonelelo , umsebenzi okanye umhlaba , aziyi kuba nokuqonda okupheleleyo ngengxaki . Iiprojekthi eziyimpumelelo kufuneka ziqonde ukuba le mingeni ineengcambu kuluhlu oluthile lwemiba yegunya nokungalingani ngokwentlalo olufuna ukuhlaselwa ukwenzela ukujongana nengxaki . Cela iqela elinye ukuba lixoxe ngoluhlu lwalo kunye neqela lilonke . Mema amanye amaqela ukuba ongeze okanye aphose igalelo kule ngxoxo . IPhepha leNgcaciso-nkqubo luxwebhu lomgaqo-nkqubo olubonisa ukuba ungaphunyezwa njani umbono karhulumente wengingqi wophuhliso ozibophelela ekuphuhliseni umgangatho wobomi babahlali nokuphumeza izidingo ngokusebenza kunye nabo ukufumana iindlela ezizinzileyo zokwenza oku . Oomasipala kufuneka balawule ezolawulo , iinkqubo zezicwangciso nohlahlo lwabiwo-mali ngendlela ebeka phambili izidingo ezisisiseko kubahlali . Imithetho-siseko ebekiweyo kwiPhepha leNgcaciso-nkqubo ixhaswa zizenzo ezahlukeneyo zepalamente . Ngawaphi amalungu eKomiti yeWadi ekufuneka enikwe imisebenzi eluxanduva yokwenza imisebenzi ? Unxibelelwano ngexesha nangendawo yentlanganiso ithuba liselihle kakhulu . Olu luxanduva lukanobhala . Kwinqanaba lamaziko , ulawulo lokhathalelo lwempilo lumandundu . ISebe lezeMpilo kutsha nje lindulule inkqubo yokuhlola ukulungela kolawulo . Ukuhlaziya okuncedisayo kumele kuquke abathunywa abakhulu abanamagunya kubasebenzi , kubume beshifu nesiqhelo sokufumana . Ezi ndlela ngeendlela zokusebenza zibandakanyekayo kulawulo lweeprojekthi zingahlulwa-hlulwa zibe ngamaqela amahlanu angala adweliswe kolu ludwe lukweli phepha lilandelayo . Bonisa umsindo wakho xa kufanelekile , kukhuselekile kwaye unako ukwenza njalo . Zama ukukulibazisa oku xa unokwenza ingxaki ibe nkulu kakhulu okanye ibangele enye . Fumana iindawo ezikhuselekileyo zokuvelisa umsindo wakho . Akufunekanga rhoqo ukubonisa umsindo okanye uphendule kuwo ; ngamanye amaxesha uvakalelo olunjalo luphela msinyane . Ukuphucula umgangatho wemfundo kwizikolo ezingaqhubi kakuhle nemfundo kumaziko aphezulu nakwiikholeji zoqeqesho . Bhekisela kumanqaku esifundo ( iphepha lama-56 ukuya kwelama-64 ) ngesixhobo sakho esingqalileyo uze ulandele inkqubo . Ukuba kuyenzeka seka iimpendulo zakho kumava akho ngewadi yakho . Yeyiphi imibutho yabahlali okanye amasebe kamasipala esifuna ukuyimema ukuba inike umboniso-ngcaciso kwiKomiti yeWadi okanye kwintlanganiso yabalandeli ? Isantya esiphakame kakhulu sotyalo-mali , notyalo-mali kumacandelo oluntu oluxinana kutyalo-mali lwabucala . Oku kuya kuxhomekeka kubambiswano lwamacandelo abucala , ukuqinisekiswa kwenkqubo nokwakha ukuzithemba ekukhuleni kwexesha elide koqoqosho . Ikwayindlela yokuqonda iimfuno ezintsokothileyo zoluntu . Endaweni yokwahlula abantu ' njengamakhaya ' okanye ' njengamahlwempu ' apho uthelekelelo lusenziwa ngabantu njengosapho olunye , uphicotho lwesini luvumela ukuqwalasela ngqo ubunyani abantu abahlangana nabo . Sahlula uphicotho lwamadoda namakhosikazi - iingxaki zabo , iimfuno nokufikelela kumagunya nakwizixhobo zokusebenza . Ngowama-2030 , uMzantsi Afrika kumele ube nesixokelelwano esibanzi sokhuseleko lwasekuhlaleni olubandakanya izibonelelo zokhuselo zoluntu , ukonga komhlalaphantsi ogunyazisiweyo , iinzuzo zomngcipheko ( ezifana nokungaqeshwa , ukufa neenzuzo zokukhubazeka ) nokonga komhlalaphantsi wokuzithandela . Ukudala imisebenzi ngakumbi ngophuhliso lwezolimo , olusekelwe ekubuyisweni komhlaba okusebenzayo nokukhula kolimo olunkcenkceshelwayo nemveliso yomhlaba . Ipesenti yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwekapitali kamasipala echithwe kwiiprojekthi eziyikapitali eziphawulwe kunyaka-mali othile ngokwee-IDP zikamasipala . Umphathi we-CBP ucacisela abathathi-nxaxheba ngesicwangciso , echaza indlela equlunqwe ngayo aze achaze banzi anabe apho kukho imfuneko . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwimibuzo enxulumene noyilo lweeprojekthi kwiiprojekthi ezithile eziya kuchaphazela imimandla yazo yoluntu . Ukuzimasa iintlanganiso zebhunga - inkqubo yebhunga yokwenziwa kwemithetho ifuna uxanduva lokunikeza inkcazo , ukungabikho mfihlo nonikezelo lweempendulo kuluntu jikelele . Uluntu jikelele lunelungelo lokuzimasa zonke iintlanganiso zebhunga . Ukusebenzisa eli lungelo , uluntu jikelele kufuneka lwazi ukuba zibanjwa nini na , phi na ezi ntlanganiso zebhunga . Kufuneka lwazi nokuba ezi ntlanganiso zimalunga nantoni na . IiKomiti zeWadi zingalunceda uluntu ngokunikezela ulwazi olu njalo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka azimase iintlanganiso zebhunga ukuze ahlale esazi njengamalungu oluntu ukuze akwazi ukugqithisa ingxelo kuluntu jikelele . UKUQINISEKISA UKUBANDAKANYWA KWESINI KUTHETHA UKUBA NASIPHI ISENZO OKANYE IIPROJEKTHI OKANYE IINKQUBO ZICWANGCISWA ZIIKOMITI ZEWADI , INZAME YAMXHELO MNYE YENZIWA UKUQINISEKISA UKUBA ISINI SIYAFAKWA KWEZI ZICWANGCISO . Ucwangciso lokuqhutywa - oku kubandakanya uqulunqo lwesicwangciso esineenkcukacha ezininzi malunga nokuba iprojekthi le iza kuqhutywa njani na . Ingabula-zigcawu ye-MSA igxininisa ukuba urhulumente weengingqi ' makabe nengqiqo yokuziqhelanisa nophuhliso olusisiseko ' . Cela abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bazahlule babe ngamaqela amancinci uze ubabhekise kwi-SWOT yamaqela yamaqela yamaqela amancinci kwiphepha lama-66 kumanqaku esifundo . Ukunyuka okugcinakalayo kwengqesho kuya kufuna uqoqosho olukhula ngokukhawuleza nokususwa kwezithintelo zezakhiwo , ezifana nemfundo ekumgangatho obuphantsi okanye iipatheni zezithuba zokuhlaliswa kwabantu ezicukula isininzi . Ezi zibaluleke kakhulu ekuphumezeni amazinga aphakame kakhulu otyalo-mali nokukhuphisana , nokwandiswa kwemveliso nokuthunyelwa kwezinto kwamanye amazwe . Ushishino , umsebenzi , uluntu kunye norhulumente kuya kufuneka basebenzisane ukuphumeza ukukhula koqoqosho okukhawulezayo . Ukuthembeka nempumelelo yayo nayiphi iprojekthi kuxhomekeka kwinkxaso yabantu abo kujongwe ukuba bazuze kwiprojekthi . Kubalulekile ke ngoko ukuba ilizwi labo bonke ababandakanyekayo liviwe ukuqinisekisa inkxaso yenkqubo . Kufakwe engqondweni ukuba amakhosikazi asoloko ejongelwe phantsi xa iinkqubo ziyilwa okanye zichongwa malunga nokuba abanye abantu bangacinga ukuba zeziphi iimfuno zawo , kubalulekile ukumamela izimvo nemibono kwaye iingcebiso ziyakhangelwa ukwenzela ukuba iprojekthi ibe nenkxaso yoluntu . Ukwenza amalungiselelo angaphaya kunganceda ekupheliseni ixhala lokugqithisa ingxelo . Khumbula : ukuba inqanaba lengingqi linqanaba apho abathabathi-nxaxheba banokuba nenxaxheba ngeyona ndlela isebenzayo . Iindibano zeengxoxo ziluncedo njengoko zinikezela ulwazi zivelise nokuqonda malunga nemiba ethile ziphinde zinikezele ithuba lophuhliso lomgaqo-nkqubo nokwenziwa kwezigqibo . Ziye ziqhutywe ngokwamaqela amancinci ukuze abathathi-nxaxheba kule ndibano yeengxoxo bakwazi ukugocagoca nzulu imiba ethile . Abathathi-nxaxheba bahlulwe babe ngamaqela uze uqwalasele iimeko kwiphepha 68 . Xoxa ngamanqanaba olawulo lomsebenzi . Landelisa oku ngengxoxo yenkqubo yokubeka iliso novavanyo . UMthetho i-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 unenjongo yokuphuhlisa inkcubeko yokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu kwimimandla nokusekwa kweendlela ezithile , iinkqubo neendlela zokusebenza ekuqinisekiseni oku . Ucacisa indlela yokugqithisa ulwazi nokumisa ngokusemthethweni izaziso zoluntu jikelele nolwamkelo kwiintlanganiso zoluntu jikelele kwakunye nendlela yokwazisa uluntu lwengingqi kwimimandla . Ukwandiswa iinkonzo zentlalo-ntle nezikimu zengqesho kawonkewonke , ukwenza ukuba urhulumente akwazi ukunikezela inkonzo nokuxhasa uluntu oluhlelelekileyo , ingakumbi olo lunamazinga aphakamileyo olwaphulo-mthetho nobugebenga . I-Batho Pele inikezela inkqubo-sikhokelo yenguqulelo yonikezelo lweenkonzo kurhulumente . I-Batho Pele , oko kukuthi ' ukubeka abantu kuqala ' iyilelwe ukuba abasebenzi bakarhulumente baziqhelanise neenkonzo kwaye bazame kangangoko banako banikezele lo msebenzi wabo ngokugqwesayo . Ivumela ukuba abathengi babambe abasebenzi bakarhulumente njengabanoxanduva lokunikeza inkcazo malunga nendlela abanikezela ngayo iinkonzo . Uvavanyo lomsebenzi kungenziwa umlinganiselo walo ngokuchaseneyo nendlela esetyenziswa ngayo iMithetho-siseko yeBatho Pele xa abasebenzi bakarhulumente besebenzisana noluntu . Ixesha - maliqwalaselwe xa ubamba intlanganiso okanye ucweyo . Ukuba isemva kwexesha kakhulu okanye ebusuku okanye ngempela-veki xa amalungu abahlali kufuneka bejonge ezabo iimfuno , okanye besemsebenzini , uya kufumana impendulo edanisayo . Eli candelo ligcina iingxelo zezinto ezenziwa ngumbhexeshi / ababhexeshi ukuphuhlisa esi sicwangciso nokuba ngubani oye wabandakanyeka . Kweli candelo umbhexeshi / ababhexeshi badwelisa iintlanganiso ezibanjiweyo negama / inani labathathi-nxaxheba nababhexeshi . Kuyimfuneko yokuqala ukuba iKomiti yeWadi ithathe inxaxheba kuphuhliso lwesicwangciso-nkqubo esiya kumisa ngendlela efanelekileyo ingqwalaselo yeenkqubo zikamasipala kummandla wayo kwixesha leminyaka emihlanu . Ngokwesiseko , le yindlela enokuthi iKomiti yeWadi iqinisekise ukuxabiseka kwayo . Oomasipala kufuneka balungise i-IDP ebandakanya ithuba leminyaka emihlanu . Inkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso neyokuziphumeza ihlanganiselwe ngokwamabakala amahlanu ngokufutshane ngezantsi . Kubalulekile ukuziqhelanisa nala mabakala ukuze unxulumanise imijikelo ye-CBP naleyo ye-IDP . Isicwangciso sophuhliso esimanyanisiweyo yinkqubo apho oomasipala balungisa khona isicwangciso sophuhliso-buqili sethuba leminyaka emihlanu . I-IDP yimveliso yenkqubo yezicwangciso zophuhliso ezimanyanisiweyo . Isicwangciso sokwenza sokungafani sifuna inkcazo eninzi kunye neenkqubo ezicingisisiweyo . Isicwangciso kufuneka sifumane iindlela zokukhuthaza ukungafani , ukuphathwa ngokulinganayo nobulungisa ngeli lixa sijonge umba wocalulo . UMgaqo-siseko woMzantsi Afrika ukwanikezela amaziko ukuba omeleze idemokhrasi yomgaqo-siseko . La maziko aziwa njenge-'Chapter 9 ' njengoko kuchaziwe kuMgaqo-siseko kwiSahluko 9 . Isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali esisebenzayo silulwahlulelano phakathi kwawo onke amaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya . IiKomiti zeWadi zingamaqonga / izakhiwo ezamkelekileyo ezisebenza njengemisele yelizwi labahlali ukuba liviwe . Ababhexeshi be-CBP kufuneka besebenze nawo onke amaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya ukuze isebenze inkqubo . IiKomiti zeWadi zingazifumana zikwimeko ekufuneka ziphendule kungquzulwano . Qwalasela ezi meko zilandelayo nokuba bobuphina ubuchule obusetyenzisiweyo . Kwesi sahluko , siya kujonga inkqubo-sikhokelo esemthethweni eseka imvelaphi yonikezelo lweenkonzo , indima ekufuneka idlalwe ziiKomiti zeWadi kunye neenkqubo ekufuneka zimisiwe ukuqinisekisa unikezelo lweenkonzo olunempumelelo . IiKomiti zeWadi zibhexesha ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu kwinkqubo yophuhliso , uhlelo ngokutsha nolawulo lozalisekiso lwe-IDP . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zibe nokuzithemba , ulwazi nezakhono ukuze zizalisekise lo msebenzi . Uluhlu sisishwankathelo sabathathi-nxaxheba , imisebenzi yabo nonxulumano kwiKomiti yeWadi . Iiyantlukwano zesini zibhekiselela kwiiyantlukwano phakathi kwamakhosikazi namadoda ezikhethwa ngokukhululekileyo kwaye zixatyiswe ngokungenacala . Kodwa ke , ' iiyantlukwano ' ezininzi phakathi kwamadoda namakhosikazi , nalapho zinokubandakanya ukuzikhethela ( umz. into omawuyinxibe ) , nangona kunjalo zizinziswe kumaqumrhu okungalingani ngokwesini , anika jikelele ixabiso eliphantsi kukhetho lwamakhosikazi kwaye agcine ukufikelela okungalinganiyo kumagunya nakwizibonelelo . Inkqubo egunyaziswe ngokwenene eyenzeka kwinkundla yomthetho kunye nejaji okanye umantyi ovelisa isigqibo sokugqibela emva kokufumana ubungqina nengxoxo esemthethweni kumacala omabini . Isigqibo sakhe siya kusekelwa kumthetho wetyala , uwiso-mthetho nokuqhutywa koku okusemthethweni . Iprojekthi nguwo nawuphi umsebenzi wokuphuhlisa inkonzo okanye imveliso kwithuba lexesha elimisiweyo . Ifanele ukongeza ixabiso okanye iveze inguquko enika ithemba ngendlela ethile . Iprojekthi inexesha elinyiniweyo asingomsebenzi oqhuba oko okanye inkqubo esisigxina kwaye inohlahlo lwabiwo-mali kananjalo olumiselwe elo xesha kuphela . Malunga nokunikwa kweenkonzo zikamasipala kukho iiprojekthi eziqhubayo , ezifana nolondolozo lweendlela . Kwiziganeko ezilolo hlobo indlela yokusebenza echazwe apha ayifanelekanga noko . Iprojekthi nganye ifana yodwa kwaye ineeseti zayo zemiceli-mingeni nemibandela efanele ukuqatshelwa . Ngoko ke siyimfuneko isicwangciso esifana sodwa ukuqinisekisa ukuba iprojekthi ibe nempumelelo egqibeleleyo . Ibhunga lingamisa imiyalelo malunga nendlela yonikezelo lwezaziso yemithetho eyilwayo kubahlali , nokuba kungeepowusta okanye amajelo eendabaAbahlali bangagqithisa izimvo ezibhaliweyo bazigqithise kwi-ofisi kamasipala . Ibhunga kufuneka lenze amalungiselelo awodwa kubahlali abangakwaziyo ukubhala , okanye abakhubazekileyo okungokunye okwenza ukuba kubenzima ukunikezela ugqithiso . OWONA MSEBENZI UPHAMBILI WEKOMITI YEWADI kukuqinisekisa ukuba abemi kwiwadi yabo bayabandakanywa bekwaziswa ngezigqibo zebhunga ezichaphazela ubomi babo . IiKomiti zeWadi ngamehlo neendlebe zabahlali nendlela ebaluleke kakhulu yokukhuthaza ukuqondana phakathi koluntu kunye nebhunga . Oku kuthetha ukuba iKomiti yeWadi kufuneka icebisane nabahlali malunga nophuhliso nezicwangciso zeenkonzo . Unxibelelwano luyafuneka ekuqinisekiseni ukuba iimbono , iinjongo nezimvo zoluntu zibandakanywa kwizigqibo ezimalunga nonikezelo lweenkonzo nophuhliso . Iinkonzo zozakuzo lorhwebo ezandisiweyo ukuxhasa ukwandiswa kwesabelo soshishino saseMzantsi Afrika kumazwe ngamazwe . Umngeni wokuqala kulawulo lweprojekthi kukuqinisekisa ukuba iprojekthi iqhutywa phakathi kwemida esikiweyo . Owesibini , nongathi ujoliswe phezulu kakhulwana wona , kukuqinisekisa ukuba kuninzi okwenziwayo ngemali ethe yabelwa iprojekthi leyo nezinye izibonelelo ezikhoyo zokufezekisa iinjongo zeprojekthi le . Ukucwangcisa indlela eza kuqhutywa ngayo iprojekthi - esi ke saziwa ngokuba sisigaba soqulunqo okanye sisigaba socwangciso lokuqhutywa . Iimeko neemfuno zinokuguquka njengokuba kusiya kufika abantu abatsha nje endaweni ; kusenokuthi kanti iimfuno zangaphambili zafezekiseka ; ngoku sekuvele ezinye ezintsha . Ezidolophini amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka amele umdla weqela labantu , umzekelo , iqela lokholo , imibutho yamanina , imibutho yolutsha , icandelo lempilo , iqela lezemidlalo , abahlali , imibutho yabahlawuli beenkonzo . Bonke abemi kufuneka baphathwe ngentlonipho novelwano . Impendulo : Endaweni yokuvula oku kwithenda , ibhunga ligqibe ekuqesheni ikhontraka X lisithi inegunya lokwenza njalo . Iinkonzo zezimali ezomeleziweyo ukuba zithobe iindleko zazo nokuphucula ufikelelo kumashishini amancinci naphakathi . Ibakala ngalinye lenziwe ngeziganeko eziliqela ezithile apho kusetyenziswa khona isixhobo se-CBP esinye okanye ngaphezulu . Kufuneka ibe yinjongo yabo bonke abasebenzi bophuhliso ( kwarhulumente , kumasipala , okanye abancedisi bangaphandle ) ukuba bakhe iindawo ekuhlalwa kuzo abalawula kuzo iiprojekthi . Abahlali banikwa amandla luphuhliso olufanelekileyo , ngakumbi xa nabo benenxaxheba kwiiprojekthi ezibachaphazelayo . Ukuba ngaba bayakufunda ukuba nempumelelo kuphuhliso lwabahlali , ezo zinto bazifundileyo abahlali baya kuthi bazisebenzise nakwezinye iinkalo zobomi babo . Baya kufunda ukwenza amalungiselelo ngempumelelo kwaye nezakhono zobunkokeli ziya kuqina . Uxanduva lokuphendula - inguqu kurhulumente wengingqi ayinakuphunyezwa ngaphandle kokuba abameli bakarhulumente wengingqi baziva bephembelelekile ukwenza njalo . Impembelelo yenguqu kufuneka ikhuthazwe . Oku kunokufuna inzame yamxhelo mnye kwicala leKomiti yeWadi echaza isimilo esivumelekileyo / esingavumelekanga , imigangatho esezantsi yezifezekiso nokuba zeziphi izohlwayo ezinikwayo ukuba le migangatho ayifunyanwanga . UMBUZO 6 Zisetyenziswe njani ? Ngubani ozisebenzisileyo ? Lungisa amaxwebhu esicwangciso kwangaphambili njengoko oko kunokuthetha ukuba iilephtophu okanye ubonelelo lokuchwetheza kufuneka lubonelelwe . Ukuncitshiswa kokukhutshwa kwegesi ziindawo ezigcina izityalo ezifuna ukukhuselwa nokuphucula ukusebenza kombane . Qinisekisa ukuba iqela liyawuqondisisa umahluko phakathi ' kokubaluleka ' ' nokufikelela ' . La magama angatolikela kulwimi lwasekuhlaleni . Ukubonelela ngeenkonzo ezisisiseko ezibangela abantu baphuhle kubunakho bokuthatha inzuzo yamathuba ngokujikeleze ilizwe , kubenza ukuba bakwazi ukuba negalelo kuluntu lwabo ngemali ethunyelwayo nangokutshintshelwa kwezakhono . Sukela ukuphela kwekhulu le-19 leminyaka , uMzantsi Afrika uxhaphaze ubutyebi bezimbiwa zawo kukho ubuncinane okanye bungekho kwaphela bokucingela okusingqongileyo . Iinguqu ziyafuneka ukukhusela okusingqongileyo kwendalo logama kuvumela ilizwe ukuba lizuze kwizimbiwa zalo . Ukongeza kubutyebi bezimbiwa ezingavuselelekiyo kwakhona obubonakalayo , ubutyebi bendalo belizwe buquka iilwandle ezimeleneyo , umhlaba , amanzi , iyantlukwano yobomi , ukukhanya kwelanga nakunxweme . Akukho zibonelelo zolonwabo kuWadi A. Oku kuchaphazela ikakhulu ulutsha oluma kwiikona zezitalato , ngamanye amaxesha besela baze baqalise imilo . Iicawa zengingqi ziye zadibana ekuxoxeni ngendlela yokusombulula le ngxaki . Badibene neKomiti yeWadi . Lo mba uxoxiwe kwiKomiti yeWadi nevumileyo ukuba uceba wewadi awandlale lo mba kwintlanganiso elandelayo yebhunga nokucela ibhunga ukuba libize intlanganiso namaqela achaphazelekayo ukuquka amashishini oluntu , amaqela olutsha , imibutho esekelwe kwinkolo , njl-njl . IKomiti yeWadi incedise ngokuhlangana namaqela achaphazelekayo awohlukeneyo ekuwaziseni malunga nengxaki kunye nesizathu sentlanganiso yamaqela achaphazelekayo . Kwabizwa intlanganiso kwaze kwagqitywa ekubeni ibala lezemidlalo elinendlwana encinci yeklabhu linganceda ulutsha ekulunikeni indawo yokuhlangana . Imibutho esekelwe kwinkolo ivumile ukusebenzisana ekunikezeleni iinkqubo nemisebenzi enokwenza ulutsha luthathe inxaxheba IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zinikwe ingxelo rhoqo malunga nokusetyenziswa kwekheshi kamasipala . ' Ukusetyenziswa kwekheshi ' kukungena nokuphuma kwemali kwi-akhawunti yebhanki kamasipala . Umsebenzi 3 Khetha amanyathelo owachonge kuMsebenzi 2 . Gqiba ngoya kukwenza ukunceda iKomiti yeWadi yakho ukuba ithathe la manyathelo . Ukungathembani - abahlali basenokungazithembi iinkokeli ezinyuliweyo , amalungu eKomiti yeWadi namagosa kamasipala ukuba bangaziphumeza ngokusebenzayo iinkqubo neeprojekthi . Oku kungabangelwa ngamava angaphambili okanye ukungabi nalwazi . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi adinga ukufumana iindlela zokukhuthaza ithemba nokuzithemba nokubona ukuba ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu kunesiphumo okanye intsingiselo . Kwicala lezopolitiko , idemokhrasi yenze kwenze inkqubela-phambili engalungelelananga . Uvukelo-mbuso lwakutsha nje kuMtla Afrika sisikhumbuzo esipheleleyo semingcipheko solawulo oluphantsi namaziko abuthathaka avumela abantu bomgangatho ophezulu ukuba bafumbe ubutyebi bedlelela abantu . Imimandla emeleneyo eyenza iWadi icelwa ukuba ithumele abameli abatyunjiweyo ukuba banike inkonzo njengamalungu eKomiti yeWadi . Shwankathela inqanam ngalinye . Ummandla owayamene nonxweme woMzantsi Afrika uphawulwe ngamaqondo aphezulu obuhlwempu nentswela-msebenzi , kukho unyimo lwengqesho kwezolimo . Inkqubo yocalucalulo yanyanzelisa uninzi lwabemi abangama-Afrika ukuba bayekuhlala kwindawo ezingavelisi kwanto zasemaphandleni . Iziphumo zaba licandelo lorhwebo ngolimo olubhekela phambili nolwahlukenenyo oluxhomekeke kubasebenzi befama abahlawulwa kancinci , noluntu oluhlelelekileyo , oluxinanisiweyo kunamathuba anyiniweyo oqoqosho neenkonzo zikarhulumente ezincinci . Iingcebiso zeKhomishoni kumaziko akhoyo oqoqosho ziquka ezezimali , ucwangciso nokugcina . Apha ke kubhalwa ezo zinto zingundoqo , kodwa zizezangaphandle ( izinto ezingaphaya kwamandla eqela leprojekthi ngokokulawulwa ) eziyimfuneko enkulu ekuphumeleleni kweprojekthi le . ULWAMKELO LOHLAHLO LWABIWO-MALI LINYATHELO ELIYIBHAKANA YOKUMISELA IXESHA LOKWENZEKA KWEENKQUBO ZE-IDP NE-CBP . Iinjongo ezichazwe kwi-logframe , zidibene nomsebenzi , zinika iinkcukacha zokuxhasa uhlahlelo lwendleko nesiqhamo . Abahlali baba ngabanini beprojekthi eyenziwayo . Oku kungakhokelela kunonophelo nangakumbi olungathatyathwa ngabahlali lophuhliso olunjengeepaka okanye izakhiwo . IBatho Pele ikhokela inkqubo karhulumente yesicwangciso-qhinga , onke amanqanam eSicwangciso soPhuhliso oluManyanisiweyo , ulawulo lokusebenza nolawulo lwembuyekezo . Isisiseko sokulungisa ubume bendawo yokusebenza yawo onke amalungu asebenza kwiinkonzo zoluntu . Iinjongo zamasebe kaZwelonke kufuneka zihliswe zibe ziinjongo nemibono zabo bonke oorhulumente bamaphondo nabengingqi . Kwangokunjalo iMimandla Yeziphumo Eziphambili ( Key Result Areas okanye iKRAs ) zabaphathi nayo kufuneka yenze ngokufanayo . Inkoliso yabahlali ihlala mhlawumbi kwizindlu zebhokisi yematshisi okanye bahlala ematyotyombeni asemva kwezindlu . Uninzi lwezindlu kule ndawo alunambane okanye amanzi aqukuqelayo . Izikolo zithathu kuphela kanti iiklinikhi zimbini kule ndawo . Ukuphucuka kuphunyeziwe ekusebenzeni kohanjiso lweenkonzo kwiipokotho zikarhulumente , ngokubonakalayo kwiNkonzo yeNgeniso yoMzantsi Afrika neeprojekthi zokulinga namaSebe emiCimbi yaseKhaya , yeMpilo noBulungisa . Ulawulo lwemisebenzi nokuphuculwa kwesixokelelwano kusesazulwini soku kulungisa , kwaye ezi mpumelelo kufuneka ziphuculwe kwiinkalo ezininzi zikarhulumente . La mava abonisa okunokuphunyezwa xa iinkokheli nabasebenzi bezinikele ekusebenzisaneni ukuphucula ukwenza . IKomiti yeWadi nganye kufuneka ithathe isigqibo ngeendidi zeekomitana nepotifoliyo efuna ukuba nazo ewadini . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi anikwa iipotifoliyo ezizodwa . Uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali akufunekanga lwenziwe njengemfihlo ! Intlanganiso yamaqela enamaqela aphambili anolwazi afana nabalimi okanye abafazi . Zinike ixesha elinokuba ngangeeyure ezimbini ngale ntlanganiso . Kuya kusebenza njani oku xa kusenziwa ? Umngeni oyintloko Mzantsi Afrika kukubuyiswa umva kobuhlwempu nokungalingani . Ukuphakamisa imigangatho yokuphila kwinqanaba elincinane okucetyiswe kwisicwangciso kuya kubandakanya indibanisela yokwanda kwengqesho , imivuzo ephakamileyo ngokukhula okuvelisayo , izibonelelo zokuphila [ 1 ] neenkonzo zoluntu zobulunga obuphezulu . Yonke le mingeni iyathungelana . Umzekelo , imfundo ephuculiweyo , iya kukhokelela kwingqesho neengeniso eziphezulu , logama ukukhula koqoqosho okukhawulezayo kuya kwandisa amathuba kubo bonke kuze kubonelele ngemithombo eyimfuneko ekuphuculeni imfundo . Ukufezekiswa kwesiCwangciso sobuTyebi obuHlanganisiweyo ( kufunyanwa ubuncinane ama-20 000MW ombane kwizinto ezihlaziywayo ) ukunciphisa ukukhutshwa kwekhabhoni esuka kumashishini ombane ukusuka kwi-0.9kg ngekhilowathi ngeyure ukuya ku-0.6kg ngekhilowathi ngeyure . Abameli beeKomiti zeeWadi banokuthabatha inxaxheba kwiQonga leeNgxoxo le-IDP . Eli qonga linika ithuba kwabachaphazeleka ngokwegunya ukuba bamele imidla yabahlali . Linika isakhiwo sengxoxo , uthetha-thethwano , ukuthathwa kwezigqibo okuhlanganelwayo phakathi kwabahlali nomasipala . Likwanika ithuba lokubeka esweni isicwangciso nokuphunyezwa kwe-IDP . Uluvo lweKhomishoni kukuba kwixesha elide , abasebenzisi kumele bahlawule isambuku sendleko kumaziko oqoqosho , kunokhuseleko olukhoyo lwemizi ehlelelekileyo . Indima karhulumente nengeniso kukubonelela iziqinisekiso eziyimfuneko ukuze iindleko zitsalwe kwixesha elithile , ngaloo ndlela kugudiswa umkhondo wexabiso . Urhulumente kumele naye abeke endaweni imithetho efanelekileyo nobume bolawulo ukuze amaziko abe asetyenziswa ngempumelelo namaxabiso abe nokubekwa kumanqanaba afanelekileyo . Kumaziko aveza ingeniso yezezimali , ityala elinyusiweyo ekwakheni amaziko kumele ibe kumaphepha okubonisa umncono amashishini karhulumente okanye kwiinkampani zabucala ezenza loo msebenzi . Iziqinisekiso kumele zisetyenziswe ngokukhethekileyo ukuthoba indleko yesixa-mali nokufumana iimali zexesha elide . Inkxaso kwimizi ehlelelekileyo kumele ithi ngqo kwaye ibonakale kangangoko . Amaziko asekuhlaleni angenzi ngeniso yamali- afana nezikolo nezibhedlele - kumele axhaswe ngemali esuka kuhlahlo-lwabiwo mali . Abahlali kufuneka bathathe inxaxheba kwinkqubo yokubeka esweni , ukwenziwa kwemilinganiselo nohlelo ngokutsha lomsebenzi , njengomasipala , emva kothethwano nabahlali bengingqi , baphuhlise bekwazalisekisa iindlela neenkqubo baphinde luphawule iinkqubo zokwenza oku . Umasipala , xa ecinga ukuba oko kunganikezela igalelo elikhulu kubahlali nokuthatha inxaxheba kwabo , angaseka iqonga leengxoxo okanye iforam yokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi angabandakanywa kule foram . Ngumsebenzi kacaba ukuseka iforam yoluntu . Yeyiphi enokwenzeka kwangoko ? Ezi njongo zifezekisa okujoliswe kuko okudandalaziswe kuMkhondo wokuKhula oKutsha . Ukuba iithagethi zokusebenza akufikelelwanga kuzo , kufuneka kwenziwe imizamo yokuncedisa umntu ukuba aziphumeze ezo ziphumo . Ukuba uyaqhubeka engasebenzi kakuhle kungathathwa amanyathelo anjengokumiswa emsebenzini , ukohlwaywa okanye ukupheliswa kwekontrakthi . Ukuze ulwazi lube luncedo , kufuneka luhlahlelwe ngokufanelekileyo . Idata kufuneka iguqulwe ngenjongo yokufumana isiphelo . Ukubeka esweni inkqubela-phambili yeprojekthi kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukuba iqhuba ngendlela efanelekileyo nokuthi imingcipheko emitsha okanye iinguquko ziyaqatshelwa kwaye zinikwa indawo yazo kwimpumezo elandelayo . Amaqela asebenza kunye kwiprojekthi asebenzisa izalathisi ukuze alandele ngoqwalaselo inkqubela-phambili . Izalathisi zizinto ekujoliswe kuzo ezibonisa ukuba ingaba iinjongo zifeziwe na . Iifreyimi zolawulo lokujikelezisa maxa wambi zibizwa ngokuba ' zizalathisi ezinyanisekisa ngaphandle kweempembelelo ' . Izalathisi kufuneka zibe nonxulumano , zanele , zingqale , zilinganiseke , zisebenzise imali ngobuchule kwaye zifumaneke . Gqibezela ngesifundwana esincinci esisekelwe kuluhlu olukwiphepha 90 . Uluhlu lunikezela iiKomiti zeWadi ngoluhlu loqinisekiso lwemiba nalapho banokuqwalasela khona naxa bedibene noluntu kummandla . IKhomishoni yokuLingana kweSini neSebe lamaBhinqa , abaNtwana naBantu abanokuKhubazeka kumele ngokuhlangeneyo bazibekele imigqalasela ecace gca ekuqhubeleni phambili amalungelo amabhinqa nokunika ingxelo kwinkqubela-phambili ngonyaka . Kweli nqanam , umxolelanisi kufuneka asebenzise umsebenzi wokusombulula ingxaki . Iprojekthi ingachazwa njengalo naliphi inyathelo ukuphuhlisa inkonzo okanye imveliso ngesithuba sexesha elibekiweyo . Kufanele yongeze ixabiso okanye izise inguqu eyakhayo ngendlela ethile . Iprojekthi inexesha elilinganiselweyo endaweni yokuba ibe yinkqubo eqhubayo okanye emi imi , inohlahlo lwabiwo-mali oluxeliweyo kwaye isoloko ilinyathelo lexesha elinye . Kukuhanjiswa kweenkonzo kukamasipala kukho iiprojekthi eziqhubelekayo , njengokulungiswa kwendlela , kwezo meko umgaqo olandelwayo ochaziweyo apha unokungafaneleki . Ukwenza umalatha-ndlela kukwanika abahlali imbono yokwandlaleka kwezithuba kwixesha langoku , imibandela echaphazela iizowuni ezahluka-hlukeneyo , imithombo eyindalo , ubume bemeko yasezidolophini nezinto ezinokukhethwa ezinokubakho zokuphucula ubume bemeko yabo ephilayo . Ukwakha i-inshorensi yempilo kazwelonke yinjongo ebalulekileyo . Kukho izinto ezine ezifunekayo : ukuphucula ubulunga bokhathalelo lwempilo yoluntu , ukuthotywa kweendleko eziphathelelene nokhathalelo lwabucala , ukugaya iingcali ngakumbi kuwo omabini amacandelo oluntu nawabucala , nokuphuhlisa isixokelelwano solwazi lwempilo olungxabalaza kubaboneleli boluntu nababucala . Oku kuhlaziya kuya kuthatha ixesha , kufuna intsebenziswano phakathi kwamacandelo oluntu nawabucala , nokunyanzelisa imithombo obubonakalayo . Ngokupheleleyo , abathathi-nxaxheba baphawula iinkqubo eziphambili kuzwelonke nakwiphondo esele ziphuhlisiwe ukuqinisekisa ukuba iinkqubo zikazwelonke nezephondo ziyahambelana nemiba ephambili kamasipala . Indlela esinamava ngayo ngongquzulwano inempembelelo kwindlela esiphendula ngayo kungquzulwano . Kukho uluhlu lwamanqanaba awenza umjikelo wongquzulwano . Lo mjikelo ungamhle okanye ungabimhle . Umjikelo yimaphu eluncedo ekucingeni ngeendlela olwenzeka ngayo ungquzulwano ebomini babantu . Abathathi-nxaxheba bafunda ibakala ngalinye , ngenye indlela umbhexeshi unako ukuchaza ibakala ngalinye , ecacisa kwaye echaza apho kukho imfuneko khona . Yintoni enokundinceda ndimamele ngendlela encomekayo ? IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zenze inzame emxhelo mnye ukuqinisekisa ukuba onke amaqela aqukiwe kwiinkqubo zokwenza izigqibo ezichaphazela uluntu kwaye aqukiwe kwiintlanganiso zokunika ingxelo nokuba izimvo zawo ziqukiwe , ingaba ngamaqela amakhosikazi , uluntu olungabafudukeli , amaqela enkonzo njl . Oku kungafuna isicwangciso sokwenza esicacileyo esiyilwe ngokukodwa ukuba siquke amaqela asingelwa phantsi . Olunye lolu lwazi lusenokuba lwahlanganiselwa ngethuba elingaphambili ziingcali ze-CBP . Qokelela iinkcukacha zemvelaphi uzicwangcise ngokolungiselelo lwesishwankathelo . Qwalasela neKomiti yeWadi kunye noceba ukuba ingaba ikhona na imithombo yolwazi enokusetyenziswa . Iqela elikhokelwa ' ngababhexeshi ' , malinike amagqabantshintshi ngemisetyenzana engundoqo neeprojekthi eziphakathi kwabahlali babo nokuba ngoobani abaniki beenkonzo . Umongameli uMbeki wagxininisa wathi , ' iinzame zokubusiphula neengcambu ubuhlwempu nokusilela kophuhliso kweli lizwe lethu kusisiseko sokuphumeza iinjongo zethu zikazwelonke zokwakha isizwe esinenkathalo nesisekelwe ebantwini . ' Oku kunika isiseko sokuba singayiqondisisa njani iBatho Pele . Ngulo mgangatho osisiseko soguquko nenguqu ezibonisa ukuba iBatho Pele inganempembelelo ngenene . IiKomiti zeWadi zingenza izincomo ngemiba echaphazela iwadi kuceba . Okanye ngokuthuma uceba kwisixeko okanye kwibhunga lengingqi okanye kwiikomiti zebhunga . Oku kungasentla zizalathisi ezinikezelwe nguMphathiswa emva kothethwano nee-MEC zephondo kurhulumente wengingqi ne-SALGA . Logama amawaka amatyala aphandwayo , ambalwa ade aye enkundleni yamatyala . Kumele kusekwe amaqela abatshutshisi aziingcali neenkundla zamatyala ezizodwa . Ukuphuhliswa kukazwelonke akuzange kube yinkqubo engumgca , kwaye nesicwangciso sophuhliso asinakuqala singumgca othe tye . Ngokuphathelelene noko , sicebisa isakhelo esintlangothi-ninzi esizisa umjikelezo olunge kanye wophuhliso , ngenkqubela kwingingqi enye exhasa ukuhambela phambili kwezinye . Inzululwazi nobugcisa kungasisixhathiso sokusombulula eminye yeyona mingeni mikhulu kwezemfundo nezempilo . Iindawo ezininzi e-Afrika ezingazange zonwabele unxibelelwano ngocingo oluzinzileyo zifumana iinkonzo ngokubanzi ngothungelwano lweefowuni zeseli olubonelela ngoluhlu lweenkonzo . Iimathiriyeli zezemfundo zingathuthwa ngeekhompyutha kwiilali ezikude . Inzululwazi yaphula imida emitsha ekulweni izifo nokuthoba indleko yokucocwa kwamanzi . IiKomiti zeWadi zingafumana ulwazi olusuka kuluhlu loovimba abohlukeneyo . Umzekelo , umasipala anganikezela ulwazi ngenani lamakhaya kummandla , okanye amaPolisa oMzantsi Afrika anganikezela ulwazi malunga namanani olwaphulo-mthetho . Kananjalo , iKomiti yeWadi ingaqalisa uvavanyo lwayo ngokutyelela kumakhaya athile ukufumana ulwazi . Abasebenzi bophuhliso loluntu nabo bangancedisa ekufumaneni ulwazi belufunela iKomiti yeWadi . Ukuveza ukukhula okukhawulezayo koqoqosho , utyalo-mali oluphezulu nokwamkelwa okukhulu kwabasebenzi . Umsebenzi ngamnye kufuneka wabelwe zonke izibonelelo eziyimfuneko kuwo ( oko kukuthi , iindleko ngokwasemalini kwakunye nezinye izibonelelo ) eziya kuba yimfuneko ekuyigqibeni . Izibonelelo ezifunekayo kufuneka zicaciswe ngokuchanekileyo . Abantu baphendula ungquzulwano ngeendlela ezohlukeneyo . Ngexa abantu abaninzi benokuphendula ngendlela enye lonke ixesha , abanye abantu bangasebenzisa ubuchule obahlukeneyo kwimeko yongquzulwano . Injongo ephambili yokulawula ungquzulwano kukusombulula ungquzulwano ngendlela eyakwenza onke amaqela asuke kwiimpikiswano eziva onwabile ngesiphumo . Oku kungaziwa njengemeko YOKUWINA / WINA . Ipesenti yemizi erhola ngaphantsi kwe-R1 100 kwinyanga nganye nefikelelayo kwiinkonzo ezisisiseko zamahala . Ingaba iKomiti yeWadi idlale indima kwinkqubo yokwenziwa kwezigqibo zebhunga ? Iiprojekthi ezincinane zasekuhlaleni ezifana nokuphuculwa kwenkqubo yeklabhu yebhola yalapha ekuhlaleni okanye ukuseka iprojekthi yegadi yokuzinceda , nazo zifuna ukuba kuqhutywa nezimiselo zolawulo lweeprojekthi , khona ukuze ziqinisekise ngokufikelelwa kweenkalo ebekujoliswe kuzo . Kwixesha elincinane , inkqubo kufuneka iphendule ngokukhawuleza nangempumelelo ekukhuseleni okusingqongileyo kwendalo nokudambisa iimpembelelo zokutshintsha kwemozulu . Kwixesha elide , izicwangciso-qhinga ezinobunganga eziyinene , nobudlelane behlabathi , uMzantsi Afrika ungalawula ukutshintshela kuqoqosho lwekhabhoni esezantsi kwisantya esingaguquguqukiyo nezibhambhathiso zikarhulumente kuluntu , kungakhange kwenzakaliswe misebenzi okanye ukuba nokhuphiswano . Qala ngokuxoxa ngezinto ezilindelekileyo nangeenkxalabo ze-CBP , yazisa abantu ngayo nangendlela engena ngayo kwinkqubo ye-IDP kamasipala , indima yeqela lababhexeshi neleKomiti yeWadi . Chonga amaqela ahluka-hlukeneyo ezentlalo phakathi koluntu . Usenokusebenzisa ukubeka ngokwezintlu zempilo-ntle ezifana nomzekelo ongezantsi . Iziko lolwazi kwingingqi - i-ofisi kamasipala wengingqi yindawo efanelekileyo yokufumana ulwazi . Lungabekwa nakwibhodi yezaziso . Uvavanyo : Abahlali okanye abathunywa babo bangadlala indima ekuvavanyeni abanokuba ngabanikezeli beenkonzo , ukuzibandakanya kwabahlali ekunikezelweni nasekubekweni esweni unikezelo lweenkonzo kunganceda . Thatha iimpendulo emaqeleni . Zama ukuchonga amanyathelo asetyenziswe ngabasombululi-ngxaki . IKomiti yeWadi ngumthundezi obaluleke kakhulu ( i-arhente yenguqulelo ) ekwenzeni ukuba abahlali bathathe inxaxheba kwimiba echaphazela abahlali kwaye ngale ndlela , kwenza iZikhokelo ezichazwe ku-1.1.1 zibe yinene . IiKomiti zeWadi zingenza njalo ngokuxhasa nokuncedisa imimandla ekwenzeni amalungiselelo . Zininzi izinto eziya kuthi zibonakalise ukuba ngaba iprojekthi le kungakwazeka na ukuyenza ; ngoko ke kufuneka kuqhutywe olunye uqulunqo lwesicwangciso esiya kuthi sibe sesokuncedisa . Zikhona izixhobo ezivunyiweyo eziye zaqulunqwa ngeenjongo zokufumanisa ukuba zeziphi na kanye ejolise kuzo iprojekthi nokuba ngaba ziyafikelelwa na ezi nkalo . Abathathi-nxaxheba basebenza ngokwamaqela ezine ukuya kwizihlanu baze baphendule imibuzo engezantsi . Ukuba iqela likhetha ukufundela ngaphandle , malifunde umbuzo omnye ngexesha , kwaye onke amaqela makaxoxe ngombuzo aze agqithele kumbuzo olandelayo . Ukuba usebenzisa ifliptshathi nika iqela ngalinye imibuzo emibini . Khumbula ukuba angaphezu kweqela elinye amaqela aya kuba nombuzo ofanayo . Amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi asenokufuna ukuphendula iintlobo ngeentlobo zabantu abasenokuba nemidla eyahlukileyo . Le midla isenokwahluka kwiimbono zamalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi . Ukusebenza nokunxibelelana nabantu abanemidla neentsukaphi ezahlukileyo kusenokukhokelela kungquzulwano . IsiCwangciso soPhuhliso sikaZwelonke bubume besicwangciso-qhinga esibanzi . Sidandalazisa indlela enamathelayo negqibeleleyo ekujonganeni nobuhlwempu nokungalingani kusekelwe kwizinto emazijongwe kuqala ezintandathu ekugxilwe kuzo nezithungeleneyo ezishwankathelwe ngezantsi . Igama elisembindini elithi Batho Pele ' ngummi njengomthengi ' . Imithetho-siseko inyanzelisa uluvo lwabo bafumana iinkonzo zoluntu njengabathengi , hayi abemi . Ngako oko abasebenzi boluntu mabangazifihli ngasemva kwabasemagunyeni , kodwa mababeke abathengi babo kuqala . Iinkcukacha eziqokelelwe kuhlalutyo lweempiliso lusetyenziselwa ukuqhuba i-SWOT yamaqela ezentlalo . Iziphumo jikelele neziphumo ezinqwenelekayo ngeqela ngalinye ziya kushwankathelwa kwifliptshathi . Wazi ntoni ngeeKomiti zeeWadi ? Ukulingana kujongene nokuphatha abantu ngendlela enye , ngaphandle kweziphumo . Kubhekiselela kwimpatho enye kunaniselwano , ubungakanani okanye iinqobo . Ukulingana kungakhokelela kukungalingani okungqongqo kumaqela ebevinjwe amathuba yinkqubo esilelayo ukuthathela ingqalelo iimeko neengqiqo zabo . Impatho elinganayo iqikelela ilungelo kwiimeko zentlalo ezinye , umvuzo , neemeko zomsebenzi kumakhosikazi namadoda . Okokuqala , umasipala kufuneka amise ukuba zeziphi iinkonzo azinikezelayo , ngubani ozifumanayo kwaye unjani umgangatho wazo . Umzekelo : Ingaba inkunkuma ilandwa kangaphi ? Umzekelo weziphumo zokulinganisa nokujonga ukungalingani ngokwesini : ( a ) Inani elandileyo labantu abasingeleke phantsi kakhulu - isini esibhalisiweyo nesihleliyo esikolweni ; ( b ) Igunya lokwenza izigqibo elandileyo kumakhosikazi malunga nenkcitho yasekhaya ; ( c ) Ukuthatha inxaxheba okulinganayo kwamakhosikazi namadoda kulawulo lobutyebi bendalo . Zama ukumamela ngenzondelelo . Umzekelo , ngexa umsindo ubonakalayo , musa : ukucacisa , ukuphazamisa , ukunika izizathu , ukugweba okanye uvavanyo . Mamela ngovelwano ngokwenza omnye umntu ukuba azi ukuba uyakuva okuthethwayo nokuviwayo . Kumaxesha amaninzi , ulwazi lokuba kukho indawo ekhuselekileyo yokuvelisa indlela oziva ngayo ivumela abantu ukuba bakwazi ukukhupha uvakalelo lwabo ukuze bakwazi ukuthatha inxaxheba ngendlela esemgangathweni ekuhambeni kwethuba . Utyalo-mali kuthutho lukawonkwonke , oluya kuzuzisa imizi enomvuzo osezantsi ngokuququzelela ukuhanjiswa . Buza abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bayayazi na i-IDP kamasipala wabo . Thatha iimpendulo . Ukuba abathathi-nxaxheba bayayazi i-IDP yabo babuze ukuba iqulethe ntoni na . Bhala kwifliptshathi . Ukuba uneekopi zee-IDP zabathathi-nxaxheba bakamasipala , mema abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bajonge i-IDP ukuze babone ukuba ingaba iqulethe amanqaku aphakanyiswe ngabathathi-nxaxheba na . Uludwe lokuqwalaselwa lunokufinyezwa , lwenziwe lula luze luqhelaniswe nemo ekubhekiselelwe kuyo yengingqi nakwimida yomsebenzi womniki wenkonzo ekubanjwe udliwano-ndlebe naye . Unxibelelwano olungcono , ukuthembeka ngakumbi nenqanaba elikhulu lokuthobeka kwabo basezikhundleni kungenza utshintsho olukhulu ekwakhiweni koluntu olungasombulula iingxaki ngobunye nangoxolo . Izicwangciso zeprojekthi aziyi kubonisa izinto njengoko zinjalo ukuba amakhosikazi akuthethwana nawo ngokupheleleyo malunga noyilo lweprojekthi kwakunye nokufezekiswa kwayo . Umsebenzi 1 Yintoni injongo yenqanam eliqwalaselwe liqela lakho ? Amanzi : Amanzi ebefunyanwa phi kudala , oku kuguquke njani kwiminyaka ngeminyaka ? Kutheni ? Ingaba zikhona iinguquko kwimigama emide ehanjwa ngabafazi xa besiya kukha amanzi ? Kutheni ? Ingaba kubekho iinguquko kudidi lwamanzi ? Ingaba ukhona umlambo ? Ingaba kukho amadama / izicwangciso zonkcenkcesho eziphuhlisiweyo ? Ingaba oku kuluchaphazele njani ufikelelo emanzini / udidi lwamanzi ? Iimpendulo zinokubandakanya : Unqongophalo lwenkxaso evela kubahlali kunye / okanye kumasipala , intlanganiso eyandulela ukwenziwa kwesicwangciso elungiselelwayo kodwa abathathi-nxaxheba bangafiki , ukunqongophala kwemithombo yezinto ezisetyenziswa ngabahlali nababhexeshi bewadi ukuze baqhube inkqubo . Inkokheli - umbhexeshi ukhokela ekwalawula inkqubo , unikezela ulwakhiwo kwintlanganiso okanye inkqubo aze abe noxanduva lwesiphumo . Isahlulo 2.3.2 sePhepha leNgcaciso yoMgaqo-nkqubo lonyaka ka-1998 lichaza ukuba ukunyuswa komgangatho wedemokhrasi yengingqi kufuneka kubonwe njengendima ephambili kuye nawuphina urhulumente kamasipala . Sicacisa imithetho-siseko emine yokuthatha inxaxheba , nequka ukuvumela abemi , nokuba ngumntu ngamnye okanye ngokwamaqela anomdla , ukuba abenegalelo kupolitiko lwengingqi nabaxhasi beenkonzo bakwazi ukuphosa igalelo labo kwindlela ekunikezelwa ngayo iinkonzo . Umgangatho wengingqi yindawo apho abemi banokuthatha inxaxheba ekwenziweni kwezigqibo ekulungiseni iindawo abahlala kuzo nokusebenzisa kwanokwandisa amalungelo abo phantsi kwedemokhrasi . Lonke uwiso-mthetho oluxhasa oku lubhalwe kukho oku engqondweni . Oku kuthetha ukuba amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka agcine ezi zimvo engqondweni xa ecinga malunga nendlela yokwenza umsebenzi wabo njengendlela yonxibelelwano phakathi kwebhunga nabemi kummandla wabo . Impumelelo yenkqubo yokwenziwa kwezicwangciso yayame kwinxaxheba yeqondo eliphezulu lamalungu ewadi . Oku kuya kunika abahlali isakhono sokuqhuba iinkqubo zabo zokwenza izicwangciso kwixesha elizayo kunciphise uxhomekeko kubabhexeshi bangaphandle . Ilungu lebhunga leWadi ngusihlalo weKomiti yeWadi . Unako ukuthuma ilungu lebhunga elimele umlinganiselo okanye naliphi ilungu leKomiti yeWadi ukuba lichophele intlanganiso . Phendula imibuzo elandelayo . Phuhlisa ibinzana elidlamkisayo kummandla wakho nelinokusetyenziswa kwiipowusta , iimemo nemateriyali engenye . Ukulawula ngobuchule - Ibhunga lasekhaya okanye umbutho ' wenza ngokungathi ' uyathethathethana ukwenza ukuba inkqubo ibe semthethweni ngaphandle kokuthethathethana kwenene . Umzekelo , umbutho okanye inkampani okanye ibhunga lithi sithethathethene kwaye abahlali bavumile kanti eyona nto yenzekileyo kukuba abantu bavele baxelelwa ukuba into ethile iyenzeka . Namhlanje iqela labasebenzi ( abo baneminyaka eli-15 ukuya kuma-64 ) benza umyinge wama-64 ekhulwini wenani labemi , nomlinganiselo wabantwana nabadala besenza izabelo ezincinane . Ngokwezizwe , umfanekiso wokufundwa kwamanani abantu abasaphilayo nabangasaphiliyo ofana nezi ixesha elininzi ayanyaniswa nokunyuka kwemivuzo , ukukhula ngokukhawuleza kwemveliso , ukonga okuphezulu nokunyuka kwamazinga okuphila . Ngenye indlela , zingakhokelela ekutshitshiseni nasekugungqiseni okusingqongileyo apho abantu abasebatsha bengenakufumana msebenzi , babenegalelo kubundlobongela , ulwaphulo-mthetho , ukusetyenziswa gwenxa kotywala nobubi obuqhubeka ekuhlaleni . Okumisela impumelelo kukuba ingaba ilizwe lingakwazi ukusebenzisa inzuzo yokuba nenani elikhulu labantu abatsha abanako nabazimisele ukusebenza . Ukwenza njalo kuthetha ukuba mababonelelwe ngemfundo nezakhono , nokunceda abo bashiya izikolo phambi kwexesha bafumane umsebenzi ovuselelayo nabaya kuthi ngawo baphumeze ulangazelelo lwabo . Ingaba ibhunga nelungu lebhunga kwiwadi zinoxanduva njani lokugqithisa inkcazo ? Ukuphawula iimfuno - ukwenza uphando okanye uhlahlelo lweemfuno ngenjongo yokuphawula imiba ephambili kummandla kwimiba yophuhliso , uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali nonikezelo lweenkonzo . UKWAZI UKUFEZEKA ( ACHIEVABLE ) - ingaba umgangatho uyafezekiseka kubasebenzi abakhoyo kwisebe , uyinene ngokomsebenzi wangoku nowangaphambili ? Kukwakho indawo yoogoba ' ityholo engekho mthethweni eqale malunga neminyaka emihlanu edlulileyo . Amanzi ale ndawo aphuma ezimpompini zikawonke-wonke kwaye zintathu kuphela iimpompo kule ndawo . Uninzi lwabahlali kule ndawo lurhweba ngokungekho sikweni kwaye abaninzi babesebenza kwezi fama bada bagxothwa . Akukho zikolo kule ndawo . Uludwe lokuqwalasela impahla exabisekileyo lunokufuna ukuqhelaniswa nommandla apho iqhuba khona i-CBP ( umz . ezidolophini , emaphandleni njl.njl. ) . Amanyathelo alandelayo athathwa neqela elifanayo elinokufikelela kwi-12 labantu . Aqala ngolungiselelo lwengxelo yeenjongo ngenjongo nganye yokusebenza . Lo msebenzi uya kwenziwa kumaqela amancinci , ilelo libe nelungu leKomiti yeWadi nabantu abanxulumeneyo abanolwazi nabaniki beenkonzo . Ukufezekisa ngempumelelo esi sicwangciso , ilizwe lifuna ubudlelane obufikelela kulo lonke uluntu olusebenzisanayo lunenjongo enye . Okwangoku , uMzantsi Afrika unamaqondo aphakamileyo okungathembani okumandla phakathi kwamadlelane asekuhlaleni . Umjikelezo olunge kanye wokwakha ukuthembana nokuthethathethana ukujongana nemingeni eyeyona ibeka uxinezelelo uyafuneka - lowo uthatha uluvo lwexesha elide . Ingaba bubuchule obahlukeneyo ? Ukuba kunjalo , bahluke njani kwaye bufezekise ntoni ? Ngokusebenzisa icwecwe lohlalutyo ngeempiliso elizaliswe ngethuba lomsebenzi odlulileyo cela abathathi-nxaxheba ukuvelisa itheyibhile efana naleyo ingezantsi . Umbono wesini kufanele ukuba ufakwe kuLuhlu lweMigqaliselo yokusebenza olulungiselelwe noluphi na uvavanyo . Imiba elandelayo kufuneka yenziwe kuvavanyo kwaye , apho kuyimfuneko , ixelwe ngendlela engahlukanisi ngokwesini ukukwenzela ukufikelela kuhlolo olululo nolupheleleyo lweziphumo zenkqubo . Ukukhula kwexesha elide notyalo-mali kufuna imbono ekwabelwana ngayo , ukuthembeka nokusebenzisana phakathi kwamashishini , abasebenzi norhulumente . Namhlanje , izinga lokuthembakala lisezantsi , kwaye ubudlelane babasebenzi bube noxinezelelo ngokungafanelekanga ( maxa wambi kunobundlongondlongo ) . Kuyaqondakala ukuba uqoqosho luya kuvela ngendlela enomsebenzi oqatha ukuba ezi meko ziyaqhubekeka . Ukuphakamisa ukukhula okukhawulezayo , okuveza imisebenzi kuthetha ukulwa olu xinezelelo ngendlela enyanisekileyo nevulelekileyo . Urhulumente wedemokrasi ukhethwa ngabantu kunyulo oluqukayo , oluzimeleyo nolungenamkhethe nolwenziwa ngokuyimfihlo . Aqinisekise ukuba ibhunga limele umsebenzi walo odlulileyo . IiKomiti zeWadi zingangathathi nxaxheba ethe ngqo kwimisebenzi kasodolophu kodwa njengabantu abanoxanduva lulonke lwebhunga , amalungu eKomiti yeWadi angaqinisekisa ukuba usodolophu wazi yonke into ngemiba yasekuhlaleni . Zama ukuqonda ukuba lo msindo ujoliswe kuwe ngqo na . Abantu abaninzi abanomsindo banovakalelo olunjalo ngaphakathi kubo ngaphambi kokuba ufike . Kungenzeka ukuba usendaweni engalunganga ngexesha elingalunganga . Kubizwe intlanganiso nguceba wewadi kunye neKomiti yeWadi yokuxoxa ngeeprojekthi ezicetywayo eziza kubandakanywa kwi-IDP ekwenziwa amalungiselelo ayo ngokwangoku . Amanye amalungu oluntu jikelele kummandla afuna iklinikhi yakhiwe kwindawo ekume kuyo amatyotyombe amaninzi , njengoko abahlali kula matyotyombe bengenamali yokuya esibhedlele okanye kwezinye iiklinikhi ezikude . Elinye iqela labahlali lifuna i-IDP iquke amalungiselelo okuphucula irenki yeeteksi njengoko le ikhoyo ingenazo izindlu zangasese okanye iindawo yabantu abathengisayo . Iqela lesithathu lifuna ukwandisa inkonzo yenkunkuma ibe ziintsuku ezimbini ngeveki kummandla wesixeko ngenxa yobuninzi benkunkuma ezitratweni . Intlanganiso ishushu njengoko iqela ngalinye ligxininisa ekubeni iiprojekthi eliziphawulileyo nekufuneka zibekwe phambili . Kubalulekile ukuba urhulumente wedemokrasi akhusele amalungelo abantu anikwe kuMgaqo-siseko . Imithetho-siseko yeBatho Pele iqinisekisa inkqubo yokuguqulwa kweenkonzo zoluntu ukuze zanelise izidingo zabahlali zifezekise amalungelo abo . Ngokwenza oku imithetho-siseko iqhubela phambili ukusebenza kwedemokrasi eMzantsi Afrika . Isicwangciso senxaxheba okanye esisekwe kubahlali sixhobisa amaqela abahlali ngamandla okusebenzisana nokuzibophelela kumalinge afanelekileyo okulamla ngokucutha intswelo kumaqela abo abahlali kwaye kufuneka sikhokelele kugunyaziso lwengingqi oluphuculweyo nakwezinye izicwangciso neenkonzo zeearhente . Ngokubhekiselele kwiphepha lama-33 kumanqaku esifundo xoxa ngenqaku ngalinye lezifundo kulo nabathathi-nxaxheba . Qala ngamabakala esicwangciso se-IDP . Thatha imizuzu embalwa uqwalasela nabo amabakala e-IDP ubachazela ukuba kuyimfuneko ukuziqhelanisa ne-IDP njengoko umjikelo we-CBP unxulumana nalowo we-IDP . Ukuthabatha inxaxheba koluntu kwenzeka kwimigangatho eyahlukeneyo . Inkqubo-sikhokelo eyilwayo sibhekisa kwi'ladder of Participation ' ebhalwe nguSherry Arnstein ( 1969 ) . Ileli ibonisa ukuba ungakhetha inyathelo libe linye ngexesha . Iqela labahlali elibanzi lidibana iiyure ezimbini , mhlawumbi ngoMgqibelo ukutshona kwelanga , okanye xa kufanelekile kubathathi-nxheba . Iqela liya kuphengulula umbono , lishiya-shiyanise iinjongo ngokokubaluleka kwazo ngesicwangciso -buqili ngasinye , izindululo zeengxowa-mali ngokwengqiqo nokunikelwa kwi-IDP . Kuluncedo ukuba nalo lonke olu lwazi kwifliptshathi . Ukuba unemithombo yobutyebi ulwazi lunokuchwethezwa luze lukotshwe . Ubuninzi besicwangciso bujongana nokuhlaziywa kwamaziko afunekayo ekupheliseni ubuthathaka kumacandelo oluntu , ngokukodwa apho ii-arhente zoluntu zingakwazi ukuhlangabezana noxanduva lwazo kuluntu oluhlelelekileyo . Ezi ngcebiso zimalunga nokuphuhliswa kweempawu eziyimfuneko ekuxhaseni isicwangciso . Ukwakha ubunakho bamaziko kuthatha ixesha nomzamo . Isiqendu ekwakheni urhulumente onakho nophuhlisayo kubonelela ngezalathisi kwindlela ekumele ilandelwe . Amaziko aphucuka ngokufunda okuqhubekekayo namanyathelo anesongezo ; kuhlaselwa ezona ngxaki zimandundu , ukuzisombulula nokudlulela kwiqalela elilandelayo . Oku kufuna ulawulo olusulungekileyo , ukuzinikezela kumsebenzi ophezulu , ukujolisa okungalalalaliyo kwiinqobo ezisesikweni nokuthakazelela ukufunda kumava . UMBUZO 1 Yintoni uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali ? Ezi mpendulo zingaluncedo kwiindawo ezithile namaxesha athile . Kodwa kumaxesha amaninzi , ziyekisa ukumamela , zityhafise abanye . Zithetha ukuba : awulunganga ngokwaneleyo , awumhlanga ngokwaneleyo , awomelelanga ngokwaneleyo ; Ndim owaziyo . UMBUZO 5 Zeziphi iziphumo zomsebenzi ezingundoqo ( KPIs ) ? Kukwakho indawo yoogob ' ityholo engekho mthethweni eqalise malunga neminyaka emihlanu edlulileyo . Amanzi ale ndawo aphuma ezimpompini zikawonke-wonke kwaye zintathu kuphela iimpompo kule ndawo . Uninzi lwabahlali kule ndawo barhweba ngokungekho sikweni kwaye baninzi abasebenza kwezi fama bada bagxothwa . Akukho zikolo kule ndawo . Indima yeKomiti yeWadi kukuqinisekisa ukuba abo banoxanduva lokwenza isicwangciso seprojekthi bayawabandakanya amaqela abahlali kwaye baqinisekisa ukuba bathabatha inxaxheba kwiprojekthi ngokupheleleyo . UMzantsi Afrika ufuna ukuba iinkokheli zisebenzisane kuluntu luphela . Njengokuguquka kusukwa kucalucalulo kwakusisisombululo esiphunyelelwa macala kunokuba lukruthwa-kruthwano ngamandla olujonge phambi kweenzwane , ukulwa ubuhlwempu nokungalingani kuya kuba neenzuzo kuye wonke ubani - omnyama nomhlophe , osisityebi nolihlwempu . Kukho iyantlukwano yelizwe yexesha elidlulileyo , iinkokheli maxa wambi zikhokelisa izigqibo ezizemidla yexeshana , emxinwa kwindleko ye-ajenda ebanzi , yexesha elide . Kuyimfuneko ukuba kuqhawulwe esi sangqa , neenkokheli ezizinikezeleyo nezinakho ukuthatha uxanduva olukhulu ekujonganeni nemingeni yoMzantsi Afrika . Ukumamela ngenene kuyenye yemiba ephambili yonxibelelwano . Abantu kufuneka bazive ukuba baviwe kwaye baqondiwe . Oku kufuna ukumamela ngenzondelelo . Ukumamela ngenzondelelo kuthetha ukuba ubona ihlabathi ngamehlo omnye umntu . Kukwaquka ukumamela ngokuzikisa ingqondo okupheleleyo nokuva uvakalelo emva kwamagama . Cela iqela ngalinye ukuba livume umbono omalunga nabahlali babo . Chaza ukuba ukuzoba umbono yinxalenye ebalulekileyo yokuphuhlisa isicwangciso sewadi njengoko umbono ' uliphupha ' loluntu . Lijonga apho uluntu lufuna ukuba khona kwixesha elizayo . Chaza ukuba lo msebenzi uthatha ixesha kwaye xa umntu esebenza ngabahlali ukuphuhlisa isicwangciso sewadi kufuneka afumene ixesha elaneleyo lokwenza njalo . Jonga inyathelo 1 ukuya kwelesi-3 uze ucacise ukuba la manyathelo anika umbhexeshi we-CBP umfanekiso wokuba ngoobani abahlali , xa kucingwa ukuba uluntu lwenziwe ngezakhiwo zentlalo ezahluka-hlukeneyo , amaqela ezoqoqosho njl . , ukufikelela kumbono omnye kuthatha ixesha , umonde nolawulo oluqaphelayo lweqela . Kwelinye icala , ungquzulwano lungakha umanyano phakathi kwamaqela ngokucacisa ukuthathana kakubi neenkolelo . Ingasisiseko sotshintsho kwaye lungakha unxulumano olutsha njengoko abantu beya kufumanisa bekwafunda ngonobangela wongquzulwano . Ngokwendalo yazo iiprojekthi zithatha umjikelo , kwaye zifuna ukusoloko zivandlakanywa zihlengahlengiswa , njengokuba ziqhutywa nje . Isigama esisetyenziswa kulawulo lweprojekthi sisenokuba nomahluko , ngokwabagunyaziswa abo baqhuba iprojekthi leyo . Ikomiti zeewadi zimele izimvo zabahlali kwiiprojekthi eziya kuthi zibachaphazele , kwaye kufuneka babandakanyeke kangangoko nabo kulo msebenzi . Iinkqubo zolawulo lweeprojekthi zinceda kakhulu kwiiprojekthi ezincinane , njengokuba zinceda nakwezinkulu . Ubuthunywa sisakhono esisisiseko sempumelelo yeBatho Pele nekufuneka bonke abaphathi nabasebenzi bayiqonde , kubaphathi ithetha ukuphathisa ngethemba igunya labo kwabanye ukuze basebenze ngokuzimeleyo engekho umphathi , kodwa uxanduva xa kukho iingxaki lubuyela kumphathi . Kumsebenzi ithetha ukugunyaziswa , ithuba lokusebenza ngokuzimeleyo , ukuphucula ukuzithemba nokunika amathuba okuphuhlisa isakhono somsebenzi . Iinkonzo zentlalo-ntle zoluntu kumele zandiswe , kunemfundo noqeqesho ngakumbi kubasebenzi boluntu nokuhlaziywa kwenkxaso-mali kwimibutho engenzi ngeniso . UKULANDELA NOKUGQITHISA INGXELO : Ukugxininisa kwiingxelo zarhoqo kwiiprojekthi zikamasipala neenkonzo kwiKomiti yeWadi nakwiintlanganiso zikawonke-wonke kwiiwadi zabo ukuze abahlali bahlale besazi ngenkqubela-phambili kunye / okanye iingxaki ezikhoyo . Iingcebiso ezakhayo zophuculo kufuneka zenziwe , nalapho kufanelekileyo , uluntu kwimimandla lungaqukwa ekusombululeni iingxaki . Ekucebiseni urhulumente namahlakani asekuhlaleni malunga nokumiliselwa kwesicwangciso . Ipesenti yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukamasipala oluchithwe kuzalisekiso lwesicwangciso salo sezakhono zasemsebenzini . Urhulumente ubeka umda weenqobo ezisesikweni kuluntu luphela . Ukuba urhwaphilizo lubonwa njengolwamkelekileyo kurhulumente , luya kubanempembelelo kwindlela uluntu oluziphatha ngayo . Oku kwenza kubaluleke ngakumbi ukuba urhulumente asebenze ukujongana namanqanaba aphezulu orhwaphilizo kwizikhundla zakhe . UMBUZO 1 Yintoni injongo yodliwano-ndlebe lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali ? Ukuqonda isini nokusebenzisa uphicotho lwesini olusisiseko zizixhobo ezibalulekileyo kwiiKomiti zeWadi ngokophuhliso . Akufanelanga de ube lidela kufa lesini elifuna ukusebenzela ukukhululwa nokulingana kwamakhosikazi ukuze usebenzise uphicotho . Wonke umntu osebenza kummandla wophuhliso loluntu ofuna ukuphucula ubomi babantu kufanele azi ukuba azisebenzise njani ezi zixhobo . Ngokuba amakhosikazi , ngakumbi kubudala obuphakathi kweminyaka eli-15 ukuya kwengama-24 , enengxaki enkulu yeHIV neAIDS , ingqalelo eyodwa kufuneka inikwe ukuqinisekisa ukuba iinkqubo neeprojekthi ezichongwe luluntu zikuthathela ingqalelo oku . Amacwecwe emiba ayanaba , kodwa kufuneka anike iinkcukacha ezaneleyo ukwenzela ukuba umasipala aqonde ukuba yeyiphi loo projekthi nokwenza isigqibo sokuba ikufanele na ukunikwa ingqalelo . Xa sele kumisiwe ukuba zeziphi iinkonzo ekufuneka zandisiwe okanye ziphuculwe , ukumiswa kwamaxesha acacileyo neethagethi kufuneka kuphuhlisiwe ukuze umasipala enze isigqibo esingcono sokufikelela kwiinjongo zakhe . Kufuneka aphinde enze isigqibo sokuba ngabaphi oovimba - abemali , izixhobo kunye nezakhono - eya kubafuna ukufikelela kwiinjongo zakhe . IiKomiti zeWadi zingabamba uvavanyo-zimvo lokungoneliseki ukubancedisa ukwenza umsebenzi wabo . Olu vavanyo-zimvo kufuneka lulawulwe ewadini ngamalungu eKomiti yeWadi phantsi kweliso likaceba nenkxaso yolawulo evela kumasipala . Uyilo lwengqesho olulungiswe yiKhomishoni lucebisa ukuba uninzi lwemisebenzi emitsha kungahle ivele kumashishini afumaneka ekhaya , nakwimizi-mveliso emincinci nephakathi esakhulayo . Logama uninzi lwemisebenzi ingadalwa ngokuthe ngqo kwimizi-mveliso ethumela kwamanye amazwe , amacandelo arhweba kumazwe ngamazwe athanda ukuba nobunakho obungaphaya ekuvuseleleni iimveliso ezivela kwicala lasekhaya . Ngenxa yesantya sokonga esisezantsi eMzantsi Afrika nemfuno yokutyala imali ngesantya esiphakamileyo , kubalulekile ukukhulisa okuthunyelwa kwamanye amazwe nokwandisa iinzuzo kulo macandelo . Imeko yorhwebo yaseMzantsi Afrika ayiphumezanga nayiphi kwezi njongo ngaphaya kweminyaka eli-15 edlulileyo . Ukwenza inkqubela-phambili kuya kuthetha ukuba kuqiniswe ukubakho kwelizwe kwihlabathi kwiingingqi ezinamathuba okhuphiswano , logama kusakhiwa izincedisi zophuhliso eziyimfuneko nezakhono . Ukuqinisekisa ukuba amalungu ebhunga kamasipala ayayazi imimandla yawo , bayayityelela rhoqo bekwamamela iingxaki neemfuno zoluntu kwimimandla . Udliwano-ndlebe olungacwangciselwanga ngokupheleleyo olwenziwa nabaniki beenkonzo abachongwe kwisazobe se-Venn . Amathuba athatha malunga neyure e-1 ukuya kwezi-1.5 . Ukuchongwa kwamanyathelo aphathekayo nanako ukwenzeka linyathelo elibalulekileyo lokwenziwa kwesicwangciso . Oku kunokubandakanya imisebenzi apho uluntu lubandakanyeka khona ngokungqalileyo ; okanye imisebenzi enokufumana inkxaso-mali kwiingxowa-mali ezikhutshwa ngokwengiqo kamasipala . Bhala igama ' ungquzulwano ' kwifliptshathi uze ucele abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bacinge igama lokuqala elifika engqondweni xa besiva eli gama ' ungquzulwano ' . Iimpendulo ezininzi ikakhulu ziya kuba yimeko engentlanga . Cacisa ukuba ungquzulwano alungomba ombi kuphela . Lungangumthundezi wenguqulelo luze lusenze sicinge ngesikukhethayo nendlela esikukhetha ngayo . Indlela esilawula ngayo ungquzulwano ngumceli-mngeni . Ukuzithemba okanye ingqondo evulekileyo - lo mntu wamkela izimvo ezintsha neengcebiso , umamela ngononophelo , akagwebi mntu , uyakwazi ukwenza izigqibo , uzithembile kwaye ubeka abantu endaweni efikelelekayo . Ukunika amalungu ekomiti iajenda phambi kwentlanganiso ukuze bakwazi okubandakanyeka kwintlanganiso baze bazilungiselele . Maxa wambi kunokufuneka ingxelo yohlobo olulodwa kummandla wepotfoliyo , ngoko ke xa umgcini-potfoliyo ekwazi oku , unokuzidibanisa nabahlali malunga nalo mbandela aze anike ingxelo evakalayo kwikomiti . Oomasipala bezixeko nabeengingqi mabaseke iikomiti zeewadi . Eyesibini , kukuqinisekisa ukuba abathathi-nxaxheba kwinkqubo ye-CBP banabameli kwiziganeko ze-IDP ngokusebenzisa amaqonga neenkqubo ezinikwa kwithuba langoku kwindlela yokusebenza ye-IDP equlethwe Kumqulu Wesikhokelo se-IDP , ngakumbi Kwiqonga Labameli be-IDP nakumaqela emisebenzi yeeprojekthi . Ukunikezela ingxelo kuluntu jikelele nolwazi nokucela uluntu jikelele kummandla ukuba luphose igalelo ngomnye wemisebenzi yelungu leKomiti yeWadi . Oku kungafuna ilungu leKomiti yeWadi libambe intlanganiso . Ukugqithisa ingxelo entlanganisweni ingangamava anzima , ingakumbi ukuba oku kukwafuna umgqithisi wolwazi ukuba asebenzise izixhobo ezinjenge-overhead projector okanye isandisi-sandi . Onke la masebe kufuneka ephuhlise ' izicwangciso zecandelo ' ; izicwangciso-nkqubo zomsebenzi eziqinisekisa unikezelo lwezibonelelo ezifanelekileyo zomsebenzi kamasipala neenkonzo ezigcinekileyo zikamasipala ngaphakathi kwicandelo . Ubuchule obubanzi buyafuneka ekuqwalaseleni uthungelwano phakathi kwamacandelo nokuqinisekisa ukuba adityanisiwe kwinkqubo yesicwangciso sisonke sikamasipala . Uhlaziyo lonyaka lomsebenzi : Ibhunga malisoloko linika ingxelo kwiiKomiti zeWadi nezabahlali ngohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwabo nangohlaziyo lomsebenzi wabo njengenxalenye yeentlanganiso zabahlali . Ukuba ikomiti yakho ayifumani rhoqo ingxelo yokusebenza evela kwibhunga , azisa usodolophu ukuba iiKomiti zeWadi zilindele ukusebenza okungcono okuvela kurhulumente wengingqi wedemokrasi . IBhodi yoLawulo lweMida kaMasipala sisiphatha-mandla esizimeleyo esiseka imida kamasipala . Idolophu ineshishini elincinci kakhulu ukuze abahlali abaninzi benze umsebenzi wokulima khona kufutshane edolophini . Inqanaba lentswela-ngqesho liphezulu kule dolophu . Kukho iifama ezintathu ezinobunini obudityanelweyo kanti abasebenzi basefama bafumana isabelo seenzuzo . Ingaba imisebenzi yenkqubo ibe negalelo kukuphuculwa kukufikelela kwamakhosikazi kwizibonelelo ( imfundo , uqeqesho , ukuvula amatyala , njl . ) ? Okwamadoda kona ? Isazobe esilandelayo sibonisa indlela ibakala ngalinye lolawulo lweprojekthi lubanga ngayo ukuhlola okubuyelelwayo kwamanyathelo nokuthi umjikelo uyajikela awulolandelelwano lweziganeko . Ukumela uluntu kumaqonga othethwano - iKomiti yeWadi kufuneka yazi yonke into malunga nemiba yoluntu kummandla kwaye iyivelise imiba enjalo kumaqonga othethwano . Uqoqosho lwamazwe amaninzi ase-Afrika lukhule ngokukhawulezileyo kwiminyaka elishumi edlulileyo , lunciphisa ngokubonakalayo ubuhlwempu obugqithisileyo okokuqala kwisiqingatha sekhulu leminyaka , kwaye ilizwekazi liqingqe ilizwe elikhulukazi kumaziko orhwebo lamazwe ngamazwe . Amaqela afunda imibuzo , ephawula imiba ephambili eveliswe kwiingxoxo zabo kwiphetshana lokushicilela iphephandaba . Ukufumana ubuncinane ama-20 000 MW wombane owenziwe mtsha ngowama-2030 , kusamkelwa umbane ovela kummandla , kungagunyaziswa i-11 000 MW kwizikhululo zombane wamalahle ezidala nokunyusa ukusebenza kotyalo-mali kumbane . Yiba buthathaka emntwini okanye iqela othetha nalo nesihloko othetha ngaso . Umzekelo , abanye abantu abaziva bekhululekile xa kuthethwa nge-HIV ne-Aids , intetho enjalo kufuneka ube buthathaka kuyo . Izalathisi zobungakanani zibhekiselela kumanani neepesenti zamakhosikazi namadoda okanye imibutho ebandakanyekayo okanye echatshazelwa lilo naliphi iqela okanye umsebenzi othile . Izalathiso zobungakanani zisebenzisa iinkqubo zedatha engahlulwanga ngesini neengxelo eziphononongwe ngethuba leenkqubo locwangciso lomgaqo-nkqubo okanye lweprojekthi . Ubukho bedatha esisiseko yobungakanani buthetha ukuba izalathisi zidla ngokuquka umba wokuseta into ekujoliswa kuyo . Umzekelo : Amakhosikazi enza enza ama-33% wamalungu ekomiti yamanzi ekupheleni koNyaka wesibini . Ngowe-2004 uphengululo lwabonisa ukuba uninzi loomasipala lwafumanisa ukuba i-Municipal Structures Act , 1998 ne-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 aziniki zinkcukacha zaneleyo ngendlela yokuseka iiKomiti zeeWadi . Iseti yezikhokelo yafakwa kwigazethi ngowama-24 June 2005 ( Government Gazette No . 27699 ) ukuncedisa oomasipala ngokubanika iinkcukacha ezithe chatha ngendlela emakwenziwe ngayo oku . Esi isigaba sibandakanya uqulunqo lwezisombululo zeengxaki eziphambili ezithe zafunyaniswa ; ngale ndlela ke ziye zibekwe iinkalo ezifanele kufikelelwa kule projekthi . Ukulawula inguqu kumhlaba omawunyathelwe , kwishedyuli nakwiindleko : Ukulawula inguqu kwiprojekthi le ngokubanzi . ' Ukunaba komhlaba ' kuxa kusenzeka iinguqulelwana ezincinane ezithi zibangele inguqu enkulu kumhlaba ebekucetywe ukuwunyathela , into ke leyo edla ngokukhokelela ekusileleni kweprojekthi . Kuyafuneka ukuba kuhlalwe kweziya zinto bezicetyiwe . Xa kuphela le seshoni yesiphumo ngasinye esibekwe ngokokubaluleka kuya kubakho iseti yeenkcukacha ezinxulunyanisiweyo eziya kusetyenziselwa ukwenza isicwangciso . Urhulumente wamakhaya ujongene nemingeni emininzi ezalanayo , kuquka nesikhundla esiphantsi , iinkqubo ezibuthathaka zolawulo , ukungenelela kopolitiko okungeyomfuneko ekuthathweni kwezigqibo zobugcisa nolawulo , isikhundla senzuzo esingalungelelananga . IKhomishoni ikholelwa ukuba phakathi kobume bomGaqo-siseko , kukho isithuba sokwabiwa kwamandla nemisebenzi okungafaniyo macala nakwiyantlukwano engakumbi emalunga nendlela ezifezekiswa ngayo izinto emazijongwe kuqala . Ukuphumeza oku , izicwangciso-qhinga zexesha elide ziyafuneka , kuquka nokujongwa kokunyanzelwa kwesikhundla , kuvunyelwa ukulinga ngakumbi kwiintlobo zamaziko nokusebenzisana norhulumente kazwelonke nowamaphondo . Namhlanje , malunga nomyinge we-17 ekhulwini wenani labemi boMzantsi Afrika liyakwazi ukufikelela kumnathazwe ( i-intanethi ) - inani elinyuka malunga nomyinge wama-20 ekhulwini ngonyaka . Ukusetyenziswa konxibelelwano lwedijithali kutshintshe uluntu ngeendlela ezingekaqondwa ngokupheleleyo okwangoku , kucacile , nangona kunjalo , ukuba abantsundu abasebatsha balamkele ijelo losasazo elitsha , kwaye oku kumela iindlela ezinokuba namandla zokukhuthaza ukubandakanywa kwasekuhlaleni . Thatha abathathi-nxaxheba kumjikelo wongquzulwano , usebenzisa amanqaku ngezifundo kwiSahluko 5 ukukuncedisa . Kwinqanam ngalinye , cela abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bacinge ngamava abo . UMnu . Mali uvela eSomalia kwaye uhlala kuWadi XYZ . Uyakhalaza kumasipala ngokusilela kokuhanjiswa kweenkonzo ngokumalunga nokususwa kwenkunkuma . Xa esiya kukhalaza uxelelwa ukuba akangommi woMzantsi Afrika kwaye akanalungelo lakukhalaza . Ekuqhubeni uphando kwimiba engundoqo enempembelelo kuphuhliso lwexesha elide . Wakuba ugqibile ngamanqaku esifundo kwiphepha lama-65 ukuya kwelama-67 bachazele ukuba kulo msebenzi baza kusebenzisa iinkcukacha eziqokelelwe kuhlalutyo ngempiliso ukuze kuqhutywe nge-SWOT yamaqela ezentlalo . Iiprojekthi aziyi kuzinanza izizathu ezingundoqo zokuba semngciphekweni , kuquka ukungalingani ngokwesini nangokwentlalo , kwaye imifuziselo esekiweyo yokungalingani ngokwesini nokungaphathwa ngokulinganayo iya kuhlala ingananzwa . Cela oo-A ukuba babuyele egumbini , bajoyine umahlulelane baze baqalise ukubalisa ibali labo . Umqondiso osekelwe kwingabula-zigcawu yomGaqo-siseko kumele uphuhliswe ze usetyenziswe kwiintlangano zesikolo . Ingabula-zigcawu kumele ixhonywe kuzo zonke iindawo zemisebenzi . Kwicala ngalinye lobomi , ukuqhubela phambili kwenziwe ekwakheni uluntu olubandakanyekayo , kutyhalelwa ngemva isithinzi sembali nokwenza banzi amathuba kuye wonke ubani . UMzantsi Afrika ukwazile ukwakha amaziko ayimfuneko esizwe sedemokhrasi nesinotshintsho . UmGaqo-siseko ufaka indlela esekelwe kumalungelo nokubanombono wedemokhrasi eyimpumelelo , engenamkhethe ngokobuhlanga nangesini neyeyabantu bayo bonke . Ukuphiliswa kwamanxeba elixa elidlulileyo nokulungiswa kokungalingani okwenziwe ngamakhulu eminyaka okubukulwa ngokobuhlanga zizinyanzeliso ezingomgaqo-siseko . Ukufikelela kwiinkonzo kunatyisiwe , uqoqosho luzinzisiwe noluntu olungenamkhethe ngokobuhlanga luyaqalisa ukubonakala . Izigidi ebezikade zicalucalulwa ziya kufikelela kwimfundo , amanzi , umbane , ukhathalelo lwempilo , izindlu nokhuseleko lwasekuhlaleni . Malunga nezigidi zabantu ezi-3 nangaphezulu ziyasebenza namhlanje xa kuthelekiswa nonyaka ka-1994 , umlinganiselo wobuhlwempu uhlile nemivuzo ephakathi ikhule ngokuthe chu kwimiqathango eyinene . Ulawulo lomngcipheko : Ukukhawulelana neenguqu kumngcipheko apha ekuhambeni kweprojekthi . Imingcipheko iza kuguquka okanye ikhawuleze ibonakale njengokuba ihamba nje iprojekthi . Isicwangciso solawulo lomngcipheko siya kufuna ukuba simana ukuhlaziywa njengokuba kusenzeka oku nje , kwaye imanejala yeprojekthi kuya kufuneka ukuba yazise bonke abachaphazelekayo ngoko . Ukufikeleleka - ngokufanayo amalungu asekuhlaleni asenokungazifumani lula izithuthi kwaye ukuba indawo yentlanganiso okanye yeseshoni yengxelo ayifikeleleki ababi nako ukuza kuba izithuthi zingaduru nexesha elichithwa endleleni eya kwindawo yentlanganiso lingabathintela ukuba beze entlanganisweni . Imigangatho yamalungiselelo ohlahlo lwabiwo-mali iboniswa kwisicwangciso esaziwa njengomjikelo wohlahlo lwabiwo-mali . Amalungu oluntu jikelele neeKomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziqonde ngalo mjikelo ukuze zikwazi ukuthatha inxaxheba enentsingiselo . Uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali oluthathu lusebenza ngaxeshanye kwibhunga likamasipala : uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lonyaka ophelileyo , uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwalo nyaka kunye nohlahlo lwabiwo-mali oluzayo lwexesha eliphakathi . Oku kwaziwa njengohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lulonke lonyaka ( multi-year budgeting ) . Bacele ukuba badwelise iziphumo ezithathu abazibeka phambili kwifliptshathi njengoko ziza kusetyenziswa kumsebenzi olandelayo . Imithetho ethile , umzekelo , i-National Land Transport Transition Act inyanzelisa amacandelo athile kumasebe ekubeni amanyanise iinkqubo zawo kwii-IDP ngexa eminye yemithetho yamacandelo ingaqwalaseli ngokukodwa lo mba . Akukho maqonga angaphakathi koorhulumente okanye imibutho ethe yayilwa ngeenjongo zenkqubo yohlelo ngokutsha lwe-IDP . Amaqonga eengxoxo akhoyo nachazwe ngasentla athi asetyenziswa . Ukwazisa iinkqubo zabasebenzi ezingoshishino ezisebenzayo neenkuthazo zokukhulisa ingqesho , ngokukodwa kubantu abatsha nakumacandelo aqesha abantu abanezakhono ezisezantsi kakhulu . Ukufuna ukuba novelwano asiyomeko yokufunda iimpendulo ' ezichanekileyo ' koko kukufunda ukubakho ngenene kuzo . Ukubakho kuthetha ingqwalaselo epheleleyo komnye umntu neengqiqo zabo , ukubeka bucala izimvo zakho , ukuba nento oyenzayo namava . Ukubakho yingqeqesho yokuzintlitha ngokuphilileyo . Aqinisekise ukuba amalungu oluntu kummandla ayaluqonda uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lokugqibela , i-SDBIP nezivumelwano zokusebenza . Indima yeKhomishoni yeNkonzo yoLuntu ekwenzeni izithethe nemigangatho esesikweni , nokulawula inkqubo yokugaya kumele yomelezwe . Kwenzeke ntoni xa ubuzama ukuhambisa iqabane lakho ulise apho ubume khona ? Zeziphi iinguquko zamaxesha athile ezisetyenziswa kwimithombo yobutyebi ( isazobe samaxesha athile sinokunceda apha ) ? Ukuya kutsho kwiminyaka yamva ku-1970 , i-Seymour yayisisithili esidume ngezolimo . Uqoqosho lwalusekelwe kwindawo enkulu yokusika amaplanga nokulungiswa kwecuba esizikithini sedolophu . Icuba , iitapile neziqhamo ezinjengee-orenji , iilamuni , bezityalelwa ukuthengiswa kummandla . Ungalubandakanya njani uluntu kwi-IDP ? Kukho iKomiti yeWadi esebenzayo kuluntu lwakho . Iintlanganiso zidla ngokubanjwa ngentsimbi yesi-6 ngorhatya phakathi evekini . Ngenxa yokuba amakhosikazi ngokwesithethe alindeleke ukuba ajonge abantwana kwaye alungiselele iintsapho zawo isidlo ngeliya xesha , amakhosikazi amaninzi awakwazi ukuya kuzo . Amanye amakhosikazi akwanexhala lokuhamba okanye lokukhwela iiteksi ezigodukayo emnyameni . Amanye akwakhalazela ukuba xa ethe akwazi ukuya kwiintlanganiso imiba nezikhalazo zawo azithathwa ngokungqongqo . Ngeli lixa amanye esithi agagana namaqabane awo angamadoda abalugcwabevu kwaye awaphatha gadalala ngokuba esiya ezintlanganisweni bengabikho emakhaya .
