Ngoku uthetha-thethwano malunga nokuphuculwa kwelokishi luyenzeka phakathi kweKomiti yeWadi norhulumente wengingqi . Amakhosikazi akhutshelwa ngaphandle . Afuna ukuqala iqumrhu lawo lamakhosikazi ngenxa yoku . Amadoda ayaliphikisa eli nyathelo , esithi amakhosikazi awadingi kuzihlanganela nanjengoko amadoda ekwazi kakuhle ukuphatha yonke imicimbi yoluntu . Ibhunga elinyuliweyo lilo ekugqibeleni eliliqonga lokwenza izigqibo kwii-IDP . Umsebenzi wedemokrasi yokuthatha inxaxheba kukwazisa , ukuthethathethana nokunika izimvo ngezo zigqibo ngelixa lenkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso / izigqibo . UMNQOPHISO KARHULUMENTE : KUKUYILA INKONZO KARHULUMENTE EBEKA ABANTU ESIZIKITHINI NENKONZO EQHUTYWA NGABANTU ELAWULWA BUBULUNGISA , UKULINGANA , UKUSEBENZA KWIXESHA ELIMISIWEYO KUNYE NENDLELA YOKUZIPHATHA EMSEBENZINI EYOMELELEYO , UKUBALASELA KOMBUTHO NONIKEZELO LWEENKONZO EZISEMGANGATHWENI . Ukuchithwa okungakumbi kotyalo-mali kuphela kwenyathelo lokuqala . UMzantsi Afrika nawo kufuneka uphucule ubulunga bale nkcitho ngokucwangciswa okungcono , izixokelelwano zokufumana ezivakalayo nokhuphiswano olukhulu kuqoqosho . Kukho imfuneko yempumelelo enkulu yenkcitho kuzo zonke iinkalo zikarhulumente , kuba isigubungelo jikelele kungahle sithande ukukhula ngokucothayo kakhulu kwixesha eliphakathi . Umgqaliselo owodwa kufuneka unikezelwe ekulawuleni umthetho oyilwayo karhulumente womvuzo , owenza ukuba ubutyebi bufikeleleke kwamanye amaqalela . Oku kuya kubandakanya ukulungelelanisa uxinezelelo olukhuphisanayo olufana nokwandiswa kwamanani abasebenzi , ngokubuyekeza ngokwanelisayo iingcali ezinezakhono nokuphucula ingxelo yenzuzo . Ingaba ibhunga lakho linayo i-PMS ? Nceda uyichaze . IiKomiti zeWadi zingabonisa ukunganeliseki ngokubhalela kusomlomo weofisi kamasipala ngokungasebenzi kukaceba . Ibhunga lingadlulisela uxanduva kwiiKomiti zeWadi . Icwecwe lemiba yeprojekthi malizaliswe ngeprojekthi nganye efuna inkxaso karhulumente , kwiiNGO okanye kwicandelo labucala . Eli cwecwe lemiba linika izizathu zobukho beprojekthi nganye efuna inkxaso kurhulumente , kwii-NGO okanye kwicandelo labucala . Eli cwecwe lemiba lichaza iprojekthi ngokunika iziqalelo zayo kwaye linoncedo kwinkqubela yokubekwa kweliso nokugcina abantu bekwazi ukuziphendulela ngamanyathelo abawathathayo . Phambi kwabo khokela ingxoxo ngeBatho Pele emsebenzini . Buza imibuzo elapha ngezantsi ubhale iimpendulo ephepheni . Ngokwesi sivumelwano , umboneleli wenkonzo uqalisa ukunikezela inkonzo ethile kamasipala egameni likamasipala kwixesha elithile elimisiweyo , uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali neethagethi . Umboneleli wenkonzo uya kuba noxanduva lokunikezela inkonzo kuluntu lulonke kummandla okanye icandelo elithile lommandla . Anganoxanduva lokunikezela inkonzo iyonke okanye umba othile wenkonzo . Umzekelo , umbutho osekelwe kuluntu kummandla ungenza isivumelwano sokuqokelela inkunkuma emizini nasezitalatweni , uyibeke kwiindawo ezithile apho iitrakhi zikamasipala ziya kuyilayisha khona . Ukuzinikela ekufumanekeni kwentengo yezinto kuluntu nabucala ngeendlela ezivuselela ishishini lasekhaya nokudala umsebenzi . Ukomeleza iiKomiti zeWadi ukuze zikwazi ukusebenzisana ngempumelelo enkulu ne-IDP njengesicwangciso esibanzi sikamasipala . Khumbula ukuba izigqibo zeKomiti yeWadi azibopheleli kuceba wewadi . IiKomiti zeWadi azinamagunya asemthethweni ngokwezigqibo zebhunga . Ke ngoko , iKomiti yeWadi kufuneka iphuhlise unxulumano olunentsebenziswano noceba luze lusebenzise amathuba achazwe ngasentla ukuqinisekisa ukuba ilizwi labahlali liyeviwa . UMgaqo-siseko ne-Municipal Structures ne-Municipal Systems Acts useka inkqubo-sikhokelo ngendlela amabhunga kamasipala ekufuneka egqithise ngayo imithetho eyilwayo . Indima ye-CDM ngokunxulumene nokudityaniswa kwe-HIV / AIDS koomasipala bengingqi . Iingcebiso kunye namaqela kumacandelo - umzekelo , imibutho yamafama ekufumaneni izimvo zayo kwizicwangciso zorhwebo olutsha . Okungaphaya kolawulo zezo zinto zangaphandle zinokuthi zibe nokuyichaphazela iprojekthi . Zizinto ezingaphaya kwamandla nolawulo lwethu , kwaye ke ziyakufuna ukuqwalaselwa , kuba zithe azahoywa zisenokuyenza ingabi nampumelelo iprojekthi . Umzekelo , ukuba ngaba uye wabekwa umhla wokwakha isiseko sesakhiwo , kuze ke kune iintsuku ezininzi , oko kwenza ulibaziseko lomsebenzi , kodwa ke akukho nto sinokuyenza . Ngoko ke , imigaqo elandelwayo kufuneka iquke izenzo nongenelelo kuyo yonke imigangatho ukuqinisekisa inguqu eyenziwe ngendlela emisiweyo , epheleleyo nelungelelaniswe ngobuchule . Ezi kufanele zibandakanye ungenelelo lwenguqu kumgangatho womntu , iqela , umbutho noluntu . Onke amalungu oluntu kummandla anelungelo lokuqwalasela intlanganiso eyodwa yebhunga xa kuxoxwa ngohlahlo lwabiwo-mali kukwavotwa ngalo . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziqinisekisa ukuba ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu jikelele kuyakhuthazwa ngokupapasha le ntlanganiso . Ukuhambela ngaphaya kweengcebiso nokuthatha inxaxheba kulwakhiwo olugcinekileyo loomahlulelane ngokuseka uthungelwano oluqhubekekayo nentsebenziswano kumanyathelo amatsha nabathathi-nxaxheba abahlukeneyo . Izalathiso iiKPI zineenjongo eziyinene , nezilinganisekayo nekuvunyelwene ngazo nabasebenzi ukuba ziza kuphunyezwa ngexesha elithile . Umsebenzi ngamnye kufuneka abe nekontrakthi yePMS nalapho iiKPI ziqukiwe , le kontrakthi ingasetyenziswa ukuba umsebenzi anike inkcazo yokungasebenzi ngokukhangela kwezi KPI . Ukuyilwa kwesicwangciso-nkqubo somgaqo-nkqubo we-HIV ne-AIDS nomgaqo-nkqubo wasemsebenzini . Isicwangciso-nkqubo sonxibelelwano - Oomasipala baphuhlisa izicwangciso-nkqubo ukuqinisekisa ukuba unxibelelwano luyagqithiswa kwisicwangciso-nkqubo luze ludityaniswe kwiinkqubo zikamasipala . Kumashumi eminyaka ezayo , njengokuba uqoqosho olusavelayo lusandisa isabelo salo kunaniselwano lwehlabathi notyalo-mali , ukuncipha okunxulumene nobu bunzima boqoqosho e-United States , eYurophu naseJapan kuya kuba neziphumo ezihamba noko kwifuthe lezopolitiko nomkhosi zawo . Oku kungakhokelela ekubumbaneni kwakhona kuzakuzo lwangaphesheya nobunzululwazi bokwakha bolawulo , kubonakalisa amaziko amatsha empembelelo . Isazobe kumaphepha alandelayo sibonisa indlela apho kumgangatho womntu , ungenelelo lolawulo lokungafani ekufuneka lujolise ngayo kwindlela iiyantlukwano zabantu ezichaphazela ngayo iingqiqo zethu , izimvo , iminqweno , iimfuno nesimilo esicacileyo . Oku kuya kusele kuhlola ukukwazi komntu ukuguqula iinkolelo , ukuqal'ugwebe , iingcinga ezisoloko zimi zakhe . Ungenelelo kufuneka lucwangciswe kumgangatho weqela ukwenzela ukunciphisa ukuqal'ugwebe neengcinga ezingenasiseko kwaye kuphawulwe imiqobo enokufunyanwa kwiinkcubeko , imigaqo-nkqubo , izixokelelwano nakwiinkqubo . Emva kwemizuzu emihlanu , misa ingxoxo . Ukungabi namagingxigingxi kubalulekile ukuze ufumane ukuthatha inxaxheba kube yimpumelelo . Abahlali bangafumaneka kuphela ngamaxesha athile kwaye izicwangciso kungadingeka ukuba zilungelelaniswe okanye ziguqulwe kuxhomekeke kwizidingo zabantu abachaphazelekayo kuloo mcimbi . Umz . Isicwangciso soMjikelo weShishini : ukucwangcisa ukhulisa ingeniso efunyanwayo yeempahla neenkonzo kwixesha elithile elinikiweyo . Ababhexeshi kufuneka baqinisekise ukuba abameli bamaqela azizisulu bayinxalenye yamaqela asebenzayo kwaye banelizwi kumaqela . Oomasipala mabaseke baze baphathe ulawulo olulolwabo , uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali nokwenza izicwangciso ukuze kubekwe phambili iimfuno zabahlali ezisisiseko . ICandelo 74a no-b le-Municipal Structures Act , 1998 licacisa imisebenzi namagunya eeKomiti zeWadi kunyanzeliso ngokutsha lweemfanelo zeeKomiti zeWadi kubahlali ekuthatheni imiba ethile egameni labo . IiKomiti zeWadi zingenza inzame eyodwa ukuqinisekisa ukuba amakhosikazi amelwe kwiintlanganiso zokunika ingxelo kwaye nezimvo zawo ziyafunyanwa kwaye ziyaqukwa kwingxelo phakathi koluntu nebhunga kunye noceba wewadi . Indlela yolawulo esulungekileyo kumele yamkelwe kwiingqesho ezikwinqanaba elisezantsi , namagosa aphezulu anikwe igunya elipheleleyo lokuqesha abasebenzi kumasebe abo . Intsebenziswano noceba wewadi - IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zakhe unxulumano olulungelelanisiweyo nolunentsebenziswano noceba wewadi njengoko ooceba bewadi bengamalungu ebhunga . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziseke inkqubo egunyazisiweyo apho zihlangana rhoqo noceba wewadi ukuze uceba ahlale esazi malunga nemiba yoluntu , kwiintlanganiso zeKomiti yeWadi , nangokuqinisekisa ukuba kubanjwa iintlanganiso zarhoqo ukuze uluntu jikelele luhlale lusazi malunga nemiba yebhunga . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziqinisekise ukuba intsebenziswano yarhoqo igciniwe noceba wewadi ukuze anikezele igalelo kulawulo lomsebenzi , uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali kunye neenkqubo zesicwangciso sophuhliso esimanyanisiweyo . Ngoku chazela abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bakuba bevumelene abahlali ngombono , kufuneka bavumelane ngeenjongo nangezicwangciso-buqili eziyilelwe injongo nganye . Jonga amanqaku ezifundo kwiphepha lama-44 nelama-45 . Oomasipala Boluhlu A ( okanye oomasipala abakhulu bezixeko ) : Ezi zizixeko ezikhulu , ezinogunyaziwe ongowazo kuphela wesigqeba nowowiso-mthetho kwimimandla yazo . Nangona kungekho nxulumano oluthe ngqo nesithethi , amalungu eKomit yeWadi analo uqhagamshelwano kwiintlanganiso zebhunga neziganeko ezithile . Chaza ukuba amaqela kufuneka acinge ngomasipala abamqhelileyo aze enze uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwalo masipala amcingayo . Ukusuka kulumano-ndlebe ukuya ekuxhotyisweni ngamandla kukhuthaza ubunini bophuhliso lweengingqi koyise uxhomekeko . Ulwakhiwo lwezikhundla kubantu abathatha inxaxheba kumaqonga abameli kwi-IDP ukuze basebenze ngenkuthalo kwinkqubo yocwangciso neyozalisekiso . Isixokelelwano sothungelwano lwamasebe karhulumente saseMzantsi Afrika sintsokothile , kodwa lo mngeni awusiso isizathu sokuzigwebela ekwenziweni mfiliba komkhondo woxanduva . Ukusekwa kweSebe lokuHlola nokuVavanya ukuSebenza linyathelo elilungileyo lokuqinisa ikhonkco lokunika ingxelo . IKhomishoni kananjalo ihlaba ikhwelo kubumbano lwabachaphazelekayo namashishini karhulumente nezivumelwano zokusebenza nabaphathiswa beKhabhinethi ukuba zidandalaziswe elubala . Ukuthintela - ukuthintela ungquzulwano yimpendulo eqhelekileyo kwaye ithemba lelokuba xa ungaluhoyi ungquzulwano , luya ' kuphela ' . Ukujongana nongquzulwano ngendlela eyakhayo kufuna izakhono , ukuziqonda nomdla ekuthatheni inxaxheba . Ukuphika yindlela eqhelekileyo yokuthintela ungquzulwano . Nangona singaziva ngathi siphendula ngokufanelekileyo , ukuthintela ungquzulwano kungabangela abantu bazive bekhathazekile , benomsindo , bebuhlungu bekwanengqumbo nenokwenza ungquzulwano luphinde luvele . Oku kungabangela imeko YOKUNGAWINI / YOKUNGAWINI kumaqela ewonke akhoyo kolu ngquzulwano . Cinga ngemva kangangoko kunokwenzeka kwaye ukhumbule isiganeko apho waqala ukuqaphela ukuba ukohluka kumakhwenkwe ukuba uyintombazana , nokohluka kumantombazana ukuba uyinkwenkwe , kwathetha ukuba wawulindelwe ukuba uziphathe ngokwahlukileyo kwaye wawuphathwa ngokwahlukileyo . Kufuneka ugxile kwiyantlukwano kwisimilo , hayi iyantlukwano yasemzimbeni . Yabelana neqabane lakho ngebali lakho . Urhulumente wengingqi kufuneka amise futhi athathe isigqibo sokuba uza kuyisebenzisa njani ingeniso nenkxaso-mali ayifumeneyo yokuhlawula iinkonzo neeprojekthi aceba ukuzizisa kubahlali . Oku kunzima ukukusa iso , ngaphandle kokuba uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali luphawulelwe imisebenzi ' ejongene namakhosikazi ' , ' ejongene namadoda ' okanye ' isini ' . UKUPHUCULWA KWENKONZO YOLUNTU NOKUNIKEZELWA KWEENKONZO KUYAQHUBEKA UKUBA NGUMCELI-MNGENI ODINGA UKUZINIKELA KWABO BONKE ABASEBENZA KWIINKONZO ZOLUNTU UKUBA BAZA KUJOLISA KUKO . BENGASEBENZELI UKUPHUMEZA IINJONGO ZIKARHULUMENTE KUPHELA KODWA BESANELISA IMINQWENO YAMALUNGU OLUNTU YOKUFIKELELA KWIINKONZO EZISEMGANGATHWENI NOBOMI OBUNGCONO KUBO BONKE . AKUKHO NTO INOKUSITHETHELELA XA SISILELA UKUPHENDULA KULE MINQWENO KUBA ISEMTHETHWENI KWAYE IPHAKAMILE . Njengoko imicimbi ephambili iqala ukuhluma , kusenokuba luncedo ukumema abaniki beenkonzo abanxulumene nezi ziphumo kumsebenzi wokwenza izicwangciso kusuku olulandelayo . Imizuzu yentlanganiso yebhunga isasaziwe kubahlali . Ukwakha indawo elungele ukunikezela iinkonzo - ku-1.2 sixoxe ngezalathisi zedemokrasi namalungelo abantu asisiseko . Amalungelo awami odwa kodwa eza noxanduva lwawo . Ukukhuthaza abahlali ukuba bathathe uxanduva ngemicimbi nemisebenzi ukuze amalungelo aqinisekiswe kuMgaqo-siseko nakuMthetho wamaLungelo adinga ukunonophelwa nokukhuthazwa . Umzekelo , ilungelo lokuhlala kwindawo ecocekileyo lubeleke uxanduva lokuba abahlali kufuneka bahlawule irhafu neenkonzo ukuze kunikezelwe iinkonzo . Isicwangciso kufuneka sinike uxanduva nemisebenzi kubantu ababodwa nokumisa ixesha lomsebenzi ngamnye . Ukuphonononga isibonelelo sezindlu nolawulo lwenkxaso ukuqinisekisa ukuba izixhobo ezisetyenzisiwe zithobela ukutshintsha okulungileyo kwinkqubo yokuhlaliswa koluntu . Ukuphucula ubulunga bemfundo kufuna ulawulo olunenkathalo , inkxaso kuwo onke amaqela anomdla nexesha . Ngokuphathelele kuphando lwangowama-2010 [ 1 ] lokuhlaziywa kwizixokelelwano zemfundo ezingama-20 ngokujikeleze ihlabathi , iindlela ezisezingqondweni ziqalisa ukuveza iziphumo malunga neminyaka emithandathu emva kokuba uhlaziyo luqalisiwe , nenzala egcinakalayo ivela emva kwexesha elide . Uludwe lokuqwalaselwa olungezatsi lunokunceda ekucwangciseni ingxoxo nommeli womniki wenkonzo njengoko ulwazi luya kwabelwa phakathi . Ingaba isicwangciso sisebenzisa ngokupheleleyo imibono , ubuchule nokukwazi ' kwamakhosikazi ' ' nokwamadoda ' ? Xa amanani alinganayo kungenzeki ukufikelela kuwo , qinisekisa ' umyinge wobungakanani ' wamakhosikazi namadoda ( okt. ubuncinane ama-30% ) . Lo msebenzi wenziwa liqela elincinci labahlali elinikwe uxanduva lokubhala isicwangciso esigqityezelwayo . Liqala ngeveki yokwenza isicwangciso lizame ukugqiba kwiveki elandelayo . Udliwano-ndlebe noluntu jikelele luye lubanjwe malunga nomba othile . Umzekelo , udliwano-ndlebe lokufumana igalelo kumthetho ocetywayo . Oku kuthetha ukuba iKomiti yeWadi lijelolonxibelelwano elinokusetyenziswa ngabahlali ukufaka izikhalazo okanye ekuveliseni iimfuno ezithile . IiKomiti zeWadi zinemfanelo kuluntu jikelele yokuthatha ezi zikhalazo zizigqithisele kwibhunga ngendlela efanelekileyo . IiKomiti zeWadi azinakuphazamisa ukusebenza kwebhunga . Oku kuquka ukunganikezeli imiyalelo kumagosa anomsebenzi wokwenza izigqibo zomgaqo-nkqubo webhunga . Kodwa ke , zinendima ebalulekileyo ekufuneka ziyidlalile njengothungelwano phakathi kwabahlali nebhunga . Qinisekisa ukuba iqela liyawuqonda umahluko phakathi ' kokubaluleka ' ' nokufikeleleka ' . La magama anokuguqulelwa kulwimi lwengingqi . I-GEP inamancedo aliqela okuXhasa ukuCwangcisa awokukunceda ukuqulunqa izikhokelo zokulawula ishishini lakho nokuqaphela izinto ezisilelayo ezinokufuna kuthathwe inyathelo . Musa ukubeka phambili ezakho izimvo . Linda ukuva ukuba abanye abantu bacinga ntoni na , uze ke uphose eyakho imbono . Oomasipala benza ukuba kubekho isixa esincinci seengxowa-mali ezikhoyo zokuxhasa ukufuzekiswa kwangoko kwesicwangciso sewadi ukuze amandla avela kwinkqubo yokwenziwa kwesicwangciso ingalahleki . Izigqibo malunga nokubuyiswa kwezi ngxowa-mali kufuneka zivele kwinkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso , inkqubo yokukhetha abasebenzi mayingafihlisi nto kwaye abahlali mabafumane ingxelo ebuyiswayo . Umsebenzi olandelayo uchaza indlela yokuphuhlisa uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwezi ngxowa-mali zewadi . Ibhunga likamasipala linokuyichitha ikomiti yeWadi xa isilela ekuzuzeni iinjongo zayo . Esi sahluko sigqabaze ngeenjongo nangemithetho-siseko yesicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali saza saqwalasela uhlobo le ndlela iqulethwe ngayo kumgaqo-nkqubo wophuhliso lukarhulumente weengingqi . I-CBP yinxalenye engundoqo yophuhliso lwamaqela abahlali , enyusa umgangatho weenkonzo neyenza ukuba imigaqo-nkqubo ephawulwe kuwiso-mthetho lukarhulumente weengingqi ikwazi ukwenzeka kananjalo nokwenza uMgaqo-siseko ube yinto yenene kubemi . Izahluko ezithathu ezilandelayo ziya kunika izakhono zobuchule ezisebenzisekayo zokusebenzisa i-CBP . Isakhono sonxibelelwano sinokuphucula indlela amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi asebenza ngayo namalungu ebhunga , amagosa aseburhulumenteni naphakathi kwawo . Iziganeko ezininzi zongquzulwano zinokuthinteleka kwaye zisombululeke lula xa kunokuphuculwa unxibelelwano . Ukusombulula iingxaki - le yeyona nkqubo ecela umngeni kuxolelwaniso njengoko kukulo mgangatho apho kuvunyelwana ngesigqibo . Umxolelanisi uncedisa amaqela ekubonisaneni ngokuvakalisa izimvo zezisombululo ezinokubakho , ebeka phambili iingcebiso ekwafumana isivumelwano esifanelekileyo kuwo onke amaqela . Umxolelanisi angafuna ukusebenzisa ubuchule obohlukeneyo bokwenza amaqela ukuba avumelane . Oku kungaquka ukuvumela amaqela ukuba agqugule , ukusebenza neqela elinye , nelinye kwakhona , ukudibanisa amaqela nokuyila isivumelwano esonelisayo kumaqela ewonke . Kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukuba ilungu ngalinye kwiqela leprojekthi likuqonda kakuhle abafanele ukukwenza , nokuba linxibelelana njani na nemisebenzi yabanye . Umzekelo , ukuba ngaba umntu onoxanduva lokukhangela indawo eza kuqhutyelwa kuyo inkomfa akakawuqoshelisi umba womhla eya kufumaneka ngawo indawo leyo , lo unoxanduva lokwenza amalungiselelo okuhamba akasoze akwazi ukuba nazo iinkcukacha eziyimfuneko ekulungiselelweni kwabameli abahamba ngeenqwelomoya okanye ekuthengweni kwamatikiti ebhasi . Ezinye iimali-mboleko zangaphandle zifunyaniswa kurhwebo lwekapitali olunjengeebhanki zorhwebo . Oomasipala abaninzi abanakhredithi , nokwenza oko kube nzima kubo ukuboleka imali . Urhulumente kusafuneka ukuba afumane iindlela zokusombulula ezi ngxaki . Uphicotho lwesini sisixhobo esiluncedo kuba lucima imibono emi imi , lutyhila iindima ezidla ngokungananzwa , lunceda ukuqinisekisa ukumelwa kokungafani kulawulo lokusingqongileyo , kwaye luchonga imibutho yasekuhlaleni exhasa uluntu . Khumbula kubalulekile ukudlan ' indlebe nabaniki beenkonzo ukuze beve izimvo zabo ngemibandela echaphazela abahlali neenkonzo zabo ukuze bakwazi ukuba nenkxaso kwaye babe negalelo njengabahlali . Umsebenzi welungu lebhunga kukuqinisekisa ukuba iinkonzo ezisisiseko ziyanikwa kanti nophuhliso luyakhuthazwa kwimimandla eliyimeleyo . Amalungu ebhunga , ekunye namagosa aseburhulumenteni , kufuneka eqinisekise ukuba yanele imali yokunika iinkonzo kananjalo akhuthaze uphuhliso olucwangcisiweyo . Ukuhlasela - isithethi esihlaselayo sikholelwa ekubeni ' Ilungile lento ndiyithethayo ' , akacingi ngokufanelekileyo , ungummameli ongekho ntweni , yonke into uyithathela kuye , uzenza umphathi , uyafundekela , unezisongelo , akanamonde . Uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali olunganonophelwanga okanye olungaqwalaselwanga nemali esetyenziswa ngokungakhathali kungekho mali eveliswayo kungabangela ukuphelelwa zimali kukamasipala . Sebenzisa umsebenzi wefowuni eyaphukileyo njengendlela yolonwabo yokubonisa indlela ekulula ngayo ukuba umyalezo ugqithiswe seyingasenguwo nomonakalo owenziwa koku njengoko kubanga amarhe kudale nezikrokro . Iingxelo zohlahlo-mali kufuneka zenziwe ngeli xesha lokwenziwa kweengxelo zokubekwa kweliso , ukuhlaziya nokuvandlakanya . Zinika umfanekiso wokuba ngaba iprojekthi le ihleli kangakanani na kolo hlahlo-mali bekuvunyelwene ngalo nowokuba ngaba ikhona na imfuneko yokuba kubekho amanyathelo athathwayo okubuyisela izinto kwisimo esifanelekileyo . Bobuphi ubuchule obusetyenziswe libhunga , bobuphi obusetyenziwe luluntu ? Enyanisweni khona ishedyuli yezibonelelo luhlahlo-mali . Kubaluleke kakhulu ukwenziwa kohlahlo-mali , njengoko ukuwa nokuphumelela kweprojekthi kuxhomekeke kulo . Ukuba lwenziwe luncinane uhlahlo-mali , oko kungathetha ukuba eminye imisebenzi akusoze kukwazeke ukuyenza . Ukuba iindleko zithe zaqikelelelwa phezulu kakhulu , kusenokuthi kube nzima ukufumana inkxaso-mali yeprojekthi leyo . Ngoku lixesha lokujonga ezona ngxaki nezona zithintelo ziphambili kule meko kuyiyo , ukuba zibangwa yintoni kwaye zinafuthe lini kweminye imiba . Amava oMzantsi Afrika kurhwebo lwamazwe ngamazwe aquka iinzuzo ezibambekayo nobunzulu obandayo . Umngeni kukuthatha amathuba enzuzo logama kukhuselwa abemi boMzantsi Afrika - ingakumbi abahlelelekileyo - kumngcipheko owayanyaniswa norhwebo olutsha neepatheni zotyalo-mali . Ngokomzekelo , uMzantsi Afrika unezinga elisezantsi lokonga kwaye uxhomekeke kwiimali zamazwe angaphandle ukuhlawulela utyalo-mali lwawo . Ukuxhomekeka kuqukuqelo lwemali lwenkunzi yamazwe angaphandle kwandisa umngcipheko wobutshaphatshapha kuqoqosho lwasekhaya . Ukukhula okucothayo kumazwe aphuhlileyo kukhatshwe sisinyanzeliso esimandla esisuka kumazwe asahlumayo , okunegalelo kulungelelaniso kwakhona olwamkelekileyo kwizinto ezithunyelwa ngaphandle zelizwe . Kodwa le ntsingiselo nayo ikwavelisa umngeni kubenzi benkqubo nabavelisi bezinto , ngenxa yokuba isinyanzeliso esikhoyo esisuka kwezoshishino ezivelayo zilinganiswa ngokubhekisele kwiimpahla zorhwebo nezinto ezingekasetyenzwa , kunebhaskithi yeemveliso ezahlukeneyo ngakumbi efunwayo ngamazwe aphuhlileyo . Umba onokuxabanisa kukuba ingaba uMzantsi Afrika ungagayela abantu abangaqeshwanga kwimveliso yoshishino oluthumela kwamanye amazwe . Abanye baxoxa besithi uqoqosho alunakhuphiswano kwimisebenzi eyenza izinto ngamandla ngokuba ubume bendleko buphakame kakhulu , isantya sotshintshiselwano sintshaphantshapha kakhulu , amaziko awanelanga nesiseko sezakhono sinyiniwe / sinciphile . Kodwa uMzantsi Afrika ungakhuphisana kwizintlu ezahlukeneyo ukuba la maxhala ajongwe - kwinxenye enkulu , angajongwa . Isantya sotshintshiselwano esintshaphantshapha sidala umqobo kwimpumelelo kwaye isicwangciso sicebisa ukuba ukusombulula iindleko zemithombo yasekhaya nokubakho kwezakhono kuya kuba nefuthe eligcinakala ngakumbi kwiindleko . Njengelizwe elinengeniso ephakathi , uMzantsi Afrika kumele ukuba ukhuphisane kwisiseko seemveliso neentlobo ezigqwesileyo , nongenelo olusebenzayo kumajelo osasazo-zimpahla kumazwe ngamazwe . . . Oku kuya kufuna ukuzinikela okukhulu kuphando nophuhliso nempembelelo yezorhwebo , iqonga elisebenzayo lolungiselelo lwenkxaso nengqiqo esebenzayo kwezoqoqosho . Inkqubo yokugaywa kwabathweswe izidanga nesicwangciso-qhinga sikarhulumente wasekhaya sokuphuhlisa izakhono kumele saziswe ukutsala umdla wabagqatswa abanobulunga obuphezulu . Ukuphuhlisa , ngendlela yexesha , izikimu ezininzi zamanzi ezintsha zokubonelela amaziko edolophu nawoshishino , izixokelelwano ezitsha zonkcenkcesho kwizibuko lomlambo u-Umzimvubu neMakatini Flats , nenkqubo kazwelonke yolondolozo lwamanzi ukuphucula ukusetyenziswa kwamanzi nokusebenza kwayo . Ngonyaka ka-1992 , imibutho yoluntu kule dolophu yaseka iforam yophuhliso lwe-Seymour esekelwe kuluntu kummandla . Yayiquka i-SANCO ( i-South African National Civics Organisation ) , i-ANC ( ukuquka ne-Youth League , ne-Women's League ) namaqela ootitshala . Imbono yeforam yayi kukuphuhlisa isicwangciso-nkqubo sophuhliso olubanzi olwalunenjongo yokuba yinzuzo kubahlali bebonke bedolophu nokomeleza uqoqosho lwengingqi . Kuya kunqongophala ithuba lokuthatha inxaxheba nobunkokeli bamakhosikazi . Izicwangciso-qhinga aziyi kugxila kukuxhotyiswa kwamakhosikazi , njengophuhliso lweenkonzo zezentlalo , iinkqubo zenkxaso yabantwana , amaziko amakhosikazi , nezinye iindawo ezikhuselekileyo . Ukumamela ngogqaliselo kufuna uvakalelo olunzulu olubandakanya ukumamela ngenjongo : ukuzuza ulwazi , ukusombulula iingxaki , ukwabelana ngemidla . Linda umntu agqibe into ayithethayo . Musa ukungenelela kuba ufuna ukubeka olwakho uluvo . Chaza ukuba inkqubo ye-CBP ifuna uphuhliso lwesicwangciso sewadi njengoko isicwangciso sewadi isisixhobo esiqinisekisa ukuba iimbono zabemi nezinto ezibekwe phambili ziyabandakanywa kwi-IDP . Bhala phantsi imiba ephambili kumakhadi amancinci okanye kwincwadi yamanqaku ukuze umane uwajonga . Nangona kukho ukulungelelana kwamanani , iimbumba ezininzi zaseMzantsi Afrika azityali mali ngokuba uqoqosho lwehlabathi luhleli lubuthathaka . Amashishini nawo anenkxalabo malunga neenguqulelo kwinkqubo nobume bowiso-mthetho obunganyusa iindleko . Kobunye ububanzi , utyalo-mali olusezantsi lukwasisiphumo samaziko anganelanga abonelelwa ngamashishini karhulumente . UMzantsi Afrika kufuneka uqhawule esi sangqa sokukhula okusezantsi notyalo-mali olusezantsi . Urhulumente unendima ebalulekileyo ekufuneka ayidlale ekwakheni ukuthembeka nokuzithemba ekukhuthazeni utyalo-mali lwexesha elide . Amashishini nawo anendima ekufuneka eyidlalile - ukuba wonke ubani utyala ngakumbi , iinzuzo zoqoqosho ziya kongezeleka kwisebe labucala . ESI SAHLUKO SIQWALASELA ABATHATHI-NXAXHEBA ABAHLUKENEYO nonxulumano lwabo kwimisebenzi yeeKomiti zeWadi . Sikwaqwalasela ubuchule bokubhexesha okufanelekileyo okunokunceda iiKomiti zeWadi ekusebenzisaneni nala maqela achaphazelekayo . Yabela isibini ngasinye umthetho-siseko ( kusenokufuneka ukuba unike umthetho-siseko ofanayo kwizibini ezingaphezu kwesinye oko kuya kuxhomekeka kwinani labathabathi-nxaxheba onabo ) uze uqwalasele indlela abaya kusebenzisa ngayo umthetho-siseko phakathi koluntu lwabo . Sisakuba sigqityiwe esi isigaba , kufuneka ke ngoku iprojekthi ichazwe ngokupheleleyo . Iindleko , uxanduva , izinto eziphambili ngokubaluleka neeshedyuli ziyaqondwa kwaye onke amaqela achaphazelekayo kufuneka aqonde ukuba impumelelo iza kungqinisiswa njani na nokuba ubungqina buza kuqokelelwa njani na . Indima yeKhomishoni eCwangcisayo kaZwelonke kukucebisa urhulumente nelizwe ngemiba echaphazela uphuhliso lwexesha elide lwelizwe . Esi sisicwangciso selizwe liphela , kwaye amacandelo onke oluntu kumele athathe uxanduva lokusenza sibe yinene . Ukufezekisa isicwangciso ngempumelelo , iKhomishoni ichonge uthotho lwezinto zempumelelo ezingundoqo . Buyela kumbuzo ngamnye uze uqwalasele ngokufutshane ukuba ingaba iKomiti yeWadi yakho inokungalingani na phakathi kwamaqela enkolo , amaqela enkcubeko , okanye amanye amaqela ? Intsebenziswano - abahlali banikwa ulwazi ngeprojekthi okanye umba baze bacelwe ukuba baphawule . Bangaphawula ngokunikwa uvavanyo-zimvo olwenziwa libhunga okanye bazibandakanye kwiprojekthi okanye kwintlanganiso yoluntu ukunika nje umzekelo . Impendulo : Amalungu ebhunga atshixe emnyango akubona inginginya yabantu isiza , aphuma kumnyango ongasemva emka . Kuza kunceda iiKomiti zeWadi ukuzalisekisa uxanduva lwabo lokwenza ikhonkco phakathi kwabahlali nebhunga noceba wewadi ukuba banesakhelo sokuthatha inxaxheba . UKWENZELA UKUQINISEKISA UPHUHLISO OLUGCINAKALAYO , kuyimfuneko ukunakana ukubaluleka kwamasondo omabini njengezinto zebhayoloji ezichaseneyo . Kukwabalulekile ukuhlonipha ukuphathwa ngokulinganayo nokulingana okupheleleyo kweendima zokuhlala ezidlalwa ngamadoda namakhosikazi ebomini babo . Indlela amadoda namakhosikazi ajongwa naphathwa ngayo ekuhlaleni yenye yamatye embombo ayo nayiphi inkqubo yopolitiko , yentlalo neyoqoqosho . Kwangeli xesha linye indlela esetyenziswa ngayo ikwayenye yemiba ebhengeza kakhulu . Esi sahluko siphicotha iinzuzo zokudibanisa imithetho-siseko yesini nokuphathwa ngokulinganayo kwiiprojekthi zophuhliso . Isahluko sivala ngengxoxo yemingeni ejongene noMzantsi Afrika ukuba umbono ophathelele nesini awuqhutywa ngokusebenzayo . Ukujolisa kukhathalelo lwempilo yoomama neentsana . Inkqubo egunyazisiweyo apho iqela elingelinye elingakhethi cala lithi lincedise ngokwenkqubo ekuphuculeni uqhagamshelwano phakathi kwamaqela , ngokuqhelekileyo kwisiseko sentlanganiso . Oku kwenziwa ngokufuna isiqulatho , ukwandisa ukutshintshiselana ngolwazi nokuncedisa nokukhokela inkqubo ukuze umsebenzi othile ugqitywe ngaphandle kobunzima . Abathathi-nxaxheba basebenza ngezibini bafunde imithetho-siseko ephambili ngendlela yokusebenza ngeempiliso ezilondolozekayo . Ikomiti yesigqeba esilawulayo okanye ikomiti kasodolophu ufumana izindululo ezisuka kwiiKomiti zepotfoliyo nabalawuli bebhunga nabaya kugqithisa i-ajenda yebhunga . Zeziphi iziganeko ezikhulu okanye izimbo zokuphila ezenzeke kuluntu lwethu kwiminyaka engama-30 ukuya kwengama-50 edlulileyo ( phambi kokuba kwenzeke iinguquko ezinkulu ) ? Ukulawula umgangatho : Ukubeka iliso kwiziphumo ezithile zeprojekthi ngeenjongo zokukhangela ukuba ngaba ziyahambelana na nomgangatho ofanelekileyo , ukukhangela nokusebenzisa iindlela zokususa konke okubangela ukungahambi ngokwanelisayo komsebenzi . Indlela esekelwe kwisithili kukhathalelo lwempilo lokuqala iyinxalenye yesigaba sokulingwa kwe-inshorensi yempilo kazwelonke . Ukuze oku kubenempumelelo , isixokelelwano sempilo sifuna abasebenzi ngakumbi ( kuquka iingcali nabasebenza kwii-ambulensi ) , iindlela ezintsha zegunya lolawulo , nokomelezwa kobume obumiswe ngokomthetho ekumeleni uluntu . Ikomiti yeWadi nganye kufuneka yenze isigqibo ngeentlobo zeekomiti ezonganyelweyo nangezikhundla efuna ukuba nazo ewadini yayo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi abelwa izikhundla ezithile . UMzantsi Afrika kufuneka ufezekise izinto emazijongwe kuqala ngokwenkqubo yezoqoqosho ngokuyimpumelelo . Ukusilela koququzelelo , ukunika ingxelo okwahlukeneyo nemiyalelo eyelelanayo zingumqobo ekufezekisweni kweenkqubo ezikhoyo . Ingxoxo namaqela kunye neqela lezicwangciso , iKomiti yeWadi okanye amaqela asebenzayo axoxe ngamacwecwe aphuhliswayo emiba yeprojekthi efuna inkxaso yangaphandle . Ukuthobela yonke into - isithethi esithobela yonke into sihlala sivumelana nomntu wonke , asikwazi kwenza zigqibo , sithethela phantsi , ucinga ukuba akakwazi kwenza msebenzi okanye akakwazi ukuphikisana nawuphina umntu nokuba unyanisile . Uhlobo lokusebenza lwe-CBP lunika oomasipala indlela yokomeleza imiba yenxaxheba ye-IDP yabo . Ngale ndlela i-CBP incedisa oomasipala ukuba ngokunika ifuthe lamandla kwiimfuneko ezikwiPhepha Lengcaciso-nkqubo nakwi-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 . Bafune ngokusebenzayo amathuba okubhekela phambili , okufunda , amava namathuba . Ukungazinzi kwenkqubo lixhala . Logama kukho iimeko apho inkqubo kumele itshintshe , urhulumente maxa wambi uthelekelela ngaphantsi impembelelo ephazamisayo kulungiso lwenkqubo olumandla . Ulungelelwano kufuneka lwenziwe kwaye okwangoku olo lungelelwano lunyamalele . Yenza isicwangciso sokuhamba endaweni engagudanga ebandakanya imiba yezithuba ephambili kwindawo leyo . Njengoko nihamba , qaphelani iimpawu ezicacileyo apho zikhoyo khona . Kuluncedo ukuthatha ezi nkcukacha zibekwe kumfanekiso wolandelelwano obonisa naziphi iimpawu ngokwelizwe okanye imibandela yophuhliso kwizowuni nganye ngokwenza njalo kunikwe imo ekubhekiselelwe kuyo yewadi njengomzekelo ongezantsi okubonisa oko . Sebenzisa uludwe lokuqwalasela imo eningqongileyo ukuqinisekisa ukuba yonke imiba ibandakanyiwe . Umahlulelane kwinkonzo kamasipala ( MSP ) sisivumelwano phakathi kukamasipala nomnikezeli wenkonzo . Umnikezeli wenkonzo ingasesinye isiphatha-mandla sikarhulumente ( esinjengebhodi yamanzi okanye umasipala wesithili ) , inkampani yabucala , umbutho ongekho phantsi kukarhulumente ( NGO ) okanye umbutho osekelwe kuluntu kummandla ( CBO ) . Umsebenzi 1 Khetha iqela lasekuhlaleni kuluntu lwenu eninolwazi ngalo - umzekelo , amafama , abahlali basematyotyombeni , abanini bamashishini amancinci , njl . Uwiso-mthetho lubonelela ngeendlela ezininzi zokuthatha inxaxheba kwabemi kulawulo emva konyulo . Amaqumrhu afana namaqela alawula isikolo , iikomiti zengingqi , amaqumrhu ogcino-cwangco kuluntu neekomiti zeekliniki abonelela ngelizwi kubemi namathuba okubumba amaziko asondele kakhulu kubo . Uluntu lungathatha inxaxheba ekuyileni izicwangciso zikarhulumente wasekhaya . Nangona kukho ezi ndlela , kukho umsantsa okhulayo phakathi kwabemi norhulumente . Ukuqhambuka kodushe kuqhankqalazo loluntu kubonisa udano hayi kwisantya sokubonelela ngeenkonzo kuphela , kodwa ikwangamaxhala okuba uluntu alumanyelwa ngokunyanisekileyo . Yahlula abathathi-nxaxheba babe ngamaqela amathandathu lize iqela ngalinye likhethe inqanam elinye le-IDP lize lixoxe ngalo ukuquka nenqanam lamalungiselelo . Abathabathi-nxaxheba babelana ngezinto abaziqwalaselayo malunga neqela liphelele . IiKomiti zeWadi aziloqumrhu lisesikweni likarhulumente nelinamagunya . Ziikomiti ezicebisayo ezenziwe ngabantu abawaziyo kakuhle ummandla nabangamnceda uceba ukuba athethane kakuhle , anike ingxelo azise nabantu aze enze izigqibo ezingcono kwibhunga . Ooceba bewadi abanaxanduva lusemthethweni ngakwikomiti yewadi - banoxanduva kwibhunga , inxalenye yalo nakubahlali . Kuya kufuneka isicwangciso samaxesha esinzulu esinika iinkcukacha zesiganeko ngasinye , sixele inani leentsuku , ( sibe sixelwe kwinyanga yesicwangciso samaxesha jikelele ) umsebenzi ngamnye ekufuneka wenziwe phantsi kweso siganeko , inqanaba lokubaluleka lwaloo msetyenzana , nokuba kufuneka ufumane bani oya kwenza loo msetyenzana . Usihlalo uvula intlanganiso aze afunde iajenda umba emva komnye . Ukuqukwa kwe-HIV ne-AIDS kwi-IDP . Iziphumo zempilo zexesha elide zibunjwe zizinto ubukhulu bazo obungaphandle kwesixokelelwano sempilo : indlela yokuphila , idayethi namazinga esondlo , imfundo , ukuziphatha ngokwesondo , umthambo , iingozi zezendlela nenqanaba lobundlobongela . IKhomishoni yenza iingcebiso kwinkalo nganye kwezi . Iinkalo ezingamaqalela ziquka ukufundiswa ngesondo , isondlo , umthambo , nokulwa ukutshaya nokusetyenziswa gwenxa kotywala . Ezi , luxanduva olulungele ukuba luthathelwe ingqalelo ngummi ngamnye , nokuphakanyiswa ziintsapho namaziko . Ukunikwa kweenkonzo kuxhomekeke kubaqeshwa nezixokelelwano zikamasipala ezisebenza ngokuncomekayo nangenkuthalo . Ukunikwa kweenkonzo okusilelayo kukholisa ukubangwa kukungalawulwa kakuhle nangumgangatho ophantsi wokusebenza . Isixokelelwano solawulo lomgangatho wokusebenza sityhila iinjongo nezinto ekujoliswe kuzo ngokuphandle ukuze abo bachaphazeleka ngokwegunya noluntu lukarhulumente balandele ngoqwalaselo lula inkqubela-phambili kananjalo bachonge neengxaki . Nangona inkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso indululwa kwaye iququzelelwa ngumasipala , ukuze isebenze , iwadi ngokwayo kufuneka ibe ngumnini wesicwangciso , imelwe yiKomiti yeWadi . Oomasipala baxhobisa amalungu ebhunga lewadi neekomiti ngamandla okuncedisa kwimpumezo yenkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso ' aya kwenza ukuba ikomiti nganye iyile ugunyaziso ngethuba layo lokubamba isikhundla ' . Umjikelo we-IDP waqalisa kwiLekgotla yeKhabhinethi yeSizwe nakwiMakgotla Exco Yephondo ezibanjwa ekuqaleni konyaka ngamnye . Ezi ntlanganiso ziphuhlisa Inkqubo Yamanyathelo ( Programme of Action - PoA ) onyaka nemibandela ebanzi yethuba eliphakathi . Ezi ziganeko zilandelwa Yinkcazo kaMongameli Yentetho Yesizwe , Inkcazo Yeentetho Zamaphondo nentetho yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali . Kuthatha ixesha elingakanani phambi kokuba amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi aneliseke kwindima yawo ? Uya kujongeka njani uMzantsi Afrika ngowama-2030 ? Ilizwe lifikelele kwinqanaba kwinguquko yalo yokufundwa kwamanani abantu abaphilayo nabangasaphiliyo apho amazinga okuzala esihla nenani labemi lizinza . Le nguquko ineempembelelo ezinzulu kubume benani labemi , isantya sokukhula kweqela labasebenzi , nebango leenkonzo ezifana nemfundo nempilo . I-Eastern Cape AIDSCouncil ( ECAC ) iya kuxhasa ukuqeshwa komlungelelanisi we-HIV / AIDS . Izalathisi zobulunga zibaluleke kakhulu . Akwanelanga ukukwazi ukuba amakhosikazi athatha inxaxheba kumsebenzi : ubulunga bokuthatha kwawo inxaxheba namava , nokuba kukwiintlanganiso zasekuhlaleni , kwiiklasi zesikolo samabanga aphantsi okanye njengabasebenzisi beenkonzo zoluntu , kubalulekile konke . Abantu abaninzi badla ngokucinga ukuba ukungafani kubhekiselela kwiiyantlukwano ezikhoyo kubantu bemvelaphi yamasiko ahlukeneyo . Abantu bakwanxulumanisa ukungafani kwiiyantlukwano zesini okanye zobudala . Kanti , ukungafani kuqulethe ngaphezulu kweeyantlukwano phakathi kwabantu ezisekelwe kwinkcubeko , isini okanye ubudala . Abantu bayahluka ngokubhekiselele kwiintlobo ngeentlobo zezinto kuquka ubudala , inkolo , inkcubeko , imvelaphi yemfundo , amava , impilo , indawo ngokwejiyografi , ingeniso , imo yabazali , imo malunga neHIV , ukukwazi ngokwasemzimbeni njalo-njalo . IBhunga leSixeko libekele bucala umhlaba osecaleni kwemizi emikhulu nebala legalufa liwubekela izindlu ezingatshoni kakhulu epokotweni . Abahlali bale mizi mikhulu abonwabanga sesi sicwangciso kuba besithi oku kuza kwehlisa amaxabiso eepropati zabo . Abahlali ecetyelwa bona le ndawo bafuna kuqhutyekwe ngesi sicwangciso kuba kukho ukusilela kwezindlu kwaye nendawo abahlala kuyo okwangoku ixinene kakhulu . Esi sigaba sokuqhutywa kweprojekthi siza kubandakanya uvandlakanyo , uhlengahlengiso nokunikwa kwengxelo rhoqo . Into yokuba kuqaliswe ngesicwangciso ayithethi ukuba zonke izinto ziya kuhlala ziyilaa nto zazicingelwe ukuba ziyiyo phaya ekuqaleni komjikelo weprojekthi , okoko iqhuba iprojekthi . Kubalulekile ukuba kumana ukuhlengahlengiswa , aze ke onke amaqela achaphazelekayo aziswe rhoqo ngohlengahlengiso olwenziweyo . Bonke abemi kufuneka bafikelele ngokulinganayo kwiinkonzo abanelungelo kuzo . ULINGANISEKE ( MEASURABLE ) - ingaba umgangatho wenkonzo uyalinganiseka kwaye ungenzeka ngexabiso elifanelekileyo nenzame ? Abantu abohlukeneyo - abahlali bahlukene kwaye banomdla owahlukeneyo , imibono neendlela ababona ngayo izinto . Ukusombulula impikiswano kudingeka ukuba kubekho iindlela zokuqinisekisa ukuba oku kwahlukana kusetyenziswa ngokwakhayo nangokunika igalelo kwiinguqu nenkqubo ezilungileyo . IPhepha Lengcaciso-nkqubo likaRhulumente Weengingqi , lowe-1998 luxwebhu lomgaqo-siseko olumisela isiseko sophuhliso olutsha lwesixokelelwano sikarhulumente wengingqi . I-IDP ikwazalisekisa imfuno echazwe kuMgaqo-siseko nowiso-mthetho oluhambelana noku ( olunjengePhepha leNgcaciso yoMgaqo-nkqubo woLawulo lweeDolophu neZithili , 1998 ) koomasipala kulwakhiwo nolawulo lweenkqubo zabo zolawulo jikelele , uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali nocwangciso ekubekeni phambili iimfuno ezisisiseko zoluntu kwimimandla nokuthatha inxaxheba kwiinkqubo zophuhliso kuzwelonke nakwiphondo . Iintlanganiso zikawonke-wonke zabahlali ngokubanzi namaqela awonganyelweyo kubandakanywa iKomiti yeWadi apho uthungelwano lwesicwangciso samanyathelo nesishwankathelo seeprojekthi ( sinokubhalwa kwifliptshathi sibekwe elubala ) kuxoxwa khona ngaso . SINGAZIPHUMEZA KUPHELA IINJONGO ZETHU ZOLAWULO OLUFANELEKILEYO XA ABANTU NGABANYE , ABAHLALI NEMIBUTHO YEZOPOLITIKO , KANTI NABO BANJONGO ZIPHAMBUKILEYO BEKHOLELWA BEKWAZIXHASA IZITHETHE ZEDEMOKRASI ZAMAZIKO " INTETHO EBALULEKILEYO KAMONGAMELI UMBEKI KWINTLANGANISO JIKELELE YONYAKA YEEKOMISHONI ZONYULO ZESADC , EDAR ES SALAAM , ETANZANIA , SEPTEMBA 1999 . Usihlalo makaqhube intlanganiso ngokusekwe kwiajenda ezotywe ngabathabathi-nxaxheba . Olu lwazi luyimfuneko ekuchongeni iimfuno zabahlali . Olu lwazi lubandakanya amanani neengxelo , ezinika intsukaphi zewadi . Umsebenzi 4 Zeziphi iziphumo zeli nqanam ? I-CBP ibandakanya ukuchongwa nokuqeqeshwa kwababhexeshi abasebenza namaqela abahlali ukuze awancedise awanike inkxaso malunga nenxaxheba yawo kwizicwangciso ezikuluntu lwawo . Oku kuyimfuneko njengoko kuya kukuncedisa ukuba uchonge iimfuno zabahlali . Inengxelo yamaqela ahluka-hlukeneyo ezentlalo phakathi koluntu , iintlobo zeempiliso , awona maqela azezona zisulu phakathi kwabahlali , imisebenzi ephambili nokuba ngoobani abaxhasi ngeenkonzo . Iziphumo , izingqinisiso neenkqubo zoqinisekiso ( imisebenzi , izibonelelo neendleko ) zinika isikhokelo sokuqulunqa iingxelo ngenkqubo yeprojekthi ( ukuthelekisa oko kwakucwangcisiwe noko kwenziweyo ) . I-CBP yinkqubo ebhexeshwayo engqiyame ngokuqinisekisa ukuba izimvo zabahlali ziyabandakanywa kuphuhliso lwabahlali . Iqela elingundoqo kubabhexeshi ababini obona buncinci ngewadi elisebenza neKomiti yeWadi yengingqi liyindlela eyiyona incomekayo . Iqela elisebenza kunye malibandakanye umbhexeshi omnye obona buncinci ovela kwiwadi nomnye ovela kumasipala , xa kunokwenzeka umbhexeshi ofakelweyo wewadi ovela kwenye iwadi . Enyanisweni ababhexeshi bakamasipala mabafunyanwe kumacandelo ahluka-hlukeneyo , ukuqinisekisa ukuba iintlobo ngeentlobo zamacandelo kamasipala ziyaxhamla kwi-CBP , nokuseka umntu ekuqhagamshelwana naye we-CBP kwisebe ngalinye lecandelo . Ingxoxo yeKomiti yeWadi yothungelwano lwesicwangciso samanyathelo nesicwangciso samanyathelo sexesha elingaphambili . Indlela yamaKhosikazi kuPhuhliso ijolise kwindlela amakhosikazi angadityaniswa ngokungcono ' kwihlabathi elenziwe ngamadoda'elikhoyo namalinge ophuhliso angqameneyo . Le ndlela ijonge umsebenzi onika iziqhamo wamakhosikazi kukhutshelwa ngaphandle umsebenzi wokwandisa , kwaye iphawulwa ziiprojekthi ezinika inzuzo kumakhosikazi ngaphandle kokujonga izizathu zenkqubo zokungalingani ngokwesini . IPhepha leNgcaciso-nkqubo malunga noRhulumente weengingqi , lowe-1998 liluxwebhu lomgaqo-nkqubo olumisela isiseko sesixokelelwano esitsha sophuhliso sikarhulumente weengingqi . Esi sixokelelwano sitsha sizinikela ekusebenzeni nabemi , amaqela kunye nabahlali ukuze kufumaneke umgangatho wobomi kuhlangatyezwane neemfuno zentlalo , zoqoqosho nezezinto eziphathekayo zamaqela oluntu . Oku kuthetha ukuba oomasipala kufuneka benze isakhiwo kwaye baphathe ulawulo lwabo , kunye neenkqubo zohlahlo lwabiwo-mali nezezicwangciso ukuze kubekwe phambili iimfuno ezisisiseko sabahlali . Ukuphuhliswa kwamazwe angaphandle nommandla kunefuthe kuMzantsi Afrika ngeendlela ezinzima . Uluvo lwethu kukuba kulungelelaniso , iintsingiselo zehlabathi zinganempembelelo elungileyo kuphuhliso loMzantsi Afrika , nangona kukho intlaninge yemingcipheko ebonakalayo . Ukuqondwa nokuphendulwa kwemingeni enzima yehlabathi ngokufanelekileyo ngumsebenzi wokuqala wesicwangciso . Oorhulumente abenza urhulumente weengingqi banikwe amandla nemisebenzi ethile . Imida yesizwe neyamaphondo nayo inamagunya nemisebenzi eyiyeyayo . Abathathi-nxaxheba kufuneka banike izizathu zokuzilandelelanisa ngolu hlobo bazilandelelanise ngazo izinto ezenziwayo besebenzisa itshathi eyibha-tshathi okanye ngokunika imizekelo . Isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali sinako kwakhona ukukhokelela kwiinguquko zeendlela oomasipala abanika ngazo iinkonzo . Umzekelo , umasipala usenokuqwalasela ukumisela ulwahlulelwano neqela elithile labahlali ukunika inkonzo ethile . Ukubandakanyeka kwabahlali ekunikweni kweenkonzo sekusenzeka kwiindawo ezifana neKwaZulu-Natal neMpuma Koloni apho abahlali bazibandakanya kubonelelo lwamanzi ucoceko lwangasese nakukhenketho . Ngethuba lebakala lokuqala leMephu Yendlela ye-CBP iqela lezicwangciso liqokelela lize lihlalutye iinkcukacha nolwazi oselukhona ngokubamba uthotho lwamathuba odliwano-ndlebe nangokusebenzisa izixhobo ezahluka-hlukeneyo zezixhobo ze-CBP . Uhlalutyo olucokisiweyo lwezi nkcukacha lunika iqela lezicwangciso ulwazi ngemvelaphi ehlanganiselweyo nangengqiqo ngemeko yabahlali , iingxaki , izithethe , izenzo , izixokelelwano nangezinto ezixabisekileyo . Oku kwenziwa ngeqela labahlali elixutyaniswe ngokubanzi kwaye luhlobo oluthile lwesixhobo . Kuthatha iiyure ezimalunga nezimbini kwaye isazobe sisetyenziselwa ukugqibezela icwecwe lokuhlalutya . Icandelo 152 -iinjongo zikarhulumente wasekhaya kukukhuthaza ukuzibandakanya kwabahlali nemibutho yasekuhlaleni kwimiba karhulumente wengingqi . Cela abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bagqibezele umsebenzi ongezantsi . Ukomeleza umsebenzi weshishini lezabasebenzi ekuphuculeni ukufunyanwa kwezakhono , ukuzalanisa abafuna umsebenzi nezithuba zomsebenzi , nokunciphisa ungquzulwano . Khumbuza abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba sisebenzisa lo msetyenzana ukwenza abathathi-nxaxheba bayazi imiceli-mingeni kuphuhliso lwesicangciso sewadi kanti asinaxesha lokuxoxa ngebakala ngalinye ngokokucukubhede balo , ngoko ke siza kuchitha imizuzu eli-10 ukuya kweli-15 kweli nyathelo , kodwa amaqela aphakamisa umbono ngokwesakhelo sexesha . Ukuba abakwazi ukugqibezela umbono wabo mabafikelele apho banako ukufikelela khona . Ulawulo lukamasipala nophuhliso lungumceli-mngeni kwaye lubandakanya intlaninge yemiba entsonkothileyo . Kuba okokuqala lubandakanya abantu , izidingo zabo , okubakhathazayo nezinyanzelo oluzidingayo ukuze lulawulwe ngendlela yokuba kufunyanwe inzuzo ephezulu sisininzi sabantu . Kodwa , ekuhlaleni sinabantu abohlukeneyo nabanomdla okhuphisanayo kwaye akwenzeki ukuba onke amaqela aneliswe ngexesha elinye . Ukuncedisa amagosa kamasipala neenkokheli ezinyuliweyo ukunika impendulo ezilungileyo kubemi abakwingingqi yabo ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu nokubandakanyeka kufanelekile . IiKomiti zeWadi zidlala indima ebalulekileyo ukunceda oku ukuba kwenzeke . Yimpendulo enjani oyiva ngaphakathi kuwe xa uthetha nomntu okumameleyo ? Lo ngumsebenzi weqela ngesampulu yabahlali abamele abahlali ngokubanzi nebandakanya ukuzoba okanye ukuphuhlisa imephu . Zinike iiyure ezimbini zomsebenzi wokwenza umalatha-ndlela . Kwinqanaba lelizwe , ubunakho obungundoqo buquka umthetho namanye amaziko , amaziko akhoyo ( uthungelwano ngocingo , amanzi , umbane nothutho ) , inkqubo yokufunda nokuqeqesha , ulawulo olugcinakalayo lokusingqongileyo , izixokelelwano zezinto ezintsha neepatheni zokuphuhliswa kwesithuba . Ubunakho boluntu buquka imfundo , impilo , ukukhuselwa kwasekuhlaleni nokhuseleko loluntu . IKhomishoni yeSini ikhuthaza umgangatho wokuhlonitshwa kokulingana ngokwesini ikwasebenzela ukukhusela , uphuhliso nokufumana ukulingana ngokwesini . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka aziqhelanise ne-ofisi yephondo yezikhomishoni ukuze bakwazi ukwazisa uluntu jikelele malunga nezi ofisi . Kukwakumdla wamashishini ukuba amazinga okungalingani ancitshiswe . Ukungalingani kuphakamisa iindleko zokuqhuba ushishino , kukekelise ubume boshishino ze ekugqibeleni kunyine amathuba okukhula . Kukwabangela ukungathembani nokubambeka . Imbuyekezo engaphaya kwicandelo lombuso olawulayo yenza kancinane ekwakheni uluntu olubandakanya ngakumbi apho wonke ubani eziva ukuba bayabelana kwiziqhamo zophuhliso . Logama ukumisa umthetho wemivuzo kungenakusebenza , ubunkokheli kufuneka buqinisekise ukuba amashishini enza ngokuba noxanduva ngakumbi . Inkqubo ye-CBP iyayamkela into yokuba amalungu abahlali aneengqiqo ezifana zodwa nezixabisekileyo malunga nophuhliso lwawo kwaye igxininisa ngakumbi kwezi zimvo . Kumsebenzi olandelayo amathuba odliwano-ndlebe nabantu abaphambili abanolwazi asetyenziselwa ukufumana izimvo ezikhokelela kwizisombululo ezinokuba khona . Ukunika ingxelo kuyimfuneko kulawulo lwesinizi . Kukho ubuthathaka obuninzi kwikhonkco lokunika ingxelo , nesiqhelo esinabileyo sokutyhola omnye . Ikhonkco lokunika ingxelo kumele lomelezwe ukusuka phezulu ukuya ezantsi . Ukuqala oku , ukunikwa kwengxelo yipalamente kubuthathaka , nePalamente isilela ukufezekisa indima yayo yokujonga okusisiseko . Iziphumo zemfundo azingekhe ziphucuke ngaphandle kokubuyiselwa kokwenziwa kwengxelo kwisixokelelwano siphela , ukusuka kwiziphumo zabafundi ukuya kuhanjiso lweencwadi zokufunda . Inani elinyukayo lokuvukela ukuhanjiswa kwenkonzo kubonisa ukuba urhulumente naye kufuneka enze kubelula kubemi ukuvakalisa iinkxalabo . Xa ungena kwisakhiwo soluntu , abemi kumele babe nokubona ukuba yeyiphi inkonzo abangayilindela , nokuba bangaya phi ukuze bathethe nabani ukuba abaxolanga . Olunye uwiso-mthetho olunokunceda xa uphendula imibuzo esuka kumalungu oluntu jikelele kwimimandla . Ukubeka eswenikwiNkqubo yoLawulo loMsebenzi - I-PMS kufuneka isekwe nguye nawuphi na umasipala ukuze uthathele ingqalelo ukusetyenziswa koovimba bakamasipala , ukuphucula inkqubela-phambili nokusebenza kwemibutho nokubonisa ukufezekiswa kweziphumo . Umasipala kufuneka aseke iSalathisi esiPhambili soMsebenzi ekwenzeni umlinganiselo wakhe kwaye kufuneka abandakanye abahlali . IKomiti yeWadi sisixhobo sokubandakanya abahlali . Ngethuba lomsetyenzana olandelayo amathuba odliwano-ndlebe nabaniki beenkonzo aqhutyelwa ukuqikelela isakhono sabaniki beenkonzo abachongwe ngethuba lomsetyenzana wangaphambili ukuba negalelo kwimpumezo , ukuxilonga iingxaki abajongene nazo , nokubabandakanya kwinkqubo yokwenza isicwangciso . Oku kuya kunceda ekwakheni izicangciso ezithembekileyo nezinako ukufezeka . Khumbula ukulungiselela la mathuba odliwano-ndlebe ithuba liselihle . UMzantsi Afrika uphelele wahlulwe wangoomasipala . Zintathu iintlobo ezahluka-hlukileyo , okanye izintlu zikamasipala . Ukukhawulezisa inkqubela-phambili , ukunabisa idemokhrasi nokwakhiwa koluntu olubandakanyekayo ngakumbi , uMzantsi Afrika kumele uguqulele ukuxhotyiswa kwezepolitiki ibe bubuncwane boqoqosho kuye wonke ubani . Kuxhomekeke kuye wonke ummi woMzantsi Afrika ukulungisa ikamva , ukusukela namhlanje . UMnu . Nkosi uhlala kwilali apho kufakelwe khona impompo yamanzi njengoko ingengawo onke amakhaya anamanzi abalekayo . Le mpompo ikufutshane ngesango lakhe langaphambili . Abantu abasebenzisa le mpompo abayivali ngokupheleleyo , ihlala njalo ichaphaza . Oku kubangela le ndawo ihlale inodaka neengcongconi . UMnu . Nkosi udikiwe kukuhlala enodaka kwisango lokungena endlwini yakhe waze wagqiba ekubeni andise iyadi yakhe aze atshixe isango . Abantu belali bayavutha ngumsindo baze bafaka isikhalazo . Bachaza ukuba uMnu . Nkosi akanaxesha lamntu , uzicingela yena yedwa njengoyena mntu ubalulekileyo kunabanye abantu kule lali . UMnu . Nkosi uthi abantu elalini abamcingeli kwaye abakhathali njengoko yena nosapho lwakhe besokola ngenxa yokungavalwa kwempompo . Ingaba kukho imimandla yohlaza lwexabiso oluthile lolondolozo okanye lokuzihlaziya , umz , imimandla yendalo neempawu ezizodwa ezifana nemithi enomtsalane nenemithunzi ? Yahlula abathabathi-nxaxheba ngokwamaqela ezi-3 . Cela iqela ngalinye ukuba licinge kwaye libhale phantsi ukuba ingaba ingulowo kwabalandelayo unaxanduva luphi . Mabacinge ngomasipala ongowabo xa bephendula . Iqela lilonke , lixoxa nabathathi-nxaxheba malunga neenjongo eziphambili zesicwangciso esisekelwe kuluntu kwimimandla , lisebenzisa amanqaku esifundo ( jonga uluhlu kwiphepha 38 ) njengesikhokelo . Ingaba iKomiti yeWadi inazo iindlela zokuphucula ukukwazi kwabasebenzi ukwenzela ukuqhuba uphicotho lwesini kwimigangatho yomgaqo-nkqubo , inkqubo neziko , nokukwazi ukuyila nokuqhuba inkqubo exhasa ukulingana ngesini ? Zeziphi ? Amaqondo aphezulu orhwaphilizo axhalabisa ubunakho boluntu ekusebenzeni ngobulungisa nangempumelelo , nobunakho bukarhulumente ekuhambiseni kumyalelo wakhe wophuhliso . Ngokuphathelelene nophononongo lorhwaphilizo lwehlabathi lweTransparency International , phakathi kowama-2001 nowama-2010 , iqondo lorhwaphilizo linyukile . Urhwaphilizo lusoloko lubandakanya abathathi nxaxheba kuwo omabini amacandelo oluntu nawabucala . Ukuqondwa kwamaqondo aphezulu okwenziwa kulwaphulo mthetho kwizikhundla eziphezulu kurhulumente kwenza ukulwa urhwaphilizo kubenzima ngakumbi . IKomiti yeWadi nababhexeshi be-CBP basebenzisa ii-SWOT zeqela leempiliso neenkcukacha ezivela kwiBakala 1 ukwenzela ingxoxo yeeyure ezintandathu . Umsebenzi 5 Nika imizekelo eyodwa malunga nendlela uluntu lwakho kummandla lungathatha ngayo inxaxheba kweli nqanam le-IDP , nezigqeba ezikhoyo ekunyuseni umgangatho wokuthatha inxaxheba koluntu jikelele . Ukwakhela phezu kweenkcukacha eziqokelelwe ngethuba lebakala lokuqala , ibakala lesibini kubandakanya uhlalutyo olucokisiweyo nokuhlanganiselwa kweenkcukacha . Kwibakala 2 iinkcukacha eziqokelelweyo ziyahlalutywa kuze kuxoxwe ngazo kumaqela amancinci . Le nkqubo idibanisa uhlalutyo lweempiliso zamaqela ezentlalo , izixhobo ze-CBP ( iimephu , ii-Venn , icandelo labahlali , ixesha elimisiweyo lemikhwa yamaxesha athile neyethuba elide ) , nezinto ezifunyaniswe kumathuba odliwano-ndlebe nabaniki beenkonzo nasebantwini abanika ulwazi abaphambili . Ekupheleni kwebakala uphengululo lwabahlali , uqwalaselo oluphinda-phindwayo nokunyanisekiswa kweenkcukacha ezihlanganiselweyo . Oku ke ngoko kunikwa iwadi kwaye kufuneka babeke phambili ngokokubaluleka iziphumo eziphambili ezihlanu ukwenzela inkqubo yokwenza izicwangciso . ICandelo 39 le-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 linika umsebenzi usodolophu , ikomiti yesigqeba esilawulayo okanye ikomiti eyodwa yamalungu ebhunga ekulawuleni uphuhliso lwe-PMS nokuyigqithisa kwibhunga . I-PMS kufuneka icacise imisebenzi noxanduva lomthathi-nxaxheba ngamnye . Ingaba uphicotho lomxholo weprojekthi luquka uphononongo lwemo yezomthetho , yentlalo neyoqoqosho yamakhosikazi ? Usingaye ( okanye ' imibandela ' ) eyimivuka yemizuzu edlulileyo -eli nqaku liquka imibandela exoxwe kwintlanganiso edlulileyo nebekufuneka amalungu ekomiti abuyise ingxelo ngayo . Kulula ukubona ukuba ngawaphi amanqaku enza ' imibandela eyimivuka ' ngokujonga amanyathelo abefanele ukuthatyathwa ngabantu . Ingaba iinkonzo ezinikezelwayo ziyalingana nemigangatho ? Ishishini lezabasebenzi eliphendula ngakumbi kumathuba oqoqosho . Oku kufuna ukufunda kobomi bonke nokubhekiselwa phambili kobungcali ; ukuthomalalisa ubume bomsebenzi ; ukomeleza amaziko okusombulula ungquzulwano ; ukuphononongwa kwemithetho nemigangatho yorhwebo oluncinci noluphakathi ; ukujongana nonxulumano lwabasebenzi kumacandelo oluntu ; ukomelezwa kokusetyenziswa kwemigangatho emincinane phakathi kwabasebenzi , ii-arhente zokugaya nabarhwebi ; ukomeleza iinkqubo ezisebenzayo kwimakethe yomsebenzi nokuzalaniswa kwabasebenzi ; nokuvumela ungenelelo lwezakhono . Isicwangciso siyiliwe kodwa sifuna ukuguqulelwa kwisicwangciso samanyathelo ukuze siphunyezwe . Nantsi indlela yokuqhuba oko . Ukwenza iingcebiso ngayo nayiphi imibandela echaphazela ibhunga kuceba okanye ngokugqitha kuceba ukuya kumasipala . Kumjikelo odlulileyo wee-IDP , abacebisi kulumano-ndlebe badlale indima enkulu kakhulu - kaninzi bekubakho iziphumo eziyingxaki . Abacebisi kulumano-ndlebe be-IDP ngokunjalo nabacwangcisi bakamasipala basuka babe ziinjineli okanye abacwangcisi beedolophu , ngoko ke baqeqeshelwe ukujolisa kwizinto eziphathekayo , nakwimibandela yezakhiwo ezisisiseko okanye kweyezithuba , kunakwinguquko zeenkqubo okanye ulumano-ndlebe noluntu . Le ngxaki iqatshelwe ngokubanzi yi-dplg nakuqeqesho kwii-IDP oluqhutywe ngowama-2001 obelusenza ilinge lokwandisa ingqiqo yophuhliso xa kuthelekiswa nokwenza izicwangciso zezinto eziphathekayo . Oomasipala Boluhlu B okanye oomasipala beengingqi : Aba ngoomasipala ababelana ngogunyaziwe wesigqeba nowowiso-mthetho noluhlu C okanye oomasipala beenqila . Bonke oomasipala beengingqi baphantsi kwemida yoomasipala beenqila . UMgaqo-siseko woMzantsi Afrika unoMthetho wamaLungelo oqinisekisa ukukhuselwa kwamalungelo . Ummi ngamnye unelungelo kukhuselo lwamalungelo oluntu . La malungelo aquka ilungelo lendawo ' engenabungozi kwimpilo nokuphila kwakho ' nophuhliso oluzinzileyo lokukhuseleka kwezinto eziphilayo nendawo eziphila kuyo nokusebenzisa imithombo yendalo xa kukhuthazwa uqoqosho olunobulungisa nophuhliso lwentlalo ' . Igatya 24 loMthetho wamaLungelo . IiKomiti zeWadi zidlala indima ebalulekileyo njengejelo lokubonisa umdla wabahlali kwi-IDP nokuqinisekisa ukuba izicwangciso zewadi kwezentlalo nezoqoqosho zihlangabezana nomdla wabahlali xa bebonke . IiKomiti zeWadi ziqhagamshelana nabahlali ngeendlela ezintathu , okokuqala njengabameli boluntu , okwesibini ngokwakha ulwalamano noluntu , okwesithathu kuxanduva lokunika inkcazo . UBE YIMPENDULO ( RESPONSIVE ) - ingaba umgangatho uyimpendulo kwiimfuno zabemi abafumana inzuzo kwinkonzo ? Ukukhuthaza ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu ngokukhuthaza ukuthatha uxanduva kwizinto zoluntu nakumalinge ukuze bakwazi ukuqwalasela iimfuno zabemi besixeko . Oku kungaquka ukulungisa iincwadana namaphetshana olwazi ukwazisa abahlali ngemicimbi . Unomathotholo wasekuhlaleni yindlela esebenzayo yokuquka abahlali kwimiba edla umzi . Umzekelo , kungabanjwa udliwano-ndlebe namalungu eKomiti yeWadi ngemicimbi yasekuhlaleni okanye unomathotholo wasekuhlaleni angasetyenziselwa ukusabalalisa umcimbi okanye ukucela umbono ngeprojekthi ecetywayo . Ukusebenzisa uludwe lokuqwalasela lwempahla yexabiso ngengxoxo ecwangciselwe ngokungaphelelanga ngeempiliso zeqela . Bhala phantsi iimpendulo . Umzekelo woludwe lokuqwalasela lwempahla exabisekileyo onokukunceda kulo msebenzi kukuqinisekisa ukuba unazo zonke iinkcukacha ozifunayo . Oku kwenziwa njengengxoxo yamaqela kwaye ithatha iiyure ezimbini ukuya kwezintathu . Abathathi-nxaxheba bathathwa kwiqela elisisiseko esibanzi samalungu abahlali , kubandakanywa ummeli wawo onke amaqela ezentlalo . Sebenzisa i-PowerPoint xa ikhona idatha projektha , kungenjalo bhala ibakala ngalinye kwifliptshathi uze ubonise abathathi-nxaxheba isazobe kumanqaku esifundo kwiphepha lama-35 . Uluhlu lwabahlali - yenza uluhlu lwemibutho ekhoyo kummandla , ukuquka iinkcukacha zoqhagamshelwano nomntu onoxanduva ukuze uqinisekise ukuba onke amaqela achaphazelekayo agcinwa esazi malunga nebhunga . Intando yopolitiko iyimfuneko ekulweni esi sifo . Intando yopolitiko ilinganiselwa ngokuvavanya isambuku semali echithwe ekulweni urhwaphilizo , ingalo yomthetho amaziko aveza urhwaphilizo anayo , ukungaxhomekeki ekungeneleleni kwepolitiki kumaqumrhu achasene norhwaphilizo nokusebenza ngokungajikajikiyo apho umthetho uye uthathe unyawo . Ukuthamba kumatyala amancinane , okanye ukuba qatha ngokungaqhelekanga kurhwaphilizo olubandakanya abachaseneyo bopolitiko , ibonisa ukujikajika . Kwakha indawo enenkxaso nenceda abantu ukuba baphole baze baqwalasele imiba ethile . UMgaqo-siseko , ka-1996 useka urhulumente wengingqi njengomgangatho ozimeleyo karhulumente onoxanduva lonikezelo lweenkonzo . Uluntu lwethu ekuhlaleni luquka iintlobo ezahlukeneyo zabantu ezineenkqubo zeenqobo ezahlukeneyo , iindlela zokuphila , iilwimi , ukhetho lwezesondo ( sexual orientations ) , iindlela zokunxiba neenkangeleko ngokwasemzimbeni . Ukuba sizijonga ezi yantlukwano ngokwakhayo singathi ' kwenza ihlabathi libe nomdla kakhulu kwaye kuyasityebisa ' . Ukuphila nokungafani ngumngeni kwaye iiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zikwazi ukusabela kule mingeni ngokwakhayo . Amaqela kuluntu ekuhlaleni aneemfuno ezahlukeneyo , ukufikelela kwizibonelelo okwahlukeneyo kunye nezinto ezilindelweyo ezahlukeneyo . Nanjengoko iiKomiti zeWadi zinoxanduva lokuqinisekisa ukuba iimfuno zoluntu ziqukiwe kucwangciso neenkqubo zikamasipala kufuneka ziqonde ngamaqela angafaniyo kuluntu lwabo ekuhlaleni kunye nokuqinisekisa ukuba amaqela aziva equkiwe kwiinkqubo zokwenza izigqibo . Umsebenzi 2 Ngawaphi amanyathelo angathathwa yiKomiti yeWadi yakho ukwenzela ukujonga ukungalingani okuchongileyo ? Zama ukuchonga inyathelo elinye ubuncinane ngokunxulumene nombuzo ngamnye kule ingentla . Vuma uze ungqinisise uvakalelo lomnye umntu onomsindo . Khumbula , kulungile ukuba nomsindo . I-logframe matrix luxwebhu olubonakalisa ezona ndawo zibaluleke kakhulu kwisicwangciso seprojekthi ngendlela elandelelaniswe ngokucwangcisekileyo . Iinkcukacha zesigaba ngasinye zizaliswa kwishedyuli yomsebenzi neyezincedisi ( zichazwa ke kweli candelo lilandelayo ) ezihamba kunye ne-logframe . Indlela esinxibelelana ngayo inako ukuthintela okanye ukuphucula imeko . Cinga ngabantu obaziyo abangabanxibeleli abalungileyo uze uchonge into eyenza ukuba babe ngabanxibeleli abalungileyo . Iinkqubo zokuvala - ziqinisekisa ukuba izinto ezilindelekileyo kwiprojekthi zenziwe , ukufumana ' isivumelwano esisayiniweyo ' ngababandakanyekayo abafanelekileyo , esenza kube sesikweni ukugqitywa kweprojekthi ngokuveliswa nokudluliswa kolwazi , ukugqitywa nokuzalisekiswa kweekhontrakthi kuquka nokulungiswa kwemiba eseleyo . Isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali asizenzekeli ngokwaso . Isicwangciso asiyonto eyenziwa yingcaphephe . Isekwa kwinxaxheba nakwimithetho-siseko yedemokrasi yezopolitiko . Inxaxheba ifuna ukuba onke amaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya amenyelwe kwinxaxheba , kubandakanywa urhulumente , abahlali , amacandelo oshishino , abasebenzi namanye amacandelo oluntu oluphantsi kukarhulumente . Khuthaza ukungabinamfihlo - musa ukugweba xa abantu bechaza izimvo zabo . Zingahluka kwezakho . Kubalulekile ukwenza isigqibo kwakwithuba langaphambili ukuba ingaba imicimbi ephambili yamaqela ahlelelekileyo iya kufumana ukujongwa kuqala na . Umzekelo , kusenokuba kuvunyelweni ngokuba esinye kwiziphumo ezihlanu masivele kula maqela . Yintoni ayenzayo eyenza ukuba kube lula ukuthetha naye ? Ukubamba iintlanganiso noluntu jikelele kunye namaqela achaphazelekayo . Imvisiswano phakathi kwamanqanaba karhulumente , nangona esahlukaniseka , anobudlelwane boxhomekeko nobonxulumano . Ababhexeshi : I-CBP ifuna iqela lababhexeshi abazinikelayo nabaqeqeshwe kakuhle abayiqonda ngokupheleleyo inkqubo ukuze bakwazi ukuyiqhuba ngenkuthalo nangokuncomekayo . Mema amaqela ahlukeneyo ukuba anyule isithethi uze umeme isithethi ukuba sizichaze nokuba simele banina . Ummeli weKomiti yeWadi noceba wewadi nabasebenza nabo bazazisile . Kuvunyelwene ngemithetho namaqela ewonke . Umzekelo : ukuvumela iqela ngalinye lichaze isicelo salo ; lithethe kumxolelanisi ; kungabizwa magama , njl-njl . Ubudlelwane nemibutho yeetekisi zasekuhlaleni kunganceda ukwaziswa ngentlanganiso , ezi zezinye zeendlela obunganceda ngayo ubudlelwane ukukhuthaza ilizwi labahlali . Ilungu / amalungu eKomiti yeWadi angeva ukuba amalungu ecandelo elithile loluntu ekuhlaleni ' ngabaqhathi ' kwaye ke ngoko naliphi na icebiso abalinikayo ukwenzela ukuhanjiswa kweenkonzo okanye iiprojekthi kufanele lingahoywa . Iikomiti ezimiyo zithungelana namasebe kamasipala kwaye zingasekwa libhunga xa kufanelekile . Ukwakha ubunakho bukarhulumente ukuze adlale indima yophuhliso nokuguqula . IiKomiti zeWadi zidla ngokunyulwa kwintlanganiso yabahlali ixesha elingangonyaka okanye emibini . Ukuba ilungu alizi ezintlanganisweni kufuneka kufakwe elinye endaweni yalo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi akhetha ngokwahlukileyo emaphandleni nasezidolophini . Kubizwa intlanganiso apho ucebawewadi ecacisa ukuba oku sisindululo ekusaxoxwayo ngaso kwaye kuza kubanjwa iintlanganiso kunye noluntu jikelele . Uye wacacisa izizathu zokusiwa kwenye indawo okucetywayo nokuquka umba wokuba umhlaba ohlala uninzi lwabantu abahlala ematyotyombeni awufanelekanga kufakelo lwemibhobho ehambisa amanzi amdaka edolophu kengoko lo mmandla awusayi kuphuhliswa njengesiza esisisigxina . Ngokwangoku , uninzi lwabahlali luyagula yimikhuhlane neengqele . Abo bahlali abanesifo sephepha ( TB ) abasayi kubangcono baze abo bahlali baphila nogawulayo nentsholongwane yakhe ( HIV / Aids ) abasayi kukwazi ukusela amayeza abo ngohlobo olufunekayo ngaphandle kweenkonzo ezaneleyo . Utshintsho lwemozulu sele lunempembelelo kuMzantsi Afrika , nokutshintsha-tshintsha kwamaqondo aphawulekayo neemvula nokunyuka kwamaqondo olwandle . Urhulumente uya kuba noxanduva kwisabelo esikhulu seengcebiso kwisicwangciso . Ukufezekisa ezi ngcebiso , uya kufuneka omeleze ikhonkco lakhe lokunika ingxelo , aphucule isikhundla sakhe , alungele ukuthatha izigqibo ezinzima nokusebenza nabanye kuluntu ekusombululeni imingeni . Oku kuthetha ukunxibelelana ngokuthembakeleyo nangenyaniso noluntu , logama besenza abemi banike ingxelo ngezenzo zabo . Iinkokheli , ingakumbi kurhulumente , kumele nazo zimelane nezigqibo ezinzima nemisebenzi . Ubunkokheli obomeleleyo bumalunga nokuthatha izigqibo ezinjalo nokucenga ngokuyimpumelelo uluntu ekutheni eyona ndlela ingcono iyalandelwa . Ukusebenza ngempumelelo ngokwasezimalini kukamasipala . Abathathi-nxaxheba bajonga amanqaku ngezifundo abonisa imvelaphi eyahlukeneyo yongquzulwano . Oomasipala bangasebenzisa imithombo esekuhlaleni . Abahlali banothotho lwezakhono namava angazuza kuwo umasipala . Oku kungalondoloza imali kumasipala kuba le mithombo ifumaneka ngoko nangoko . Ukuphucula amatyotyombe kwimihlaba enikezelweyo efanelekileyo . Amathuba ophengululo onyaka ngomgangatho wokusebenza - ibhunga malinike ingxelo kwiiKomiti zeeWadi nakubahlali ngohlahlo lwabiwo-mali nangeenjongo zalo ngomgangatho wokusebenza . Iinkqubo zokufuna igunya lokusungula iprojekthi - zikhokela ukugunyaziswa kweprojekthi ngababandakanyekayo bonke . Isivumelwano nogunyaziso aluyi kufuneka ekuqaleni kweprojekthi kuphela koko kuzo zonke izigaba ezahlukeneyo . Inkxaso ebanzi efikelela kuluntu lonke iyafuneka ekufezekisweni ngokuyimpumelelo kwesicwangciso . Kulawulo lwesininzi oluzele udlamko , le nkxaso ayiyi kuba nagxeke . Ingxoxo-mpikiswano engamandla ibalulekile ekwakheni imvumelwano nobunini obunesiseko esibanzi besicwangciso . Ingxoxo-mpikiswano eyakhayo nayo inegalelo ekwakheni isizwe ngokwenza abemi boMzantsi Afrika baphuhlise ukuqonda okungcono nokubanga ubunini bamaqalela abo ahlanganisiweyo . Iinxenye ezahlukileyo zesicwangciso zifuna ukuzithengela nokuncama kumasebe awahlukileyo . Xa ukwahluka kusenzeka , kubalulekile ukuba izizathu zokungavumelani zixoxwe kwaye zicaciswe ngokucacileyo , ukuze kubekho imvumelwano yokubheka phambili . IKhomishoni yesiCwangciso sikaZwelonke ingasebenzisa amandla ayo okuhlanganisa ukudibanisa abanini bezinto kunye ukuququzelela uthethwathethwano nezisombululo ezinzulu . I-CBP ikhuthaza eminye imiba yomgaqo-nkqubo karhulumente efana neLetsema kunye neVuk'uzenele , ilungise amqela abahlali nabemi ukuba balawule okubangqongileyo ngokuzinikela njengamavolontiya . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi adinga ukubeka esweni ukuchithwa kwemali ukubona ukuba usebenza kakuhle kangakanani umasipala ukuhlangabezana nezicwangciso zabo . Ukwamkelwa kohlahlo lwabiwo-mali yeminye yemisebenzi ebalulekileyo eyenziwa ngooceba . Ooceba badinga ukuthethathethana neeKomiti zeWadi phambi kokwamkela uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka akhangele uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali oluchaphazela abantu abakwiwadi . Izinto ezingaphandle kwiprojekthi zisenokuguquka nanini na , into ke leyo ethetha ukuba kubalulekile ukuba imingcipheko ivandlakanywe ngalo lonke ixesha lokuqhutywa kweprojekthi . INKQUBO YOLAWULO LOMSEBENZI KAMASIPALA IQUKA INKQUBO-SIKHOKELO ECACISA NEKWAMELE INDLELA YOKUQHUTYWA , UKUQUQUZELELWA NOKULAWULWA KOMJIKELO NEENKQUBO ZIKAMASIPALA , UKUBEKA ILISO , UKWENZA UMLINGANISELO , UVAVANYO , UGQITHISO LWENGXELO NOKUPHUCULWA KWAWO , UKUQUKA NOKUMISA IINDIMA ZABATHATHI-NXAXHEBA ABOHLUKENEYO . Kwinqanaba likaRhulumente Weengingqi iMakgotla ibanjwa ngoMatshi zii-Exco zikaMasipala nabaphathi ukuze balungise inkqubo yonyaka wemali . Urhulumente weengingqi naye uqalisa ngophuhliso lwe-IDP yeminyaka emithathu . Urhulumente weengingqi njengomsunguli : Urhulumente weengingqi unokusebenzisana namanye amanqanaba karhulumente ekuchongeni isakhono esikummandla okwimida kamasipala . Oku kunika ulwazi kwizicwangciso nakwizicwangciso ezinobuqili ezinokukhuthaza ukukhula koqoqosho kummandla lowo . Ukukhawulezisa uphuhliso , uMzantsi Afrika ufuna inkxaso esebenzayo evela kubo bonke abemi , ubunkokheli kuwo onke amasebe abeka yonke imidla yelizwe ngaphambi kweenjongo ezimxinwa , nezexesha elifutshane , nokuphucula ngokugqibeleleyo ukusebenza kukarhulumente . Kumanye amaxesha , ukutshintsha kwenkqubo kungayimfuneko , kodwa kwiingingqi ezininzi kumalunga nokufumana ilungelo elisisiseko , ukuphunyezwa kweenkqubo zikarhulumente , ukwenza abantu banike ingxelo ngemisebenzi yabo nokufumana izisombululo kwizinto ezintsha kwimiceli-mngeni enzima . Amaqela anikwa umsebenzi . Amaqela anikwa imizuzu eli-10 ukuya kweli-15 ukuya kuxoxa ngemisebenzi yabo nokwabelana ngeempendulo kwiseshoni epheleleyo . IiKomiti zeWadi kunye nabantu ezibameleyo zinelungelo lokulindela unikezelo lweenkonzo . Kufuneka kukhunjulwe ukuba uluntu kwimimandla nalo lunoxanduva lokuqinisekisa umgangatho nobungakanani beenkonzo obuchazwe kwimigangatho yeenkonzo . Umzekelo , kufuneka lunikezele ulwazi oluchanekileyo , lucacise imeko yalo ngokuthembekileyo luze luziphathe kakuhle nangentlonipho kubanikezeli beenkonzo , njl-njl . IiKomiti zeWadi zidlala indima ekuqinisekiseni ukuba iimfuno zoluntu kummandla zigqithiswa ngokuchanekileyo nangokufanelekileyo . Kufuneka ziqinisekise ukuba amalungu oluntu ayazi ngolwazi , apho lufumaneka khona nendlela yokufikelela kulo . Ugxininiso lwengxelo emiswe ngokufanelekileyo esuka kwibhunga isiya kwiKomiti yeWadi . Xoxa ngoluhlu lweendlela eziza kusetyenziswa ukuqinisekisa ubandakanyo , zidwelise kwifliptshathi . Abathathi-nxaxheba banikwa ithuba lokongeza naziphi iinkcukacha ebezishiyelelwe ngethuba lonxulumaniso lwakuqala . Imibutho echongwe kwiBakala 1 ingqanyaniswa nesiphumo esibekwe phambili ngokokubaluleka kwaso . Intlanganiso inethuba lokongeza iinkcukacha ezivela kumathuba odliwano-ndlebe nabaniki beenkonzo nakwimisebenzi ize ixilonge kwaye iqwalasele kangangoko iziphumo ezinxulumene nesishwankathelo se-IDP , icwecwe lempilo-ntle lamaqela ezentlalo kunye necwecwe leenkcukacha zobume bemeko ebangqongileyo kunye nezithuba . Kufundwa imizuzu - kuqinisekiswe ukuba iyingxelo echanekileyo yentlanganiso edlulileyo . Wonke umntu makavume ukuba imizuzu ichanekile njengoko imizuzu iyingxelo yasemthethweni yeentlanganiso . IiKomiti zeWadi azinamagunya ngokusesikweni ngaphandle kokungenisa izinto ngokungqalileyo kwibhunga okanye bazingenise kuceba . Abanamagunya okwenza izigqibo ezingabophelela nabani na kumasipala . Uceba nguye ummeli wewadi kwibhunga zaye zonke iinkqubo nezigqibo zenziwa libhunga . Uluntu jikelele kufuneka lube nethuba lokugqithisa izimvo zalo kwidrafti ngaphambi kokuba kwamkelwe i-IDP . Iikomiti zeeWadi zinelungu lebhunga leWadi ongusihlalo kunye namalungu abahlali abanokufikelela kwi-10 . Ilungu lebhunga leWadi lingusihlalo wekomiti . Amalungu ekomiti yeWadi awahlawulwa ngenkonzo yawo kwikomiti yeWadi . Isiganeko ngasinye kwiMephu Yendlela sifuna ukwenzela isicwangciso ngokuqaphela . Ababhexeshi be-CBP bafuna ukwazi oko bafanele ukukwenza njengoko oku kusakha ukuzithemba kwabahlali kwinkqubo . Iinkcukacha eziza mva zibandakanya iinkcukacha ezazibhalwe phambi kwebakala lokwenza izicwangciso kwaye ziquka amanani , iingxelo nemizuzu yeentlanganiso kunye namanqaku , iincwadi zeengxelo zeziphatha-mandla zengingqi kunye nezintlu zezinto ngokwamanani . Iintlanganiso zikawonke-wonke nazo zikwanikezela ithuba logqithiso lweengxelo nokwabelana ngolwazi kodwa njengoko kuqhelekile ukuba zibanjwe nenani elikhulu labantu , ithuba liba lincinci lokuxovula ngokubanzi imiba ethile . Ziluncedo ngokukodwa kugqithiso lwengxelo ngemisebenzi yebhunga okanye kwimiba ebiveliswe kwintlanganiso egqithileyo . Sebenzisa imibuzo ukufumana ulwazi okanye ukucaciselwa ngeyona nto ethethwa ngomnye umntu . Iikomiti zeewadi azingekhe ziqhube ulawulo lweeprojekthi ezinkulu zokuhanjiswa kweenkonzo kwiiwadi zazo ; olo luxanduva olusemagxeni kamasipala . Inxaxheba yabo baxhamla ezi nkonzo , kambe iyafuneka nayo ekuqinisekiseni ukuba ukunikwa kweenkonzo kuba nempumelelo nasekubetheleleni ulawulo lwentando yesininzi , idemokhrasi . Kwiindawo apho kukho khona izithabazi ezikhulu okanye amanani aphezulu abantu , iikomiti ezonganyelweyo zimiselwa ngokusekwa kwizikhundla . Ngale ndlela , amalungu eKomiti yeWadi anako ukuya nzulu malunga nemibandela echaphazela amaqela abahlali kwiindibano . Oku kunokomeleza ukuzibandakanya kwabahlali nokweekomiti zeeWadi kwimicimbi yokuthathwa kwezigqibo libhunga . Ngaphandle kwezigqeba eziqhelekileyo / amaqonga eengxoxo kuthethwano noluntu jikelele njengeeKomiti zeWadi namaQonga eeNgxoxo aBameli be-IDP , oomasipala banethuba lokwenza banzi ithuba lothethwano nonxibelelwano noluntu kwimimandla ngaphakathi kwimimandla yabo yolawulo . Anokuseka amaqela achaphazelekayo apho anokudibanisa amaqela achaphazelekayo asuka kumaqela ahlukeneyo anomdla ngokuhambelana nenkqubo yamaqela njengoko isebenza njalo kwiipotfoliyo zabo ezahlukeneyo . Iikomiti zePotfoliyo - yiba noluhlu olugcweleyo lweekomiti zepotfoliyo yebhunga lakho neenkcukacha zoqhagamshelwano zamalungu ekomiti yepotfoliyo ukuze ukwazi ukuwanika ulwazi rhoqo negalelo kwimiba ebalulekileyo kwiiKomiti zabo . Cela iikopi zale Mithetho kumasipala wakho xa uzifuna . Ukuvala - lo ngumgangatho obaluleke kakhulu kwinkqubo yoxolelwaniso kwaye umxolelanisi kufuneka aqinisekise ukuba isivumelwano sishicilelwe saze sasayinwa ngamaqela ewonke . Amalinge okuthatha inxaxheba ekwenzeni uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali nokujoliswe ekuqhobosheleni izinto eziphambili kubahlali kwiinkqubo zotyalo-mali kwizinto ezibambekayo . Abacebisi bezobugcisa banako kwaye bayayidlala indima ebalulekileyo njengoko benika izakhono zobugcisa nobungcaphephe ekunokwenzeka ukuba abahlali abanazo , ngoko ke kubalulekile nokumema abacebisi ngezobugcisa / abaniki beenkozo abakumanqanaba aphezulu kurhulumente wengingqi , ii-NGO okanye icandelo labucala . Inxaxheba yabacebisi bezobugcisa mayibe kukuncedisa kwinkqubo yokunika amagalelo , ngaphandle kokulawula iziphumo . Umzekelo ukubandakanyeka kwabacebisi bezobugcisa kuluncedo xa amaqela abahlali ekhetha izicwangciso-buqili neeprojekthi ukuze bazuze iinjongo zabo , o.k.t. malunga nosuku lwesine lwenkqubo yokwenza isicwangciso . Ukumanyaniswa kwenzame kwakunye nezinga eliphezulu lolungelelaniso kuyimfuneko ukwenzela ukuqinisekisa ukuba imisebenzi yokuqinisekisa ukubandakanywa kwesini njengenkqubo epheleleyo ejoliswe ekuguqulweni kwamaqumrhu adala kwaye agcine ukungalingani ngokwesini , endaweni yokujolisa kungenelelo ngokuthe chu . Eminye imiba njengohlanga / isithethe , iklasi / iqela lezentlalo nobudala nayo inegalelo kwindlela aphendulwa ngayo amakhosikazi . Ukungalingani ngokwesini akunakujongwa ngokwaneleyo ngaphandle kokuba ukungalingani okuvela kwezi zinto zahlukeneyo nako kuyajongwa . Ukuphuhlisa iinjongo linyathelo elilandelayo njengoko oku kumisela indlela abahlali abaya kuzuza ngayo umbono wabo . Iinjongo kufuneka zingqale , zibe nako ukwenzeka kwaye zibe mfutshane ngokwaneleyo ukuze abantu bazibone iinzuzo . Isakhelo sexesha elinako ukusebenziseka sokumisela iinjongo singaphezu kwethuba leminyaka emithathu . IiKomiti zeWadi kufanele ziqinisekise ukuba onke amaqela namacandelo oluntu ayaqukwa ekuqinisekiseni nasekomelezeni ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu . Ungquzulwano lungabonwa njengendlela engentlanga kwaye lungadala iimeko ezinobungozi ebantwini . Umzekelo , imeko yongquzulwano ingabangela ubundlobongela , ukonzakala kwabantu nokudala ukungonwabi noloyiko . Ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu kummandla kuyafuneka ekuhlangabezeni iimfuno zomthetho ezichazwe kwi-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 ne-Municipal Structures Act , 1998 . IiKomiti zeWadi zisebenza njengesikhokelo sonxibelelwano phakathi kwamaqela achaphazelekayo ukuba senzeke , ngokoke kufuneka ziziqhelanise neenkqubo ezisebenzayo zonxibelelwano . I-PMS kamasipala kufuneka iquke imiba ebiphawuliwe libhunga njengenxulumene ngqo neendawo eziphambili zomsebenzi kumasipala walo . Ii-IDP zikamasipala ziphawula iiprojekthi namaxesha okuzigqiba acacileyo nezalathisi zenkqubela-phambili . Amalungu ebhunga anendima ebalulekileyo yokubeka iliso kumsebenzi kamasipala ngokweenkalo ekufuneka kufikelelwe kuzo . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka ziqinisekise ukuba ziya ziqhelanisa nee-KPI neethagethi zomsebenzi ezichazwe kwi-IDP kamasipala wazo ukuze zikwazi ukuvavanya inkqubela-phambili . Umzekelo ongezantsi ubonisa indlela i-KPI efikelela ngayo kwiimfuno zeMimiselo . Le misebenzi ibandakanya ukubekwa kweliso kwinkqubo nokuvandlakanywa kwayo ngeenjongo zokuqinisekisa ukuba iinjongo zeprojekthi le ziyafezekiswa , ezokukhangela ukumka kwisicwangciso okwenzekileyo , khona ukuze kucetywe amanyathelo okulungisa anokuthi athathwe . Kananjalo ibandakanya namanyathelo othintelo eengxaki ezinokuthi zivele . Ibandakanya nokuthelekiswa nomsebenzi lowo wenziweyo kwakunye nalowo ubucetyiwe . Ngubani ohlawulela isincedisi sophuhliso lwezoqoqosho ? Ezinye iintlobo zamaziko zibonelela ngeenzuzo zasekuhlaleni nezoqoqosho ezibanzi . Kodwa ukuba sifuna ukufumana okuphambi kwethu kuthetha ukuba amaxabiso mawanyuke kwixesha elifutshane neliphakathi ukwenza iinkonzo zimelane ngokwezimali . Into yokuba isikhululo sombane esinye ( esivelisa ama-4 800MW ombane ) kuxabise ngokuphindwe kabini isitokhwe sesixa-mali iyonke ehlayo kwizikhululo zombane ezikhoyo ( ezivelisa ama-40 000MW ) kubonisa umngeni . Ngaphaya koko , amaqondo aphezulu okungabikho kwemisebenzi nokungalingani kwenza ezinye zezi nkonzo zingafikeleleki ngexabiso kubantu abaninzi ngaphandle kokuba ziyaxhaswa . Izinto zasekuhlaleni ezinamandla zidlala indima enegalelo . Ukuqondwa kokuba ubume boqoqosho abunabulungisa , ukungalingani kwembali neentlobo ezintsha zokuxhobisa eziye zazuzwa ngabantu abaqhagamshelene ngokwezopolitiko kuphembelela inkcubeko apho urhwaphilizo lubhekela phambili , kurhulumente nakumashishini . Ezi zenzeko zisekelwa ekuhlaleni kumele kujongwane nazo njengenxalenye yokulwa urhwaphilizo . Nika amaqela imizuzu emalunga neli-15 yokuqhuba ufundo-nzulu ngesiganeko . Umntu ongumongikazi odla umhlalaphantsi kunye nongumsebenzi bayafuneka ekuncediseni kwiprojekthi nasekuhanjisweni kwezinye iipasile zokutya kwiintsapho ezihluphekileyo . Kufuneka abo bafumene iipasile zokutya basayiniswe kwaye ke kufuneka nokuba kugcinwe zonke iimpepha ekubhalwe kuzo zonke izihlandlo zotyelelo lwabaniki bolondolozo , oonokhaya . Inyathelo 1 - Vumelana ngexesha , umjikelo wocwangciso , ixesha lokugqithisa ingxelo . Amaqela achaphazelekayo aquka amalungu ebhunga kwiwadi , amagosa kamasipala , abasebenzi bophuhliso loluntu kwimimandla , amalungu oluntu kummandla namaqela anomdla . Yabela iqela ngalinye omnye kule misebenzi ilandelayo . Ubuchule obusekelwe kumaqela bunikezela ithuba kumacandelo ahlukeneyo okanye amaqela ukuba adibane , aze asebenzisane phantsi kwenjongo enye . Amacandelo ahlukeneyo namaqela ayadibana ekusebenzisaneni kwiprojekthi ethile . Yeyiphi inkcukacha ekufuneka siyichazile ukuze siqonde izicwangciso-nkqubo ? IiKomiti zeWadi kuya kufuneka zilawule ukungafani kwiimeko ezininzi , ukusuka kukungafani phakathi kwamalungu eKomiti yeWadi ukuya kukungafani kuluntu ekuhlaleni . Le modyuli igxilisa kukungafani kuluntu ekuhlaleni nendlela okunegalelo ngayo kuphuhliso . Bonke ababandakanyekayo ngakumbi kulawulo lwengingqi lokuthatha inxaxheba kudingeka ukuba babe nolwazi olusisiseko ngorhulumente wengingqi , iinjongo zakhe , nemisebenzi yakhe . IiKomiti zeWadi zinganceda ngokunika ulwazi kubahlali . Yintoni oyenzayo ekwenza kube lula ukuthetha nabo ? Ulawulo lukamasipala lunamagosa aseburhulumenteni kamasipala . Amagosa kamasipala aseburhulumenteni aphethe ulawulo anoxanduva lokubonelela abahlali ngeenkonzo zikamasipala . Amagosa , ngakumbi akumanqanaba aphezulu olawulo , aqeshwe ngenxa yezakhono nolwazi lawo . Uhlalutyo lweempiliso sisixhobo esisiseko senkqubo ye-CBP kuba lwakha ingqiqo ngeempiliso zamaqela ezentlalo ahluka-hlukeneyo eluntwini , kubandakanywa impahla yabo exabisekileyo , imiceli-mngeni , iziphumo namathuba anqwenelekayo . Imiceli-mngeni neziphumo ziya kwenza isiseko sokwenza izicwangciso . I-ofisi yophuhliso : Esi sesinye seziphumo ezibaluleke kakhulu ekusekeni iMasincedane Development Corporation . IMasincedane inikezela uphuhliso neenkonzo zenkxaso kuluntu kummandla , ukuquka idesika yamashishini asakhulayo , iziko leegadi zenkxaso zoluntu kunye neziko leengcebiso elinikezela inkxaso kwezomthetho nasentlalweni . Ubume bayo njenge-Section 21 company kwenze ukuba ikhuthaze ngempumelelo inkxaso kwezemali , ukulawula oovimba nokuzama ukuphucula iimeko zengingqi . Ukongeza koku , ubukho bayo esizikithini sedolophu kuyenze yayindawo yokuqhagamshelana nee-arhente zangaphandle zophuhliso kunye noluntu lwengingqi . Ngelishwa , ukunqongophala kwenkxaso yemali kwiminyaka yakutshanje kunempembelelo engentlanga kwimisebenzi yayo . Ubhala phantsi abakhoyo . Ukuba nenkqubela-phambili enentsingiselo , ekhawulezileyo negcinakalayo ekunciphiseni ubuhlwempu nokungalingani kwiminyaka engamashumi amabini ezayo , uMzantsi Afrika kufuneka ulungise ixa elizayo , ukuqalela namhlanje . Esi sicwangciso sandlala indlela yophuhliso entsha efuna ukubandakanya uluntu , ulutsha , abasebenzi , abangaqeshwanga namashishini anobudlelwano norhulumente onobunakho ngakumbi . Injongo kukuphuhlisa ubunakho bomntu oyedwa nobelizwe , kudalwa amathuba abo bonke . Ngokubalulekileyo , isicwangciso sibethelela imfuneko engxamisekileyo yokuba nenkqubela-phambili ekhawuleza kakhulu kubuganga obuyintlaninge ekunciphiseni ngexesha elide ubuhlwempu nokungalingani . Ukwenziwa kogqithiso - ugqithiso lungenziwa kwilungu lebhunga kwiwadi okanye lwenziwe ngqo kwibhunga malunga neemfuno ezithile zoluntu . Ukuba uyakholelwa ukuba uphose igalelo kunobangela womsindo , musa ukucacisa oko , cela uxolo okanye uphendule xa omnye umntu sele ewubonisile owakhe umsindo .
