Kude kwenzeke oku , usenokungakwazi ukubamba ingxoxo eyakhayo . Ubudlelwane -Abahlali basebenzisana nebhunga baze banike igalelo ngokuhlanganyela ekucwangciseni nasekwenzeni izigqibo . Ekugqibeleni libhunga elinika isigqibo . Chonga uluhlu angena kulo umasipala wenu . Uphuhliso lwamaqonga eengxoxo othetha-thethwano kuluntu kummandla . Kuneendleko ezingakanani ukuqhuba unyulo lweWadi ? Ukwenza inkonzo yesipolisa ibe nobungcali . Inkqubo yokuziphatha yamapolisa nenkqubo yobungcali kumele zidityaniswe ukuphakamisa nokuqeqesha kwinkonzo . Ukugaya kumele kutsale umdla weengcali ezinokusebenza , ezinezakhono ngesixokelelwano esinemikhondo emibini ; esinye isesamagosa agunyazisiweyo ze esinye sibe sesamagosa angagunyaziswanga . Amancedo e-GEP enkxaso yobuchwepheshe aya kukunceda ukwenza iintelekelelo ezithile malunga nengomso leshishini lakho . Oku kuquka ukuqhuba uphando oluhleliweyo nolucwangcisiweyo lweenyaniso zonke ezifunekayo nedata , ukuqulunqa amaxwebhu omthetho afunekayo nokuhlola iingozi ezinxulumene nokuqhuba ishishini lakho ngempumelelo . Nika abathathi-nxaxheba imizuzu eli-10-15 yokuqwalasela imibuzo . Imikhethe enzima kumele ukuba yenziwe . Ukuphakamisa ukudalwa kwemisebenzi kulinganiso olukhulu , ukusebenza kweshishi lezemisebenzi kumele kuphucuke . IKhomishoni yenza iingcebiso ezijolise ekuncedeni abaselula bangene kwishishini lezabasebenzi , ithothomalisa imithetho yamashishini amancinci , kuncitshiswa ukungavani nongquzulwano , nokucacisa iinkqubo zokugxothwa nokungaziphathi kakuhle . Ingqwalasela engakumbi kufuneka nayo inikezelwe kuqeqesho oluqhubekayo kubasebenzi abakhoyo nokubonelela ngamakhondo obungcali kubo bonke abasebenzi . Urhulumente wengingqi kufuneka anike ingxelo kuluntu yokuba isetyenziswa njani na imali abanayo . Benza oku ngokwenza iingxelo eziphicothiweyo zezimali zifumaneke . Ingcinga esoloko imi yintetho equkanisayo malunga neqela labantu okanye iziganeko . Nayiphi na inkcazelo malunga nodidi lwabantu kulindelekile ukuba ibe yingcinga esoloko imi . Iingcinga ezisoloko zimi azisoloko zichitha kwaye abantu abaninzi bayakholelwa kwezinye iingcinga ezisoloko zimi . . . Amalungu ebhunga ngabantu abakhethwe ngabavoti kwaye bamele bona abavoti kwibhunga likamasipala . Bakhethwa qho emva kweminyaka emihlanu ukuba bahlale kwibhunga likamasipala . Izindlu noluntu . Ukutya okufanelekileyo nedayethi , ingakumbi kubantwana abangaphantsi kweminyaka emithathu , kuyimfuneko kubume bomzimba obulungileyo nokuphuhla kwengqondo . IKhomishoni yenza iingcebiso kwisondlo somntwana , inceda abazali neentsapho ekuqhawuleni isangqa sobuhlwempu , nokubonelela olona lungiselelo lungcono kubantwana abaselula - kuquka nengcebiso yokuba umntwana ngamnye kumele abe nobuncinane neminyaka emibini yokuhamba isikolo sangaphambili . UMBUZO 3 Ingaba unalo uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwarhoqo ngenyanga ? Abanikezeli beenkonzo bagcinelwe iiprojekthi ezizodwa , umz. ulwakhiwo lweendlela , kwaye kufuneka kubanjwe uthethwano nabo ukuze bagcinwe besazi malunga neemfuno zoluntu kummandla . Umsebenzi wabo kukunikezela iinkonzo abanezivumelwano zokuba bazinikezele . Intlanganiso eyandulela ukwenziwa kwesicwangciso yenziwa njengengxoxo nabameli abavela kubahlali , kubandakanywa uceba , iKomiti yeWadi , iinkokeli zezimvo , iinkokeli zomthonyama namanye amaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya afanelekileyo . Kweli nqanam , umxolelanisi uququmbela inkqubo . Intshayelelo - injongo yalo mgangatho kukuphuhlisa ukuthembana nokuzingca kwamaqela kwinkqubo . Ngexesha lalo mgangatho , onke amaqela ( ukuquka nomxolelanisi ) avumelana ngemithetho esisiseko kwinkqubo . Umzekelo , amaqela avumelana ngokuba ngexa elinye iqela ligqithisa ingxelo yalo , lingenza njalo ngaphandle kokuphazamiseka . Umxolelanisi - umbhexeshi ngumncedi kwaye angafuna ukungenelela ukuqinisekisa ukuba inkqubo ifezekisa isiphumo esifunekayo . Umbhexeshi ikwangumsombululi wongquzulwano . Icandelo 195 ( e ) - ngokwemigqaliselo yeenqobo ezisisiseko nemithetho-siseko , kurhulumente wolawulo loluntu - izidingo zabantu kufuneka ziqwalaselwe , kwaye uluntu kufuneka lukhuthazwe ukuba luthathe inxaxheba xa kuqulunqwa umgaqo-nkqubo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi nababhexeshi be-CBP abazalise amacwecwe ohlalutyo lweempiliso abamba ingxoxo yamaqela . Ukwenziwa kohlahlo lwabiwo-mali olungcono kuphucula unikezelo lweenkonzo . Isicwangciso esimanyanisiweyo , uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali nokubeka iliso kumsebenzi wonikezelo lweenkonzo komeleza uthungelwano phakathi kweenkonzo ezinikezelwa lisebe kunye nenzuzo namaxabiso ezi nkonzo . Imilinganiselo yomsebenzi yenza ukungabinakhethe noxanduva oluphuculweyo kulawulo nokusetyenziswa koovimba bakarhulumente ngokunyanisekileyo . Ibakala 3 lijolisa ingxam yokuqulunqwa kwesicwangciso . Ukuqhuba inkqubo yenyathelo ngenyathelo , abahlali bathatha iinkcukacha ezihlanganiselweyo neziphumo bazishiya-shiyanise ngokokuba phambili kwazo baziqukanise zibe ngumbono , inkcazelo yenjongo , izicwangciso-buqili , iiprojekthi nemisebenzi ukuze kuphuculwe ubomi babahlali . Ukwandisa iinkqubo zengqesho zikawonkewonke kubathathi-nxaxheba abasisigidi esi-1 ngowama-2015 nezigidi ezi-2 ngowama-2020 . Njengoko inani lemisebenzi kumacandelo asemthethweni nangekho semthethweni lisanda , iinkqubo zemisebenzi kawonkewonke ingathotywa . Qala ngemizekelo yezinto ezenzeke ngokugqithiseleyo , umzekelo , owona nyaka ubumbi kakhulu , ngabaphi abantu abanokunxulumana nale mizekelo ngokweqondo lobuzaza . Uxanduva lokunika inkcazo : Ukubonisa ukuba izinto ezizizibonelelo zisetyenziswa ngentelekelelo nangokohlobo ebicetywe ngalo iprojekthi phaya ekuqaleni nangokwezivumelwano ezihamba nenkxaso-mali . IKomiti yeWadi inoceba nabantu abalishumi abangabavoti kwiwadi nabanyulwe ngabahlali ababasebenzelayo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufanele amele amacandelo ahlukeneyo abahlali ( oomama , ulutsha , abahlali abangasiwaso , njl. ) Ubulungu bawo kwezopolitiko mabungaphembeleli ukunyulwa kwabo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi athatha inxaxheba ngokuzithandela . . . Ukuvandlakanya iprojekthi - ukubeka iliso nokuvandlakanya kusetyenziswa ezo ziphumo bekuthe kwajoliswa kuzo ekujongeni ukuba ngaba iprojekthi iqhuba njani na , zeziphi na iingxaki ezithe zavela kwaye ingahlengahlengiswa njani na le ndlela kusetyenzwa ngayo . Indawo yoogobityholo yakhiwe kufuphi nesitishi sombane . Amalungu oogobityholo aba neentloko eziqaqambayo nezifo zesifuba ezisoloko zithe gqolo . Bayathandabuza ukufuduka kuba kuba kwindawo abasebenza kuyo . Impendulo : IKomiti yeWadi igqibe ekuthatheni le meko iyise enkundleni . Umntu obhexesha inguqulelo - iKomiti yeWadi ibandakanya uluntu jikelele ekwenzeni isigqibo ngemigaqo-nkqubo karhulumente wengingqi nezicwangciso njengoko ukuthatha inxaxheba kwabahlali kubalulekile ekumiseni iimfuno zoluntu kumanqanam ewonke kwinkqubo yocwangciso . Yahlula abathathi-nxaxheba babe ngamaqela amancinci lize iqela ngalinye libe nombuzo kwedweliswe ngezantsi . Njengoko imibuzo imithathu kuphela , amanye amaqela aya kuphendula imibuzo efanayo . Ezinye iiprojekthi ezichongwe ngenkqubo ye-CBP maziphuhliswe zibe zizindululo ezinikelwa kwi-IDP kuba ziqulethe iinkcukacha ezixabisekileyo malunga neemfuno zabahlali ngokunjalo nezisombululo eziyiliweyo ezineengcambu ezendele kubahlali , kodwa zisenokuba nkulu zingakwazi kufezekiswa kwinqanaba lewadi . Esi sishwankathelo sichaza indlela ekuphuhliswa ngayo iminikelo engeniswa kwi-IDP . Ukukhethwa kwamaphulo neeprojekthi nokucwangciswa kwazo ngokokushiyana kwazo ngokubaluleka kuyimfuneko kakhulu ekuqinisekiseni ukuba ziyafikelelwa iziphumo eziya kuthi zibe lulutho kakhulu kubahlali . Ngawaphi amaqonga eengxoxo zabahlali iKomiti yeWadi efuna ukuba afumane umelo , efana nemibutho yezempilo okanye yabahlali ? Ikhontrakthi yenkonzo sisivumelwano phakathi kukamasipala nomnikezeli wenkonzo ekunikezeleni umba othile wenkonzo kamasipala kwixesha elifutshane ( kunyaka okanye iminyaka emibini ) . Umasipala unikezela uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali aze abeke iliso kumsebenzi womnikezeli wenkonzo ukuqinisekisa ukuba usemgangathweni omhle nakuhlahlo lwabiwo-mali olwabiweyo . Ikomiti yesigqeba esidityanelweyo yonyulwa libhunga nekomiti kasodolophu eyonyulwe ngusodolophu wesigqeba . Zombini ezi komiti zilawulwa ngusodolophu . Ezi komiti ziqulathe amalungu ebhunga aneepotfoliyo ezizodwa . Oonomakhaya bonke bafuna ukuba banikwe uqeqesho kulondolozo lwasemakhaya . Baya kuthi ke basakuba beqeshiwe kufuneke ukuba kubekho uchintsana abamnikwayo kwakunye nento yokutya . Urhulumente ophuhlisayo ulwa oonobangela abendeleyo bobuhlwempu nokungalingani . Urhulumente ophuhlisayo woMzantsi Afrika uya kungenelela ekuxhaseni nokukhokela uphuhliso ukuze iinzuzo ezifunyenwe zijikeleza kulo lonke uluntu ( ingakumbi kwabahlelelekileyo ) , nokwakha imvumelwano ukuze imidla kazwelonke yexesha elide yoyise amaxhala amacandelo , exesha elifutshane . Kwinxalenye yokuqala yeBakala 4 CBP abathathi-nxaxheba banikwa izikhokelo zezinto ezinokwenzeka malunga nezindululo eziza kungenisa kwi-IDP namacwecwe emiba yeeprojekthi enokufuna inkxaso yangaphandle . Uphuhliso lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwengxowa-mali yewadi ngokwengqiqo kamasipala luvumela abahlali ukuba bahambele phambili kwangoko ngesicwangciso sabo , kuyaxoxwa ngalo . Inxalenye yesibini yeBakala 4 igxininisa ukuba isicwangciso samanyathelo esinobucukubhede sibalulekile ekwenzeni isicwangciso sibe yinto ekhoyo . Iphawula ngendlela iiprojekthi ekufuneka zicazululwe ngayo zibe sisicwangciso samanyathelo senyathelo emva kwelinye esichaza indlela yokubhala amaxwebhu esicwangciso . Ibakala liphetha ngokungenisa isiswangciso esigqityezelweyo kumphathi we-CBP ukwenzela ulwamkelo lohlahlo lwabiwo-mali ngokwengqiqo kamasipala . Sakuba samkelwe kufuneka kulungiselelwe intlanganiso yengxelo ebuyiswayo kubahlali ukuze bagcinwe benolwazi olutsha . Oovimba bakamasipala basetyenziswa ekumanyaniseni imimandla esemaphandleni nemimandla esezidolophini kwakunye nokwandisa iinkonzo kubantu abathwaxwa yindlala . Abathathi-nxaxheba babelana ngamava abo abanawo ngokunxulumene nonikezelo lweenkonzo , ezintle noba zimbi . Umthathi-nxaxheba omnye okanye ababini yenza ukuba abelane nabanye ngamava akhe uze ubabuze ukuba kufuneka kwenziwe ntoni na ukuphucula oku , ukuba amava ebengamahlanga . Sebenzisa amanqaku ezifundo kwiSahluko 2 , 2.2 ukukuncedisa emva kokuba ufumene ingxelo esuka kumaqela . Kukho iintlobo ezininzi ezahlukeneyo zolawulo lweprojekthi ezisetyenziswayo kwicandelo lophuhliso . Ezi zidla ngokwahluka kwiimodeli ezisetyenziswa kushishino . Kwakhona zidla ngokwahluka phakathi kwamazwe . Kumxholo waseMzantsi Afrika akukho modeli yecandelo loluntu emisiweyo kwaye kuya kubakho umahluko nakwiimodeli ezisetyenziswa ngamasebe karhulumente ahlukeneyo . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufanele azi ngolawulo lomjikelo weprojekthi nanjengoko le modeli isoloko isetyenziswa . Ukuhlahlelwa namagama ezigaba zomjikelo weprojekthi zingahluka ngokuxhomekeke kwiarhente yenkxaso-mali okanye isebe likarhulumente . Abemi badlala indima ebalulekileyo kwizigqibo ezichaphazela ubomi babo nokuqinisekisa ukuba iinkokeli ezinyuliweyo zifezekisa indima nemisebenzi yazo . Oku kudlulela ngaphaya kokuvota kunyulo . Ukuthatha inxaxheba ngokusebenzayo kuthetha ukuba abantu badlala indima ebalulekileyo phakathi konyulo . Kuwo onke amacandelo karhulumente abemi kufuneka baqinisekise ukuba baba negalelo kwiingxoxo ezimalunga nokuyilwa kwemithetho emitsha ngokubakho kudliwano-ndlebe loluntu jikelele okanye ukuzisa ngaphambili igalelo . UMBUZO 1 Yeyiphi indima yakho njengelungu leKomiti yeWadi kwinkqubo yohlahlo lwabiwo-mali ? Thatha iimpendulo . Kwiqela lilonke ncamathisela iitheyibhile zamaqela onke eludongeni ze ukhethe amanqaku afanayo kwitheyibhile ngokusebenzisa imibuzo yengxoxo ekuMsebenzi 4 . Isicwangciso masibandakanye iinkcukacha malunga nabahlali , iziganeko phakathi koluntu nezixhobo neendlela ezinokusetyenziselwa ukuyila ulwazi olufunekayo . Kwiphepha elilandelayo kukho umzekelo wesicwangciso nendlela yokusibhala . Oku kwenzelwa ukunika umfanekiso wesiqulatho sokuba isicwangciso sewadi kufuneka sibandakanye ntoni . UMzantsi Afrika unezabelo ezikhulu kumazwe ngamazwe kumaqela esinyithi seplathinamu , igolide , iidayimani , imanganisi , ilahle , intsimbi neyureniyamu . Kodwa kwiminyaka elishumi edlulilelyo , ezemigodi zasekhaya zisilele ukulingana nentsingiselo yokukhula yehlabathi ekuthunyelweni kwezimbiwa kwamanye amazwe ngenxa yokuba phantsi kwamaziko akhoyo , kuhambisana nobume bowiso-mthetho nenkqubo oluthintela utyalo-mali . UMzantsi Afrika ungazuza kakhulu kwimfuno ekhulayo yase-Asia yeempahla zorhwebo . Ukwenza oko kuthetha ukuphuculwa kwamanzi , uthutho namaziko ombane , nokubonelela ngenkqubo nengqiniseko yolawulo emandla kubatyali-mali . Oku kuya kubangela icandelo lemigodi ukuba lusasaze izakhono , imithombo , ukwazi nezimali ezifumanekayo , kwaye kuvumele urhulumente anyuse iingeniso zerhafu ngakumbi kunokuba esenza ngoku . Ukuhlaziya inkqubo yokucwangcisa kurhulumente kazwelonke , isicwangciso esingaququzelelwanga kakuhle saphakathi koorhulumente , ukuqhawuka koqhagamshelwano kwimida yoomasipala nokunyinwa kwezicwangciso zophuhliso ezihlanganisiweyo . Uluntu lukarhulumente luphakamisa uphuhliso nokumanyana koluntu . Kwiingingqi ezihlelelekileyo ezininzi , imibutho yezentlalo-ntle engeyiyo ekarhulumente ( NGO ) neminye imibutho esekwe kuluntu ziqhuba iinkqubo ezibalulekileyo zasekuhlaleni nengqesho . Ukwazisa inkqubo yesondlo kumabhinqa akhulelweyo nabantwana abancinci nokwandisa iinkonzo zophuhliso zabantwana abasebancinci kubantwana abaphantsi kweminyaka emihlanu . Yeyiphi imibutho yabahlali okanye amasebe kamasipala esifuna ukuyimema ukuze yenze ingcaciso kwikomiti yewadi okanye kwintlanganiso yabavoti ? Imihla apho umasipala eya kuba ebambe ulumano-ndlebe onokuthanda ukuba khona kulo , olufana nolwe-IDP nohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lonyaka . Unikezelo ngempumelelo lweenkonzo ezigcinekileyo zezibonelelo zomsebenzi luxhomekeke ekuqondeni okucacileyo kweendima noxanduva lwamaqela achaphazelekayo kumalungiselelo ezibonelelo zomsebenzi . Uxanduva lolawulo lomsebenzi lujongene nomanejala kamasipala . UMzantsi Afrika unemfuno yoqoqosho ebandakanya ngakumbi , olunamandla kakhulu noluneziqhamo zokukhula ekwabelwana ngazo ngokulinganayo . Ngowama-2030 , uqoqosho kumele lubekufutshane kwingqesho epheleleyo , luxhobise abantu ngezakhono abazifunayo , luqinisekise ukuba ubunini bemveliso bahlukene kwaye buyakwazi ukukhula ngokukhawuleza , ze lubonelele ngemithombo ukuhlawulela utyalo-mali olungabantu buqu nakwindalo . Imithombo yeenkcukacha ikopi Isicwangciso Sophuhliso Esimanyanisiweyo ( Copy of the municipality Integrated Development Plan ) , Isicwangciso Esisekwe kubahlali neSikhokelo se-IDP ( Community-Based Planning and the IDP Guide ) 2 ( i-AICDD Nemisebenzi Yophuhliso ) , i-PowerPoint ( ngokuzikhethela ) . Indima yamaqalela okuqeshwa koluntu , efana nenkqubo yemisebenzi yoluntu eyandisiweyo , nayo kumele iqwalaselwe . Nokuba uMzantsi Afrika uphumeza ukukhula kweGDP okungaphaya komyinge we-5 ekhulwini ngonyaka kwaye nengqesho inyuka ngokukhawuleza kwiminyaka elishumi ezayo , kuya kuhlala kukho imfuno yeenkqubo ezinjalo . Besebenza kwangezibini ezifanayo abathathi-nxaxheba benza isaziso esikhulu esishwankathela amaxwebhu emigaqo-nkqubo eyahlukeneyo nowiso-mthetho olwenza isakhelo sophuhliso kurhulumente wengingqi . Abathathi-nxaxheba kwakhona bayamanisa kwiiwadi zabo baze bachaze ukuba injani impembelelo yomgaqo-nkqubo nowiso-mthetho ekuhlaleni . Inqaku lokuqala kulo naluphina udidi longquzulwano kukuphawula ukuba yintoni na ungquzulwano . Ungquzulwano lusenokungabi yinto embi . Ungquzulwano lungasebenza njengomthundezi wotshintsho okanye inguqulelo . Eli gama ungquzulwano luvela kulwimi lwesiLatini elithi ' conflictus ' noluthetha ' ukulwa kunye ' . Umzekelo , ukuba udibanisa imicinga emibini , uyakwazi ukulayita umlilo wokupheka okanye wokwenza shushu . Indlela esiphendula ngayo kungquzulwano iya kuhlala imisa ukuba ungquzulwana luya kuhambela phambili na , oko kukuthi , lube ngamandla okanye luphele , oko kukuthi , lunciphe . Ungquzulwano oluninzi lungangasonjululwa kodwa ukuqwalasela iimfuno zabantu abathatha inxaxheba kuya kunceda ekupheliseni imeko enjalo . Ikomiti yeWadi inako ukuseka ikomiti eyonganyelweyo enye okanye ngaphezulu ize ibandakanye imibutho yabahlali kwezi komiti zonganyelweyo . Bonke abachaphazelekayo ngokwegunya ewadini bakhuthazwa ukuba bathathe inxaxheba kwiiKomiti ezonganyelweyo ezibalulekileyo kwimimandla yomdla wabo . Ukuba ufuna ukusombulula ingxaki ebangele ukuba ube nomsindo , jongana bucala nomsindo wakho kunye nengxaki . Lumkela ukwenza izigqibo ezibalulekileyo xa umsindo wakho ukulawula . Uluntu oluhlala kwindawo yamatyotyombe kufutshane nombindi wesixeko lugqithiselwe kwindawo entsha yolwakhiwo-zindlu emalunga neekhilomitha ezingama-20 ukusuka esixekweni . Esinye sezizathu ezisasazwe kule ndawo yamatyotyombe esibangele ukuba kufudukwe kukuba abanye babahlali kula matyotyombe banikwe amakhaya asisigxina ebebeqeshe kuwo . Abahlali abaninzi banomsindo njengoko bebekuludwe lwabahlali abalindele izindlu ixesha elide kwaye bathi kukho ikhethe kwabo bahlali ababelwe amakhaya ukuba bawaqeshise kuba oko kukhusela abanye abahlali ekubeni bafumane nabo amakhaya . Ngaxeshanye , bakwathi abafuni kufuduka njengoko kukude kakhulu kwidolophu kwaye uninzi lwabo lusebenza edolophini kwaye lungenayo imali yezithuthi . Abahlali bathi abasayi kufuduka . Kudliwano-ndlebe kunye namajelo eendaba , usihlalo wekomiti yabahlali uthe ukuba kwakuthethwe nabo ngaphambi kokwenziwa kwezi zicwangciso ngebekwazile ukucacisa ukuba kutheni na bengafuni ukufuduka kunye nokuba isizathu sabanye abahlali abanikezwe amakhaya sokuba baqeshise ngamakhaya abo kukuba kuduru kakhulu kubo ukuya emsebenzini yonke imihla . IKhomishoni iqinisela isicwangciso samanqaku asixhenxe athiwe thaca sisixokelelwano sobulungisa obujongene nolwaphulo-mthetho , esixoxwe ngokuthe vetshe kwisiqendu se-12 . Isicwangciso sixhasa injongo karhulumente yokutshintshela ngokuthe chu imithombo karhulumente isiwe kutyalo-mali oluthi lubumbe kwakhona uqoqosho , lwenze banzi amathuba nokwandisa ubunakho . Ngenxa yoko , ezinye iinxenye zohlahlo-lwabiwo mali lukazwelonke ziya kufuna ukukhula ngokuthe chu . Ukuququzelela ukuthabatha inxaxheba kuza kubandakanya abachaphazelekayo abohlukeneyo ngamaxesha ahlukeneyo njengamavolontiya , imibutho yasekuhlaleni , imibutho yobudlelwane , amalungu asekuhlaleni , amagosa nabantu abamele ezopolitiko . Umsindo luvakalelo lwendalo emntwini noluvela ikakhulu xa abantu beziva besoyikiswa okanye behlaselwa . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi angazifumana ekwiimeko apho ajongene neqela labantu elinomsindo okanye umntu omnye , ngakumbi iiKomiti zeWadi ezisebenza njengothungelwano phakathi kukamasipala , uceba wewadi nabahlali . Abahlali bangaziva bekhathazekile baze babe nomsindo ngemiba enjengokusilela okanye ukungabikho konikezelo lweenkonzo okanye ukulinda emigceni ukuze ukufaka amabango okanye ukufumana amaxwebhu athile . Unxibelelwano olusebenzayo luquka ukwazi ukujongana nomsindo nezoyikiso . Njengoko oku kungumqukumbelo wale modyuli , phinda ubuye umva uye kwiingongoma eziphambili kwesi sahluko , wenze isishwankathelo ngeenkcukacha ezivela kuzo zonke izahluko , khona ukuze abathathi-nxaxheba bawuqonde ngokupheleleyo umsebenzi . Sebenzisa iingcaciso ezibhaliweyo njengezincedisi zakho . Indima yeengcebiso - ukucebisa nokuncedisa ucebaukuze azi ngemiba eqhubeka kummandla lize lona ligqithisele imiba leyo kwibhunga . Ulingano kwezengqesho namanye amanyathelo okulungisa kumele enziwe abeyimpumelelo ngakumbi ngokujolisa kubume apho ubunakho buphuhliswayo . Ukuphathwa ngokulinganayo kujongene nokulingana kweziphumo . Kubhekiselela ngokuphambili kubulungisa , kwaye kungafuna impatho eyahlukeneyo , okanye amanyathelo awodwa , kubantu okanye amaqela athile . Ukuphathwa ngokulingana kuqwalasela iimeko ezithile okanye iimpawu zomntu ngamnye , iqela , isondo , isini , iklasi , inkolo okanye ubudala . Kufuna ukunciphisa yonke imiqobo kumathuba ezoqoqosho nawezopolitiko kunye nokufikelela kwimfundo neenkonzo ezisisiseko , ngohlobo lokuba amadoda namakhosikazi obudala bonke , iimeko nezikhundla angafumana la mathuba kwaye azuze kuwo . Ukuphathwa ngokulingana ngokwesini kuthetha ubulungisa bokuphatha amakhosikazi namadoda , ngokweemfuno zabo . Oku kungaquka ukulingana kwempatho eyahlukileyo kodwa ebonwa ngokuba iyalingana ngokwamalungelo , iinzuzo , izibophelelo namathuba . Akwazi ukucinga kwangaphambili aze aphawule iinkonzo azinqwenelayo zoluntu lwawo kwimimandla kwiminyaka embalwa . Ii-IDP zikamasipala ziphawula iiprojekthi nezinemihla yokugqitywa komsebenzi ecacileyo nezalathisi zenkqubela-phambili . Indima ebalulekileyo yamalungu ebhunga kukongamela umsebenzi kamasipala ngokweenkalo ezingundoqo ekufuneka zifikelelwe . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi kufuneka aqinisekise ukuba aziqhelanisile nezalathisi ezingundoqo zomsebenzi neethagethi zomsebenzi nezisekwe kwi-IDP kamasipala wabo ukuze akwazi ukuvavanya inkqubela-phambili . Ukuba iwadi iquka indawo enkulu lungiselela iintlanganiso kwiindawo ezingaphezu kwendawo enye ukuze bonke bayazi into eyenzekayo . AMALUNGU EEKOMITI ZEWADI AYASEBENZISANA nelungu lebhunga kunye nabahlali . Ikomiti yeWadi inokukhetha ukwabela amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi iipotfoliyo . Oku kwenza kube lula ukusebenza nomasipala nokumela amaqela abahlali ngemibandela ebachaphazelayo . Kananjalo inxaxheba yeKomiti yeWadi ibandakanya ukwenza amalinge abahlali okufikelela kwiinkalo ebezibekiwe ayafezekiseka kwiiprojekthi abaziqhuba ngokwabo . Amaqela asebenzayo okanye iikomiti ezithe zamiselwa apha ekuhlaleni ukuba ziqhube iiprojekthi ezithile ziba nezikuvunayo kulwazi oluphambili lokulawulwa kweprojekthi . IiKomiti zeWadi zisungulwe zizisombululo zebhunga . Imisebenzi yeeKomiti zeWadi ixhomekeke ekudluliseni izisombululo ezicacileyo kwibhunga . Le yinkqubo egunyazisiweyo yokwenziwa kwesigqibo esidityanelweyo apho ahlangana khona amaqela , ngoncedo okanye ngaphandle koncedo lweqela elingelinye , ekufuneni isisombululo esamkelweyo kumaqela ewonke nokufikelela kwisivumelwano okanye ukusombulula eyona ngxaki okanye ukungavisisani . Ukulandelela nokunika ingxelo : makuqononondiswe ukunikezelwa kweengxelo ngeeprojekthi neenkonzo zikamasipala kwiKomiti yeWadi kwiintlanganiso zoluntu eziwadini zazo ukuze abemi bagcinwe benolwazi ngenkqubela nangeengxaki . Iingcebiso ezakhayo zokuphucula osekwenziwe mazenziwe , apho kunokwenzeka , abahlali bangafakwa ekusombululeni ingxaki . IiKomiti zeWadi kufuneka zidlale indima eyomeleleyo kulawulo lokwenziwa komsebenzi njengoko i-PMS isisixhobo esisebenzayo sokulandela umkhondo wenkqubela-phambili kamasipala ngokuchaseneyo neethagethi zomsebenzi nezalathisi zokwenziwa komsebenzi ezisekele zona . Oku kufuna intsebenziswano ekufutshane noceba wewadi nekufuneka lithethane neeKomiti zeWadi kuyo yonke imigangatho yolawulo lokwenziwa komsebenzi . Onke amasebe karhulumente , akazwelonke nawamaphondo , anyanzelwa ngumthetho okwiPhepha leNgcaciso-nkqubo yeeNguqu kwiiNkonzo zoLuntu , uMthetho ka-1995 ukwenza unikezelo lweenkonzo umba ophambili . IBatho Pele Handbook izama ukunika abaphathi emsebenzini ulwazi olubavumela ukuba basebenzise iinkqubo ezizodwa nezisisiseko zokunikezela iinkonzo . Urhulumente uxhomekeke kwicandelo loluntu ukunikezela iinkonzo ezifunekayo ngokwanelisayo nangokuqinisekileyo . Esi sesinye sezizathu ezenza ukuba iBatho Pele ihlale ibalulekile kurhulumente , kaloku yazisa zonke iinkqubo ' ukususela kwezesicwangciso-qhinga , onke amanqanam eSicwangciso soPhuhliso esiManyanisiweyo , uLawulo loKusebenza noLawulo lweMbuyekezo kwaye kufuneka ibe nobungqina obubonakalayo ngalo lonke ixesha umsebenzi karhulumente edibana nommi . Izimvo mazingashiywa kwiqondo elingangqaliswanga , kufuneka zicazululwe ngemisebenzi yenyathelo emva kwenyathelo . Ukuba imisebenzi ayingqaliswa ayinakwenzeka . Eli libakala lokugqibela lokuphuhlisa isicwangciso sophuhliso kwaye kufuneka sithathele ingqalelo uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwenkxaso-mali olufunekayo ngokwengqiqo ukuze isicwangciso siqhutyelwe phambili , sona esivela kwiziphatha-mandla zengingqi nakwiiprojekthi ekufuneka zifakelwe uqwalaselo kwi-IDP . Mhlawumbi olona phawu kubalulekileyo ukuluqwalasela kwizigaba zeprojekthi kukuba azihambi indlela engumgca wempuku ( engumgca othe tse ) , apho isigaba esithile siza kukhokelela kwesilandelayo , kungekho ndawo iza kuphindwa kwezi zidlulileyo izigaba . Ubuninzi bezigaba ziyaphinda-phindwa njengokuba uhamba nje umjikelo weprojekthi . Umzekelo , isigaba ngasinye kufuneka siqosheliswe phambi kokuba siqale esilandelayo Amandla abemi - abantu bayazimela izenzo zabo kwaye abaxhomekeki komnye umntu ukuba abamele . Umzekelo , kukho umngxuma ongagqunywanga endleleni kwaye uyingozi . Abahlali bagqiba ekubeni bahlangane banyule ikomiti ukuba ise le ngxaki ngokungqalileyo kwibhunga lesixeko . Ngeli xesha besalindile bafaka uphawu ukulumkisa abahlali . Bayawulandelela lo mba lide ibhunga liwulungise . Thetha ngokucacileyo ukuze wonke umntu akuve . Sebenzisa ulwimi olwaziwayo ngabantu othetha nabo kungenjalo baya kuphelelwa ngumdla koko ekufuneka ukuthethile . IKhomishoni yamaLungelo eNkcubeko , iNkolo noLwimi ikhuthaza umgangatho wokuhlonitshwa kwala malungelo ize inyuse umgangatho ikwaphuhlisa uxolo , ubuhlobo , ubuntu , ukunyamezelana nobunye kuzwelonke . Ngokusebenzisa isazobe kwiphepha lama-35 lamanqaku esifundo ( sebenzisa i-PowerPoint ukuba ikhona , kungenjalo sebenzisa amanqaku ezifundo njengomalathisi uze wenze isazobe kwifliptshathi ngebakala ngalinye ngexesha ) , chaza ukuba umjikelo we-CBP kufuneka unxulumane nalowo we-IDP . Khanyisa ukuba isizathu kukuba i-CBP izama ukuqinisekisa ukuba iimfuno zabahlali ziyachongwa kwaye ziyabandakanywa kwi-IDP . I-CBP ne-IDP ziinkqubo eziyimijikelo kwaye kufuneka ziqhelaniswe . Icandelo labahlali lifana nokwahlulwa kwabahlali abakhethelwe ukukhanyisa ukusetyenziswa komhlaba okungundoqo kwindawo leyo . Lichonga imibandela engqalileyo yezithuba nophuhliso ebonwa ibalulekile ngabahlali ewadini . Iinkqubo zogqithiso lwengxelo - Yeyiphi inkqubo ekhoyo yokuqinisekisa ukuba abahlali bafumana ingxelo yarhoqo malunga nemiba yebhunga nolwazi rhoqo ngebhunga kwakunye nengxelo esuka kubahlali ? UKUPHUHLISWA KWESICWANGCISO SOPHUHLISO OLUMANYANISIWEYO ( IDP ) ngoomasipala yimfuno kaRhulumente weNgingqi : Municipal Systems Act , 2000 . ISahluko 5 se-MSA , 2000 sifuna ' umasipala ngamnye amkele isicwangciso senkqubo-qhinga yophuhliso lukamasipala ' ( icandelo 25(1) ) . Isicwangciso siqhutywa kwiminyaka emihlanu kwaye siyinkqubo-sikhokelo ebanzi yophuhliso ngaphakathi kummandla . Ivavanywa rhoqo ngonyaka . I-IDP ikhokela isicwangciso senyathelo likamasipala kukwafuneka ( ngokusemthethweni ) ukuba iphuhliswe ngokucebisana noluntu kummandla . Ukungalingani ngokwesini kudla ngokuchaphazela ngokungqongqo amakhosikazi ngaphezulu kwamadoda . Oku kungqina umgqalelo wokuqala ngoondoqo koko kungalingani kunyathela amakhosikazi . Onke amasebe kazwelonke nawamaphondo kufuneka abalule ekwamisa ekujoliswe kuko ukwandisa ufikelelo oluqhubekayo kwiinkonzo zabo kwabo babengazifumani ngaphambili . Aqinisekise ukuba amalungu eKomiti yeWadi athatha inxaxheba kumaqonga eengxoxo othetha-thethwano . Inkxaso kumashishini amancinci ngoququzelelo olungcono lweearhente ezinxulumene noko , ukuphuhliswa kwamaziko ezezimali , nezifukamisi zoluntu nabucala . IBatho Pele inomfanekiso wokunikezela iinkonzo equka ukuzivuma ngokupheleleyo izidingo zabathengi nokuzimanya ' zonke njengomqulu ' weempendulo nezisombululo . UHLAHLO LWABIWO-MALI SISICWANGCISO SEZEMALI . Lumisa imisebenzi yonyaka-mali ozayo ngokuvelisa amaxabiso ale misebenzi nalapho uza kuvela khona umvuzo wokuhlawula iindleko . Ukwakha umoya wokuphendula ngezenzo zakho , okhululekileyo nowenza izinto elubala kulawulo loluntu okanye ukusebenzisa igunya loluntu okanye ukusebenzisa umsebenzi woluntu ngokuphumeza ilungelo lesenzo solawulo esinobulungisa . IBatho Pele yenzelwe ukubumba isimo senkonzo yoluntu ukuqinisekisa ukuba intsingiselo yeBatho Pele iyathathwa isiwe kwinkonzo enikezelwayo kubemi belizwe . Kuthatha ixesha elingakanani ukuba amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi adlale iindima zawo ngokuncomekayo ? Amathuba odliwano-ndlebe nabaniki beenkonzo abaphambili - mawamiselwe kuselithuba ukuqinisekisa inxaxheba ebanzi . Unxibelelwano yinkqubo apho kutshintshiselwana khona ngezimvo neembono . Ukuze abantu bakwazi ukunxibelelana ngendlela esebenzayo kufuneka bahlele iingcinga zabo , bazigqithisele ngokucacileyo kwabanye baze bakwazi ukumamela ngendlela enogqaliselo . Unxibelelwano olungasebenziyo lunokukhokelela kungquzulwano . I-ajenda yebhunga ixoxwa kwigqugula leqela kwizikhundla zeqela lezopolitiko malunga nemiba ekwi-ajenda ngaphambi kwentlanganiso yebhunga . I-Municipal Systems Act , 2000 imisela izixokelelwano zoomasipala ezenza ukuba bakwazi ukusebenza baqhubele phambili ukuya ekuphuculweni kwezentlalo nezoqoqosho phakathi kwamaqela oluntu lwengingqi kwaye kuqinisekiswe ufikelelo jikelele kwiinkonzo ezibalulekileyo wonke umntu anako ukuzihlawulela . Ukufunda isifundo : Ukubhalwa kwerekhodi ngokusesikweni ngazo zonke izinto ezithe zenzeka kumjikelo weprojekthi kuya kunika isiseko solunye uhlaziyo , kwaye kunjalo nje kuya kuba siso nesiseko sezifundo eziya kunceda nakwezinye iiprojekthi eziya kuthi ziqhutywe kwixesha elizayo . Iinkqubo zezicwangciso zeeprojekthi zisenokufuna ukuba ziguqulwe , kwaye ke kubalulekile ukuba kubekho uvimba weenkcukacha ekuya kumana kusiyiwa kudimbaza kuye . Esi sahluko sinika isakhelo esenzeka kuso isicwangciso esisekwe kubahlali . Abathathi-nxaxheba baya kuqwalasela iinjongo , izinto ezirheshiweyo ezinokwenzeka zokusebenzisa i-CBP , imithetho-siseko nentsukaphi yomgaqo-nkqubo malunga nale ndlela . Esi sahluko sinika abathathi-nxaxheba isiseko ekunokubekwa kuso i-CBP . Lubonisa , luxhasa kwaye lubeka kwimo eyenzekayo iingcinga ezisoloko zimi nokuqal'ugwebe kwiqela . Ucinga ukuba iqela lakho lenze ntoni esebenzileyo kakuhle ? Zinyanga ezintlanu amalungu eKomiti yeWadi egqibele ukubamba intlanganiso . Uceba lithi lixakekile , amalungu eKomiti yeWadi aziva engahoywanga . Ingxabano iyakheka phakathi kwamalungu eKomiti yeWadi nelungu lebhunga . Abahlali nabo bacinga ukuba uceba akabathatheli ngqalelo njengoko engazange ahlangana nabo okanye aphendule izikhalazo zalo . Uluntu luququzelele umngcelele oya kwiBhunga ayokhalaza . Isiseko sezakhono esandisiweyo ngemfundo engcono noqeqesho lomsebenzi . Ababhexeshi bakamasipala - basenokuvela kumacandelo ahluka-hlukeneyo kamasipala okanye kumagosa ezobuchule aseburhulumenteni avela kumasebe enqila okanye ephondo . Umsebenzi 4 Jonga uMgaqo-siseko , uze uchonge injongo karhulumente womanyaniso kunye nobudlelwane boorhulumente . Ubudlelwane nesitishi sikanomathotholo wasekuhlaleni kuza kunceda iiKomiti zeWadi ukunikezela abahlali ulwazi nokufumana iimpendulo . Eli nyathelo linika umfanekiso wabahlali , ngoobani abahlali , oko kukuthi , amaqela ezentlalo , iimvelaphi neentlobo zeempiliso zabahlali , imisebenzi engundoqo yabahlali nabaniki beenkonzo . Icandelo elikwisicwangciso sewadi lahlulwe ngokweenxalenye ezintathu . Eyokuqala , yintsukaphi yabahlali izimbo zemikhwa yabo ezingundoqo ; eyesibini , ngoobani abahlali ( amaqela ezentlalo ) nokuba ziintoni iimpiliso zabo , ukuze eyesithathu ibe yimisebenzi neenkonzo . Kutheni ucinga ukuba uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali lufanele ukufumaneka kumaqela abahlali ? Zininzi iindlela zokulawula imeko yongquzulwano . Kwesi sahluko siqwalasela indlela ekholisa ukusetyenziswa , indlela yokusombulula ingxaki . Amaqela ngamaqela achaphazelekayo kwiprowujekthi kufuneka akhangelwe , kuvandlakanywe nezakhono zawo . Le nto ke ithetha ukuthi iqela leprojekthi liya kuba namanakani okuba ngaba la maqela ngamaqela abachaphazelekayo anethemba lokuba siya kuba yintoni na isiqhamo sale projekthi , nokuba ngaba iqela ngalinye lifuna ntoni na ngakwicala lengxelo nokuba lingayinceda njani na iprojekthi le izeziphi na izibonelelo elinokunikezela ngazo . IBatho Pele asiyonkqubo esecaleni neyahlukileyo ingumthetho-siseko osisikhokelo kulo lonke unikezelo leenkonzo . Ngako oko , nokuba hlobo luni na lokulamla , nokuba luvela kwiofisi engaphambili okanye kwengasemva yokuphatha okanye luvela kunxibelelwano lwangaphakathi okanye kolwangaphandle , kufuneka lufumane ulwazi kumthetho-siseko nakumoya weBatho Pele . Iiprojekthi zinokukwazeka ukuqhutywa , into leyo ethetha ukuba iinjongo zinokukwazi ukufezekiseka naphantsi kwezo meko ziqhutywa phantsi kwazo nezakhono zabo bagunyaziselwe ukuyiqhuba . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwiikomiti namaqonga eengxoxo - amabhunga angaseka iikomiti zeengcebiso nezinye iikomiti namaqonga eengxoxo anjengeforam yophuhliso olumanyanisiweyo . IiKomiti zeWadi zingasebenzisa ezi zigqeba ekunikezeleni igalelo xa kusenziwa izigqibo ezichaphazela abahlali kummandla . Uluntu lwamaphandle aseMzantsi Afrika kumele lube namathuba amakhulu kakhulu okuthatha inxaxheba ngokugcweleyo kuqoqosho , ekuhlaleni nakubomi bezopolitiko belizwe , bexhaswa yimfundo enobulunga obuchanekileyo , ukhathalelo lwempilo , uthutho nezinye iinkonzo ezisisiseko . Ukuhlaziywa kabutsha komhlaba okuyimpumelelo , ukudala imisebenzi nokunyuka kwemveliso yezolimo kuya kubanegalelo kuphuhliso loqoqosho lwasemaphandleni olubandakanyayo . Ukubeka esweni : Abahlali bangacela umasipala ukuba atyumbe ikomiti yabathunywa babahlali ukubeka esweni iinkqubo nokucebisa umasipala ngezinto emazibekwe phambili ukwandisa nokuphucula iinkonzo . Amalungu eeKomiti zeWadi anganika inkonzo njengamalungu ekomiti . Ukwandisa okuthunyelwa kwamanye amazwe , kujoliswe kwezo ngingqi apho uMzantsi Afrika sele unomnikelo kuzo neenzuzo ezithelekisekayo , ekufana nemigodi , ulwakhiwo , ukwenza okunezakhono eziphakathi , ezolimo nokusetyenzwa komhlaba , imfundo ephakamileyo , ukhenketho neenkonzo zamashishini . Iziphumo ziinkalo zojoliso ezenza ukuba kukwazeke ukubeka iliso , ukuhlaziya nokuvandlakanya ukuba ngaba iprojekthi iyazifezekisa na iinjongo zayo . Ziziphumo izinto eziya kuthi zibonakalise ukuba ngaba isicwangciso siyakufuna na ukuhlengahlengiswa , nokuba ngaba zikhona na izifundo ezifundwayo eziya kusetyenziswa kwezinye iiprojekthi ezinokuthi ziqhutywe kwixa elizayo . Ukungafani : Indlela ukuthatha inxaxheba okwenziwe ngayo iziko nekwakhiwe ngayo kwenzelwe ukuba kwamkele ukungafani o.k.t. ngokuthatha inxaxheba ngendlela nangezithethe ezahlukeneyo . Nangona kufuneka ukuba kubekho isiseko esifanayo sokumisela ukuthatha inxaxheba okwenziwe iziko kweli lizwe , esi siseko kufuneka sibe banzi ngokwaneleyo ukuba singalungelelaniswa ukuba senziwe ngamaphondo nangoomasipala . Isikhokelo se-logframe sinika isishwankathelo seenkalo eziphambili kwiprojekthi ngendlela yesiqhelo . Ngoko ke sinceda abo banoxanduva lokukhangela ukuba ngaba umhlaba nolandelelwano ziyanxibelelana na kwindlela ezilandelelana ngayo okanye olo tyalo-mali luphakanyisiweyo . Yiya phandle uze uchazele oo-A ukuba kufuneka bacinge ibali umntu afuna ukwabelana ngalo kunye nomahlulelane wakhe . Iziphumo neenkqubo zoqinisekiso zinika isikhokelo sokuqulunqwa kwesicwangciso sokubekwa kweliso novandlakanyo esineenkcukacha ezithe kratya esiza kuqulunqwa sisetyenziswe ziimanejala zeprojekthi . Umgangatho : Kufuneka bathobelane nemigangatho kazwelonke ngokwezinga lezifundo namava . Ukuthatha inxaxheba kwababandakanyekayo kungumceli-mngeni kumasipala , kooceba bewadi , nakwiiKomiti zeWadi . Izikhokelo ezikwi-IDP Guide Pack ziqaqambisa imithetho-siseko yokuthatha inxaxheba . Le mithetho-siseko ingancedisa iiKomiti zeWadi ekunikeni inkxaso kumasipala ukuze athathe indlela efanelekileyo enze izakhiwo ezifanelekileyo ukuqinisekisa ukuthatha inxaxheba okusebenzayo . UKUKHETHWA KWEPROJEKTHI YOKUQALA isigaba esilandelayot kukuqulunqa isicwangciso , esinabileyo ngeenkcukacha , sokuba iprojekthi le iza kuqhutywa njani na . Esi sicwangciso ke kuye kuthiwe ukubizwa kwaso sisikhokelo soLawulo loMjikelo weProjekthi ( Project Cycle Management ) . Sivelisa isicwangciso somsebenzi , obuqalwe phaya kwiSahluko 2 , iSigaba 1 , esiba luxwebhu lokusebenza olucacisa ngokuzeleyo ukuba , kanye , kanye , yintoni ekufuneka yenziwe , iza kwenziwa ngubani , iza kubekelwa awaphi amaxesha , lusithini uhlahlo-mali lwayo . Isixhobo esisetyenziswayo ekuncediseni ngokucinga nakuqulunqo lwesikhokelo kuthiwa ukubizwa kwaso yi-Logical Framework Matrix , ethi ke ikholise ngokushunqulelwa kuthiwe yi-logframe . Ngokusebenzisa amagama aphambili , abathathi-nxaxheba bakha ingxelo yombono . Fundela abafundi umzekelo wengxelo yombono . Chaza ulandelelwaniso lwamagama ombono afanele ukukhanyisa ulandelelwaniso lweziphumo ezibekwe phambili zewadi . IsiCwangciso sobuTyebi obuHlanganisiweyo sinyanzelisa ixabiso lesithunzi elisebenzayo kwikhabhoni . Ukuvuselelwa kweemali zikarhulumente okuncedisayo kuyafuneka ukwandisa ixabiso kwikhabhoni ukomeleza ukusebenza koqoqosho olubanzi notyalo-mali kubuchwepheshe obunengeniso ngakumbi . Qonda unobangela womsindo wakho . Zama ukuphawula olunye uvakalelo oluvayo olunjengokoyika okanye ukukhathazeka . Ukuphumeza ulangazelelo lukarhulumente onobunakho nophuhlisayo , ilizwe kufuneka landise indima yokujonga yePalamente , uzinzise ukusebenzisana kulawulo lwepolitiki , kwenziwe inkonzo yoluntu ibe nobungcali , ukunyusa izakhono nokuphucula ukusebenzisana . Ukwafuna indlela esebenza ngakumbi nesebenza kakhulu ekulawulweni kwesixokelelwano sothungelwano loorhulumente ukuqinisekisa ukulingana okungcono phakathi koxanduva nesikhundla . Ngokulinganayo , urhulumente kufuneka alungele ukuvavanya , ukufunda kumava , nokwamkela iindlela ezahlukeneyo ukufikelela kwiinjongo ezinye . Amaqela enza le misebenzi eqinisekisa ukuba ayavumelana ngemiba ebaluleke kakhulu , aze agqithise ingxelo ngokwamaqela ewonke . Nika iqela ngalinye amaphepha efliptshathi neemakha ukuze azisebenzise ekwenzeni lo msebenzi . Umasipala kufuneka aphuhlise ii-KPI zeeyunithi zakhe zizonke , abasebenzi kunye nabanikezeli beenkonzo . IKomiti yeWadi asililo iqonga lezopolitiko kwiqela elinye lezopolitiko okanye iqela elithile , umgqatswa okanye iqela elinomdla wokuba lisetyenziswe . IKomiti yeWadi inikezela iqonga lokuvula iingxoxo ukuze isisombululo okanye isicwangciso senyathelo elithile sisekwe kummandla woluntu uwonke njengenzuzo ekunokufunyanwa kuyo . Indleko encitshisiweyo yokulungelana nemithetho , ingakumbi kwimizi-mveliso emincinci nephakathi . IiKomiti zeWadi zidlala indima ephambili kulungiso nohlaziyo ngokutsha lwe-NSDP njengoko isekelwe kwigalelo elisuka kurhulumente wengingqi . I-logframe inika isikhokelo sokuvandlakanya , njengoko icacisa kakuhle ukuba yintoni ekujoliswe ekuyifezekiseni ( iziphumo nenjongo ) , ezi zinto zifezekisiweyo ziza kuqinisekiswa njani ( iziphumo neenkqubo zoqinisekiso ) nokuba ziintoni na izinto ezingaphaya kolawulo eziphambili . Kubalulekile ukukhumbula ukuba amalungu asekuhlaleni asuka kwiinkcubeko , imvelaphi ngokobuhlanga , ulwimi okanye iinkolo ezahlukeneyo okanye amaqela ngokweminyaka okanye amanye amaqela anomdla . Xa uthetha , kubalulekile ukuqonda okwaziwa njengendlela yokuziphatha eyamkelekileyo kwiqela elithile . Sebenzisa ulwimi oluqondwayo ngabantu othetha nabo kungenjalo baya kuphelelwa ngumdla kwinto oyithethayo . I-HIV / AIDS ibe nempembelelo enzulu kwinani labemi , inyusa jikelele inani lokufa ngokubonakalayo ukusukela ngo-2000 ze yanciphisa umlinganiselo wamabhinqa akwixabiso lokuzala . Kukho iimpawu zokuba ilizwe liqalisa ukutshintsha kwimpendulo yephulo elisebenzayo lemfundo nonyango . Izinga lolosulelo lweHIV luzinzile malunga nomyinge we-10 ekhulwini . Usuleleko olutsha phakathi kwabantu abatsha lwehlile kwaye ixesha elilindelekileyo lokuphila liyanyuka . Nangona kukho ezi nzuzo , kuya kusoloko kukho inani elibalekayo leenkedama ze-AIDS nabantwana abafuna inkxaso kurhulumente nakuluntu ngamxhel'omnye kumashumi eminyaka ezayo . Izalathisi kufuneka ziphuhliswe ngokudityaniswa namaqela axhamlayo . Kunokwenzeka kuphela ukumisa izinto ekujoliswa kuzo kwinguqu yobulunga ukuba idatha esisiseko ikhona . Oku kufuna iimvavanyo-zimvo ezisisiseko . Kwiminyaka emininzi elandelayo uqoqosho lwehlabathi kulindeleke ukuba lukhule ngesantya esifanelekileyo . Kwezi meko , amashishini oMzantsi Afrika kufuneka acinge nzulu malunga nakuvelisayo , kwawaphi amashishini , kusetyenziswa obuphi ubunakho . Njengoqoqosho oluncinci oluvulekileyo , uMzantsi Afrika ungaphuhlisa iimveliso ezinomtyhi . Ukufumanisa isabelo esincinci semfuno yehlabathi kwiingingqi apho imizi-mveliso yasekhaya ingakhuphisana kunganempembelelo enkulu . Ngokomzekelo , uMzantsi Afrika ungayinkokheli yehlabathi kwizinto ezenziweyo neenkonzo zeshishini lezemigodi , apho unolwazi olomeleleyo . Oku kuyakwenza igalelo elibalulekileyo kushishino kumtyhi woshishino lwehlabathi . Ibakala 1 liqala ngokuqokelela zonke iinkcukacha ezifumanekayo ngewadi ukuseka imo ekubhekiselelwe kuyo yokwenza izicwangciso . Oku kubandakanya imicimbi ephambili ye-IDP , imimandla enokunikwa inkxaso-mali ngumasipala kunye neenkcukacha ngabaniki beenkonzo . Isishwankathelo esingezantsi sigqabaza ngendlela yokuqokelela olu lwazi . Ukubhexesha izimvo kubuchule bokuthatha inxaxheba kumasipala nezigqeba ezisekiweyo ekuthatheni inxaxheba koluntu . IiKomiti zeeWadi zisetyenziswe banzi njengendlela yokwenza isakhiwo sobudlelwana phakathi kukamasipala nabahlali . Xa kuhlanganiselwa i-IDP , iiKomiti zeWadi zidlala indima ebalulekileyo ekunikeni igalelo labahlali nakuhlolo lweemfuno olunokungxala i-IDP kodwa kananjalo kuncediseni kuphengululo lukawonke-wonke lwempumezo ye-IDP nakumgangatho wokusebenza kamasipala xa kuthelekiswa ne-IDP . Amandla anikeziweyo - Ibhunga lasekhaya linoxanduva lokwenza izigqibo nokuxhasa iiprojekthi ngemali . Nakuba kunjalo , banganikezela olunye uxanduva kubathunywa babahlali ukubanceda ukuphumeza umsebenzi . Enye yezona ndima zibaluleke kakhulu iKomiti yeWadi enazo kukufumana igalelo elisuka kubahlali nge-IDP nokuqinisekisa ukuba umasipala unalo olu lwazi . Oku kungenzeka ngokubamba iintlanganiso zikawonke-wonke okanye uvavanyo ngokungena kwindlu ngendlu ekuphawuleni imiba ephambili ekuhlaleni . Eli linqanam elifuna inyathelo elinjengempendulo okanye ekufuneka lenziwe . Umzekelo , impendulo ingaquka ukuthukisela okanye ukulwa okanye ukukhetha ukushiya le meko . Abantu bayaphendula kungquzulwano olunempembelelo ebangelwa yingqokelela yabo yezimvo nokukholelwa . Kuthelekiswa nemigangatho egqwesileyo yamanye amazwe , iziko le-ICT liphelele . Iziko lolwazi olusebenzayo oluphakamisa ukukhula koqoqosho nokubandakanya okukhulu kufuna ibroadband enamandla nothungelwano lokunxibelelana ngefowuni , namaxabiso asezantsi . Iinzuzo zoqoqsho nengqesho zogqitha iindleko . UVAVANYO LOKUQALA LWEMIGAQO-NKQUBO EKHOYO INGQINISISE UKUBA UMZANTSI AFRIKA UNEMIGAQO-NKQUBO UKUQINISEKISA UNIKEZELO OLUGCINEKILEYO LWEZIBONELELO ZOMSEBENZI NEENKONZO . AMALUNGISELELO EENKONZO ZEZIBONELELO ZOMSEBENZI KAMASIPALA EZINGAGCINEKANGA KENGOKO AZINAKUDITYANISWA NOKUNQONGOPHALA KOWISO-MTHETHO . I-Division of Revenue Act , 1997 sisixhobo sohlahlo lwabiwo-mali esinikeza iinkcukacha malunga nendlela ingeniso kazwelonke ( efunyenwe kwiirhafu ) yabiwa ngayo phakathi kwemigangatho karhulumente ekuxhaseni ukuzalisekiswa kweenkqubo ezahlukeneyo zikarhulumente . Iwiswa ngokusemtthethweni kanye ngonyaka . Ngaphezu kokukhuthaza inxaxheba eyiyeyona iphezulu , intlanganiso imele ithuba labahlali ngokubanzi ukuze iqonde izinto eziluncedo malunga ne-CBP . Amaqela amancinci abantu ababini ukuya kwabathathu abanomdla nobungcaphephe kwinjongo / isicwangciso-buqili / kwiprojekthi anikwa icwecwe lemiba . Uya kufuna iyure enye ukuya kwezimbini ngecwecwe lemiba . I-MUNICIPAL SYSTEMS ACT , 2000 , iSahluko 4 no-5 , sifuna ukuba amabhunga kamasipala aphuhlise iindlela zothethwano aze abandakanye abahlali nemibutho yoluntu . Oku kuxhaswa yiNkqubo-sikhokelo yoMgaqo-nkqubo kaZwelonke yokuThatha iNxaxheba kukaWonke-wonke , 2005 nocacisa ukuthatha inxaxheba kukawonke-wonke ' njengenkqubo evulekileyo nethembekileyo apho umntu ngamnye namaqela kwimimandla yoluntu akhethiweyo anokuthi atshintshiselane ngeembono nempembelelo kulwenziwo lwezigqibo ' . Esi sahluko siqwalasela ubuchule bonxibelelwano obunokuthi busetyenziswe ekuncediseni iiKomiti zeWadi ekukhuthazeni nasekwandiseni ukuthatha inxaxheba kukawonke-wonke . Ezoqoqosho : Ezi ke zizinto abanokuthi abantu bazisebenzise ekuziphiliseni , izinto ezifana nemali , utyalo-mali / ugcino-mali , izitora zombona , imfuyo , izixhobo zokusebenza nezinye izinto ezisetyenziswayo . Imimandla yasemaphandleni isenokuba neeWadi ezinkulu kakhulu kwaye abantu bathi saa kwiilali nasezifama . Imbalwa kakhulu imibutho esebenzayo . Ilali nganye okanye iqela leefama ngalinye belinokunyula ummeli ukuba anike inkonzo kwiKomiti yeWadi . Phambi kokuthatha eli nyathelo , ababhexeshi kufuneka babe nekopi yeIDP ukuze bakwazi ukuchonga imicimbi ephambili jikelele ye-IDP . Ukuba abathathi-nxaxheba banekopi ye-IDP , banike imizuzu emihlanu yokudwelisa iinkcukacha ezivela kumalungu uzibhale uze uchonge umba ophambili ovela kwi-IDP yabo . Chaza ukuba eli candelo lesicwangciso sewadi ligcina okwenziwe ngababhexeshi ukuphuhlisa isicwangciso nokuba ngubani oye wabandakanyeka . Nika iqela ngalinye imizuzu embalwa yokugcina amagama ' ababhexeshi ' namagama abanye abathathi-nxaxheba abangamalungu abahlali . Ukufumanisa ukuba yeyiphi imisebenzi efuna izixhobo zokusebenza zangaphandle okanye ukuba ingaba kubhetele isetyenziswe ngokwesikali sikamasipala . Kufuneka zona zifakwe kwi-IDP . I-CBP ixhomekeke kwinxaxheba yabahlali ukuze iinkonzo zisebenziseke ngokuncomekayo . Iqondo nobunzulu benxaxheba bubalulekile ekusebenzeni kwe-CBP . Ifuna ukuzinikela kwamaqela achaphazeleka ngokwegunya ukuba athathe inxaxheba ngokusebenzayo ukuze oku kukhuthaze amanyathelo nokuxhotyiswa ngamandla kwabahlali . Ikomiti yeWadi inelungu lebhunga leWadi nabantu abalishumi abangabavoti ewadini nabanyulwe ngabahlali ababakhonzayo . Amalungu ekomiti yeWadi mawabe nabameli ngokubanzi ngokwamacandelo ahluka-hlukileyo abahlali ( abafazi , ulutsha , amaqela abahlali abahlelelekileyo , njl.njl. ) . Ukuzimanya kwabo neqela lezopolitiko elithile makungachaphazeli ukukhetha kwabo . Amalungu ekomiti yeWadi athatha inxaxheba ngokwentando yawo . Iindima zesini zizimo ezifundwayo ekuhlaleni , kuluntu oluthile okanye elinye iqela lasekuhlaleni . Zilawula imisebenzi , imisebenzi noxanduva ukuze ke ibonwe le misebenzi njengeyamadoda okanye eyabasetyhini . Ithathwa ngokuba yindalo , kodwa akunjalo . Iindima zesini zichatshazelwa bubudala , iklasi , uhlanga , isithethe nenkolo , kunye nemo yejiyografi , ezoqoqosho neyezopolitiko . Kwakhona zidla ngokuba ziwacinezele amakhosikazi . Umzekelo , isondo lenkosikazi lenza ukuba ibe ngumsebenzi wakhe ukuba ancancise umntwana . Kodwa xa umntwana elunyulwe , isekwangumsebenzi wenkosikazi ukufunza umntwana kuba uluntu lulindele oko kuye . Le yindima yakhe yesini . Indoda nayo ingakwazi ukuwenza lula umsebenzi nanjengoko kungekho nto yebhayoloji eyithintelayo ekuyeni ezivenkileni , ekuphekeni ukutya nasekufunzeni umntwana . Amadoda amaninzi awawenzi umsebenzi wasendlwini nanjengoko ubonwa ngokuba ngumsebenzi wamakhosikazi . Abahlali beWadi A bebejongene nolwaphulo-mthetho olukhulu . Nangona abahlali bezichazile ezi ziganeko zolwaphulo-mthetho kumapolisa engingqi , imeko isaqhubeka . Abahlali bafake isikhalazo kwilungu leKomiti yeWadi kwingingqi nelithe lasigqithisela kwiKomiti yeWadi ukuba isiqwalasele kwintlanganiso yabo yokugqibela . IKomiti yeWadi nocebawewadi bagqibe ekubeni babize intlanganiso yabahlali . Entlanganisweni , kunikezwe inani leengcebiso ekuzameni nasekuphuculeni le meko nokunciphisa ulwaphulo-mthetho . Izimvo eziphambili ekuvunyelwene ngazo yaba kukudibana nebhunga lengingqi ekwandiseni inani lezibane kummandla njengoko ukukhanya kungekuhlanga kwaye uninzi lolwaphulo-mthetho lwenziwa ebusuku , kwakunye nokuseka iForam yobuPolisa ekuhlaleni ( CPF ) . Intlanganiso igqibe ekubeni kusekwe ikomiti encinci eququzelelayo nequka amalungu amabini eKomiti yeWadi , ilungu lebhunga nabahlali ababini . Abathathi-nxaxheba benza amaqela anabantu aba-4 ukuya kwaba-6 ze benze Umsebenzi 1 . Qinisekisa ukuba iqela ngalinye likhethe iqela lasekuhlaleni elahlukileyo kuluntu lwalo . UMkhuseli woLuntu udlala indima ebaluleke kakhulu ekulweni nasekuphandeni indlela yokuziphatha engeyiyo kwicandelo likarhulumente . I-ofisi yoMkhuseli woLuntu inamagunya okuphanda nayiphina indlela yokuziphatha kwimicimbi karhulumente okanye kulawulo lukarhulumente kuwo nawuphina umgangatho karhulumente nenokuthi ingabikho semgangathweni okanye enokubangela iimposiso okanye nawuphina umonakalo , ukuxelwa kwendlela enjalo yokuziphatha nokuthathwa kwamanyathelo afanelekileyo enyathelo lolungiso . IsiCwangciso soPhuhliso sikaZwelonke sisekelwe kuphando olumandla , uqhagamshelwano nokubandakanya . Logama singafezekanga kwaye singagqitywanga , sibeka iingcebiso eziluqilima ekusombululeni iingxaki zelizwe , nasekunabiseni ukubandakanywa kwabemi baseMzantsi Afrika kuzo zonke iindidi ekwakhiweni kwekamva lethu . Amaziko anempumelelo nokhuphiswano ngakumbi . Amaziko okuququzelela imisebenzi yoqoqosho elungele ukukhula nokudala imisebenzi . Indlela yokwenza oko iya kuphuhliswa ukomeleza iinkonzo ezingundoqo ezifana nothutho lorhwebo , umbane , uthungelwano ngocingo namanzi , logama kuqinisekiswa ukumelana nokugcinakala . Ukwakhiwa komgaqo wamalahle omtsha ukuvulela ukugcinwa kwamalahle eWaterberg , kusandiswa iindlela zamalahle kwizibuko elikumbindi nokuphuculwa kwendlela eya eRichards Bay nendlela yothutho lwentsimbi eya eSaldanha . Amaqumrhu karhulumente wengingqi njengabalawuli abakhethiweyo ( kuquka umeya nequmrhu eliphetheyo ) , nomsebenzi wowiso-mthetho namabhunga . Inkqubo yolawulo lukarhulumente wengingqi ayivulelwanga uluntu , kodwa kwinkqubo yowiso-mthetho luvulelwe uluntu . Umzekelo osetyenziswayo wophuhliso kurhulumente wengingqi ugxininisa ekwenzeni izinto elubala , ozimelayo izenzo zakhe , obamba uthethathethwano , noququzelela ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu nobuqabane . Ingaba amanye amaqela awuqale njani lo msebenzi ? Amalungu eeKomiti zeeWadi anemfuno yezakhono zobuchule bokunxibelelana kakuhle ukuqinisekisa ukuba iyaqondakala into abayithethayo nokwakha ukuthembana phakathi kwabahlali nebhunga . Lakuba ibhunga liphengulule uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali ngokwengqiqo laza lavuma ukunika inkxaso kulungiselelwa intlanganiso yeqela elikhulu ukuze kunikwe ingxelo ebuyiswayo kubahlali phambi kokuphumeza . Ukucwangcisa ukuba iprojekthi le kuthenjwa ukuba iya kuza nantoni na - ngamanye amaxesha ke kuye kuthiwe le nto sisiphumo okanye ucwangciso lweziphumo kwaye ke ibandakanya wonke umsebenzi wamalungiselelo nowokukhangela ukuba iprojekthi le ingakwazeka na ukuqhutywa . Kubalulekile ukutshintsha izimo zengqondo kwakunye neengqiqo ezingakhiyo , iinkqubo zengcinga okanye imibono emi imi malunga nalo naliphi na iqela ukuba sifuna ukuhlonipha ukungafani kwenkcubeko . Iingqiqo zizinziswa ngezinto ezininzi . Jonga ulwazi olungezantsi nendlela iiKomiti zeWadi ezingatshintsha ngayo ezi ngqiqo ngendlela ezinokusabela ngayo kwimiba . UNkz . Smith ukhalaze amatyeli aliqela kumasipala ngomngxuma ovulekileyo esitalatweni sakhe . Izibane ezisesitalatweni azikhanyisi kakuhle kwaye amatyeli amathathu abantu ababuya emsebenzini sekuhlwile batshona okanye baphantse ukutshona kulo mngxuma . Abahlali baxhalabile kuba hleze kuwele umntwana ngaphakathi kwaye angasweleka . Ufaka isikhalazo kumasipala . Lo mba uqwalaselwa ngokukhawuleza . Ukudala amajelo onxibelelwano asesikweni angakhethi cala ngokunjalo njengomahlulelane wentsebenziswano phakathi kwabahlali nebhunga . IBhunga lenze isisombululo sokufakela imitha yamanzi endlwini emva kokudlaliswa ngamanzi . Ikhontraka kufuneka iqeshiwe ukwenza lo msebenzi . IKomiti yeWadi kamasipala i-ABC ihlala njalo izimasa iintlanganiso zebhunga . IKomiti yeWadi ibhale uluhlu lwamagama amalungu eKomiti yeWadi nemihla ekufuneka azimase ngayo iintlanganiso zebhunga . La malungu afumana iikopi zemizuzu aze babelane ngolwazi kunye namanye amalungu . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi agqithisa ingxelo rhoqo kubahlali . Amalungu eKomiti yeWadi asebenzisa imizuzu yebhunga ukujonga ukuba izigqibo ezithatyathiweyo ziyalandelwa na . Baqhagamshelana noceba wewadi aze avelise imiba egameni labahlali noceba ukuba azise kwibhunga . Ukuba ayise ngaphambili kwibhunga . Umthetho oyilwayo wakutshanje woomahlulelane babucala eluntwini ( PPP ) wondlalwa aze amalungu eKomiti yeWadi enza amalungiselelo entlanganiso nabahlali yokuxoxa ngalo mba baze banikezele ingxelo kwibhunga . Ukuhamba kwemali ngalo lonke ixesha lokuqhutywa kweprojekthi le ( kuchazwe ngokwekota ngeenjongo zokulungiselela iminyaka-mali yabaniki benkxaso-mali abahlukeneyo ) . Amanqaku ku-3.2.1 ukuya ku-3.2.5 . Abathathi-nxaxheba bahlulwa ngokwamaqela amane . Bhala imibuzo kwifliptshathi . Abathathi-nxaxheba basebenze ngababini ( bathethe nomntu osecaleni kwakhe ) baze babonisane ngokuvakalisa izimvo zabo ( banike 10-15 yemizuzu yokuqwalasela imibuzo ) . Usibonda wonyulwa libhunga ukuba alungelelanise umsebenzi webhunga . Usodolophu wenza nayiphina imisebenzi esesikweni nemisebenzi egunyaziswe libhunga . Usibonda wesigqeba esilawulayo unawo onke amagunya esigqeba . Cacisa ukuba uhlahlo lwabiwo-mali luquka IINDLEKO NOMVUZO . IiKomitizeeWadi zingaba nenxaxheba enkulu eziyithathayo ke kwesi sigaba , njengoko zinokuyazi imeko yabo baza kuba ngabaxhamli kule projekthi nokuba ziintoni na iimfuno zabo . Kananjalo ziza kukwazi ukuncedisa ekuvandlakanyeni amaqela achaphazelekayo kwakhona ngexesha lomjikelo weprojekthi ngeenjongo zokuqinisekisa ukuba zikhawulelwa ngemfezeko iimfuno zamaqela achaphazelekayo . Ikomiti yewadi inqwenela ukwenza eziphi iiprojekthi ? Qwalasela izinto ezifana neeprojekthi zophuhliso loqoqosho lwengingqi , ukuqeqeshwa kwabaniki-lukhathalelo olusekwe ekhaya ? Ingaba sinako ukuzenza ezi projekthi neminye imibutho yabahlali ? Cinga ngamanqanaba oburhulumente nendlela abemi abanokuthatha ngayo inxaxheba kwibanga ngalinye . Zama nawe indlela yokuzola . Lumkela iimpendulo zomsindo . Ulwazi ngonikezelo lweenkonzo kufuneka lugqithiselwe kubanikezeli beenkonzo kunye nabo bafumana inzuzo kunikezelo lweenkonzo . Ukuba unikezelo lweenkonzo ezisemgangathweni kuyinkqubela-phambili , uluntu kwimimandla kufuneka lufundiswe malunga nabanokukulindela nokufumanekayo kubo . Ukwenza abemi bathathe inxaxheba ekubekweni kwenkqubo yembono yesithuba nokucwangcisa . Kukho abarhwebi abaninzi abathengisa ecaleni lesitishi . Kunezikhalazo ezivela kubanini beevenkile zokuba abarhwebi basezitalatweni abayihlawuli irenti ngako oko bangathengisa tshiphu impahla yabo nokuba bashiya ukungcola ecaleni kwendlela xa bapakishayo belungiselela ukugoduka . Sebenzisa u-POWERPOINT A ukubonisa amanqanaba e-IDP . Kungenjalo , xelela abathathi-nxaxheba ukuba bajonge kwiphepha 18 kumanqaku esifundo baze babhale inqanam ngalinye kwifliptshathi . Inkxaso kumashishini asakhulayo : Ngonyaka ka-1994 , i-arhente yoncedo yaseBrithani yaxhasa ngezimali ukusekwa kwedesika ye-LED . Injongo yale diesika ye-LED kukunikezela uqeqesho , inkxaso kumashishini asakhulayo kunye nemali-mboleko . Ngaphandle kweli nyathelo , amashishini asakhulayo kummandla afumene izinga eliphezulu kakhulu lokungaphumeleli ngenxa yokunqongophala kwemveliso yoshishino kule dolophu , imivuzo ephantsi yabahlali abaninzi , ukunqongophala kwezithuthi kubavelisi ukuze bathengise imveliso yabo kwezinye iindawo kunye nokunqongophala jikelele koqeqesho . Gcina ulwazi lulula kwaye uthethe lento ofuna ukuyithetha kuphela . Inxenye yendlela yethu kukhuseleko lwasekuhlaleni kungomvuzo wokuphila , oquka izikolo ezingahlawulwa mali , iinkonzo ezisisiseko ezisimahla , nothutho loluntu oluxhaswayo . Ukongeza ekudalweni kwemisebenzi ngakumbi kwicandelo labucala , ukwandiswa okubonakalayo kweenkqubo zengqesho yoluntu nazo ziya kunceda ekuqinisekiseni ukuba yimizi embalwa ephila ngaphantsi kwenqanaba lengeniso elichongiweyo . Ilungu / amalungu eKomiti yeWadi angeva ukuba amalungu ecandelo elithile loluntu ekuhlaleni ' ngabaqhathi ' kwaye ke ngoko naliphi na icebiso abalinikayo ukwenzela ukuhanjiswa kweenkonzo okanye iiprojekthi kufanele lingahoywa . UNGQALISE ( SPECIFIC ) - ingaba umgangatho wenkonzo uchaza ngokukodwa okulinganiswayo ? Okokugqibela ke , luya kubandakanya nokuqosheliswa kweprojekthi leyo , ukuvandlakanya umgangatho wayo okanye wenkonzo leyo nokuqoshelisa iikhontrakthi nohlahlo-mali .
